def _setting_item(factory, **kwargs):
    link_alias = kwargs.pop("link_alias", None)
    item = factory(**kwargs)
    if link_alias is not None:
        try:
            setattr(item, "link_alias", str(link_alias))
        except Exception:
            pass
    return item


def Header(**kwargs):
    return _setting_item(_NativeHeader, **kwargs)


def Divider(**kwargs):
    return _setting_item(_NativeDivider, **kwargs)


def Switch(**kwargs):
    return _setting_item(_NativeSwitch, **kwargs)


def Selector(**kwargs):
    return _setting_item(_NativeSelector, **kwargs)


def Text(**kwargs):
    return _setting_item(_NativeText, **kwargs)


def Input(**kwargs):
    return _setting_item(_NativeInput, **kwargs)


def _get_private_field_silent(obj, name, default=None):
    try:
        if obj is None or not name:
            return default
        cls = obj.getClass()
        while cls is not None:
            try:
                fld = cls.getDeclaredField(name)
                fld.setAccessible(True)
                return fld.get(obj)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                cls = cls.getSuperclass()
            except Exception:
                cls = None
        return default
    except Exception:
        return default

_PINNED_LANG_CODES = ("en", "pt", "ru")
_PINNED_LANG_OPTIONS = []
_SORTABLE_LANG_OPTIONS = []
for _lang_name, _lang_code in OLD_LANG_OPTIONS:
    if _lang_code in _PINNED_LANG_CODES:
        _PINNED_LANG_OPTIONS.append((_lang_name, _lang_code))
    else:
        _SORTABLE_LANG_OPTIONS.append((_lang_name, _lang_code))

LANG_OPTIONS = list(_PINNED_LANG_OPTIONS) + sorted(
    _SORTABLE_LANG_OPTIONS,
    key=lambda item: str(item[0] or "").strip().lower(),
)

PLUGIN_LANG_OPTIONS = [
    ("System", "system"),
    ("English", "en"),
    ("Portuguese", "pt"),
    ("Russian", "ru"),
]

    ("dynamic", "settings_translate_service_dynamic"),
]

LANG_CODES = [code for _, code in LANG_OPTIONS]


def _ji(v):
    v = int(v) & 0xFFFFFFFF
    if v >= 0x80000000:
        v -= 0x100000000
    return int(v)


class TLLiteChatCreateHook(MethodHook):
    def __init__(self, plugin):
        self.plugin = plugin
    def after_hooked_method(self, param):
        try:
            fragment = param.thisObject
            run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self.plugin._attach_apple_button(fragment))
            self.plugin._schedule_floating_sync(fragment, 0.18)
            run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self.plugin._ensure_chat_floating_menu_item(fragment))
            run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self.plugin._ensure_native_assist_cycle_ui(fragment))
            run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self.plugin._schedule_apple_stabilize(fragment))
            run_on_ui_thread(self.plugin._maybe_show_first_install_welcome)
        except Exception as e:
            self.plugin._dlog(f"chat create hook fail: {e}")


class TLLiteChatResumeHook(MethodHook):
    def __init__(self, plugin):
        self.plugin = plugin
    def after_hooked_method(self, param):
        try:
            fragment = param.thisObject
            run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self.plugin._attach_apple_button(fragment))
            self.plugin._schedule_floating_sync(fragment, 0.08)
            run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self.plugin._ensure_chat_floating_menu_item(fragment))
            run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self.plugin._ensure_native_assist_cycle_ui(fragment))
            run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self.plugin._schedule_apple_stabilize(fragment))
            run_on_ui_thread(self.plugin._maybe_show_first_install_welcome)
        except Exception as e:
            self.plugin._dlog(f"chat resume hook fail: {e}")


class TLLiteChatPauseHook(MethodHook):
    def __init__(self, plugin):
        self.plugin = plugin
    def after_hooked_method(self, param):
        try:
            self.plugin._floating_sync_nonce = int(getattr(self.plugin, "_floating_sync_nonce", 0) or 0) + 1
            run_on_ui_thread(lambda: (self.plugin._detach_assist_button(), self.plugin._detach_apple_button(), self.plugin._detach_floating_button(), self.plugin._cleanup_native_assist_cycle_ui()))
        except Exception as e:
            self.plugin._dlog(f"chat pause hook fail: {e}")


class TLLiteAvatarLongUserHook(MethodHook):
    def __init__(self, plugin):
        self.plugin = plugin

    def before_hooked_method(self, param):
        try:
            cell = param.args[0] if param.args and len(param.args) > 0 else None
            if self.plugin._handle_avatar_long_action(None, cell):
                param.setResult(True)
        except Exception as e:
            self.plugin._dlog(f"avatar user long hook fail: {e}")

class TLLiteMessageContextMenuHook(MethodHook):
    def __init__(self, plugin):
        self.plugin = plugin

    def after_hooked_method(self, param):
        try:
            if bool(param.getResult()):
                run_on_ui_thread(lambda: (self.plugin._inject_channel_summary_context_item(param.thisObject), self.plugin._inject_favorite_context_item(param.thisObject)))
        except Exception as e:
            self.plugin._dlog(f"message context menu hook fail: {e}")


class TLLiteFavoriteIncomingCellHook(MethodHook):
    def __init__(self, plugin):
        self.plugin = plugin

    def after_hooked_method(self, param):
        try:
            msg_obj = param.args[0] if param.args and len(param.args) > 0 else None
            if msg_obj is not None:
                self.plugin._maybe_translate_favorite_incoming(msg_obj)
        except Exception as e:
            self.plugin._dlog(f"favorite incoming cell hook fail: {e}")


class TLLiteFavoriteTranslationGuardHook(MethodHook):
    def __init__(self, plugin):
        self.plugin = plugin

    def before_hooked_method(self, param):
        try:
            msg_obj = param.thisObject
            if self.plugin._is_favorite_message_locked(msg_obj):
                param.setResult(False)
        except Exception as e:
            self.plugin._dlog(f"favorite translation guard fail: {e}")


class TLLiteSendLongClickHook(MethodHook):
    def __init__(self, plugin):
        self.plugin = plugin

    def before_hooked_method(self, param):
        try:
            enter_view = param.thisObject
            fragment = getattr(self.plugin, "_chat_fragment_ref", None)
            if fragment is None:
                return
            if not self.plugin._native_assist_mode_selected():
                return
            try:
                source_plain_text = str(self.plugin._get_compose_text(fragment) or "").strip()
            except Exception:
                source_plain_text = ""
            if not self.plugin._assist_can_open_for_text(source_plain_text):
                try:
                    run_on_ui_thread(self.plugin._open_plugin_settings)
                except Exception:
                    try:
                        self.plugin._open_plugin_settings()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                param.setResult(True)
                return
            if self.plugin._assist_native_button_opens_panel():
                try:
                    run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self.plugin._show_compose_assist_sheet(fragment))
                except Exception:
                    try:
                        self.plugin._show_compose_assist_sheet(fragment)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                param.setResult(True)
                return
            if self.plugin._native_assist_apply_and_send(fragment, enter_view):
                param.setResult(True)
        except Exception as e:
            self.plugin._dlog(f"native assist send long hook fail: {e}")


class TLLiteSettingsHeaderHook(MethodHook):
    def __init__(self, plugin):
        self.plugin = plugin

    def after_hooked_method(self, param):
        try:
            activity = param.thisObject
            items = param.args[0] if param.args and len(param.args) > 0 else None
            if items is None:
                return
            self.plugin._inject_settings_header(activity, items)
        except Exception as e:
            self.plugin._dlog(f"settings header hook fail: {e}")


class TLLiteDialogsCreateHook(MethodHook):
    def __init__(self, plugin):
        self.plugin = plugin

    def after_hooked_method(self, param):
        try:
            self.plugin._push_on_dialogs_shown(param.thisObject)
        except Exception as e:
            self.plugin._dlog(f"dialogs create push hook fail: {e}")


class TLLiteDialogsResumeHook(MethodHook):

        self.plugin = plugin

    def after_hooked_method(self, param):
        try:
            self.plugin._push_on_dialogs_shown(param.thisObject)
        except Exception as e:
            self.plugin._dlog(f"dialogs resume push hook fail: {e}")


class TLLiteDialogsPauseHook(MethodHook):
    def __init__(self, plugin):
        self.plugin = plugin

    def after_hooked_method(self, param):
        try:
            self.plugin._push_on_dialogs_hidden()
        except Exception as e:
            self.plugin._dlog(f"dialogs pause push hook fail: {e}")

        self._live_preview_timer = None
        self._live_preview_generation = 0
        self._live_preview_prompt = None
        self._live_preview_data = None

        self._live_log_enabled = bool(self.get_setting("tlite_live_log", False))

        self._push_last_error = ""
        self._push_poll_timer = None
        self._channel_summary_request_nonce = 0

    def _looks_error_log(self, message):
        try:
            msg = str(message or "").lower()
            if not msg:
                return False
            error_markers = (
                " fail",
                "failed",
                " error",
                "error:",
                "timeout",
                "exception",
                "traceback",
                "denied",
                "unavailable",
            )
            return any(marker in msg for marker in error_markers)
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _append_live_log(self, message, level="info"):
        try:
            ts = time.strftime("%H:%M:%S")
            lvl = "ERROR" if str(level or "").lower() == "error" else "INFO"
            full_msg = "[{0}][{1}] [TranslaticaPro] {2}".format(ts, lvl, str(message or ""))
            self._log_buffer.append((lvl, full_msg))
            if bool(getattr(self, "_live_log_enabled", False)):
                self._update_live_log()
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _is_debug_on(self):
        try:
            return bool(self.get_setting("tlite_debug_logs", False))
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _native_log(self, message):
        try:
            msg = str(message or "")
            if self._is_debug_on():
                log(f"[TranslaticaPro] {msg}")
                self._append_live_log(msg, "info")
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _dlog(self, message):
        try:
            msg = str(message or "")
            is_error = self._looks_error_log(msg)
            if self._is_debug_on():
                self._append_live_log(msg, "error" if is_error else "info")
                log(f"[TranslaticaPro] {msg}")
            elif is_error:
                self._append_live_log(msg, "error")
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _wlog(self, message):
        try:
            if self._is_debug_on():
                self._append_live_log("[Welcome] {0}".format(str(message or "")), "info")
                log(f"[TranslaticaPro][Welcome] {message}")
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _push_on_dialogs_shown(self, fragment):
        try:
            self._push_dialogs_fragment = fragment
            self._push_dialogs_visible = True
            self._push_refresh_ui()
            self._push_fetch_if_needed(force=True)
            self._push_schedule_poll(immediate=False)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"push dialogs shown fail: {e}")

    def _push_on_dialogs_hidden(self):
        try:
            self._push_dialogs_visible = False
            self._push_cancel_poll()
            self._push_hide_view()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"push dialogs hidden fail: {e}")

    def _push_get_seen_ids(self):
        try:
            return set(json.loads(str(self.get_setting("tlite_push_seen_ids", "[]") or "[]")))
        except Exception:
            return set()

    def _push_set_seen_ids(self, seen_ids):
        try:
            self.set_setting("tlite_push_seen_ids", json.dumps(sorted(set(str(x) for x in (seen_ids or set()) if str(x or "").strip())), ensure_ascii=True))
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _push_mark_seen(self, push_id):
        try:
            seen = self._push_get_seen_ids()
            seen.add(str(push_id or "").strip())
            self._push_set_seen_ids(seen)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _push_is_supported_dialogs_context(self, fragment):
        try:
            if fragment is None:
                return False
            if int(_get_private_field_silent(fragment, "folderId") or 0) != 0:
                return False
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            cls = fragment.getClass()
            while cls is not None:
                try:
                    method = cls.getDeclaredMethod("getRightSlidingProgress")
                    method.setAccessible(True)
                    return float(method.invoke(fragment) or 0.0) <= 0.85
                except Exception:
                    cls = cls.getSuperclass()
        except Exception:
            pass
        return True

    def _push_cancel_poll(self):
        try:
            if self._push_poll_timer is not None:
                self._push_poll_timer.cancel()
            self._push_poll_timer = None
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _push_schedule_poll(self, immediate=False):
        try:
            self._push_cancel_poll()
            if not self._push_dialogs_visible:
                return
            delay = 1.2 if bool(immediate) else float(PUSH_FETCH_TTL_SEC)
            timer = threading.Timer(delay, self._push_poll_tick)
            timer.daemon = True
            self._push_poll_timer = timer
            timer.start()
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _push_poll_tick(self):
        try:
            if self._push_dialogs_visible:
                self._push_fetch_if_needed(force=True)
        finally:
            self._push_schedule_poll()

    def _push_fetch_if_needed(self, force=False):
        try:
            if self._push_fetch_inflight:
                return
            if not force and (time.time() - float(self._push_last_fetch_ts or 0.0)) < float(PUSH_FETCH_TTL_SEC):
                self._push_refresh_ui()
                return
            self._push_fetch_inflight = True
            def _worker():
                try:
                    req = Request(PUSH_FEED_URL_TRANSLATICA, headers={"User-Agent": "TranslaticaPush/1.0", "Cache-Control": "no-cache"})
                    with urlopen(req, timeout=8) as resp:
                        parsed = json.loads(resp.read().decode("utf-8", errors="replace") or "{}")
                    items = parsed.get("items") if isinstance(parsed, dict) else parsed
                    out = []
                    if isinstance(items, list):
                        for item in items:
                            if not isinstance(item, dict):
                                continue
                            push_id = str(item.get("id", "") or "").strip()
                            title = str(item.get("title", "") or "").strip()
                            description = str(item.get("description", "") or "").strip()
                            if push_id and title and description:
                                out.append({
                                    "id": push_id,
                                    "title": title,
                                    "description": description,
                                    "primary_text": str(item.get("primary_text", "Open") or "Open").strip(),
                                    "primary_url": str(item.get("primary_url", "") or "").strip(),
                                    "primary_clickable": bool(item.get("primary_clickable", bool(item.get("primary_url")))),
                                    "secondary_text": str(item.get("secondary_text", "Ok, thanks!") or "Ok, thanks!").strip(),
                                })
                    self._push_items = out
                    self._push_last_error = ""
                except Exception as e:
                    self._push_last_error = str(e)
                    self._dlog(f"push fetch fail: {e}")
                finally:
                    self._push_fetch_inflight = False
                    self._push_last_fetch_ts = time.time()
                    self._push_refresh_ui()
            threading.Thread(target=_worker, daemon=True).start()
        except Exception as e:
            self._push_fetch_inflight = False
            self._dlog(f"push fetch gate fail: {e}")

    def _push_next_item(self):
        seen = self._push_get_seen_ids()
        for item in reversed(list(self._push_items or [])):
            if str(item.get("id", "") or "").strip() not in seen:
                return item
        return None

    def _push_refresh_ui(self):
        try:
            run_on_ui_thread(self._push_refresh_ui_impl)
        except Exception:
            self._push_refresh_ui_impl()

    def _push_refresh_ui_impl(self):
        try:
            fragment = self._push_dialogs_fragment
            if fragment is None or not self._push_dialogs_visible or not self._push_is_supported_dialogs_context(fragment):
                return self._push_hide_view_impl()
            top_panel = _get_private_field_silent(fragment, "topPanelLayout")
            item = self._push_next_item()
            if top_panel is None or item is None:
                return self._push_hide_view_impl()
            if self._push_view is None or self._push_top_panel != top_panel:
                self._push_hide_view_impl()
                self._push_top_panel = top_panel
                self._push_view = self._push_build_view(top_panel.getContext())
                try:
                    layout_helper_cls = JClass.forName("org.telegram.ui.Components.LayoutHelper")
                    params = layout_helper_cls.createLinear(int(getattr(layout_helper_cls, "MATCH_PARENT")), int(getattr(layout_helper_cls, "WRAP_CONTENT")))
                    top_panel.addView(self._push_view, params)
                except Exception:
                    top_panel.addView(self._push_view)
            self._push_bind_item(item)
            self._push_set_top_panel_visible(top_panel, self._push_view, True)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"push refresh fail: {e}")

    def _push_hide_view(self):
        try:
            run_on_ui_thread(self._push_hide_view_impl)
        except Exception:
            self._push_hide_view_impl()

    def _push_hide_view_impl(self):
        try:
            if self._push_view is not None:
                parent = self._push_view.getParent()
                if parent is not None:
                    parent.removeView(self._push_view)
        except Exception:
            pass
        self._push_view = None
        self._push_top_panel = None

    def _push_set_top_panel_visible(self, top_panel, view, visible):
        try:
            top_panel.setViewVisible(view, bool(visible))
        except Exception:
            try:
                view.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if visible else View.GONE)
            except Exception:
                pass

    def _push_build_view(self, context):
        root = LinearLayout(context)
        root.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
        root.setPadding(int(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)), int(AndroidUtilities.dp(12)), int(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)), int(AndroidUtilities.dp(8)))
        bg = GradientDrawable()
        bg.setColor(0)
        bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
        root.setBackground(bg)
        for tag_name, size, color_key in (
            ("title", 14, Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteBlackText),
            ("description", 13, Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteGrayText),
        ):
            tv = TextView(context)
            tv.setTag(tag_name)
            tv.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
            tv.setTextSize(1, size)
            tv.setTextColor(int(Theme.getColor(color_key)))
            if tag_name == "title":
                try:
                    tv.setTypeface(AndroidUtilities.bold())
                except Exception:
                    pass
            else:
                try:
                    tv.setLineSpacing(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(2)), 1.0)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            lp = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(-1, -2)
            if tag_name == "description":
                lp.topMargin = int(AndroidUtilities.dp(4))
            root.addView(tv, lp)
        buttons = LinearLayout(context)
        buttons.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
        buttons.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
        lp_buttons = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(-1, -2)
        lp_buttons.topMargin = int(AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
        root.addView(buttons, lp_buttons)
        buttons.addView(View(context), LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, 1, 1.0))
        for tag_name, color_key in (("primary", Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteBlueText4), ("secondary", Theme.key_text_RedBold)):
            tv = TextView(context)
            tv.setTag(tag_name)
            tv.setPadding(int(AndroidUtilities.dp(10)), int(AndroidUtilities.dp(5)), int(AndroidUtilities.dp(10)), int(AndroidUtilities.dp(7)))
            tv.setTextSize(1, 14.22)
            tv.setTextColor(int(Theme.getColor(color_key)))
            try:
                tv.setTypeface(AndroidUtilities.bold())
            except Exception:
                pass
            buttons.addView(tv, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(-2, int(AndroidUtilities.dp(30))))
            buttons.addView(View(context), LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, 1, 1.0))
        return root

    def _push_find_tagged_child(self, root, tag_name):
        try:
            if str(root.getTag() or "") == str(tag_name):
                return root
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            for idx in range(int(root.getChildCount() or 0)):
                found = self._push_find_tagged_child(root.getChildAt(idx), tag_name)
                if found is not None:
                    return found
        except Exception:
            pass
        return None

    def _push_bind_item(self, item):
        try:
            for tag_name, value in (
                ("title", item.get("title", "")),
                ("description", item.get("description", "")),
                ("primary", item.get("primary_text", "Open")),
                ("secondary", item.get("secondary_text", "Ok, thanks!")),
            ):
                view = self._push_find_tagged_child(self._push_view, tag_name)
                if view is not None:
                    view.setText(str(value or ""))
            primary = self._push_find_tagged_child(self._push_view, "primary")
            secondary = self._push_find_tagged_child(self._push_view, "secondary")
            if primary is not None:
                primary.setOnClickListener(OnClickListener(lambda _v=None: self._push_on_primary(item)))
            if secondary is not None:
                secondary.setOnClickListener(OnClickListener(lambda _v=None: self._push_on_secondary(item)))
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"push bind fail: {e}")

    def _push_consume_and_refresh(self, push_id):
        self._push_mark_seen(push_id)
        self._push_refresh_ui()

    def _push_on_primary(self, item):
        try:
            if bool(item.get("primary_clickable", False)) and str(item.get("primary_url", "") or "").strip():
                self._open_external_url(str(item.get("primary_url", "") or ""), self._push_dialogs_fragment)
            self._push_consume_and_refresh(str(item.get("id", "") or ""))
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"push primary fail: {e}")

    def _push_on_secondary(self, item):
        try:
            self._push_consume_and_refresh(str(item.get("id", "") or ""))
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"push secondary fail: {e}")

    def _load_favorite_sender_ids(self):
        try:
            raw = self.get_setting("tlite_favorite_senders", "[]")
            data = json.loads(str(raw or "[]")) if isinstance(raw, str) else raw
            self._favorite_sender_ids = set(str(x) for x in data if str(x or "").strip()) if isinstance(data, list) else set()
        except Exception:
            self._favorite_sender_ids = set()

    def _save_favorite_sender_ids(self):
        try:
            self.set_setting("tlite_favorite_senders", json.dumps(sorted(self._favorite_sender_ids), ensure_ascii=False))
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"save favorite sender ids fail: {e}")

    def _load_favorite_incoming_cache(self):
        try:
            os.makedirs(_CACHE_DIR, exist_ok=True)
            if os.path.exists(FAVORITE_INCOMING_CACHE_FILE):
                with open(FAVORITE_INCOMING_CACHE_FILE, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                    data = json.load(f)
                self._favorite_incoming_cache = data if isinstance(data, dict) else {}
            else:
                self._favorite_incoming_cache = {}
        except Exception as e:
            self._favorite_incoming_cache = {}
            self._dlog(f"load favorite incoming cache fail: {e}")

    def _save_favorite_incoming_cache_now(self):
        try:
            os.makedirs(_CACHE_DIR, exist_ok=True)
            data = self._favorite_incoming_cache
            if len(data) > 800:
                keys = list(data.keys())[-800:]
                data = {k: data[k] for k in keys if k in data}
                self._favorite_incoming_cache = data
            with open(FAVORITE_INCOMING_CACHE_FILE, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                json.dump(data, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
            self._favorite_incoming_dirty = False
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"save favorite incoming cache fail: {e}")

    def _schedule_favorite_incoming_cache_save(self):
        try:
            self._favorite_incoming_dirty = True
            if self._favorite_incoming_timer is not None:
                return
            def _flush():
                try:
                    self._save_favorite_incoming_cache_now()
                finally:
                    self._favorite_incoming_timer = None
            timer = threading.Timer(1.0, _flush)
            timer.daemon = True
            self._favorite_incoming_timer = timer
            timer.start()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"schedule favorite incoming cache save fail: {e}")

    def _favorite_cache_key(self, text, lang):
        try:
            return "{0}::{1}".format(str(lang or "").strip().lower(), str(text or "").strip())
        except Exception:
            return ""

    def _favorite_cache_get(self, text, lang):
        try:
            return str(self._favorite_incoming_cache.get(self._favorite_cache_key(text, lang), "") or "").strip() or None
        except Exception:
            return None

    def _favorite_cache_put(self, text, lang, translated):
        try:
            key = self._favorite_cache_key(text, lang)
            if not key:
                return
            self._favorite_incoming_cache[key] = str(translated or "")
            self._schedule_favorite_incoming_cache_save()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"favorite cache put fail: {e}")

    def _favorite_sender_id_from_message(self, msg_obj):
        try:
            mo = getattr(msg_obj, "messageOwner", None)
            from_id = getattr(mo, "from_id", None) if mo is not None else None
            user_id = getattr(from_id, "user_id", 0) if from_id is not None else 0
            return str(int(user_id)) if int(user_id or 0) > 0 else ""
        except Exception:
            return ""

    def _is_favorite_sender_message(self, msg_obj):
        try:
            sid = self._favorite_sender_id_from_message(msg_obj)
            return bool(sid and sid in self._favorite_sender_ids)
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _toggle_favorite_sender_message(self, msg_obj):
        try:
            sid = self._favorite_sender_id_from_message(msg_obj)
            if not sid:
                return None
            added = sid not in self._favorite_sender_ids
            if added:
                self._favorite_sender_ids.add(sid)
            else:
                self._favorite_sender_ids.discard(sid)
            self._save_favorite_sender_ids()
            return added
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"toggle favorite sender fail: {e}")
            return None

    def _sender_user_from_message(self, msg_obj):
        try:
            sid = self._favorite_sender_id_from_message(msg_obj)
            if not sid:
                return None
            account = int(getattr(UserConfig, "selectedAccount", 0) or 0)
            mc = MessagesController.getInstance(account)
            if mc is None:
                return None
            return mc.getUser(int(sid))
        except Exception:
            return None

    def _open_user_profile(self, fragment, user_id):
        try:
            if fragment is None or int(user_id or 0) == 0:
                return False
            ProfileActivity = find_class("org.telegram.ui.ProfileActivity")
            if ProfileActivity is None:
                return False
            try:
                target = ProfileActivity.of(int(user_id))
            except Exception:
                target = None
            if target is None:
                return False
            fragment.presentFragment(target)
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"open user profile fail: {e}")
            return False

    def _favorite_target_lang_for_message(self, msg_obj):
        try:
            lang = str(self._favorite_incoming_lang_code() or "").strip()
            if lang:
                return lang
        except Exception:
            pass
        return str(self._global_target_lang() or "en")

    def _incoming_text_for_favorite_translate(self, msg_obj):
        try:
            if msg_obj is None or msg_obj.isOut():
                return ""
            mo = getattr(msg_obj, "messageOwner", None)
            media_like = False
            try:
                media_like = bool(
                    msg_obj.isSticker() or msg_obj.isGif() or msg_obj.isRoundVideo() or
                    msg_obj.isVoice() or msg_obj.isPhoto() or msg_obj.isVideo() or
                    self._avatar_document_kind(msg_obj) in ("document", "plugin")
                )
            except Exception:
                media_like = False
            if media_like:
                caption = ""
                try:
                    caption = str(getattr(msg_obj, "caption", None) or "").strip()
                except Exception:
                    caption = ""
                if not caption and mo is not None:
                    try:
                        caption = str(getattr(mo, "caption", None) or "").strip()
                    except Exception:
                        caption = ""
                return caption
            text = getattr(msg_obj, "messageText", None)
            if not text and mo is not None:
                text = getattr(mo, "message", None)
            return str(text or "").strip()
        except Exception:
            return ""

    def _open_external_url(self, url, fragment=None):
        try:
            target_url = str(url or "").strip()
            try:
                lowered = target_url.lower()
                if lowered.startswith("https://t.me/") or lowered.startswith("http://t.me/") or lowered.startswith("https://telegram.me/") or lowered.startswith("http://telegram.me/"):
                    parts = [p for p in re.split(r"/+", re.sub(r"^https?://(?:t\.me|telegram\.me)/", "", target_url, flags=re.I)) if p]
                    if len(parts) >= 2 and parts[0] == "c" and str(parts[1]).isdigit():
                        post = str(parts[2]) if len(parts) >= 3 and str(parts[2]).isdigit() else ""
                        if post:
                            target_url = "tg://privatepost?channel={0}&post={1}".format(parts[1], post)
                    elif parts:
                        domain = url_quote(str(parts[0]), safe="")
                        post = str(parts[1]) if len(parts) >= 2 and str(parts[1]).isdigit() else ""
                        if post:
                            target_url = "tg://resolve?domain={0}&post={1}".format(domain, post)
                        else:
                            target_url = "tg://resolve?domain={0}".format(domain)
            except Exception:
                pass
            from android.content import Intent
            from android.net import Uri
            target = fragment if fragment is not None else self._chat_fragment_ref
            activity = None
            try:
                activity = target.getParentActivity() if target is not None and hasattr(target, "getParentActivity") else None
            except Exception:
                activity = None
            if activity is not None:
                try:
                    intent = Intent(Intent.ACTION_VIEW, Uri.parse(target_url))
                    activity.startActivity(intent)
                    return True
                except Exception:
                    pass
            try:
                self.open_url(target_url)
                return True
            except Exception:
                return False
        except Exception:
            try:
                self.open_url(target_url)
                return True
            except Exception:
                return False

    def _open_support_url(self, ctx=None, url="https://github.com/sponsors/ageekapple/"):
        try:
            target_url = str(url or "").strip()
            from android.content import Intent
            from android.net import Uri
            context = ctx
            if context is None:
                try:
                    frag = self.get_last_fragment()
                except Exception:
                    frag = None
                try:
                    context = frag.getParentActivity() if frag is not None and hasattr(frag, "getParentActivity") else None
                except Exception:
                    context = None
            if context is None:
                context = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext
            if context is not None:
                try:
                    intent = Intent(Intent.ACTION_VIEW, Uri.parse(target_url))
                    try:
                        intent.addFlags(Intent.FLAG_ACTIVITY_NEW_TASK)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    context.startActivity(intent)
                    return True
                except Exception:
                    pass
            return bool(self._open_external_url(target_url))
        except Exception:
            try:
                return bool(self._open_external_url(url))
            except Exception:
                return False

    def _apply_favorite_native_translation(self, message_object, translated_text, target_lang):
        def _ui():
            try:
                mo = getattr(message_object, "messageOwner", None)
                if not mo:
                    return
                TLRPC = find_class("org.telegram.tgnet.TLRPC")
                NC = find_class("org.telegram.messenger.NotificationCenter")
                Integer = find_class("java.lang.Integer")
                if TLRPC is None or NC is None:
                    return
                te = TLRPC.TL_textWithEntities()
                te.text = str(translated_text or "")
                te.entities = ArrayList()
                mo.translatedText = te
                mo.translatedToLanguage = str(target_lang or "")
                try:
                    message_object.translated = True
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    message_object.applyNewText(te.text)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    message_object.generateCaption()
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    message_object.resetLayout()
                except Exception:
                    pass
                self._favorite_translated_messages.add((message_object.getDialogId(), message_object.getId()))
                try:
                    self._usage_stats_record("favorite", target_lang, message_object.getDialogId())
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    fragment = self._chat_fragment_ref
                    adapter = _get_private_field_silent(fragment, "chatAdapter") if fragment is not None else None
                    if adapter is not None and hasattr(adapter, "notifyDataSetChanged"):
                        adapter.notifyDataSetChanged()
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    list_view = _get_private_field_silent(self._chat_fragment_ref, "chatListView") if self._chat_fragment_ref is not None else None
                    if list_view is not None:
                        list_view.invalidate()
                        list_view.requestLayout()
                except Exception:
                    pass
            except Exception as e:
                self._dlog(f"apply favorite native translation fail: {e}")
        run_on_ui_thread(_ui)

    def _apply_message_summary_to_bubble(self, message_object, summary_text, target_lang=None, fragment=None):
        def _ui():
            try:
                mo = getattr(message_object, "messageOwner", None)
                if not mo:
                    return
                TLRPC = find_class("org.telegram.tgnet.TLRPC")
                if TLRPC is None:
                    return
                cleaned = self._strip_summary_links(summary_text)
                if not cleaned:
                    return
                te = TLRPC.TL_textWithEntities()
                te.text = str(cleaned or "")
                te.entities = ArrayList()
                mo.summaryText = te
                mo.summarizedOpen = True
                try:
                    mo.translatedText = None
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    mo.translatedSummaryText = None
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    mo.translatedSummaryLanguage = str(target_lang or "")
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    message_object.summarized = True
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    message_object.translated = False
                except Exception:
                    pass
                updated = False
                try:
                    updated = bool(message_object.updateTranslation(True))
                except Exception:
                    updated = False
                try:
                    MessagesStorage.getInstance(int(UserConfig.selectedAccount)).updateMessageCustomParams(message_object.getDialogId(), mo)
                except Exception as inner_e:
                    self._dlog(f"apply message summary storage fail: {inner_e}")
                try:
                    NotificationCenter.getInstance(int(UserConfig.selectedAccount)).postNotificationName(NotificationCenter.messageTranslated, message_object, True)
                except Exception as inner_e:
                    self._dlog(f"apply message summary notify fail: {inner_e}")
                self._dlog(f"apply message summary ok updated={updated} len={len(te.text)}")
                if not updated:
                    try:
                        message_object.applyNewText(te.text)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        message_object.generateCaption()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        message_object.resetLayout()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                try:
                    active_fragment = fragment if fragment is not None else self._chat_fragment_ref
                    adapter = _get_private_field_silent(active_fragment, "chatAdapter") if active_fragment is not None else None
                    if adapter is not None and hasattr(adapter, "notifyDataSetChanged"):
                        adapter.notifyDataSetChanged()
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    active_fragment = fragment if fragment is not None else self._chat_fragment_ref
                    list_view = _get_private_field_silent(active_fragment, "chatListView") if active_fragment is not None else None
                    if list_view is not None:
                        list_view.invalidate()
                        list_view.requestLayout()
                except Exception:
                    pass
            except Exception as e:
                self._dlog(f"apply message summary fail: {e}")
        run_on_ui_thread(_ui)

    def _request_channel_post_summary(self, msg_obj, target_lang=None):
        try:
            source_text = self._avatar_action_text_strict(msg_obj)
            if not source_text:
                return None
            target_lang = str(target_lang or self._global_target_lang() or "en")
            if self._channel_summary_provider_index() == 0:
                native_summary = self._request_native_summary_message(msg_obj, target_lang)
                if native_summary and not self._looks_weak_native_summary(source_text, native_summary):
                    self._dlog("channel summary accepted native result")
                    return self._strip_summary_links(native_summary)
                self._dlog("channel summary native fallback engaged")
                fallback = self._build_local_summary_text(source_text)
                if not fallback:
                    return self._strip_summary_links(native_summary)
                target_code = str(target_lang or "").strip().lower()
                owner = getattr(msg_obj, "messageOwner", None)
                source_lang = str(getattr(owner, "originalLanguage", "") or "").strip().lower()
                if target_code and target_code not in ("und", source_lang):
                    translated = (
                        self._translate_text_native(fallback, target_code, wait_sec=18)
                        or self._translate_text(fallback, target_code)
                    )
                    if translated:
                        return self._strip_summary_links(translated)
                return self._strip_summary_links(fallback)
            if not self._is_assist_ai_configured():
                return "__missing_config__"
            base_text = self._translate_text_native(source_text, target_lang, wait_sec=18) or self._translate_text(source_text, target_lang) or source_text
            out = self._request_ai_summary(source_text, base_text, target_code=target_lang)
            return self._strip_summary_links(out)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"request channel post summary fail: {e}")
            return None

    def _run_channel_post_summary(self, fragment, msg_obj, target_lang_override=None):
        try:
            if fragment is None or msg_obj is None:
                return False
            BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("avatar_ai_loading_summary"))
            target_lang = str(target_lang_override or self._global_target_lang() or "en")
            try:
                self._channel_summary_request_nonce = int(getattr(self, "_channel_summary_request_nonce", 0) or 0) + 1
            except Exception:
                self._channel_summary_request_nonce = 1
            request_nonce = int(self._channel_summary_request_nonce or 0)
            def _worker():
                try:
                    result = self._request_channel_post_summary(msg_obj, target_lang)
                    def _finish():
                        try:
                            if int(getattr(self, "_channel_summary_request_nonce", 0) or 0) != int(request_nonce):
                                self._dlog(f"channel summary stale result ignored nonce={request_nonce}")
                                return
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        if result == "__missing_config__":
                            BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_missing_config"))
                            return
                        if result:
                            try:
                                self._usage_stats_record("summary", target_lang, msg_obj.getDialogId())
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            provider_subtitle = self._lang_label_from_code(target_lang)
                            self._show_avatar_native_result_sheet(
                                fragment,
                                self._tr("avatar_ai_native_summary_title"),
                                provider_subtitle,
                                result,
                                target_lang,
                                lambda picked_code: self._run_channel_post_summary(fragment, msg_obj, picked_code),
                            )
                        else:
                            BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty"))
                    run_on_ui_thread(_finish)
                except Exception as inner_e:
                    def _fail():
                        BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty"))
                        self._dlog(f"channel post summary worker fail: {inner_e}")
                    run_on_ui_thread(_fail)
            try:
                from client_utils import run_on_queue
                run_on_queue(_worker)
            except Exception:
                threading.Thread(target=_worker, daemon=True).start()
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"run channel post summary fail: {e}")
            return False

    def _is_favorite_message_locked(self, msg_obj):
        try:
            return (
                msg_obj is not None
                and (msg_obj.getDialogId(), msg_obj.getId()) in self._favorite_translated_messages
                and bool(getattr(msg_obj, "translated", False))
                and getattr(getattr(msg_obj, "messageOwner", None), "translatedText", None) is not None
            )
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _maybe_translate_favorite_incoming(self, msg_obj):
        try:
            if msg_obj is None or msg_obj.isOut() or not self._is_favorite_sender_message(msg_obj):
                return
            source_text = self._incoming_text_for_favorite_translate(msg_obj)
            if not source_text:
                return
            target_lang = str(self._favorite_target_lang_for_message(msg_obj) or "en")
            mo = getattr(msg_obj, "messageOwner", None)
            if mo is not None and getattr(mo, "translatedText", None) is not None and str(getattr(mo, "translatedToLanguage", "") or "") == target_lang:
                return
            key = "{0}:{1}:{2}".format(msg_obj.getDialogId(), msg_obj.getId(), target_lang)
            if key in self._favorite_incoming_in_progress:
                return
            cached = self._favorite_cache_get(source_text, target_lang)
            if cached:
                self._apply_favorite_native_translation(msg_obj, cached, target_lang)
                return
            self._favorite_incoming_in_progress.add(key)
            def _worker():
                try:
                    translated = str(self._translate_text_native(source_text, target_lang) or "").strip()
                    if translated:
                        self._favorite_cache_put(source_text, target_lang, translated)
                        self._apply_favorite_native_translation(msg_obj, translated, target_lang)
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"favorite incoming translate fail: {e}")
                finally:
                    self._favorite_incoming_in_progress.discard(key)
            try:
                from client_utils import run_on_queue
                run_on_queue(_worker)
            except Exception:
                threading.Thread(target=_worker, daemon=True).start()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"maybe translate favorite incoming fail: {e}")

    def _copy_text_to_clipboard(self, text):
        try:
            from android.content import Context
            ctx = None
            try:
                ctx = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext
            except Exception:
                ctx = None
            if ctx is None:
                try:
                    ctx = AndroidUtilities.getApplicationContext()
                except Exception:
                    ctx = None
            if ctx is None:
                return False
            cm = None
            try:
                cm = ctx.getSystemService(Context.CLIPBOARD_SERVICE)
            except Exception:
                cm = None
            if cm is None:
                try:
                    cm = ctx.getSystemService("clipboard")
                except Exception:
                    cm = None
            if cm is None:
                return False
            cm.setPrimaryClip(ClipData.newPlainText("translatica_logs", str(text or "")))
            return True
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _remove_live_log(self, target_view=None):
        try:
            captured_view = target_view if target_view is not None else self._live_log_view
            def _rem():
                try:
                    if captured_view is not None:
                        par = captured_view.getParent()
                        if par is not None and hasattr(par, "removeView"):
                            par.removeView(captured_view)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    if self._live_log_view is captured_view:
                        self._live_log_view = None
                        self._live_log_expanded = None
                        self._live_log_chip = None
                        self._log_text_view = None
                        self._log_scroll_view = None
                except Exception:
                    pass
            run_on_ui_thread(_rem)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _set_live_log_enabled(self, enabled, host_ctx=None, prefer_collapsed=None):
        try:
            self._native_log("live_log set enabled={0} prefer_collapsed={1}".format(bool(enabled), prefer_collapsed))
            self._live_log_enabled = bool(enabled)
            self.set_setting("tlite_live_log", bool(enabled))
            if enabled and prefer_collapsed is not None:
                self._live_log_collapsed = bool(prefer_collapsed)
                self.set_setting("tlite_live_log_collapsed", bool(prefer_collapsed))
            if not enabled:
                self._remove_live_log()
                BulletinHelper.show_info("Translatica Logs disabled")
            else:
                BulletinHelper.show_success("Translatica Logs enabled")
                self._show_live_log(host_ctx)
        except Exception as e:
            self._native_log("live_log toggle fail: {0}".format(e))

    def _toggle_live_log(self, host_ctx=None, prefer_collapsed=None):
        try:
            self._set_live_log_enabled(not bool(getattr(self, "_live_log_enabled", False)), host_ctx, prefer_collapsed)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _clamp_live_log_margins(self, root=None):
        try:
            root = root or self._live_log_view
            if root is None:
                return
            par = root.getParent()
            if par is None:
                return
            lp = root.getLayoutParams()
            if lp is None:
                return
            dw = int(par.getWidth() or 0)
            dh = int(par.getHeight() or 0)
            w = int(lp.width or 0)
            h = int(lp.height or 0)
            if dw <= 0 or dh <= 0 or w <= 0 or h <= 0:
                return
            lp.rightMargin = max(0, min(int(getattr(lp, "rightMargin", 0) or 0), dw - w))
            lp.topMargin = max(0, min(int(getattr(lp, "topMargin", 0) or 0), dh - h))
            root.setLayoutParams(lp)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _attach_live_log_drag_listener(self, target_view, drag_mode):
        try:
            touch_cls = find_class("android.view.View$OnTouchListener")
            MotionEvent = jclass("android.view.MotionEvent")
            if touch_cls is None or target_view is None:
                return
            plugin = self

            class _Drag(dynamic_proxy(touch_cls)):
                def onTouch(self_obj, v, event):
                    try:
                        action = int(event.getActionMasked())
                        root = plugin._live_log_view
                        if root is None:
                            return False
                        par = root.getParent()
                        if par is None:
                            return False
                        lp = root.getLayoutParams()
                        if lp is None:
                            return False
                        dw = int(par.getWidth() or 0)
                        dh = int(par.getHeight() or 0)
                        if action == MotionEvent.ACTION_DOWN:
                            plugin._log_drag_moved = False
                            plugin._log_drag_sx = float(event.getRawX())
                            plugin._log_drag_sy = float(event.getRawY())
                            plugin._log_drag_rm0 = int(getattr(lp, "rightMargin", 0) or 0)
                            plugin._log_drag_tm0 = int(getattr(lp, "topMargin", 0) or 0)
                            return True
                        if action == MotionEvent.ACTION_MOVE:
                            dx = float(event.getRawX()) - plugin._log_drag_sx
                            dy = float(event.getRawY()) - plugin._log_drag_sy
                            if abs(dx) > 6 or abs(dy) > 6:
                                plugin._log_drag_moved = True
                            w = int(lp.width or 0)
                            h = int(lp.height or 0)
                            lp.rightMargin = max(0, min(int(plugin._log_drag_rm0 - dx), max(0, dw - w)))
                            lp.topMargin = max(0, min(int(plugin._log_drag_tm0 + dy), max(0, dh - h)))
                            root.setLayoutParams(lp)
                            return True
                        if action in (MotionEvent.ACTION_UP, MotionEvent.ACTION_CANCEL):
                            if plugin._log_drag_moved:
                                plugin.set_setting("tlite_live_log_rm", int(getattr(lp, "rightMargin", 0) or 0))
                                plugin.set_setting("tlite_live_log_tm", int(getattr(lp, "topMargin", 0) or 0))
                            elif drag_mode == "chip" and action == MotionEvent.ACTION_UP:
                                plugin._set_live_log_collapsed(False)
                            return True
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    return False

            target_view.setOnTouchListener(_Drag())
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _set_live_log_collapsed(self, collapsed):
        try:
            collapsed = bool(collapsed)
            self._live_log_collapsed = collapsed
            self.set_setting("tlite_live_log_collapsed", collapsed)
            def _ui():
                try:
                    if self._live_log_view is None:
                        return
                    if self._live_log_expanded is not None:
                        self._live_log_expanded.setVisibility(View.GONE if collapsed else View.VISIBLE)
                    if self._live_log_chip is not None:
                        self._live_log_chip.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if collapsed else View.GONE)
                    lp = self._live_log_view.getLayoutParams()
                    if lp is not None:
                        lp.width = AndroidUtilities.dp(48) if collapsed else AndroidUtilities.dp(272)
                        lp.height = AndroidUtilities.dp(48) if collapsed else AndroidUtilities.dp(204)
                        self._live_log_view.setLayoutParams(lp)
                        self._clamp_live_log_margins(self._live_log_view)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            run_on_ui_thread(_ui)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _build_live_log_text(self):
        try:
            debug_on = bool(self._is_debug_on())
            entries = list(self._log_buffer or [])
            if not debug_on:
                entries = [entry for entry in entries if str((entry[0] if isinstance(entry, (tuple, list)) and len(entry) > 1 else "INFO") or "").upper() == "ERROR"]
            if not entries:
                fallback = "No errors yet." if not debug_on else "No logs yet."
                ssb = SpannableStringBuilder()
                ssb.append(str(fallback))
                return ssb
            ssb = SpannableStringBuilder()
            for idx, entry in enumerate(entries):
                if isinstance(entry, (tuple, list)) and len(entry) > 1:
                    level = str(entry[0] or "INFO").upper()
                    text = str(entry[1] or "")
                else:
                    level = "INFO"
                    text = str(entry or "")
                start = len(str(ssb))
                ssb.append(text)
                end = len(str(ssb))
                if level == "ERROR":
                    try:
                        ssb.setSpan(ForegroundColorSpan(_ji(0xFFFF6B6B)), start, end, Spanned.SPAN_EXCLUSIVE_EXCLUSIVE)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                if idx < len(entries) - 1:
                    ssb.append("\n")
            return ssb
        except Exception:
            try:
                return "\n".join(
                    str(entry[1] if isinstance(entry, (tuple, list)) and len(entry) > 1 else entry or "")
                    for entry in list(self._log_buffer or [])
                )
            except Exception:
                return ""

    def _update_live_log(self):
        try:
            def _upd():
                try:
                    if self._log_text_view is None:
                        return
                    self._log_text_view.setText(self._build_live_log_text())
                    if self._log_scroll_view is not None:
                        self._log_scroll_view.post(lambda: self._log_scroll_view.fullScroll(View.FOCUS_DOWN))
                except Exception:
                    pass
            run_on_ui_thread(_upd)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _show_live_log(self, host_ctx=None):
        try:
            self._native_log("live_log show start")
            frag = None
            try:
                from client_utils import get_last_fragment
                frag = get_last_fragment()
            except Exception:
                frag = None
            ctx = frag.getParentActivity() if frag and frag.getParentActivity() else None
            if ctx is None and host_ctx is not None and hasattr(host_ctx, "getWindow"):
                ctx = host_ctx
            if ctx is None:
                BulletinHelper.show_info("Couldn't open Translatica Logs right now")
                return
            if self._live_log_view is not None:
                try:
                    par = self._live_log_view.getParent()
                    if par is not None:
                        BulletinHelper.show_info("Translatica Logs is already active")
                        return
                except Exception:
                    pass
                self._live_log_view = None
                self._live_log_expanded = None
                self._live_log_chip = None
                self._log_text_view = None
                self._log_scroll_view = None

            collapsed = bool(getattr(self, "_live_log_collapsed", False))
            root = FrameLayout(ctx)
            expanded = LinearLayout(ctx)
            expanded.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            bg = GradientDrawable()
            bg.setColor(_ji(0xAA000000))
            bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(10)))
            expanded.setBackground(bg)
            expanded.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))

            header_row = LinearLayout(ctx)
            header_row.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            header_row.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            header = TextView(ctx)
            header.setText("Translatica Logs")
            header.setTextSize(11)
            try:
                header.setTypeface(None, 1)
            except Exception:
                pass
            header.setTextColor(_ji(0xFF8BE28B))
            header_row.addView(header, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1.0))
            min_btn = FrameLayout(ctx)
            try:
                min_bg = GradientDrawable()
                min_bg.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
                min_bg.setColor(_ji(0x223C4658))
                min_btn.setBackground(min_bg)
                min_btn.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
            except Exception:
                pass
            min_icon = ImageView(ctx)
            min_res = 0
            try:
                res = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources()
                pkg = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName()
                for icon_name in ("arrow_more", "msg_close", "msg_remove", "collapse_up"):
                    min_res = int(res.getIdentifier(icon_name, "drawable", pkg) or 0)
                    if min_res:
                        break
            except Exception:
                min_res = 0
            if min_res:
                try:
                    min_icon.setImageResource(min_res)
                    min_icon.setColorFilter(_ji(0xFFD7D7D7))
                    min_icon.setScaleType(ImageView.ScaleType.CENTER_INSIDE)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            else:
                fallback_tv = TextView(ctx)
                fallback_tv.setText("→")
                fallback_tv.setTextSize(1, 20)
                fallback_tv.setTextColor(_ji(0xFFD7D7D7))
                fallback_tv.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
                min_btn.addView(fallback_tv, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(24), AndroidUtilities.dp(24), Gravity.CENTER))
            if min_res:
                min_btn.addView(min_icon, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(20), AndroidUtilities.dp(20), Gravity.CENTER))
            min_btn.setOnClickListener(OnClickListener(lambda _v=None: self._set_live_log_collapsed(True)))
            header_row.addView(min_btn, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(34), AndroidUtilities.dp(34)))
            expanded.addView(header_row)

            scroll = ScrollView(ctx)
            self._log_scroll_view = scroll
            log_tv = TextView(ctx)
            log_tv.setTextSize(9)
            log_tv.setTextColor(_ji(0xFFE8E8E8))
            try:
                log_tv.setMinimumHeight(AndroidUtilities.dp(148))
                log_tv.setClickable(True)
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._log_text_view = log_tv
            try:
                log_tv.setText(self._build_live_log_text())
            except Exception:
                pass
            scroll.addView(log_tv)
            def _copy_live_logs():
                try:
                    copied = self._copy_text_to_clipboard(str(log_tv.getText() or "").strip())
                    if copied:
                        BulletinHelper.show_info("Logs copied to clipboard")
                        return True
                except Exception:
                    pass
                return False
            log_tv.setOnClickListener(OnClickListener(lambda _v=None: _copy_live_logs()))
            try:
                scroll.setClickable(True)
                scroll.setOnClickListener(OnClickListener(lambda _v=None: _copy_live_logs()))
            except Exception:
                pass

            long_listener_cls = find_class("android.view.View$OnLongClickListener")
            if long_listener_cls is not None:
                class _ClearLogs(dynamic_proxy(long_listener_cls)):
                    def onLongClick(self_obj, _v):
                        try:
                            self._log_buffer.clear()
                            if self._log_text_view is not None:
                                self._log_text_view.setText("")
                            BulletinHelper.show_info("Logs cleared")
                            return True
                        except Exception:
                            return False
                log_tv.setOnLongClickListener(_ClearLogs())
                try:
                    scroll.setOnLongClickListener(_ClearLogs())
                except Exception:
                    pass
            expanded.addView(scroll, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(-1, AndroidUtilities.dp(148)))
            self._live_log_expanded = expanded

            chip = FrameLayout(ctx)
            chip_bg = GradientDrawable()
            chip_bg.setColor(_ji(0xDD101010))
            chip_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(24)))
            chip.setBackground(chip_bg)
            chip.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
            log_icon = ImageView(ctx)
            try:
                res = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources()
                pkg = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName()
                lid = res.getIdentifier("device_phone_ios", "drawable", pkg)
                if not lid:
                    lid = res.getIdentifier("msg_log", "drawable", pkg)
                if lid:
                    log_icon.setImageResource(int(lid))
                    log_icon.setColorFilter(_ji(0xFFE24444))
            except Exception:
                pass
            chip.addView(log_icon, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(30), AndroidUtilities.dp(30), Gravity.CENTER))
            self._live_log_chip = chip

            expanded.setVisibility(View.GONE if collapsed else View.VISIBLE)
            chip.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if collapsed else View.GONE)
            root.addView(expanded, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(-1, -1, Gravity.TOP | Gravity.LEFT))
            root.addView(chip, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(48), AndroidUtilities.dp(48), Gravity.TOP | Gravity.RIGHT))

            window = ctx.getWindow() if hasattr(ctx, "getWindow") else None
            decor = window.getDecorView() if window is not None else None
            if decor is None or not hasattr(decor, "addView"):
                BulletinHelper.show_info("Couldn't show Translatica Logs on screen")
                return

            tw = AndroidUtilities.dp(48) if collapsed else AndroidUtilities.dp(272)
            th = AndroidUtilities.dp(48) if collapsed else AndroidUtilities.dp(204)
            dw = int(decor.getWidth() or 0) or AndroidUtilities.dp(360)
            dh = int(decor.getHeight() or 0) or AndroidUtilities.dp(720)
            rm = self.get_setting("tlite_live_log_rm", None)
            tm = self.get_setting("tlite_live_log_tm", None)
            rm = AndroidUtilities.dp(10) if rm is None else int(rm)
            tm = AndroidUtilities.dp(60) if tm is None else int(tm)
            rm = max(0, min(rm, dw - tw))
            tm = max(0, min(tm, dh - th))
            lp = FrameLayout.LayoutParams(tw, th)
            lp.gravity = Gravity.TOP | Gravity.RIGHT
            lp.topMargin = tm
            lp.rightMargin = rm
            decor.addView(root, lp)
            self._live_log_view = root
            self._set_live_log_collapsed(collapsed)
            try:
                root.bringToFront()
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                if hasattr(root, "setElevation"):
                    root.setElevation(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(24)))
                if hasattr(chip, "setElevation"):
                    chip.setElevation(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(26)))
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._attach_live_log_drag_listener(chip, "chip")
            self._attach_live_log_drag_listener(header_row, "header")
            try:
                decor.post(lambda: self._clamp_live_log_margins(root))
            except Exception:
                pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._native_log("live_log show failed: {0}".format(e))

    def _stats_enabled(self):
        try:
            v = self.get_setting("tlite_stats_enabled", True)
            if isinstance(v, bool):
                return v
            if isinstance(v, (int, float)):
                return bool(int(v))
            s = str(v or "").strip().lower()
            if s in ("1", "true", "on", "yes", "enabled"):
                return True
            if s in ("0", "false", "off", "no", "disabled"):
                return False
            return bool(v)
        except Exception:
            return True

    def _load_telemetry_queue(self):
        try:
            raw = self.get_setting("tlite_stats_queue_v1", "[]")
            arr = raw if isinstance(raw, list) else json.loads(str(raw or "[]"))
            self._telemetry_queue = arr if isinstance(arr, list) else []
        except Exception:
            self._telemetry_queue = []

    def _save_telemetry_queue(self):
        try:
            self.set_setting("tlite_stats_queue_v1", json.dumps(list(self._telemetry_queue or []), ensure_ascii=True, separators=(",", ":")))
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _telemetry_install_id_get(self):
        try:
            if self._telemetry_install_id:
                return str(self._telemetry_install_id)
            cached = str(self.get_setting("tlite_stats_install_id", "") or "").strip()
            if cached:
                self._telemetry_install_id = cached
                return cached
            sid = "tl_{0:x}{1:x}".format(int(time.time() * 1000), random.randint(0, 0xFFFFFF))
            self.set_setting("tlite_stats_install_id", sid)
            self._telemetry_install_id = sid
            return sid
        except Exception:
            return "tl_unknown"

    def _telemetry_app_snapshot(self):
        out = {
            "app_id": "unknown",
            "app_variant": "unknown",
            "app_version": "unknown",
            "plugin_version": str(__version__),
            "mode": "lite",
        }
        try:
            ctx = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext
            if ctx is None:
                return out
            pkg = str(ctx.getPackageName() or "unknown").strip() or "unknown"
            out["app_id"] = pkg
            l = pkg.lower()
            if "ayu" in l:
                out["app_variant"] = "ayugram"
            elif "extera" in l:
                out["app_variant"] = "exteragram"
            try:
                pm = ctx.getPackageManager()
                pi = pm.getPackageInfo(pkg, 0)
                out["app_version"] = str(getattr(pi, "versionName", "") or getattr(pi, "versionCode", "unknown"))
            except Exception:
                pass
        except Exception:
            pass
        return out

    def _telemetry_queue_event(self, event_name, feature=None, count=1, force_flush=False):
        try:
            if not self._stats_enabled():
                return
            name = str(event_name or "").strip()
            if not name:
                return
            ev = {
                "ts": int(time.time()),
                "event": name,
                "feature": str(feature or "").strip(),
                "count": int(count or 1),
            }
            with self._telemetry_lock:
                q = list(self._telemetry_queue or [])
                q.append(ev)
                if len(q) > 180:
                    q = q[-180:]
                self._telemetry_queue = q
            self._save_telemetry_queue()
            now_ts = int(time.time())
            if force_flush or (now_ts - int(self._telemetry_last_flush_ts or 0) >= 20):
                self._telemetry_flush_async()
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _telemetry_flush_async(self):
        try:
            if not self._stats_enabled():
                return
            with self._telemetry_lock:
                if self._telemetry_sending:
                    return
                queue = list(self._telemetry_queue or [])
                if not queue:
                    return
                self._telemetry_sending = True
            payload = {
                "plugin": "translatica_pro",
                "install_id": self._telemetry_install_id_get(),
                "sent_at": int(time.time()),
                "app": self._telemetry_app_snapshot(),
                "events": queue[:120],
            }

            def _worker():
                ok = False
                try:
                    ok = self._telemetry_post(payload)
                except Exception:
                    ok = False
                try:
                    with self._telemetry_lock:
                        if ok:
                            cur = list(self._telemetry_queue or [])
                            drop = min(len(cur), len(payload.get("events", []) or []))
                            self._telemetry_queue = cur[drop:]
                            self._telemetry_last_flush_ts = int(time.time())
                            self._save_telemetry_queue()
                        self._telemetry_sending = False
                except Exception:
                    self._telemetry_sending = False

            threading.Thread(target=_worker, daemon=True).start()
        except Exception:
            self._telemetry_sending = False

    def _telemetry_post(self, payload):
        try:
            raw = json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=True, separators=(",", ":")).encode("utf-8")
            headers = {
                "User-Agent": "TranslaticaLiteStats/1.0",
                "Content-Type": "application/json",
                "Cache-Control": "no-cache",
            }
            token = str(GEEKSTATS_INGEST_TOKEN or "").strip()
            if token:
                headers["X-Ingest-Token"] = token
            req = Request(GEEKSTATS_INGEST_URL, data=raw, headers=headers, method="POST")
            with urlopen(req, timeout=6) as resp:
                code = int(getattr(resp, "status", 200) or 200)
                return 200 <= code < 300
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"stats post fail: {e}")
            return False

    def _current_ui_lang(self):
        try:
            pidx = int(self.get_setting("tlite_plugin_lang", 0) or 0)
            if pidx < 0 or pidx >= len(PLUGIN_LANG_OPTIONS):
                pidx = 0
            forced = str(PLUGIN_LANG_OPTIONS[pidx][1] or "system")
            if forced != "system":
                return forced
            from java.util import Locale
            return str(Locale.getDefault().getLanguage() or "en").strip().lower()[:2]
        except Exception:
            return "en"
