    def _get_user_first_name(self):
        try:
            UserConfig = find_class("org.telegram.messenger.UserConfig")
            uc = UserConfig.getInstance(UserConfig.selectedAccount)
            u = uc.getCurrentUser() if uc else None
            if u:
                name = str(getattr(u, "first_name", "") or "").strip()
                if name:
                    return name
        except Exception:
            pass
        return "User"

    def _resolve_current_user(self):
        try:
            account = int(getattr(UserConfig, "selectedAccount", 0))
        except Exception:
            account = 0
        uc = None
        mc = None
        try:
            uc = UserConfig.getInstance(account)
        except Exception:
            uc = None
        try:
            mc = MessagesController.getInstance(account)
        except Exception:
            mc = None

        user = None
        try:
            if uc:
                user = uc.getCurrentUser()
        except Exception:
            user = None
        if user is None:
            try:
                if uc and mc:
                    user = mc.getUser(uc.getClientUserId())
            except Exception:
                user = None
        try:
            self._dlog(f"resolve user: {'ok' if user is not None else 'none'}")
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            if user is not None:
                uid = str(getattr(user, "id", "") or "")
                uname = str(getattr(user, "first_name", "") or getattr(user, "username", "") or "").strip()
                self._wlog(f"resolve_current_user=ok id={uid} name={uname}")
            else:
                self._wlog("resolve_current_user=none")
        except Exception:
            pass
        return user

    def _make_avatar_fallback_drawable(self, user=None):
        try:
            if user is not None:
                try:
                    return AvatarDrawable(user)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            d = AvatarDrawable()
            try:
                name = str(self._get_user_first_name() or "User").strip()
                try:
                    d.setInfo(0, name, "", False)
                except Exception:
                    try:
                        d.setInfo(0, name, "")
                    except Exception:
                        pass
            except Exception:
                pass
            return d
        except Exception:
            return AvatarDrawable()

    def _bind_logged_user_avatar(self, avatar_view, size_dp=108):
        try:
            if avatar_view is None:
                return False
            account = int(UserConfig.selectedAccount)
            mc = MessagesController.getInstance(account)
            uc = UserConfig.getInstance(account)
            user = None
            if mc and uc:
                user = mc.getUser(uc.getClientUserId())
            if user is None and uc:
                try:
                    user = uc.getCurrentUser()
                except Exception:
                    user = None
            if user is None:
                self._wlog("bind_avatar aborted: no user")
                return False

            avatar_drawable = None
            try:
                avatar_drawable = AvatarDrawable(user)
            except Exception:
                try:
                    avatar_drawable = AvatarDrawable()
                    avatar_drawable.setInfo(user)
                except Exception:
                    avatar_drawable = None

            # Always set a visible fallback first (never leave avatar invisible).
            try:
                if avatar_drawable is not None:
                    avatar_view.setImageDrawable(avatar_drawable)
            except Exception:
                pass

            try:
                if hasattr(avatar_view, "setForUserOrChat") and avatar_drawable is not None:
                    try:
                        avatar_view.setForUserOrChat(user, avatar_drawable)
                        self._wlog("bind_avatar setForUserOrChat(user, drawable)=ok")
                        return True
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        avatar_view.setForUserOrChat(user)
                        self._wlog("bind_avatar setForUserOrChat(user)=ok")
                        return True
                    except Exception:
                        pass
            except Exception:
                pass
            return avatar_drawable is not None
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"bind logged user avatar fail: {e}")
            self._wlog(f"bind_avatar fail: {e}")
        return False

    def _load_translations_local(self):
        return

    def _load_translations_from_plugin_file(self):
        return

    def _load_translations_remote(self):
        return

    def _load_header_image_remote(self):
        try:
            os.makedirs(_CACHE_DIR, exist_ok=True)
            for urls, path in (
                ((HEADER_IMAGE_URL_DARK, HEADER_IMAGE_FALLBACK_URL_DARK), HEADER_IMAGE_CACHE_FILE_DARK),
                ((HEADER_IMAGE_URL_LIGHT, HEADER_IMAGE_FALLBACK_URL_LIGHT), HEADER_IMAGE_CACHE_FILE_LIGHT),
                ((AVATAR_TOOLS_HEADER_IMAGE_URL_DARK, AVATAR_TOOLS_HEADER_FALLBACK_URL_DARK), AVATAR_TOOLS_HEADER_CACHE_FILE_DARK),
                ((AVATAR_TOOLS_HEADER_IMAGE_URL_LIGHT, AVATAR_TOOLS_HEADER_FALLBACK_URL_LIGHT), AVATAR_TOOLS_HEADER_CACHE_FILE_LIGHT),
            ):
                loaded = False
                for url in urls:
                    try:
                        req = Request(url, headers={"User-Agent": "TranslaticaLite/1.0"})
                        with urlopen(req, timeout=15) as resp:
                            data = resp.read()
                        if not data:
                            continue
                        with open(path, "wb") as f:
                            f.write(data)
                        loaded = True
                        break
                    except Exception as ie:
                        self._dlog(f"header image load fail for {url}: {ie}")
                if not loaded:
                    self._dlog(f"header image sources exhausted for {path}")
            self._dlog("header images cached")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"header image load fail: {e}")

    def _load_top_icon_remote(self):
        try:
            os.makedirs(_CACHE_DIR, exist_ok=True)
            for url, path in (
                (TOP_ICON_URL_DARK, TOP_ICON_CACHE_FILE_DARK),
                (TOP_ICON_URL_LIGHT, TOP_ICON_CACHE_FILE_LIGHT),
            ):

                        continue

        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"top icon load fail: {e}")

                        f.write(data)

                except Exception as ie:
                    self._dlog(f"assist icon load fail for {url}: {ie}")
        except Exception as e:

    def _sync_translations(self):
        try:
            prev = str(self.get_setting("tlite_translations_plugin_version", "") or "")
        except Exception:
            prev = ""
        try:
            if prev != str(__version__):
                self._dlog(f"translations force refresh by version: {prev} -> {__version__}")
                self._load_translations_remote()
                self.set_setting("tlite_translations_plugin_version", str(__version__))
            else:
                self._load_translations_remote()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"sync translations fail: {e}")

    def _show_resources_loading_dialog(self, ctx):
        try:
            if ctx is None:
                return None
            b = AlertDialogBuilder(ctx)
            b.set_title(self._tr("resources_loading_title"))
            b.set_message(self._tr("resources_loading_text"))
            return b.show()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"resources loading dialog fail: {e}")
            return None

    def _download_translations_async(self, ctx=None, close_dialog=None, bulletin_key="resources_done_bulletin"):
        try:
            loading_dialog = self._show_resources_loading_dialog(ctx)
        except Exception:
            loading_dialog = None

        def _worker():
            ok = False
            try:
                self._force_asset_sync_once = True
                self._load_translations_remote()
                self._sync_assets()
                try:
                    self.set_setting("tlite_translations_plugin_version", str(__version__))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                ok = True
            except Exception as e:
                self._dlog(f"download translations async fail: {e}")

            def _finish():
                try:
                    if loading_dialog is not None:
                        loading_dialog.dismiss()
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    if close_dialog is not None:
                        close_dialog.dismiss()
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    BulletinHelper.show_success(self._tr(bulletin_key) if ok else self._tr("resources_failed_bulletin"))
                except Exception:
                    pass

            try:
                run_on_ui_thread(_finish)
            except Exception:
                _finish()

        try:
            from client_utils import run_on_queue
            run_on_queue(_worker)
        except Exception:
            threading.Thread(target=_worker, daemon=True).start()

    def _sync_assets(self):
        try:
            try:
                os.makedirs(_CACHE_DIR, exist_ok=True)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                force = bool(getattr(self, "_force_asset_sync_once", False))
            except Exception:
                force = False
            if not force:
                try:
                    if all(os.path.exists(p) for p in ASSET_CACHE_FILES):
                        self._dlog("sync assets skipped: cache complete")
                        return
                except Exception:
                    pass
            self._load_header_image_remote()
            self._load_support_icon_remote()
            self._load_top_icon_remote()
            self._load_extended_icon_remote()
            self._load_about_avatar_remote()
            self._load_dotted_avatar_remote()
            self._load_welcome_bg_remote()
            self._load_chat_icon_remote()
            self._load_assist_icon_remote()
            try:
                self._force_asset_sync_once = False
            except Exception:
                pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"sync assets fail: {e}")

    def _open_dotted_chat(self):
        try:
            try:
                from client_utils import get_messages_controller, get_last_fragment
                get_messages_controller().openByUserName("DottedChat", get_last_fragment(), 1)
            except Exception:
                self.open_url("https://t.me/DottedChat")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"open dotted fail: {e}")

    def _show_welcome_sheet(self, ctx_override=None):
        try:
            log("[TranslaticaPro][Welcome] show request")
            self._wlog("show begin")
            ctx = ctx_override
            if ctx is None:
                frag = self.get_last_fragment()
                ctx = frag.getParentActivity() if frag and frag.getParentActivity() else ApplicationLoader.applicationContext
            if not ctx:
                log("[TranslaticaPro][Welcome] no context")
                self._wlog("show abort: no ctx")
                return False
            try:
                self._dismiss_keyboard_focus(ctx)
            except Exception:
                pass

            sheet = BottomSheet(ctx, False)
            try:
                sheet.setApplyTopPadding(False)
                sheet.setApplyBottomPadding(False)
                try:
                    sheet.setBackgroundColor(0x00000000)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            except Exception:
                pass
            root = FrameLayout(ctx)
            try:
                root.setBackgroundColor(0x00000000)
            except Exception:
                pass
            hero = FrameLayout(ctx)
            content = LinearLayout(ctx)
            content.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            content.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL)
            hero_bg = None
            hero_radius = float(AndroidUtilities.dp(22))
            try:
                content.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(20), AndroidUtilities.dp(22), AndroidUtilities.dp(20), AndroidUtilities.dp(20))
                hero_bg = GradientDrawable(GradientDrawable.Orientation.TOP_BOTTOM, jarray(jarray.int)([
                    0x00000000,
                    0x00000000,
                    0x00000000,
                ]))
                hero_bg.setCornerRadius(hero_radius)
                try:
                    hero_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), Color.parseColor("#2A3A58"))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                hero.setBackground(hero_bg)
                hero.setClipToOutline(True)
                hero.setOutlineProvider(ViewOutlineProvider.BACKGROUND)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                bg_wrap = FrameLayout(ctx)
                try:
                    wrap_bg = GradientDrawable()
                    wrap_bg.setColor(0x00000000)
                    wrap_bg.setCornerRadius(hero_radius)
                    bg_wrap.setBackground(wrap_bg)
                    bg_wrap.setClipToOutline(True)
                    bg_wrap.setOutlineProvider(ViewOutlineProvider.BACKGROUND)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                bg = ImageView(ctx)
                bg.setScaleType(ImageView.ScaleType.CENTER_CROP)
                if os.path.exists(WELCOME_BG_CACHE_FILE):
                    bmp_bg = BitmapFactory.decodeFile(WELCOME_BG_CACHE_FILE)
                    if bmp_bg:
                        bg.setImageBitmap(bmp_bg)
                bg_wrap.addView(bg, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(FrameLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, FrameLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, Gravity.CENTER))
                hero.addView(bg_wrap, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(FrameLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, FrameLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, Gravity.CENTER))
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                overlay = View(ctx)
                ov = GradientDrawable(
                    GradientDrawable.Orientation.TOP_BOTTOM,
                    jarray(jarray.int)([
                        0x55000000,
                        0x33000000,
                        0x99000000,
                    ]),
                )
                try:
                    ov.setCornerRadius(hero_radius)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                overlay.setBackground(ov)
                hero.addView(
                    overlay,
                    FrameLayout.LayoutParams(
                        FrameLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT,
                        FrameLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT,
                        Gravity.CENTER,
                    ),
                )
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                handle = View(ctx)
                hb = GradientDrawable()
                hb.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(2)))
                hb.setColor(Color.parseColor("#88FFFFFF"))
                handle.setBackground(hb)
                lp_handle = FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(44), AndroidUtilities.dp(4), Gravity.TOP | Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL)
                lp_handle.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
                hero.addView(handle, lp_handle)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                from android.animation import ValueAnimator, ArgbEvaluator
                if hero_bg is not None:
                    evaluator = ArgbEvaluator()
                    anim = ValueAnimator.ofFloat(0.0, 1.0)
                    anim.setDuration(2600)
                    anim.setRepeatCount(-1)
                    anim.setRepeatMode(ValueAnimator.REVERSE)

                    class _Upd(dynamic_proxy(ValueAnimator.AnimatorUpdateListener)):
                        def onAnimationUpdate(self_obj, va):
                            try:
                                t = float(va.getAnimatedValue())
                                c1 = int(evaluator.evaluate(t, Color.parseColor("#0A0F16"), Color.parseColor("#0B1020")))
                                c2 = int(evaluator.evaluate(t, Color.parseColor("#101827"), Color.parseColor("#13203A")))
                                c3 = int(evaluator.evaluate(t, Color.parseColor("#0C1320"), Color.parseColor("#0E1524")))
                                try:
                                    hero_bg.setColors(jarray(jarray.int)([c1, c2, c3]))
                                except Exception:
                                    pass
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                    anim.addUpdateListener(_Upd())
                    anim.start()
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                grain_view = ImageView(ctx)
                try:
                    gw = 220
                    gh = 220
                    grain = Bitmap.createBitmap(gw, gh, Bitmap.Config.ARGB_8888)
                    import random
                    rnd = random.Random(73)
                    for yy in range(gh):
                        for xx in range(gw):
                            a = 8 + rnd.randint(0, 18)
                            c = (a << 24) | (255 << 16) | (255 << 8) | 255
                            grain.setPixel(xx, yy, c)
                    grain_view.setImageBitmap(grain)
                    grain_view.setScaleType(ImageView.ScaleType.FIT_XY)
                    grain_view.setAlpha(0.09)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                hero.addView(grain_view, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(FrameLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, FrameLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, Gravity.CENTER))
            except Exception:
                pass

            avatar_shell = FrameLayout(ctx)
            try:
                sh = GradientDrawable()
                sh.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
                sh.setColor(0x00000000)
                avatar_shell.setBackground(sh)
                avatar_shell.setClipToOutline(True)
                avatar_shell.setOutlineProvider(ViewOutlineProvider.BACKGROUND)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                avatar_shell.setAlpha(1.0)
                avatar_shell.setScaleX(1.0)
                avatar_shell.setScaleY(1.0)
                avatar_shell.setTranslationY(0.0)
                avatar_shell.setRotation(0.0)
            except Exception:
                pass
            avatar_view = None
            try:
                avatar_view = BackupImageView(ctx)
                self._wlog("avatar_view created: BackupImageView")
            except Exception as e:
                self._wlog(f"avatar_view create fail: {e}")
                avatar_view = None
            if avatar_view is not None:
                try:
                    avatar_view.setRoundRadius(AndroidUtilities.dp(18))
                except Exception as e:
                    self._wlog(f"avatar_view setRoundRadius fail: {e}")
                try:
                    user = self._resolve_current_user()
                except Exception:
                    user = None
                try:
                    if user is not None:
                        drawable = AvatarDrawable(user)
                        avatar_view.setForUserOrChat(user, drawable)
                        self._wlog("avatar_view setForUserOrChat(user, AvatarDrawable(user))=ok")
                    else:
                        avatar_view.setImageDrawable(AvatarDrawable())
                        self._wlog("avatar_view fallback AvatarDrawable()=ok")
                except Exception as e:
                    self._wlog(f"avatar_view bind fail: {e}")
                    try:
                        avatar_view.setImageDrawable(AvatarDrawable())
                    except Exception:
                        pass
            if avatar_view is None:
                iv = ImageView(ctx)
                try:
                    iv.setScaleType(ImageView.ScaleType.CENTER_CROP)
                    try:
                        iv.setBackgroundColor(Color.TRANSPARENT)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        iv.setImageDrawable(self._make_avatar_fallback_drawable(None))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                except Exception:
                    pass
                avatar_view = iv
            avatar_shell.addView(avatar_view, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(108), AndroidUtilities.dp(108), Gravity.CENTER))
            self._wlog("avatar_view added to avatar_shell")
            try:
                avatar_view.setAlpha(1.0)
                avatar_view.setScaleX(1.0)
                avatar_view.setScaleY(1.0)
                avatar_view.setTranslationY(0.0)
                avatar_view.setRotationY(0.0)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                class _RetryAvatar(dynamic_proxy("java.lang.Runnable")):
                    def run(self_obj):
                        try:
                            user = self._resolve_current_user()
                            if user is not None and hasattr(avatar_view, "setForUserOrChat"):
                                avatar_view.setForUserOrChat(user, AvatarDrawable(user))
                                self._wlog("avatar retry setForUserOrChat=ok")
                            elif hasattr(avatar_view, "setImageDrawable"):
                                avatar_view.setImageDrawable(AvatarDrawable())
                                self._wlog("avatar retry fallback drawable=ok")
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                avatar_view.postDelayed(_RetryAvatar(), 140)
            except Exception:
                pass
            lp_avatar = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(108), AndroidUtilities.dp(108))
            lp_avatar.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(6)
            content.addView(avatar_shell, lp_avatar)
            self._wlog("avatar_shell added to content")

            title_wrap = LinearLayout(ctx)
            title_wrap.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            try:
                title_wrap.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))
                title_wrap.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL)
            except Exception:
                pass

            welcome_title = TextView(ctx)
            welcome_title.setText(str(self._tr("first_welcome_text") or ""))
            welcome_title.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
            welcome_title.setTextSize(30)
            try:
                welcome_title.setTypeface(AndroidUtilities.getTypeface("fonts/rmedium.ttf"))
                welcome_title.setTextColor(Color.WHITE)
                welcome_title.setLineSpacing(0.0, 1.0)
            except Exception:
                pass
            title_wrap.addView(welcome_title, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            lp_title = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_title.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
            content.addView(title_wrap, lp_title)

            desc = TextView(ctx)
            try:
                desc.setTextColor(Color.parseColor("#E3ECF8"))
                desc.setTextSize(15)
                desc.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
                desc.setText(self._tr("welcome_divider"))
                desc.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(4), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(0))
            except Exception:
                pass
            content.addView(desc, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            open_btn = TextView(ctx)
            open_btn.setText(self._tr("first_welcome_button"))
            open_btn.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
            open_btn.setTextSize(18)
            try:
                open_btn.setTextColor(Color.BLACK)
                btn_bg = GradientDrawable()
                btn_bg.setColor(Color.parseColor("#F4FAFF"))
                btn_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(22)))
                open_btn.setBackground(btn_bg)
                open_btn.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(22), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(22), AndroidUtilities.dp(14))
            except Exception:
                pass

            class _OpenSettings(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        self._open_plugin_settings()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        sheet.dismiss()
                    except Exception:
                        pass

            open_btn.setOnClickListener(_OpenSettings())
            hero.addView(open_btn, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(FrameLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, FrameLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, Gravity.BOTTOM | Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL))
            try:
                blp = open_btn.getLayoutParams()
                blp.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(24)
                blp.rightMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(24)
                blp.bottomMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(22)
                open_btn.setLayoutParams(blp)
            except Exception:
                pass
            content_lp = FrameLayout.LayoutParams(FrameLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, FrameLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, Gravity.TOP | Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL)
            content_lp.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(18)
            hero.addView(content, content_lp)
            self._wlog("content added to hero")

            lp_hero = FrameLayout.LayoutParams(FrameLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, AndroidUtilities.dp(458), Gravity.CENTER)
            lp_hero.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(16)
            lp_hero.rightMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(16)
            lp_hero.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(16)
            lp_hero.bottomMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(18)
            root.addView(hero, lp_hero)
            sheet.setCustomView(root)
            try:
                self._style_welcome_sheet_surface(sheet)
            except Exception:
                pass
            run_on_ui_thread(sheet.show)
            try:
                class _AfterShow(dynamic_proxy("java.lang.Runnable")):
                    def run(self_obj):
                        try:
                            self._style_welcome_sheet_surface(sheet)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                root.postDelayed(_AfterShow(), 32)
            except Exception:
                pass
            log("[TranslaticaPro][Welcome] show queued")
            try:
                class _InspectAvatar(dynamic_proxy("java.lang.Runnable")):
                    def run(self_obj):
                        try:
                            av_w = int(avatar_view.getWidth()) if avatar_view is not None else -1
                            av_h = int(avatar_view.getHeight()) if avatar_view is not None else -1
                            av_v = int(avatar_view.getVisibility()) if avatar_view is not None else -1
                            av_a = float(avatar_view.getAlpha()) if avatar_view is not None else -1.0
                            sh_w = int(avatar_shell.getWidth())
                            sh_h = int(avatar_shell.getHeight())
                            sh_v = int(avatar_shell.getVisibility())
                            self._wlog(f"inspect avatar w={av_w} h={av_h} vis={av_v} alpha={av_a} shell_w={sh_w} shell_h={sh_h} shell_vis={sh_v}")
                        except Exception as e:
                            self._wlog(f"inspect avatar fail: {e}")
                root.postDelayed(_InspectAvatar(), 260)
            except Exception:
                pass
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            log(f"[TranslaticaPro][Welcome] show fail: {e}")
            self._dlog(f"welcome sheet fail: {e}")
            return False

    def _style_welcome_sheet_surface(self, sheet):
        try:
            if not sheet:
                return
            targets = []
            try:
                c = sheet.getContainer()
                if c is not None and c not in targets:
                    targets.append(c)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                c2 = getattr(sheet, "containerView", None)
                if c2 is not None and c2 not in targets:
                    targets.append(c2)
            except Exception:
                pass
            for fname in ("containerView", "container", "sheetContainer", "sheetView"):
                try:
                    v = _get_private_field_silent(sheet, fname)
                except Exception:
                    v = None
                if v is not None and v not in targets:
                    targets.append(v)
            for v in targets:
                try:
                    try:
                        v.setBackgroundColor(0x00000000)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        v.setBackground(None)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        v.setPadding(0, 0, 0, 0)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        v.setAlpha(1.0)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        v.setElevation(0.0)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                except Exception:
                    pass
            try:
                w = sheet.getWindow()
            except Exception:
                w = None
            if w is None:
                return
            try:
                w.setBackgroundDrawable(None)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                w.setDimAmount(0.0)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                w.clearFlags(WindowManager.LayoutParams.FLAG_DIM_BEHIND)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                if int(Build.VERSION.SDK_INT) >= 31:
                    w.setBackgroundBlurRadius(0)
            except Exception:
                pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"welcome sheet style fail: {e}")

    def _maybe_show_first_install_welcome(self):
        try:
            if bool(self.get_setting("tlite_first_welcome_done", False)):
                self._dlog("first welcome skip: already done")
                return
            if bool(getattr(self, "_tlite_welcome_launching", False)):
                self._dlog("first welcome skip: launching")
                return
            self._tlite_welcome_launching = True
            self._dlog("first welcome: start")

            def _worker():
                try:
                    target_ctx = None
                    for _ in range(40):
                        try:
                            from client_utils import get_last_fragment
                            frag = get_last_fragment()
                            if frag:
                                act = frag.getParentActivity()
                                if act:
                                    target_ctx = act
                                    break
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        try:
                            time.sleep(0.25)
                        except Exception:
                            break
                    if target_ctx is None:
                        self._dlog("first welcome: no activity context")
                        return
                    try:
                        if not os.path.exists(WELCOME_BG_CACHE_FILE):
                            self._load_welcome_bg_remote()
                    except Exception:
                        pass

                    def _show():
                        try:
                            shown = bool(self._show_welcome_sheet(target_ctx))
                            self._dlog(f"first welcome: show={shown}")
                            if shown:
                                self.set_setting("tlite_first_welcome_done", True)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                    run_on_ui_thread(_show)
                finally:
                    self._tlite_welcome_launching = False

            threading.Thread(target=_worker, daemon=True).start()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"first welcome check fail: {e}")

    def _is_our_settings_activity(self, activity):
        try:
            if activity is None:
                self._dlog("show usage stats sheet fail: no activity")
                return False
            p = None
            try:
                p = _get_private_field_silent(activity, "plugin")
            except Exception:
                p = None
            if not p:
                return False
            pid = ""
            try:
                pid = str(p.getId() or "").strip().lower()
            except Exception:
                pid = ""
            if pid == str(__id__).strip().lower():
                return True
            try:
                nm = str(p.getName() or "").strip().lower()
            except Exception:
                nm = ""
            return nm == str(__name__).strip().lower()
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _build_settings_header_view(self, ctx):
        try:
            compact = False
            try:
                dm = ctx.getResources().getDisplayMetrics()
                screen_w_dp = float(dm.widthPixels) / float(dm.density or 1.0)
                font_scale = float(getattr(ctx.getResources().getConfiguration(), "fontScale", 1.0) or 1.0)
                compact = bool(screen_w_dp < 372.0 or font_scale > 1.08)
            except Exception:
                compact = False
            try:
                is_dark = bool(Theme.isCurrentThemeDark())
            except Exception:
                is_dark = True

            panel_color = _ji(0xFF0F172A) if is_dark else _ji(0xFFFFFFFF)
            card_color = _ji(0xFF182336) if is_dark else _ji(0xFFF8FAFC)
            text_color = _ji(0xFFF8FAFC) if is_dark else _ji(0xFF111827)
            sub_color = _ji(0xFFAAB7CF) if is_dark else _ji(0xFF6B7280)
            stroke_color = _ji(0x22FFFFFF) if is_dark else _ji(0x160F172A)
            accent = _ji(0xFF3B82F6)

            outer = LinearLayout(ctx)
            outer.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            try:
                outer.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(6))
            except Exception:
                pass

            hero = FrameLayout(ctx)
            hero_bg = GradientDrawable()
            hero_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(28)))
            hero_bg.setColor(0x00000000)
            hero.setBackground(hero_bg)

            content = LinearLayout(ctx)
            content.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            try:
                content.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18))
            except Exception:
                pass

            top_row = LinearLayout(ctx)
            top_row.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            top_row.setGravity(Gravity.TOP)

            texts = LinearLayout(ctx)
            texts.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            lp_texts = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1.0)

            title = TextView(ctx)
            title.setText("Translatica Pro")
            title.setTextSize(1, 24)
            title.setTextColor(text_color)
            try:
                title.setTypeface(title.getTypeface(), 1)
            except Exception:
                pass
            texts.addView(title)

            subtitle = TextView(ctx)
            hero_subtitle = str(self._tr("first_welcome_divider") or "")
            docs_line = ""
            if "Docs: @Translatica" in hero_subtitle:
                hero_subtitle = hero_subtitle.replace(" Docs: @Translatica", "").replace("\nDocs: @Translatica", "")
                docs_line = "Docs: @Translatica"
            subtitle.setText(hero_subtitle)
            subtitle.setTextSize(1, 13)
            subtitle.setTextColor(sub_color)
            try:
                subtitle.setMaxLines(3)
            except Exception:
                pass
            subtitle.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(6), 0, 0)
            texts.addView(subtitle)
            if docs_line:
                docs_tv = TextView(ctx)
                docs_tv.setText(docs_line)
                docs_tv.setTextSize(1, 13)
                try:
                    docs_tv.setTextColor(accent)
                    docs_tv.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(4), 0, 0)
                    docs_tv.setClickable(True)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    class _OpenTranslatica(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                        def onClick(self_obj, v):
                            try:
                                from client_utils import get_messages_controller, get_last_fragment
                                get_messages_controller().openByUserName("Translatica", get_last_fragment(), 1)
                            except Exception:
                                try:
                                    self._open_external_url("https://t.me/Translatica")
                                except Exception:
                                    try:
                                        self.open_url("https://t.me/Translatica")
                                    except Exception:
                                        pass
                    docs_tv.setOnClickListener(_OpenTranslatica())
                except Exception:
                    pass
                texts.addView(docs_tv)
            top_row.addView(texts, lp_texts)

            top_icon = ImageView(ctx)
            try:
                top_icon.setScaleType(ImageView.ScaleType.CENTER_INSIDE)
                top_path = TOP_ICON_CACHE_FILE_DARK if is_dark else TOP_ICON_CACHE_FILE_LIGHT
                if os.path.exists(top_path):
                    bmp_t = BitmapFactory.decodeFile(top_path)
                    if bmp_t:
                        top_icon.setImageBitmap(bmp_t)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                top_icon.setClickable(True)
                top_icon.setFocusable(True)
            except Exception:
                pass

            class _OpenExtera(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):

                    try:
                        from client_utils import get_messages_controller, get_last_fragment
                        get_messages_controller().openByUserName("exteraDevPlugins", get_last_fragment(), 1)

                        try:
                            self.open_url("https://t.me/exteraDevPlugins")
                        except Exception:
                            pass

            try:

            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                class _TopLong(dynamic_proxy(View.OnLongClickListener)):

                            self._dlog(f"header icon long press fail: {e}")

                pass
            top_actions = LinearLayout(ctx)
            top_actions.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            top_actions.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)

            live_chip = TextView(ctx)
            live_chip.setText("Live")
            live_chip.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
            live_chip.setTextSize(1, 12)
            try:
                live_chip.setTypeface(live_chip.getTypeface(), 1)
            except Exception:

            except Exception:

                live_chip.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(6), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(6))
            except Exception:

            lp_top_icon = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(24), AndroidUtilities.dp(24))

            top_actions.addView(top_icon, lp_top_icon)

            content.addView(top_row)

            dotted_card = LinearLayout(ctx)
            dotted_card.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            dotted_card.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            dotted_bg = GradientDrawable()
            dotted_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(22)))
            dotted_bg.setColor(_ji(0xFFF1BFB8) if is_dark else card_color)
            dotted_card.setBackground(dotted_bg)
            try:

            except Exception:
                pass

            avatar_wrap = FrameLayout(ctx)
            avatar_bg = GradientDrawable()
            avatar_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(22)))
            avatar_bg.setColor(_ji(0x14FFFFFF) if is_dark else _ji(0xFFEFF6FF))
            avatar_wrap.setBackground(avatar_bg)

                avatar_wrap.setClipToOutline(True)
                avatar_wrap.setOutlineProvider(ViewOutlineProvider.BACKGROUND)
            except Exception:
                pass
            avatar = ImageView(ctx)
            try:
                avatar.setScaleType(ImageView.ScaleType.CENTER_CROP)
                av_bg = GradientDrawable()
                av_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(22)))
                av_bg.setColor(0x00000000)
                avatar.setBackground(av_bg)
                avatar.setClipToOutline(True)
                avatar.setOutlineProvider(ViewOutlineProvider.BACKGROUND)

            switch_title.setText(self._tr("settings_enable"))
            switch_title.setTextSize(1, 15)
            switch_title.setTextColor(text_color)

            switch_desc.setText(self._tr("settings_hero_enable_desc"))
            switch_desc.setTextSize(1, 12)
            switch_desc.setTextColor(sub_color)
            switch_desc.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(3), 0, 0)
            switch_texts.addView(switch_desc)
            switch_row.addView(switch_texts, lp_switch_texts)

            toggle = AndroidSwitch(ctx)
            try:
                toggle.setChecked(bool(self.get_setting("tlite_enabled", True)))
                toggle.getThumbDrawable().setTintList(ColorStateList.valueOf(_ji(0xFFFFFFFF)))
                toggle.getTrackDrawable().setTintList(ColorStateList.valueOf(accent if bool(self.get_setting("tlite_enabled", True)) else _ji(0x33515B70)))
            except Exception:
                pass
            checked_listener_cls = find_class("android.widget.CompoundButton$OnCheckedChangeListener")
            if checked_listener_cls is not None:
                plugin = self
                class _EnableChanged(dynamic_proxy(checked_listener_cls)):
                    def onCheckedChanged(self_obj, _button, is_checked):
                        try:
                            plugin.set_setting("tlite_enabled", bool(is_checked))
                            try:
                                toggle.getTrackDrawable().setTintList(ColorStateList.valueOf(accent if bool(is_checked) else _ji(0x33515B70)))
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            BulletinHelper.show_info(plugin._tr("bulletin_enabled") if bool(is_checked) else plugin._tr("bulletin_disabled"))
                        except Exception as e:
                            plugin._dlog(f"hero enable switch fail: {e}")
                try:
                    toggle.setOnCheckedChangeListener(_EnableChanged())
                except Exception:
                    pass
            switch_row.addView(toggle)

            outer.addView(hero, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            return outer
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"build settings header fail: {e}")
            return None

    def _build_settings_image_header_view(self, ctx):
        try:
            hero_height_dp = 200
            try:
                dm = ctx.getResources().getDisplayMetrics()
                screen_w_dp = float(dm.widthPixels) / float(dm.density or 1.0)
                font_scale = float(getattr(ctx.getResources().getConfiguration(), "fontScale", 1.0) or 1.0)
                if screen_w_dp < 360.0 or font_scale > 1.15:
                    hero_height_dp = 184
            except Exception:
                hero_height_dp = 200
            outer = LinearLayout(ctx)
            outer.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            try:
                outer.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(6), AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(6))
            except Exception:
                pass
            hero = FrameLayout(ctx)
            try:
                hero_bg = GradientDrawable()
                hero_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
                hero_bg.setColor(0x00000000)
                hero.setBackground(hero_bg)
                hero.setClipToOutline(True)
                hero.setOutlineProvider(ViewOutlineProvider.BACKGROUND)
            except Exception:
                pass
            banner = ImageView(ctx)
            try:
                banner.setScaleType(ImageView.ScaleType.CENTER_CROP)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                is_dark = bool(Theme.isCurrentThemeDark())
            except Exception:
                is_dark = True
            try:
                avatar_banner_path = AVATAR_TOOLS_HEADER_CACHE_FILE_DARK if is_dark else AVATAR_TOOLS_HEADER_CACHE_FILE_LIGHT
                fallback_banner_path = HEADER_IMAGE_CACHE_FILE_DARK if is_dark else HEADER_IMAGE_CACHE_FILE_LIGHT
                banner_path = avatar_banner_path if os.path.exists(avatar_banner_path) else fallback_banner_path
                if os.path.exists(banner_path):
                    bmp = BitmapFactory.decodeFile(banner_path)
                    if bmp:
                        banner.setImageBitmap(bmp)
            except Exception:
                pass
            hero.addView(
                banner,
                FrameLayout.LayoutParams(
                    FrameLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT,
                    AndroidUtilities.dp(hero_height_dp),
                ),
            )
            outer.addView(hero, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, AndroidUtilities.dp(hero_height_dp)))
            return outer
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"build image header fail: {e}")
            return None

        except Exception as e:
