            return None

    def _build_home_quick_cards_view(self, ctx):
        try:
            try:
                is_dark = bool(Theme.isCurrentThemeDark())
            except Exception:
                is_dark = True
            text_color = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteBlackText))
            sub_color = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteGrayText2))
            card_color = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhite))
            accent = _ji(0xFF3B82F6)

            root = HorizontalScrollView(ctx)
            try:
                root.setHorizontalScrollBarEnabled(False)
                root.setOverScrollMode(View.OVER_SCROLL_NEVER)
                root.setFillViewport(False)
            except Exception:
                pass
            row = LinearLayout(ctx)
            row.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            try:
                row.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(6), AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(6))
            except Exception:
                pass

            def _make_quick_card(icon_name, title_text, desc_text, callback):
                card = LinearLayout(ctx)
                card.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
                card.setGravity(Gravity.TOP)
                card_bg = GradientDrawable()
                card_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(20)))
                card_bg.setColor(card_color)
                card.setBackground(card_bg)
                try:
                    card.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14))
                    card.setMinimumHeight(AndroidUtilities.dp(144))
                    card.setClickable(True)
                    card.setFocusable(True)
                except Exception:
                    pass

                icon_wrap = FrameLayout(ctx)
                icon_bg = GradientDrawable()
                icon_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(14)))
                icon_bg.setColor(_ji(0x143B82F6) if is_dark else _ji(0x103B82F6))
                icon_wrap.setBackground(icon_bg)

                icon = ImageView(ctx)
                try:
                    icon.setScaleType(ImageView.ScaleType.CENTER_INSIDE)
                    rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier(str(icon_name or ""), "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                    if rid:
                        icon.setImageResource(rid)
                        icon.setColorFilter(accent)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                icon_wrap.addView(icon, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), Gravity.CENTER))
                card.addView(icon_wrap, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(36), AndroidUtilities.dp(36)))

                title_v = TextView(ctx)
                title_v.setText(title_text)
                title_v.setTextSize(1, 15)
                title_v.setTextColor(text_color)
                try:
                    title_v.setTypeface(title_v.getTypeface(), 1)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                title_v.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(12), 0, 0)
                card.addView(title_v)

                desc_v = TextView(ctx)
                desc_v.setText(desc_text)
                desc_v.setTextSize(1, 12)
                desc_v.setTextColor(sub_color)
                try:
                    desc_v.setMaxLines(3)
                    desc_v.setEllipsize(TextUtils.TruncateAt.END)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                desc_v.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(6), 0, 0)
                card.addView(desc_v)

                if callback is not None:
                    class _CardOpen(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                        def onClick(self_obj, v):
                            try:
                                callback()
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                    try:
                        card.setOnClickListener(_CardOpen())
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                return card

            ai_card = _make_quick_card(
                "ai_chat_remix",
                "Assist",
                self._tr("settings_ai_custom_open_desc"),
                lambda: self._open_assist_home_entry(),
            )
            chat_card = _make_quick_card(
                "tabs_chats_solar",
                self._tr("settings_ai_avatar_tools"),
                self._tr("settings_ai_avatar_tools_desc"),
                lambda: self._open_home_via_native_item("tlite_ai_avatar_tools_subfragment"),
            )
            perf_card = _make_quick_card(
                "boosts",
                "Core",
                self._tr("settings_performance_open_desc"),
                lambda: self._open_home_via_native_item("tlite_performance_subfragment"),
            )
            stats_card = _make_quick_card(
                "msg_stats_solar",
                "Insights",
                self._tr("settings_usage_stats_open_desc"),
                lambda: self._open_home_via_native_item("tlite_usage_stats_subfragment"),
            )

            card_w = AndroidUtilities.dp(164)
            card_h = AndroidUtilities.dp(144)
            lp_ai = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(card_w, card_h)
            lp_chat = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(card_w, card_h)
            lp_chat.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
            lp_perf = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(card_w, card_h)
            lp_perf.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
            lp_stats = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(card_w, card_h)
            lp_stats.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
            row.addView(ai_card, lp_ai)
            row.addView(chat_card, lp_chat)
            row.addView(perf_card, lp_perf)
            row.addView(stats_card, lp_stats)
            root.addView(row, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(FrameLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, FrameLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            return root
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"build home quick cards fail: {e}")
            return None

    def _build_usage_stats_header_view(self, ctx):
        try:
            text_color = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteBlackText))
            sub_color = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteGrayText2))
            card_color = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhite))
            accent = _ji(0xFF3B82F6)
            palette = [_ji(0xFFFB923C), _ji(0xFF4ADE80), _ji(0xFF8B5CF6), _ji(0xFF60A5FA), _ji(0xFFFACC15)]
            rows = self._usage_stats_language_rows(5)
            chat_rows = self._usage_stats_chat_rows(5)
            stats = self._usage_stats_get()
            lang_map = self._usage_stats_target_lang_map(stats)
            total = int(sum(int(v or 0) for v in dict(lang_map).values()) or 0)
            enabled = bool(self._usage_stats_enabled())
            summary_total = int(self._usage_stats_action_count("summary") or 0)
            translation_total = max(0, int(stats.get("total", 0) or 0) - summary_total)

            def _round_bg(color_value, radius_dp=24):
                bg = GradientDrawable()
                bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(radius_dp)))
                bg.setColor(int(color_value))
                return bg

            def _make_icon(icon_name, tint):
                icon = ImageView(ctx)
                try:
                    icon.setScaleType(ImageView.ScaleType.CENTER_INSIDE)
                    rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier(str(icon_name or ""), "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                    if rid:
                        icon.setImageResource(rid)
                        icon.setColorFilter(int(tint))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                return icon

            def _make_action_card(icon_name, title_text, summary_text, callback):
                card = LinearLayout(ctx)
                card.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
                card.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
                card.setBackground(_round_bg(card_color, 20))
                try:
                    card.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14))
                    card.setMinimumHeight(AndroidUtilities.dp(78))
                    card.setClickable(True)
                    card.setFocusable(True)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                icon_wrap = FrameLayout(ctx)
                icon_wrap.setBackground(_round_bg(_ji(0x143B82F6), 14))
                icon_wrap.addView(_make_icon(icon_name, accent), FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), Gravity.CENTER))
                card.addView(icon_wrap, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(36), AndroidUtilities.dp(36)))
                texts = LinearLayout(ctx)
                texts.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
                lp_texts = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1.0)
                lp_texts.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(12)
                title_v = TextView(ctx)
                title_v.setText(str(title_text or ""))
                title_v.setTextSize(1, 16)
                title_v.setTextColor(text_color)
                try:
                    title_v.setTypeface(title_v.getTypeface(), 1)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                texts.addView(title_v)
                summary_v = TextView(ctx)
                summary_v.setText(str(summary_text or ""))
                summary_v.setTextSize(1, 13)
                summary_v.setTextColor(sub_color)
                try:
                    summary_v.setMaxLines(2)
                    summary_v.setEllipsize(TextUtils.TruncateAt.END)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    summary_v.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(4), 0, 0)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                texts.addView(summary_v)
                card.addView(texts, lp_texts)
                card.addView(_make_icon("msg_arrowright", sub_color), LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
                if callback is not None:
                    class _CardClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                        def onClick(self_obj, v):
                            try:
                                callback()
                            except Exception as ce:
                                self._dlog(f"usage stats card open fail: {ce}")
                    try:
                        card.setOnClickListener(_CardClick())
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                return card

            outer = LinearLayout(ctx)
            outer.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            try:
                outer.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
            except Exception:
                pass

            chart_card = LinearLayout(ctx)
            chart_card.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            chart_card.setBackground(_round_bg(card_color, 28))
            try:
                chart_card.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18))
            except Exception:
                pass

            title = TextView(ctx)
            title.setText(self._tr("settings_usage_stats_chart_title"))
            title.setTextSize(1, 18)
            title.setTextColor(text_color)
            try:
                title.setTypeface(title.getTypeface(), 1)
            except Exception:
                pass
            chart_card.addView(title)

            subtitle = TextView(ctx)
            subtitle_text = self._tr("settings_usage_stats_chart_desc")
            if enabled and int(stats.get("total", 0) or 0) > 0:
                subtitle_text = f"{translation_total} {self._tr('settings_usage_stats_total_label')} - {summary_total} {self._tr('settings_usage_stats_summaries_label')}"
            subtitle.setText(subtitle_text)
            subtitle.setTextSize(1, 12)
            subtitle.setTextColor(sub_color)
            try:
                subtitle.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(6), 0, 0)
            except Exception:
                pass
            chart_card.addView(subtitle)

            if enabled and total > 0:
                total_wrap = LinearLayout(ctx)
                total_wrap.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
                total_wrap.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL)
                try:
                    total_wrap.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(16), 0, AndroidUtilities.dp(12))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                total_v = TextView(ctx)
                total_v.setText(str(total))
                total_v.setTextSize(1, 34)
                total_v.setTextColor(text_color)
                try:
                    total_v.setTypeface(total_v.getTypeface(), 1)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                total_wrap.addView(total_v)
                total_label = TextView(ctx)
                total_label.setText(self._tr("settings_usage_stats_total_label"))
                total_label.setTextSize(1, 13)
                total_label.setTextColor(sub_color)
                total_wrap.addView(total_label)
                chart_card.addView(total_wrap)

                bar = LinearLayout(ctx)
                bar.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
                for idx_row, row_item in enumerate(rows[:5]):
                    seg = View(ctx)
                    seg.setBackground(_round_bg(palette[idx_row % len(palette)], 999))
                    lp_seg = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(12), max(1, int(row_item.get("percent", 0) or 0)))
                    if idx_row < len(rows[:5]) - 1:
                        lp_seg.rightMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(6)
                    bar.addView(seg, lp_seg)
                if bar.getChildCount() == 0:
                    filler = View(ctx)
                    filler.setBackground(_round_bg(_ji(0x143B82F6), 999))
                    bar.addView(filler, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(12), 1))
                chart_card.addView(bar, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

                legend = LinearLayout(ctx)
                legend.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
                try:
                    legend.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(14), 0, 0)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                for idx_row, row_item in enumerate(rows[:4]):
                    item_row = LinearLayout(ctx)
                    item_row.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
                    item_row.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
                    if idx_row > 0:
                        try:
                            item_row.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(8), 0, 0)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                    dot = View(ctx)
                    dot.setBackground(_round_bg(palette[idx_row % len(palette)], 999))
                    item_row.addView(dot, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(12)))
                    name = TextView(ctx)
                    name.setText(f"{str(row_item.get('label', '')).strip()} {int(row_item.get('percent', 0) or 0)}%")
                    name.setTextSize(1, 13)
                    name.setTextColor(text_color)
                    lp_name = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1.0)
                    lp_name.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
                    item_row.addView(name, lp_name)
                    count = TextView(ctx)
                    count.setText(str(int(row_item.get('count', 0) or 0)))
                    count.setTextSize(1, 13)
                    count.setTextColor(accent)
                    item_row.addView(count)
                    legend.addView(item_row)
                chart_card.addView(legend)
            else:
                empty = TextView(ctx)
                empty.setText(self._tr("settings_usage_stats_chart_empty"))
                empty.setTextSize(1, 13)
                empty.setTextColor(sub_color)
                try:
                    empty.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(16), 0, 0)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                chart_card.addView(empty)

            reset_row = LinearLayout(ctx)
            reset_row.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            reset_row.setGravity(Gravity.END)
            try:
                reset_row.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(14), 0, 0)
            except Exception:
                pass
            reset_btn = TextView(ctx)
            reset_btn.setText(self._tr("settings_usage_stats_reset"))
            reset_btn.setTextSize(1, 13)
            reset_btn.setTextColor(accent)
            reset_btn.setBackground(_round_bg(_ji(0x143B82F6), 999))
            try:
                reset_btn.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
                reset_btn.setClickable(True)
                reset_btn.setFocusable(True)
            except Exception:
                pass
            class _ResetClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        self._reset_usage_stats()
                        run_on_ui_thread(self.reload_settings)
                    except Exception as re:
                        self._dlog(f"usage stats reset click fail: {re}")
            try:
                reset_btn.setOnClickListener(_ResetClick())
            except Exception:
                pass
            reset_row.addView(reset_btn)
            chart_card.addView(reset_row)
            outer.addView(chart_card, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            lang_summary = self._tr("settings_usage_stats_empty")
            if rows:
                top_lang = rows[0]
                lang_summary = f"{str(top_lang.get('label', '')).strip()} • {int(top_lang.get('percent', 0) or 0)}%"
            if rows:
                top_lang = rows[0]
                lang_summary = f"{str(top_lang.get('label', '')).strip()} - {int(top_lang.get('percent', 0) or 0)}%"
            lang_card = _make_action_card(
                "msg_language",
                self._tr("settings_usage_stats_languages"),
                lang_summary,
                lambda: self._show_usage_stats_sheet(self._tr("settings_usage_stats_languages"), self._usage_stats_language_rows(12), "msg_language"),
            )
            lp_lang = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_lang.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(12)
            outer.addView(lang_card, lp_lang)

            chat_summary = self._tr("settings_usage_stats_empty")
            if chat_rows:
                top_chat = chat_rows[0]
                chat_summary = f"{str(top_chat.get('title', '')).strip()} • {int(top_chat.get('percent', 0) or 0)}%"
            if chat_rows:
                top_chat = chat_rows[0]
                chat_summary = f"{str(top_chat.get('title', '')).strip()} - {int(top_chat.get('percent', 0) or 0)}%"
            chat_card = _make_action_card(
                "msg_viewchats",
                self._tr("settings_usage_stats_chats"),
                chat_summary,
                lambda: self._show_usage_stats_sheet(self._tr("settings_usage_stats_chats"), self._usage_stats_chat_rows(5), "msg_viewchats"),
            )
            lp_chat = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_chat.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
            outer.addView(chat_card, lp_chat)
            return outer
            is_dark = bool(Theme.isCurrentThemeDark())
            bg_color = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhite))
            title_color = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteBlackText))
            sub_color = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteGrayText2))
            accent = _ji(0xFF3B82F6)
            rows = self._usage_stats_language_rows(5)
            stats = self._usage_stats_get()
            total = int(stats.get("total", 0) or 0)
            enabled = bool(self._usage_stats_enabled())

            def _paint_color(value, fallback):
                try:
                    iv = int(value)
                    # Força o valor para o intervalo de um signed int32 do Java (-2147483648 a 2147483647)
                    iv &= 0xFFFFFFFF
                    if iv > 0x7FFFFFFF:
                        iv -= 0x100000000
                    return int(iv)
                except Exception:
                    try:
                        fb = int(fallback)
                        fb &= 0xFFFFFFFF
                        if fb > 0x7FFFFFFF:
                            fb -= 0x100000000
                        return int(fb)
                    except Exception:
                        return 0xFF3B82F6

            outer = LinearLayout(ctx)
            outer.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            try:
                outer.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
            except Exception:
                pass

            card = LinearLayout(ctx)
            card.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            card_bg = GradientDrawable()
            card_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(28)))
            # Tratamento seguro para a cor do card
            try:
                card_bg.setColor(int(_paint_color(bg_color, 0xFFFFFFFF)))
            except Exception:
                pass
            card.setBackground(card_bg)
            try:
                card.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18))
            except Exception:
                pass

            title = TextView(ctx)
            title.setText(self._tr("settings_usage_stats_chart_title"))
            title.setTextSize(1, 18)
            # Tratamento seguro para a cor do texto do título
            try:
                title.setTextColor(int(_paint_color(title_color, 0xFF000000)))
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                title.setTypeface(title.getTypeface(), 1)
            except Exception:
                pass
            card.addView(title)
            subtitle = TextView(ctx)
            subtitle.setText(self._tr("settings_usage_stats_chart_desc"))
            subtitle.setTextSize(1, 12)
            # Tratamento seguro para a cor do subtítulo
            try:
                subtitle.setTextColor(int(_paint_color(sub_color, 0xFF888888)))
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                subtitle.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(6), 0, 0)
            except Exception:
                pass
            card.addView(subtitle)

            if enabled:
                graph = ImageView(ctx)
                try:
                    graph.setScaleType(ImageView.ScaleType.CENTER_INSIDE)
                    size = AndroidUtilities.dp(192)
                    bmp = Bitmap.createBitmap(size, size, Bitmap.Config.ARGB_8888)
                    canvas = Canvas(bmp)
                    paint = Paint()
                    paint.setAntiAlias(True)
                    paint.setStyle(Paint.Style.STROKE)
                    paint.setStrokeCap(Paint.Cap.ROUND)
                    paint.setStrokeWidth(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
                    rect = RectF(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)), float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)), float(size - AndroidUtilities.dp(18)), float(size - AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
                    track = Paint()
                    track.setAntiAlias(True)
                    track.setStyle(Paint.Style.STROKE)
                    track.setStrokeCap(Paint.Cap.ROUND)
                    track.setStrokeWidth(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
                    track_color = _ji(0x18FFFFFF) if is_dark else _ji(0x140F172A)
                    track.setColor(int(_paint_color(track_color, 0x22000000)))
                    canvas.drawArc(rect, -90.0, 360.0, False, track)
                    palette = [0xFFFB923C, 0xFF4ADE80, 0xFF8B5CF6, 0xFF60A5FA, 0xFFFACC15]
                    start_angle = -90.0
                    segs = rows if rows else [{"percent": 100}]
                    for idx_seg, row_item in enumerate(segs[:5]):
                        pct = max(1, int(row_item.get("percent", 0) or 0))
                        sweep = float(360.0 * (float(pct) / 100.0))
                        paint.setColor(int(_paint_color(palette[idx_seg % len(palette)], 0xFF3B82F6)))
                        canvas.drawArc(rect, start_angle, sweep - 3.0, False, paint)
                        start_angle += sweep
                    center_paint = Paint()
                    center_paint.setAntiAlias(True)
                    center_paint.setTextAlign(Paint.Align.CENTER)
                    center_paint.setColor(int(_paint_color(title_color, 0xFFFFFFFF if is_dark else 0xFF111827)))
                    try:
                        center_paint.setTypeface(Typeface.DEFAULT_BOLD)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    center_paint.setTextSize(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(26)))
                    cx = float(size) / 2.0
                    cy = float(size) / 2.0 - float(AndroidUtilities.dp(4))
                    canvas.drawText(str(total), cx, cy, center_paint)
                    center_paint.setTypeface(Typeface.DEFAULT)
                    center_paint.setTextSize(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(12)))
                    center_paint.setColor(int(_paint_color(sub_color, 0xFF94A3B8 if is_dark else 0xFF64748B)))
                    canvas.drawText(self._tr("settings_usage_stats_total_label"), cx, cy + float(AndroidUtilities.dp(20)), center_paint)
                    graph.setImageBitmap(bmp)
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"build usage stats graph fail: {e}")
                lp_graph = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(192), AndroidUtilities.dp(192))
                lp_graph.gravity = Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL
                lp_graph.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(18)
                card.addView(graph, lp_graph)

                legend = LinearLayout(ctx)
                legend.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
                try:
                    legend.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(8), 0, 0)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                palette = [0xFFFB923C, 0xFF4ADE80, 0xFF8B5CF6, 0xFF60A5FA, 0xFFFACC15]
                for idx_row, row_item in enumerate(rows[:4]):
                    item_row = LinearLayout(ctx)
                    item_row.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
                    item_row.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
                    dot = View(ctx)
                    dot_bg = GradientDrawable()
                    dot_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(6)))
                    # Tratamento seguro para a cor do ponto da legenda
                    try:
                        dot_bg.setColor(int(_paint_color(palette[idx_row % len(palette)], 0xFF3B82F6)))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    dot.setBackground(dot_bg)
                    item_row.addView(dot, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(12)))
                    txt = TextView(ctx)
                    txt.setText(f"{row_item.get('label', '')}  {row_item.get('percent', 0)}%")
                    txt.setTextSize(1, 13)
                    # Tratamento seguro para a cor do texto da legenda
                    try:
                        txt.setTextColor(int(_paint_color(title_color, 0xFF000000)))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    lp_txt = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1.0)
                    lp_txt.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
                    item_row.addView(txt, lp_txt)
                    cnt = TextView(ctx)
                    cnt.setText(str(int(row_item.get("count", 0) or 0)))
                    cnt.setTextSize(1, 13)
                    # Tratamento seguro para a cor do contador
                    try:
                        cnt.setTextColor(int(_paint_color(accent, 0xFF3B82F6)))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    item_row.addView(cnt)
                    legend.addView(item_row, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
                if rows:
                    lp_legend = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
                    lp_legend.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(6)
                    card.addView(legend, lp_legend)
            else:
                note = TextView(ctx)
                note.setText(self._tr("settings_usage_stats_empty"))
                note.setTextSize(1, 13)
                # Tratamento seguro para a cor da nota
                try:
                    note.setTextColor(int(_paint_color(sub_color, 0xFF888888)))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    note.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(14), 0, 0)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                card.addView(note, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            outer.addView(card, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            return outer
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"build usage stats header fail: {e}")
            return None

    def _inject_settings_header(self, activity, items):
        try:
            if not self._is_our_settings_activity(activity):
                return
            try:
                self._settings_activity_ref = activity
            except Exception:
                pass
            fragment_kind = "home"
            try:
                fragment_kind = self._settings_fragment_kind(items)
            except Exception:
                fragment_kind = "home"
            if fragment_kind == "ai_assist":
                return
            try:
                has_header = False
                has_version = False
                has_home_quick_cards = False
                for i in range(items.size()):
                    it = items.get(i)
                    mk = str(getattr(it, "object2", "") or "")
                    if mk == "__tlite_settings_header__":
                        has_header = True
                    elif mk == "__tlite_settings_version__":
                        has_version = True
                    elif mk == "__tlite_home_quick_cards__":
                        has_home_quick_cards = True
            except Exception:
                has_header = False
                has_version = False
                has_home_quick_cards = False

            ctx = activity.getContext() if hasattr(activity, "getContext") else None
            if not ctx:
                return
            try:
                if (not bool(self.get_setting("tlite_first_welcome_done", False))) and (not bool(getattr(self, "_tlite_welcome_launching", False))):
                    self._tlite_welcome_launching = True
                    def _show_once():
                        try:
                            shown = bool(self._show_welcome_sheet(ctx))
                            if shown:
                                self.set_setting("tlite_first_welcome_done", True)
                        finally:
                            self._tlite_welcome_launching = False
                    run_on_ui_thread(_show_once)
            except Exception:
                pass
            UItem = find_class("org.telegram.ui.Components.UItem")
            if not UItem:
                return
            if not has_header and fragment_kind not in ("performance", "usage_stats"):
                view = self._build_settings_image_header_view(ctx) if fragment_kind == "avatar_tools" else self._build_settings_header_view(ctx)
                if view:
                    hi = UItem.asCustom(view)
                    try:
                        hi.object2 = "__tlite_settings_header__"
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        hi.setTransparent(True)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    items.add(0, hi)
                    try:
                        items.add(1, UItem.asShadow())
                    except Exception:
                        pass
            if not has_version and fragment_kind == "home":
                v = self._build_settings_version_view(ctx)
                if v:
                    vi = UItem.asCustom(v)
                    try:
                        vi.object2 = "__tlite_settings_version__"
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        vi.setTransparent(True)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    items.add(vi)
            if fragment_kind == "home" and not has_home_quick_cards:
                try:
                    insert_idx = -1
                    remove_indices = []
                    open_item_map = {}
                    for i in range(items.size()):
                        try:
                            it = items.get(i)
                        except Exception:
                            continue
                        key = str(self._get_uitem_setting_key(it) or "").strip()
                        txt = str(self._get_uitem_text(it) or "").strip().lower()
                        si = getattr(it, "settingItem", None)
                        la = str(getattr(it, "link_alias", "") or (getattr(si, "link_alias", "") if si else "") or "").strip()
                        joined = " | ".join([key, la, txt]).lower()
                        if key == "tlite_ai_correction_subfragment" or la == "tlite_ai_correction_subfragment" or txt == "assist":
                            open_item_map["tlite_ai_correction_subfragment"] = it
                            remove_indices.append(i)
                            continue
                        if key == "tlite_ai_avatar_tools_subfragment" or la == "tlite_ai_avatar_tools_subfragment" or txt == str(self._tr("settings_ai_avatar_tools") or "").strip().lower():
                            open_item_map["tlite_ai_avatar_tools_subfragment"] = it
                            remove_indices.append(i)
                            continue
                        if key == "tlite_performance_subfragment" or la == "tlite_performance_subfragment" or txt == "core":
                            open_item_map["tlite_performance_subfragment"] = it
                            remove_indices.append(i)
                            continue
                        if key == "tlite_usage_stats_subfragment" or la == "tlite_usage_stats_subfragment" or txt == "insights":
                            open_item_map["tlite_usage_stats_subfragment"] = it
                            remove_indices.append(i)
                            continue
                        if insert_idx < 0 and ("tlite_channel_summary_provider" in joined or txt == str(self._tr("ai_sheet_summary") or "").strip().lower()):
                            insert_idx = i + 2
                    if insert_idx >= 0:
                        self._dlog(f"home quick cards map correction={bool(open_item_map.get('tlite_ai_correction_subfragment'))} avatar={bool(open_item_map.get('tlite_ai_avatar_tools_subfragment'))} performance={bool(open_item_map.get('tlite_performance_subfragment'))} stats={bool(open_item_map.get('tlite_usage_stats_subfragment'))} insert_idx={insert_idx}")
                        for idx_rm in reversed(sorted(list(set(remove_indices)))):
                            try:
                                items.remove(idx_rm)
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                        try:
                            self._home_open_item_map = open_item_map
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        quick = self._build_home_quick_cards_view(ctx)
                        if quick:
                            qi = UItem.asCustom(quick)
                            try:
                                qi.object2 = "__tlite_home_quick_cards__"
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            try:
                                qi.setTransparent(True)
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            items.add(insert_idx, qi)
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"inject home quick cards fail: {e}")
            if fragment_kind == "usage_stats":
                try:
                    insert_idx = -1
                    remove_indices = []
                    for i in range(items.size()):
                        it = items.get(i)
                        probe = " | ".join([
                            str(getattr(it, "key", "") or ""),
                            str(getattr(it, "link_alias", "") or ""),
                            str(getattr(it, "object2", "") or ""),
                            str(getattr(getattr(it, "settingItem", None), "link_alias", "") or ""),
                        ]).lower()
                        if "tlite_usage_stats_enabled" in probe:
                            insert_idx = i + 1
                        if "__tlite_usage_stats_graph_marker__" in probe or "__tlite_usage_stats_custom__" in probe:
                            remove_indices.append(i)
                    for idx_rm in reversed(remove_indices):
                        try:
                            items.remove(idx_rm)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                    if insert_idx >= 0:
                        graph_view = self._build_usage_stats_header_view(ctx)
                        if graph_view:
                            gi = UItem.asCustom(graph_view)
                            try:
                                gi.object2 = "__tlite_usage_stats_custom__"
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            try:
                                gi.setTransparent(True)
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            items.add(insert_idx, gi)
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"inject usage stats graph fail: {e}")
            if fragment_kind == "avatar_tools":
                try:
                    self._inject_avatar_tools_extras(activity, items)
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"inject avatar tools extras fail: {e}")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"inject settings header fail: {e}")

    def _inject_avatar_tools_extras(self, activity, items):
        try:
            UItem = find_class("org.telegram.ui.Components.UItem")
            Utilities = find_class("org.telegram.messenger.Utilities")
            if UItem is None or Utilities is None or items is None:
                return
            insert_idx = -1
            remove_idx = -1
            for i in range(items.size()):
                try:
                    it = items.get(i)
                except Exception:
                    continue
                probe = []
                for attr_name in ("key", "link_alias", "object2", "text"):
                    try:
                        val = getattr(it, attr_name, None)
                        if val is not None:
                            probe.append(str(val))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                joined = " | ".join(probe).lower()
                if "__tlite_floating_alpha_marker__" in joined:
                    insert_idx = i
                    remove_idx = i
                    break
            if insert_idx < 0:
                return
            try:
                items.remove(remove_idx)
            except Exception:
                pass
            current = self._floating_alpha_index()
            if current < 0:
                current = 0
            if current > 3:
                current = 3
            labels = self._floating_alpha_options()
            CallbackInterface = Utilities.Callback
            String = jclass("java.lang.String")
            plugin = self

            class _FloatingAlphaSlideCallback(dynamic_proxy(CallbackInterface)):
                def run(self_cb, value):
                    try:
                        raw = str(value or "").strip()
                        try:
                            v = int(raw)
                        except Exception:
                            if raw == plugin._tr("settings_floating_alpha_default"):
                                v = 0
                            elif raw == "50%":
                                v = 1
                            elif raw == "70%":
                                v = 2
                            elif raw == "90%":
                                v = 3
                            else:
                                v = 0
                    except Exception:
                        v = 0
                    if v < 0:
                        v = 0
                    if v > 3:
                        v = 3
                    try:
                        plugin.set_setting("tlite_floating_alpha", v)
                        plugin._dlog(f"floating alpha changed raw={str(value or '')} parsed={v}")
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        plugin._sync_floating_button(plugin._chat_fragment_ref)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        plugin.reload_settings()
                    except Exception:
                        pass

            slide_items = jarray(String)(labels)
            items.add(insert_idx, UItem.asSlideView(slide_items, current, _FloatingAlphaSlideCallback()))
            try:
                items.add(insert_idx + 1, UItem.asShadow())
            except Exception:
                pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"inject avatar tools slide fail: {e}")

    def _settings_fragment_kind(self, items):
        try:
            if items is None:
                return "home"
            found_ai = False
            found_home = False
            found_avatar_tools = False
            found_performance = False
            found_usage_stats = False
            for i in range(items.size()):
                try:
                    it = items.get(i)
                except Exception:
                    continue
                candidates = []
                for attr_name in ("key", "link_alias", "object2", "text"):
                    try:
                        val = getattr(it, attr_name, None)
                        if val is not None:
                            candidates.append(str(val))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                probe = " | ".join(candidates).lower()
                if "tlite_ai_custom_url" in probe or "tlite_ai_custom_key" in probe or "tlite_ai_custom_model" in probe or "tlite_ai_mode_custom_prompt" in probe:
                    found_ai = True
                if "tlite_ai_avatar_action" in probe or "tlite_ai_avatar_summary_lang" in probe or "tlite_live_preview_enabled" in probe or "tlite_live_preview_delay" in probe:
                    found_avatar_tools = True
                if "tlite_perf_" in probe or "settings_performance_intro" in probe or "core" in probe:
                    found_performance = True
                if (
                    "tlite_usage_stats_" in probe
                    or "settings_usage_stats_" in probe
                    or "insights" in probe
                    or str(self._tr("settings_usage_stats_intro") or "").strip().lower() in probe
                    or str(self._tr("settings_usage_stats_languages") or "").strip().lower() in probe
                    or str(self._tr("settings_usage_stats_chats") or "").strip().lower() in probe
                ):
                    found_usage_stats = True
                if "tlite_target_lang" in probe or "tlite_service" in probe or "tlite_plugin_lang" in probe:
                    found_home = True
            if found_usage_stats and not found_home:
                return "usage_stats"
            if found_performance and not found_home:
                return "performance"
            if found_avatar_tools and not found_home:
                return "avatar_tools"
            if found_ai and not found_home:
                return "ai_assist"
            return "home"
        except Exception:
            return "home"

    def _show_debug_quick_popup(self, anchor_view):
        try:
            if anchor_view is None:
                return
            ctx = anchor_view.getContext()
            LinearLayoutCls = find_class("android.widget.LinearLayout")
            TextViewCls = find_class("android.widget.TextView")
            PopupWindow = find_class("android.widget.PopupWindow")
            GradientDrawable = find_class("android.graphics.drawable.GradientDrawable")
            TypedValue = find_class("android.util.TypedValue")
            if not LinearLayoutCls or not TextViewCls or not PopupWindow:
                return

            enabled = bool(self.get_setting("tlite_debug_logs", False))
            stats_enabled = bool(self._stats_enabled())
            root = LinearLayoutCls(ctx)
            root.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            try:
                bg = GradientDrawable()
                bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(12)))
                bg.setColor(int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_actionBarDefaultSubmenuBackground)))
                root.setBackground(bg)
                root.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
            except Exception:
                pass

            row = LinearLayoutCls(ctx)
            row.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            row.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            try:
                row.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
            except Exception:
                pass

            tv = TextViewCls(ctx)
            tv.setText(self._tr("settings_debug_logs"))
            try:
                tv.setTextColor(int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteBlackText)))
                tv.setTextSize(TypedValue.COMPLEX_UNIT_DIP, 16)
                tv.setTypeface(AndroidUtilities.getTypeface("fonts/rmedium.ttf"))
            except Exception:
                pass
            row.addView(tv, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            cb = LinearLayoutCls(ctx)
            cb.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
            try:
                cb_bg = GradientDrawable()
                cb_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(6)))
                cb_bg.setColor(0x00000000)
                if enabled:
                    cb_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_switchTrackChecked)))
                else:
                    cb_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteGrayText)))
                cb.setBackground(cb_bg)
            except Exception:
                pass

            mark = TextViewCls(ctx)
            mark.setText("\u2713" if enabled else "")
            try:
                mark.setTextSize(TypedValue.COMPLEX_UNIT_DIP, 14)
                mark.setTypeface(AndroidUtilities.getTypeface("fonts/rmedium.ttf"))
                mark.setTextColor(int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteBlackText)))
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                cb.addView(mark, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            except Exception:
                cb.addView(mark)
            lp_cb = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(24), AndroidUtilities.dp(24))
            lp_cb.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
            row.addView(cb, lp_cb)

            root.addView(row, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            row_stats = LinearLayoutCls(ctx)
            row_stats.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            row_stats.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            try:
                row_stats.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
            except Exception:
                pass

            tv_stats = TextViewCls(ctx)
            tv_stats.setText(self._tr("stats_enabled"))
            try:
                tv_stats.setTextColor(int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteBlackText)))
                tv_stats.setTextSize(TypedValue.COMPLEX_UNIT_DIP, 16)
                tv_stats.setTypeface(AndroidUtilities.getTypeface("fonts/rmedium.ttf"))
            except Exception:
                pass
            row_stats.addView(tv_stats, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            cb_stats = LinearLayoutCls(ctx)
            cb_stats.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
            try:
                cb_stats_bg = GradientDrawable()
                cb_stats_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(6)))
                cb_stats_bg.setColor(0x00000000)
                if stats_enabled:
                    cb_stats_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_switchTrackChecked)))
                else:
                    cb_stats_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteGrayText)))
                cb_stats.setBackground(cb_stats_bg)
            except Exception:
                pass

            mark_stats = TextViewCls(ctx)
            mark_stats.setText("\u2713" if stats_enabled else "")
            try:
                mark_stats.setTextSize(TypedValue.COMPLEX_UNIT_DIP, 14)
                mark_stats.setTypeface(AndroidUtilities.getTypeface("fonts/rmedium.ttf"))
                mark_stats.setTextColor(int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteBlackText)))
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                cb_stats.addView(mark_stats, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            except Exception:
                cb_stats.addView(mark_stats)
            lp_cb_stats = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(24), AndroidUtilities.dp(24))
            lp_cb_stats.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
            row_stats.addView(cb_stats, lp_cb_stats)

            root.addView(row_stats, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            popup = PopupWindow(root, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, True)
            try:
                popup.setOutsideTouchable(True)
                popup.setFocusable(True)
            except Exception:
                pass

            def _toggle(_v=None):
                try:
                    nv = not bool(self.get_setting("tlite_debug_logs", False))
                    self.set_setting("tlite_debug_logs", nv)
                    if nv:
                        try:
                            BulletinHelper.show_success(";)")
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                    try:
                        self.reload_settings()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        run_on_ui_thread(self._refresh_settings_screen)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"debug toggle fail: {e}")
                try:
                    popup.dismiss()
                except Exception:
                    pass

            class _Click(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    _toggle()
            row.setOnClickListener(_Click())

            def _toggle_stats(_v=None):
                try:
                    nv = not bool(self._stats_enabled())
                    self.set_setting("tlite_stats_enabled", nv)
                    try:
                        BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("bulletin_stats_enabled") if nv else self._tr("bulletin_stats_disabled"))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    if nv:
                        try:
                            self._telemetry_queue_event("session_start", feature="", count=1, force_flush=True)
                            if not bool(self.get_setting("tlite_stats_install_event_sent_v1", False)):
                                self._telemetry_queue_event("install", feature="", count=1, force_flush=True)
                                self.set_setting("tlite_stats_install_event_sent_v1", True)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"stats toggle fail: {e}")
                try:
                    popup.dismiss()
                except Exception:
                    pass

            class _StatsClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    _toggle_stats()
            row_stats.setOnClickListener(_StatsClick())

            try:
                popup.showAsDropDown(anchor_view, 0, AndroidUtilities.dp(8), Gravity.START)
            except Exception:
                try:
                    popup.showAsDropDown(anchor_view, 0, AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
                except Exception:
                    popup.showAsDropDown(anchor_view)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"debug popup fail: {e}")

    def _refresh_settings_screen(self):
        try:
            try:
                from client_utils import get_last_fragment
                activity = get_last_fragment()
            except Exception:
                activity = None
            if not activity:
                return
            for name in ("rebuildAllItems", "updateRows", "updateVisibleRows", "notifyDataSetChanged"):
                try:
                    m = activity.getClass().getDeclaredMethod(name)
                    m.setAccessible(True)
                    m.invoke(activity)
                    self._dlog(f"settings refresh via {name}")
                    return
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    methods = activity.getClass().getDeclaredMethods()
                    for m in methods:
                        try:
                            if str(m.getName()) != name:
                                continue
                            ptypes = m.getParameterTypes()
                            if not ptypes or len(ptypes) != 1:
                                continue
                            m.setAccessible(True)
                            try:
                                m.invoke(activity, False)
                            except Exception:
                                m.invoke(activity, True)
                            self._dlog(f"settings refresh via {name}(bool)")
                            return
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                except Exception:
                    pass
            try:
                adapter = _get_private_field_silent(activity, "adapter")
                if adapter:
                    m = adapter.getClass().getMethod("notifyDataSetChanged")
                    m.invoke(adapter)
                    self._dlog("settings refresh via adapter.notifyDataSetChanged")
                    return
            except Exception:
                pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"settings refresh fail: {e}")

    def _setup_settings_header_hook(self):
        try:
            PSA = find_class("com.exteragram.messenger.plugins.ui.PluginSettingsActivity")
            if not PSA:
                return
            arr_cls = find_class("java.util.ArrayList")
            ua_cls = find_class("org.telegram.ui.Components.UniversalAdapter")
            if not arr_cls or not ua_cls:
                return
            m = PSA.getClass().getDeclaredMethod("fillItems", arr_cls, ua_cls)
            m.setAccessible(True)
            self._settings_header_hook = self.hook_method(m, TLLiteSettingsHeaderHook(self))
            self._dlog("settings header hook ok")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"settings header hook fail: {e}")

    def _show_about_sheet(self, ctx_override=None):
        try:
            try:
                log("[TranslaticaPro] about sheet open requested")
            except Exception:
                pass
            ctx = ctx_override
            if ctx is None:
                frag = self.get_last_fragment()
                ctx = frag.getParentActivity() if frag and frag.getParentActivity() else None
            if ctx is None:
                ctx = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext
            if not ctx:
                try:
                    log("[TranslaticaPro] about sheet open aborted: no BottomSheet or context")
                except Exception:
                    pass
                return
            try:
                self._dismiss_keyboard_focus(ctx)
            except Exception:
                pass

            sheet = BottomSheet(ctx, True)
            outer = LinearLayout(ctx)
            outer.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            outer.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(12))

            root = LinearLayout(ctx)
            root.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            root.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(12))
            try:
                root_bg = GradientDrawable()
                root_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(14)))
                root_bg.setColor(int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_dialogBackground)))
                root.setBackground(root_bg)
            except Exception:
                pass

            row = LinearLayout(ctx)
            row.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            row.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            row.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
            try:
                row_bg = GradientDrawable()
                row_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(14)))
                row_bg.setColor(int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_dialogBackground)))
                row.setBackground(row_bg)
            except Exception:
                pass

            avatar = ImageView(ctx)
            try:
                avatar.setScaleType(ImageView.ScaleType.CENTER_CROP)
                av_bg = GradientDrawable()
                av_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(14)))
                av_bg.setColor(0x00000000)
                avatar.setBackground(av_bg)
                avatar.setClipToOutline(True)
                avatar.setOutlineProvider(ViewOutlineProvider.BACKGROUND)
                if os.path.exists(ABOUT_AVATAR_CACHE_FILE):
                    bmp = BitmapFactory.decodeFile(ABOUT_AVATAR_CACHE_FILE)
                    if bmp:
                        avatar.setImageBitmap(bmp)
                avatar.setCameraDistance(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(800)))
                avatar.setAlpha(0.0)
                avatar.setTranslationY(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(26)))
                avatar.setRotationY(-120.0)
            except Exception:
                pass
            row.addView(avatar, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(72), AndroidUtilities.dp(72)))

            desc = TextView(ctx)
            desc.setText(self._tr("about_desc"))
            desc.setTextSize(15)
            try:
                desc.setTextColor(int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteGrayText)))
            except Exception:
                pass
            lp_desc = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1.0)
            lp_desc.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
            row.addView(desc, lp_desc)
            root.addView(row, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            btn = TextView(ctx)
            btn.setText(self._tr("about_button"))
            btn.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
            btn.setTextSize(16)
            try:
                btn.setTextColor(int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_featuredStickers_buttonText)))
                btn_bg = GradientDrawable()
                btn_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(12)))
                btn_bg.setColor(int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_featuredStickers_addButton)))
                btn.setBackground(btn_bg)
                btn.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))
            except Exception:
                pass

            extended_btn = ImageView(ctx)
            try:
                extended_btn.setScaleType(ImageView.ScaleType.CENTER_INSIDE)
                is_dark = bool(Theme.isCurrentThemeDark())
                icon_path = EXTENDED_ICON_CACHE_FILE_DARK if is_dark else EXTENDED_ICON_CACHE_FILE_LIGHT
                if os.path.exists(icon_path):
                    bmp = BitmapFactory.decodeFile(icon_path)
                    if bmp:
                        extended_btn.setImageBitmap(bmp)
                extended_btn.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(4), AndroidUtilities.dp(4), AndroidUtilities.dp(4), AndroidUtilities.dp(4))
            except Exception:
                pass

            class _AboutOpen(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        log("[TranslaticaPro] about button click -> GitHub Sponsors")
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        sheet.dismiss()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    def _open_later():
                        try:
                            view_ctx = None
                            try:
                                view_ctx = v.getContext() if v is not None and hasattr(v, "getContext") else None
                            except Exception:
                                view_ctx = None
                            self._open_support_url(view_ctx, "https://github.com/sponsors/ageekapple/")
                        except Exception:
                            try:
                                self._open_support_url(ctx, "https://github.com/sponsors/ageekapple/")
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                    try:
                        AndroidUtilities.runOnUIThread(dynamic_proxy(Runnable, dict(run=_open_later))(), 120)
                    except Exception:
                        _open_later()

            btn.setOnClickListener(_AboutOpen())
            class _ExtendedOpen(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        self.open_url("tg://resolve?domain=ApplesBio&post=4")
                    except Exception:
                        try:
                            from client_utils import get_messages_controller, get_last_fragment
                            get_messages_controller().openByUserName("ApplesBio", get_last_fragment(), 1)
                        except Exception:
                            try:
                                self.open_url("https://t.me/ApplesBio/4")
                            except Exception:
                                pass

            extended_btn.setOnClickListener(_ExtendedOpen())

            actions = LinearLayout(ctx)
            actions.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            actions.setGravity(Gravity.END | Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            lp_actions = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_actions.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)

            lp_ext = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(36), AndroidUtilities.dp(36))
            lp_ext.rightMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(8)
            actions.addView(extended_btn, lp_ext)

            lp_btn = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(120), LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            actions.addView(btn, lp_btn)
            root.addView(actions, lp_actions)
            try:
                max_w = int(AndroidUtilities.displaySize.x) - AndroidUtilities.dp(36)
            except Exception:
                max_w = LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT
            lp_root = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(max_w, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_root.gravity = Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL
            outer.addView(root, lp_root)

            sheet.setCustomView(outer)
            try:
                run_on_ui_thread(sheet.show)
            except Exception:
                sheet.show()
            try:
                avatar.post(lambda: avatar.animate().translationY(0.0).alpha(1.0).rotationY(0.0).setDuration(620).start())
            except Exception:
                try:
                    avatar.animate().translationY(0.0).alpha(1.0).rotationY(0.0).setDuration(620).start()
                except Exception:
                    pass
            try:
                log("[TranslaticaPro] about sheet shown")
            except Exception:
                pass
        except Exception as e:
            try:
                log(f"[TranslaticaPro] about sheet fail: {e}")
            except Exception:
                pass

    def _open_plugin_settings(self):
        try:
            def _show():
                try:
                    plugin = None
                    fragment = None
                    try:
                        from client_utils import get_last_fragment
                        fragment = get_last_fragment()
                    except Exception:
                        fragment = None
                    try:
                        controller = PluginsController.getInstance()
                        plugin = controller.plugins.get(self.id) if controller else None
                    except Exception:
                        plugin = None
                    if plugin is None or fragment is None:
                        self._dlog("open settings skipped: plugin/fragment unavailable")
                        return
                    fragment.presentFragment(PluginSettingsActivity(plugin))
                    self._dlog("open settings ok")
                except Exception as inner_e:
                    self._dlog(f"open settings fail: {inner_e}")
            run_on_ui_thread(_show)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"open settings fail: {e}")

    def _toggle_floating_from_chat_menu(self):
        try:
            if not self._floating_enabled():
                self.set_setting("tlite_floating_enabled", True)
            new_state = not bool(self.get_setting("tlite_floating_visible", True))
            self.set_setting("tlite_floating_visible", bool(new_state))
            try:
                BulletinHelper.show_info("Floating visible" if new_state else "Floating hidden")
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                run_on_ui_thread(lambda: (self._sync_floating_button(self._chat_fragment_ref), self._refresh_settings_screen()))
            except Exception:
                pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"toggle floating from chat menu fail: {e}")

    def _ensure_chat_floating_menu_item(self, frag=None):
        try:
            if not self._floating_enabled():
                try:
                    host_hide = frag
                    if host_hide is None:
                        from client_utils import get_last_fragment
                        host_hide = get_last_fragment()
                    if host_hide is not None:
                        header_hide = get_private_field(host_hide, "headerItem")
                        if header_hide is not None and header_hide.hasSubItem(int(TLITE_FLOATING_CHAT_MENU_ITEM_ID)):
                            try:
                                header_hide.showSubItem(int(TLITE_FLOATING_CHAT_MENU_ITEM_ID), False)
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                except Exception:
                    pass
                return False
            host = frag
            if host is None:
                try:
                    from client_utils import get_last_fragment
                    host = get_last_fragment()
                except Exception:
                    host = None
            if host is None or "ChatActivity" not in str(host.getClass().getName() or ""):
                return False
            header_item = get_private_field(host, "headerItem")
            if header_item is None:
                return False
            try:
                if header_item.hasSubItem(int(TLITE_FLOATING_CHAT_MENU_ITEM_ID)):
                    try:
                        header_item.showSubItem(int(TLITE_FLOATING_CHAT_MENU_ITEM_ID), True)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    return True
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                icon_res = int(ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("msg_view_file", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName()))
            except Exception:
                icon_res = 0
            try:
                item = header_item.lazilyAddSubItem(int(TLITE_FLOATING_CHAT_MENU_ITEM_ID), int(icon_res), "Floating")
            except Exception as e:
                self._dlog(f"create floating chat menu item fail: {e}")
                return False
            listener_cls = find_class("android.view.View$OnClickListener")
            if listener_cls is not None and item is not None:
                plugin = self
                class _Click(dynamic_proxy(listener_cls)):
                    def onClick(self_obj, _v):
                        try:
                            header_item.closeSubMenu()
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        plugin._toggle_floating_from_chat_menu()
                try:
                    item.setOnClickListener(_Click())
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"attach floating chat menu click fail: {e}")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"ensure floating chat menu item fail: {e}")
            return False

    def _add_menu_items(self):
        try:
            self._chat_menu_item = self.add_menu_item(
                MenuItemData(

                    text="Translatica Logs",
