                )
            )
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"add logs menu item fail: {e}")

    def _find_popup_layout_view(self, root):
        try:
            if root is None:
                return None
            cls_name = str(root.getClass().getName() or "")
            if "ActionBarPopupWindow$ActionBarPopupWindowLayout" in cls_name:
                return root
            if isinstance(root, ViewGroup):
                count = int(root.getChildCount() or 0)
                for idx in range(count):
                    found = self._find_popup_layout_view(root.getChildAt(idx))
                    if found is not None:
                        return found
            return None
        except Exception:
            return None

    def _popup_child_text(self, view):
        try:
            if view is None:
                return ""
            getter = getattr(view, "getText", None)
            if callable(getter):
                try:
                    return str(getter() or "").strip()
                except Exception:
                    pass
            if isinstance(view, ViewGroup):
                count = int(view.getChildCount() or 0)
                for idx in range(count):
                    text = self._popup_child_text(view.getChildAt(idx))
                    if text:
                        return text
            return ""
        except Exception:
            return ""

    def _is_channel_post_summary_eligible(self, chat_activity, msg_obj=None):
        try:
            if chat_activity is None:
                self._native_log("channel summary skipped: chat_activity missing")
                return False
            if msg_obj is None:
                msg_obj = _get_private_field_silent(chat_activity, "selectedObject")
            if msg_obj is None:
                self._native_log("channel summary skipped: selectedObject missing")
                return False
            text = self._avatar_action_text_strict(msg_obj)
            text_len = len(str(text or ""))
            words = re.findall(r"[^\W\d_]+", str(text or ""), flags=re.UNICODE)
            owner = getattr(msg_obj, "messageOwner", None)
            owner_post = bool(getattr(owner, "post", False))
            current_chat = None
            try:
                current_chat = chat_activity.getCurrentChat() if hasattr(chat_activity, "getCurrentChat") else None
            except Exception:
                current_chat = None
            ChatObject = find_class("org.telegram.messenger.ChatObject")
            channel_post = False
            if current_chat is not None and ChatObject is not None:
                try:
                    channel_post = bool(ChatObject.isChannel(current_chat)) and not bool(getattr(current_chat, "megagroup", False))
                except Exception:
                    channel_post = False
            if not channel_post and not owner_post:
                self._native_log("channel summary skipped: not a channel post")
                return False
            if not text:
                self._native_log("channel summary skipped: empty text")
                return False
            if text_len < self._native_summary_min_chars() or len(words) < 8:
                self._native_log(f"channel summary skipped: text too short len={text_len} words={len(words)}")
                return False
            self._dlog(f"channel summary eligible: owner_post={owner_post} len={text_len} words={len(words)}")
            return True
        except Exception:
            self._dlog("channel summary eligibility fail")
            return False

    def _inject_channel_summary_context_item(self, chat_activity):
        try:
            if chat_activity is None:
                return
            msg_obj = _get_private_field_silent(chat_activity, "selectedObject")
            if not self._is_channel_post_summary_eligible(chat_activity, msg_obj):
                return
            popup = getattr(chat_activity, "scrimPopupWindow", None)
            if popup is None:
                return
            content = popup.getContentView() if hasattr(popup, "getContentView") else None
            popup_layout = self._find_popup_layout_view(content)
            if popup_layout is None:
                return
            try:
                child_count = int(popup_layout.getChildCount() or 0)
            except Exception:
                child_count = 0
            for idx in range(child_count):
                try:
                    child = popup_layout.getChildAt(idx)
                    if str(getattr(child, "getTag", lambda: "")() or "") == "__tlite_channel_summary__":
                        return
                except Exception:
                    pass
            ActionBarMenuSubItem = find_class("org.telegram.ui.ActionBar.ActionBarMenuSubItem")
            if ActionBarMenuSubItem is None:
                return
            parent = chat_activity.getParentActivity() if hasattr(chat_activity, "getParentActivity") else None
            if parent is None:
                return
            theme_delegate = _get_private_field_silent(chat_activity, "themeDelegate")
            try:
                cell = ActionBarMenuSubItem(parent, False, False, theme_delegate)
            except Exception:
                try:
                    cell = ActionBarMenuSubItem(parent, False, False)
                except Exception:
                    return
            rid = 0
            try:
                res = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources()
                pkg = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName()
                for name in ("premium_ai_editor", "menu_quote_specific", "msg_aiask", "msg_translate"):
                    rid = int(res.getIdentifier(name, "drawable", pkg) or 0)
                    if rid:
                        break
            except Exception:
                rid = 0
            label = self._tr("ai_sheet_summary")
            try:
                cell.setTextAndIcon(label, rid)
            except Exception:
                try:
                    cell.setText(label)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            try:
                cell.setTag("__tlite_channel_summary__")
            except Exception:
                pass

            class _SummaryClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        chat_activity.closeMenu()
                    except Exception:
                        try:
                            popup.dismiss()
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                    try:
                        self._run_channel_post_summary(chat_activity, msg_obj)
                    except Exception as inner_e:
                        self._dlog(f"channel summary click fail: {inner_e}")

            cell.setOnClickListener(_SummaryClick())
            insert_index = -1
            try:
                for idx in range(child_count):
                    child = popup_layout.getChildAt(idx)
                    child_text = str(self._popup_child_text(child) or "").lower()
                    if "emoji" in child_text or "pack" in child_text:
                        insert_index = idx
                        break
            except Exception:
                insert_index = -1
            try:
                if insert_index >= 0:
                    popup_layout.addView(cell, insert_index)
                else:
                    popup_layout.addView(cell)
            except Exception:
                popup_layout.addView(cell)
            try:
                popup_layout.precalculateHeight()
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                content.requestLayout()
                content.invalidate()
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._dlog("channel summary context item injected")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"inject channel summary context item fail: {e}")

    def _inject_favorite_context_item(self, chat_activity):
        try:
            if chat_activity is None:
                return
            msg_obj = _get_private_field_silent(chat_activity, "selectedObject")
            if msg_obj is None or msg_obj.isOut():
                return
            sender_id = self._favorite_sender_id_from_message(msg_obj)
            if not sender_id:
                return
            popup = getattr(chat_activity, "scrimPopupWindow", None)
            if popup is None:
                return
            content = popup.getContentView() if hasattr(popup, "getContentView") else None
            popup_layout = self._find_popup_layout_view(content)
            if popup_layout is None:
                return
            try:
                child_count = int(popup_layout.getChildCount() or 0)
            except Exception:
                child_count = 0
            for idx in range(child_count):
                try:
                    child = popup_layout.getChildAt(idx)
                    if str(getattr(child, "getTag", lambda: "")() or "") == "__tlite_favorite_contact__":
                        return
                except Exception:
                    pass
            ActionBarMenuSubItem = find_class("org.telegram.ui.ActionBar.ActionBarMenuSubItem")
            if ActionBarMenuSubItem is None:
                return
            parent = chat_activity.getParentActivity() if hasattr(chat_activity, "getParentActivity") else None
            if parent is None:
                return
            theme_delegate = _get_private_field_silent(chat_activity, "themeDelegate")
            try:
                cell = ActionBarMenuSubItem(parent, False, False, theme_delegate)
            except Exception:
                try:
                    cell = ActionBarMenuSubItem(parent, False, False)
                except Exception:
                    return
            label = self._tr("translatica_favorite_remove") if sender_id in self._favorite_sender_ids else self._tr("translatica_favorite_add")
            rid = 0
            try:
                rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("msg_fave", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                if not rid:
                    rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("msg_unfave", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                if not rid:
                    rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("msg_pin_solar", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
            except Exception:
                rid = 0
            try:
                cell.setTextAndIcon(label, rid)
            except Exception:
                try:
                    cell.setText(label)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            try:
                cell.setTag("__tlite_favorite_contact__")
            except Exception:
                pass

            class _FavoriteClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        added = self._toggle_favorite_sender_message(msg_obj)
                        if added is True:
                            BulletinHelper.show_success(self._tr("translatica_favorite_add"))
                        elif added is False:
                            BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("translatica_favorite_remove"))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        chat_activity.closeMenu()
                    except Exception:
                        try:
                            popup.dismiss()
                        except Exception:
                            pass

            cell.setOnClickListener(_FavoriteClick())
            try:
                popup_layout.addView(cell)
            except Exception:
                popup_layout.addView(cell)
            try:
                popup_layout.precalculateHeight()
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                content.requestLayout()
                content.invalidate()
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._dlog("favorite context item injected")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"inject favorite context item fail: {e}")

    def _on_about_click(self, _view=None):
        try:
            log("[TranslaticaPro] about item clicked")
        except Exception:
            pass
        ctx = None
        try:
            if _view is not None and hasattr(_view, "getContext"):
                ctx = _view.getContext()
        except Exception:
            ctx = None
        try:
            run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self._show_about_sheet(ctx))
        except Exception:
            self._show_about_sheet(ctx)

    def _set_settings_subfragment_callback(self, activity, callback):
        try:
            if activity is None or callback is None:
                return False
            try:
                _set_private_field(activity, "createSubFragmentCallback", callback)
            except Exception:
                try:
                    activity.createSubFragmentCallback = callback
                except Exception:
                    pass
            return True
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _open_settings_subfragment(self, callback):
        try:
            activity = getattr(self, "_settings_activity_ref", None)
            if callback is None:
                return
            try:
                if activity is not None:
                    self._set_settings_subfragment_callback(activity, callback)
                    try:
                        self.reload_settings()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        adapter = _get_private_field_silent(activity, "adapter")
                        if adapter:
                            m = adapter.getClass().getMethod("notifyDataSetChanged")
                            m.invoke(adapter)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    return
            except Exception:
                pass
            from client_utils import get_last_fragment
            fragment = get_last_fragment()
            controller = PluginsController.getInstance()
            plugin = controller.plugins.get(self.id) if controller else None
            if not plugin or fragment is None:
                return
            sub_activity = PluginSettingsActivity(plugin)
            try:
                self._set_settings_subfragment_callback(sub_activity, callback)
            except Exception:
                pass
            fragment.presentFragment(sub_activity)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"open settings subfragment fail: {e}")

    def _open_home_via_native_item(self, setting_key):
        try:
            activity = getattr(self, "_settings_activity_ref", None)
            item_map = getattr(self, "_home_open_item_map", None)
            target_item = item_map.get(str(setting_key or "").strip()) if isinstance(item_map, dict) else None
            if not target_item or activity is None:
                self._dlog(f"home native item missing key={setting_key}")
                return
            UItemCls = find_class("org.telegram.ui.Components.UItem")
            ViewCls = find_class("android.view.View")
            IntType = find_class("java.lang.Integer").TYPE
            FloatCls = jclass("java.lang.Float")
            if not UItemCls or not ViewCls or not IntType or not FloatCls:
                self._dlog(f"home native item open unavailable key={setting_key}")
                return
            click_method = activity.getClass().getDeclaredMethod("onClick", UItemCls, ViewCls, IntType, FloatCls.TYPE, FloatCls.TYPE)
            click_method.setAccessible(True)

            def _invoke():
                try:
                    click_method.invoke(activity, target_item, None, jint(0), FloatCls(0.0), FloatCls(0.0))
                    self._dlog(f"home native item opened key={setting_key}")
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"home native item invoke fail key={setting_key}: {e}")

            run_on_ui_thread(_invoke)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"home native item open fail key={setting_key}: {e}")

    def _open_assist_home_entry(self):
        try:
            if bool(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_assist_home_unlocked", False)):
                self._open_home_via_native_item("tlite_ai_correction_subfragment")
                return
            self._show_assist_home_gate_sheet()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"assist home entry fail: {e}")

    def _show_assist_home_gate_sheet(self):
        try:
            activity = getattr(self, "_settings_activity_ref", None)
            ctx = None
            try:
                ctx = activity.getParentActivity() if activity is not None and hasattr(activity, "getParentActivity") else None
            except Exception:
                ctx = None
            if ctx is None:
                ctx = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext
            if ctx is None:
                return
            sheet = BottomSheet(ctx, False)
            try:
                sheet.setApplyTopPadding(False)
                sheet.setApplyBottomPadding(False)
            except Exception:
                pass

            root = LinearLayout(ctx)
            root.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            try:
                root.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(20), AndroidUtilities.dp(22), AndroidUtilities.dp(20), AndroidUtilities.dp(20))
            except Exception:
                pass

            try:
                card_bg = GradientDrawable()
                card_bg.setColor(_ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhite)))
                card_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(24)))
                root.setBackground(card_bg)
            except Exception:
                pass

            title = TextView(ctx)
            title.setText("Translatica Assist")
            title.setTextSize(1, 22)
            try:
                title.setTypeface(title.getTypeface(), 1)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                title.setTextColor(_ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteBlackText)))
            except Exception:
                pass
            root.addView(title)

            desc = TextView(ctx)
            desc.setText(self._tr("settings_ai_custom_gate_desc"))
            desc.setTextSize(1, 14)
            try:
                desc.setTextColor(_ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteGrayText2)))
                desc.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(10), 0, 0)
            except Exception:
                pass
            root.addView(desc)

            unlock_btn = TextView(ctx)
            unlock_btn.setText(self._tr("settings_ai_custom_gate_button"))
            unlock_btn.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
            unlock_btn.setTextSize(1, 16)
            try:
                unlock_btn.setTypeface(unlock_btn.getTypeface(), 1)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                unlock_btn.setTextColor(_ji(0xFFFFFFFF))
                btn_bg = GradientDrawable()
                btn_bg.setColor(_ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_featuredStickers_addButton)))
                btn_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(22)))
                unlock_btn.setBackground(btn_bg)
                unlock_btn.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(13), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(13))
            except Exception:
                pass

            class _UnlockAssist(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        self.set_setting("tlite_ai_assist_home_unlocked", True)
                        try:
                            sheet.dismiss()
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        try:
                            BulletinHelper.show_success(self._tr("bulletin_ai_custom_gate_enabled"))
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        self._open_home_via_native_item("tlite_ai_correction_subfragment")
                    except Exception as e:
                        self._dlog(f"assist home unlock fail: {e}")

            try:
                unlock_btn.setOnClickListener(_UnlockAssist())
            except Exception:
                pass

            btn_lp = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            try:
                btn_lp.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(18)
            except Exception:
                pass
            root.addView(unlock_btn, btn_lp)
            sheet.setCustomView(root)
            sheet.show()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"assist home gate sheet fail: {e}")

    def _get_uitem_setting_key(self, it):
        try:
            if it is None:
                return ""
            for name in ("object2", "object"):
                try:
                    v = getattr(it, name, None)
                    if isinstance(v, str):
                        return v
                    if v is not None:
                        s = str(v)
                        if s and s != "null":
                            return s
                except Exception:
                    pass
        except Exception:
            pass
        return ""

    def _get_uitem_text(self, it):
        try:
            if it is None:
                return ""
            try:
                v = getattr(it, "text", None)
                if v:
                    return str(v)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                si = getattr(it, "settingItem", None)
                if si is not None:
                    tv = getattr(si, "text", None)
                    if tv:
                        return str(tv)
            except Exception:
                pass
        except Exception:
            pass
        return ""

    def _migrate_target_lang_index_order(self):
        try:
            if bool(self.get_setting("tlite_lang_order_v2_done", False)):
                return
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            raw = self.get_setting("tlite_target_lang", 0)
            idx = int(raw)
        except Exception:
            idx = 0
        new_idx = 0
        try:
            if 0 <= idx < len(OLD_LANG_CODES):
                code = str(OLD_LANG_CODES[idx] or "").strip()
                if code and code in LANG_CODES:
                    new_idx = int(LANG_CODES.index(code))
            elif 0 <= idx < len(LANG_CODES):
                new_idx = int(idx)
        except Exception:
            new_idx = 0
        try:
            self.set_setting("tlite_target_lang", int(new_idx))
            self.set_setting("tlite_lang_order_v2_done", True)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _global_target_lang(self):
        self._migrate_target_lang_index_order()
        try:
            raw = self.get_setting("tlite_target_lang", 0)
            idx = int(raw)
            if 0 <= idx < len(LANG_CODES):
                return LANG_CODES[idx]
        except Exception:
            pass
        return "en"

    def _channel_summary_provider_index(self):
        try:
            idx = int(self.get_setting("tlite_channel_summary_provider", 0) or 0)
        except Exception:
            idx = 0
        return 0 if idx <= 0 else 1

    def _channel_summary_provider_options(self):
        return [
            self._tr("settings_translate_service"),
            self._tr("settings_ai_provider"),
        ]

    def _lite_mode_class(self):
        try:
            return find_class("org.telegram.messenger.LiteMode")
        except Exception:
            return None

    def _lite_mode_is_enabled_setting(self, flag):
        try:
            LiteMode = self._lite_mode_class()
            if LiteMode is None:
                return True
            return bool(LiteMode.isEnabledSetting(int(flag)))
        except Exception:
            return True

    def _usage_stats_enabled(self):
        try:
            v = self.get_setting("tlite_usage_stats_enabled", False)
            if isinstance(v, bool):
                return v
            if isinstance(v, (int, float)):
                return bool(int(v))
            s = str(v or "").strip().lower()
            if s in ("1", "true", "on", "yes", "enabled"):
                return True
            if s in ("0", "false", "off", "no", "disabled"):
                return False
            return bool(v)
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _load_usage_stats(self):
        fallback = {
            "total": 0,
            "by_lang": {},
            "by_target_lang": {},
            "by_chat": {},
            "by_action": {},
            "updated_at": 0,
        }
        try:
            raw = self.get_setting("tlite_usage_stats_v1", "")
            if not raw:
                self._usage_stats_cache = dict(fallback)
                return self._usage_stats_cache
            data = raw if isinstance(raw, dict) else json.loads(str(raw or "{}"))
            if not isinstance(data, dict):
                data = {}
            out = dict(fallback)
            out["total"] = int(data.get("total", 0) or 0)
            out["updated_at"] = int(data.get("updated_at", 0) or 0)
            out["by_lang"] = data.get("by_lang", {}) if isinstance(data.get("by_lang", {}), dict) else {}
            out["by_target_lang"] = data.get("by_target_lang", {}) if isinstance(data.get("by_target_lang", {}), dict) else {}
            out["by_chat"] = data.get("by_chat", {}) if isinstance(data.get("by_chat", {}), dict) else {}
            out["by_action"] = data.get("by_action", {}) if isinstance(data.get("by_action", {}), dict) else {}
            self._usage_stats_cache = out
            return out
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"load usage stats fail: {e}")
            self._usage_stats_cache = dict(fallback)
            return self._usage_stats_cache

    def _usage_stats_get(self):
        try:
            if self._usage_stats_cache is None:
                return self._load_usage_stats()
            return self._usage_stats_cache
        except Exception:
            return self._load_usage_stats()

    def _usage_stats_target_lang_map(self, stats=None):
        try:
            data = stats if isinstance(stats, dict) else self._usage_stats_get()
            by_target_lang = data.get("by_target_lang", {}) if isinstance(data, dict) else {}
            if isinstance(by_target_lang, dict) and by_target_lang:
                return by_target_lang
            by_lang = data.get("by_lang", {}) if isinstance(data, dict) else {}
            return by_lang if isinstance(by_lang, dict) else {}
        except Exception:
            return {}

    def _usage_stats_action_count(self, *action_keys):
        try:
            if not action_keys:
                return 0
            by_action = self._usage_stats_get().get("by_action", {})
            if not isinstance(by_action, dict):
                return 0
            total = 0
            for key in action_keys:
                action_key = str(key or "").strip().lower()
                if action_key:
                    total += int(by_action.get(action_key, 0) or 0)
            return total
        except Exception:
            return 0

    def _save_usage_stats_now(self):
        try:
            data = self._usage_stats_get()
            if not isinstance(data, dict):
                return
            self.set_setting("tlite_usage_stats_v1", json.dumps(data, ensure_ascii=True, separators=(",", ":")))
            self._usage_stats_dirty = False
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"save usage stats fail: {e}")

    def _schedule_usage_stats_save(self):
        try:
            self._usage_stats_dirty = True
            if self._usage_stats_timer is not None:
                return
            def _flush():
                try:
                    self._save_usage_stats_now()
                finally:
                    self._usage_stats_timer = None
            timer = threading.Timer(2.5, _flush)
            timer.daemon = True
            self._usage_stats_timer = timer
            timer.start()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"schedule usage stats save fail: {e}")

    def _usage_stats_record(self, action_kind="translate", lang_code=None, dialog_id=None):
        try:
            if not self._usage_stats_enabled():
                return
            stats = self._usage_stats_get()
            stats["total"] = int(stats.get("total", 0) or 0) + 1
            stats["updated_at"] = int(time.time())
            action_key = str(action_kind or "translate").strip().lower() or "translate"
            by_action = stats.get("by_action", {})
            by_action[action_key] = int(by_action.get(action_key, 0) or 0) + 1
            stats["by_action"] = by_action
            code = str(lang_code or "").strip().lower()
            if code:
                by_lang = stats.get("by_lang", {})
                by_lang[code] = int(by_lang.get(code, 0) or 0) + 1
                if len(by_lang) > 48:
                    keep = sorted(by_lang.items(), key=lambda kv: int(kv[1] or 0), reverse=True)[:24]
                    by_lang = {str(k): int(v) for k, v in keep}
                stats["by_lang"] = by_lang
                by_target_lang = stats.get("by_target_lang", {})
                by_target_lang[code] = int(by_target_lang.get(code, 0) or 0) + 1
                if len(by_target_lang) > 48:
                    keep = sorted(by_target_lang.items(), key=lambda kv: int(kv[1] or 0), reverse=True)[:24]
                    by_target_lang = {str(k): int(v) for k, v in keep}
                stats["by_target_lang"] = by_target_lang
            if dialog_id:
                by_chat = stats.get("by_chat", {})
                did_key = str(int(dialog_id))
                by_chat[did_key] = int(by_chat.get(did_key, 0) or 0) + 1
                if len(by_chat) > 80:
                    keep = sorted(by_chat.items(), key=lambda kv: int(kv[1] or 0), reverse=True)[:24]
                    by_chat = {str(k): int(v) for k, v in keep}
                stats["by_chat"] = by_chat
            self._usage_stats_cache = stats
            self._schedule_usage_stats_save()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"usage stats record fail: {e}")

    def _reset_usage_stats(self):
        try:
            self._usage_stats_cache = {
                "total": 0,
                "by_lang": {},
                "by_target_lang": {},
                "by_chat": {},
                "by_action": {},
                "updated_at": int(time.time()),
            }
            self._usage_stats_dirty = True
            self._save_usage_stats_now()
            try:
                BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("bulletin_usage_stats_reset"))
            except Exception:
                pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"reset usage stats fail: {e}")

    def _usage_stats_language_rows(self, limit=4):
        try:
            stats = self._usage_stats_get()
            lang_map = self._usage_stats_target_lang_map(stats)
            total = int(sum(int(v or 0) for v in dict(lang_map).values()) or 0)
            rows = []
            if total <= 0:
                return rows
            for code, count in sorted(dict(lang_map).items(), key=lambda kv: int(kv[1] or 0), reverse=True)[:max(1, int(limit or 4))]:
                cnt = int(count or 0)
                pct = int(round((float(cnt) / float(total)) * 100.0)) if total > 0 else 0
                rows.append({
                    "code": str(code or "").strip().lower(),
                    "label": str(self._lang_label_from_code(code) or str(code or "").upper()).strip(),
                    "count": cnt,
                    "percent": pct,
                })
            return rows
        except Exception:
            return []

    def _usage_stats_chat_title(self, dialog_id):
        try:
            did = int(dialog_id or 0)
            if did == 0:
                return self._tr("settings_usage_stats_unknown_chat")
            mc = MessagesController.getInstance(int(UserConfig.selectedAccount))
            if did < 0:
                chat = mc.getChat(abs(did))
                title = str(getattr(chat, "title", "") or "").strip() if chat is not None else ""
                return title or f"Chat {abs(did)}"
            user = mc.getUser(did)
            if user is not None:
                name = str(getattr(user, "first_name", "") or getattr(user, "username", "") or "").strip()
                last = str(getattr(user, "last_name", "") or "").strip()
                if name and last:
                    return f"{name} {last}".strip()
                if name:
                    return name
            return f"User {did}"
        except Exception:
            return self._tr("settings_usage_stats_unknown_chat")

    def _usage_stats_chat_rows(self, limit=5):
        try:
            stats = self._usage_stats_get()
            total = int(sum(int(v or 0) for v in dict(stats.get("by_chat", {})).values()) or 0)
            rows = []
            if total <= 0:
                return rows
            for dialog_id, count in sorted(dict(stats.get("by_chat", {})).items(), key=lambda kv: int(kv[1] or 0), reverse=True)[:max(1, int(limit or 5))]:
                cnt = int(count or 0)
                pct = int(round((float(cnt) / float(total)) * 100.0)) if total > 0 else 0
                rows.append({
                    "dialog_id": str(dialog_id),
                    "title": self._usage_stats_chat_title(dialog_id),
                    "count": cnt,
                    "percent": pct,
                })
            return rows
        except Exception:
            return []

    def _show_usage_stats_sheet(self, title_text, rows, icon_name="msg_stats_solar"):
        try:
            activity = None
            try:
                activity = self._settings_activity_ref.getParentActivity() if self._settings_activity_ref is not None else None
            except Exception:
                activity = None
            if activity is None:
                return False
            ctx = activity
            is_dark = bool(Theme.isCurrentThemeDark())
            bg_color = _ji(0xFF1F2937) if is_dark else _ji(0xFFF7F8FC)
            card_color = _ji(0xFF233041) if is_dark else _ji(0xFFFFFFFF)
            primary_text = _ji(0xFFFFFFFF) if is_dark else _ji(0xFF1F2937)
            secondary_text = _ji(0xFF9CA3AF) if is_dark else _ji(0xFF64748B)
            accent = _ji(0xFF3B82F6)
            sheet = BottomSheet(ctx, False)
            outer = LinearLayout(ctx)
            outer.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            bg = GradientDrawable()
            bg.setColor(bg_color)
            bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(28)))
            outer.setBackground(bg)
            try:
                outer.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(20), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(20), AndroidUtilities.dp(20))
            except Exception:
                pass
            title = TextView(ctx)
            title.setText(str(title_text or ""))
            title.setTextSize(1, 22)
            title.setTextColor(primary_text)
            try:
                title.setTypeface(title.getTypeface(), 1)
            except Exception:
                pass
            outer.addView(title)
            if not rows:
                empty = TextView(ctx)
                empty.setText(self._tr("settings_usage_stats_empty"))
                empty.setTextSize(1, 14)
                empty.setTextColor(secondary_text)
                try:
                    empty.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(14), 0, 0)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                outer.addView(empty)
            else:
                host = LinearLayout(ctx)
                host.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
                try:
                    host.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(14), 0, 0)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                for row in rows:
                    cell = LinearLayout(ctx)
                    cell.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
                    cell.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
                    cell_bg = GradientDrawable()
                    cell_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
                    cell_bg.setColor(card_color)
                    cell.setBackground(cell_bg)
                    try:
                        cell.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    icon = ImageView(ctx)
                    try:
                        rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier(str(icon_name or ""), "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                        if rid:
                            icon.setImageResource(rid)
                            icon.setColorFilter(accent)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    cell.addView(icon, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
                    texts = LinearLayout(ctx)
                    texts.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
                    lp_texts = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1.0)
                    lp_texts.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(12)
                    name = TextView(ctx)
                    name.setText(str(row.get("title", "") or row.get("label", "") or ""))
                    name.setTextSize(1, 15)
                    name.setTextColor(primary_text)
                    try:
                        name.setTypeface(name.getTypeface(), 1)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    texts.addView(name)
                    meta = TextView(ctx)
                    meta.setText(f"{int(row.get('percent', 0) or 0)}% • {int(row.get('count', 0) or 0)}")
                    meta.setTextSize(1, 12)
                    meta.setTextColor(secondary_text)
                    texts.addView(meta)
                    cell.addView(texts, lp_texts)
                    lp_cell = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
                    if host.getChildCount() > 0:
                        lp_cell.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
                    host.addView(cell, lp_cell)
                outer.addView(host)
            try:
                sheet.setCustomView(outer)
                sheet.show()
            except Exception:
                return False
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"show usage stats sheet fail: {e}")
            return False

    def _set_lite_mode_flag(self, flag, enabled):
        try:
            LiteMode = self._lite_mode_class()
            if LiteMode is None:
                return
            LiteMode.toggleFlag(int(flag), bool(enabled))
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"set lite mode flag fail: {e}")

    def _lite_mode_optimization_enabled(self, flag):
        try:
            return not bool(self._lite_mode_is_enabled_setting(flag))
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _set_lite_mode_optimization(self, flag, enabled):
        try:
            self._set_lite_mode_flag(flag, not bool(enabled))
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"set lite mode optimization fail: {e}")

    def _assist_target_lang(self, fragment=None):
        try:
            did = int(self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=fragment) or 0)
        except Exception:
            did = 0
        try:
            if did:
                cfg = self._chat_config(did)
                lang = str(cfg.get("lang") or "").strip()
                if lang:
                    return lang
        except Exception:
            pass
        return str(self._global_target_lang() or "en")

    def _lang_label_from_code(self, code):
        try:
            target = str(code or "").strip()
            for label, item_code in LANG_OPTIONS:
                if str(item_code or "").strip() == target:
                    return str(label)
        except Exception:
            pass
        return str(code or "").strip().upper()

    def _translate_service_mode(self):
        try:
            raw = self.get_setting("tlite_service", "appleai")
            if isinstance(raw, str):
                mode = str(raw or "").strip().lower()
                if mode == "native":
                    return "appleai"
                valid = [str(item[0] or "").strip().lower() for item in SERVICE_OPTIONS]
                if mode in valid:
                    return mode
            idx = int(raw or 0)
            if idx <= 0:
                return "appleai"
            if idx == 1:
                return "translatica"
            if idx == 2:
                return "alternative"
            if idx == 3:
                return "dynamic"
        except Exception:
            pass
        return "appleai"

    def _translate_service_index(self):
        mode = str(self._translate_service_mode() or "native").strip().lower()
        for idx, item in enumerate(SERVICE_OPTIONS):
            if str(item[0] or "").strip().lower() == mode:
                return int(idx)
        return 0

    def _translate_service_option_labels(self):
        return [
            "AppleAI",
            "Translatica",
            "Alternative",
            self._tr("settings_translate_service_dynamic"),
        ]

    def _avatar_ai_action_options(self):
        return [
            self._tr("ai_sheet_summary"),
            self._tr("settings_ai_avatar_action_translate"),
            self._tr("settings_ai_avatar_action_both"),
        ]

    def _avatar_ai_action_mode(self):
        try:
            raw = self.get_setting("tlite_ai_avatar_action", "both")
            if isinstance(raw, str):
                mode = str(raw or "").strip().lower()
                if mode in ("summary", "translate", "both"):
                    return mode
            idx = int(raw or 2)
            if idx == 0:
                return "summary"
            if idx == 1:
                return "translate"
        except Exception:
            pass
        return "both"

    def _avatar_ai_action_index(self):
        mode = str(self._avatar_ai_action_mode() or "both").strip().lower()
        if mode == "summary":
            return 0
        if mode == "translate":
            return 1
        return 2

    def _avatar_summary_lang_code(self):
        try:
            raw = self.get_setting("tlite_ai_avatar_summary_lang", "")
            code = str(raw or "").strip()
            if code in LANG_CODES:
                return code
        except Exception:
            pass
        return str(self._assist_target_lang(self._chat_fragment_ref) or self._global_target_lang() or "en")

    def _avatar_summary_lang_index(self):
        code = str(self._avatar_summary_lang_code() or "en").strip()
        try:
            return LANG_CODES.index(code)
        except Exception:
            return 0

    def _favorite_incoming_lang_code(self):
        try:
            raw = self.get_setting("tlite_favorite_incoming_lang", "")
            code = str(raw or "").strip()
            if code in LANG_CODES:
                return code
        except Exception:
            pass
        return str(self._global_target_lang() or "en")

    def _favorite_incoming_lang_index(self):
        code = str(self._favorite_incoming_lang_code() or "en").strip()
        try:
            return LANG_CODES.index(code)
        except Exception:
            return 0

    def _floating_enabled(self):
        try:
            return bool(self.get_setting("tlite_floating_enabled", False))
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _floating_visible(self):
        try:
            if not self._floating_enabled():
                return False
            return bool(self.get_setting("tlite_floating_visible", True))
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _open_advanced_color_picker(self, ctx, initial_color, callback, allow_secondary=False, initial_secondary=0):
        try:
            if ctx is None or callback is None:
                return
            try:
                is_dark = bool(Theme.isCurrentThemeDark())
            except Exception:
                is_dark = True
            surface_color = _ji(0xFF243141 if is_dark else 0xFFF4F7FB)
            input_bg_color = _ji(0x22111F2C if is_dark else 0xFFE6EDF5)
            primary_text_color = _ji(0xFFFFFFFF if is_dark else 0xFF111827)
            secondary_ring_color = _ji(0xFF111827 if is_dark else 0xFFCBD5E1)
            action_text_color = _ji(0xFF4DA3FF if is_dark else 0xFF2563EB)
            touch_cls = find_class("android.view.View$OnTouchListener")
            MotionEvent = jclass("android.view.MotionEvent")
            EditText = jclass("android.widget.EditText")
            if touch_cls is None or MotionEvent is None:
                raise RuntimeError("touch interfaces unavailable")

            base_color = int(initial_color) & 0xFFFFFFFF
            second_color = int(initial_secondary or 0) & 0xFFFFFFFF
            r = ((base_color >> 16) & 0xFF) / 255.0
            g = ((base_color >> 8) & 0xFF) / 255.0
            b = (base_color & 0xFF) / 255.0
            h, _s, _v = colorsys.rgb_to_hsv(r, g, b)
            initial_hue = max(0, min(360, int(round(h * 360.0))))
            if second_color:
                r2 = ((second_color >> 16) & 0xFF) / 255.0
                g2 = ((second_color >> 8) & 0xFF) / 255.0
                b2 = (second_color & 0xFF) / 255.0
                h2, _s2, _v2 = colorsys.rgb_to_hsv(r2, g2, b2)
                initial_hue2 = max(0, min(360, int(round(h2 * 360.0))))
            else:
                initial_hue2 = 180
            state = {"color": base_color, "hue": initial_hue, "color2": second_color, "hue2": initial_hue2, "second": bool(allow_secondary and second_color)}

            container = LinearLayout(ctx)
            container.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            container.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))
            try:
                panel_bg = GradientDrawable()
                panel_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
                panel_bg.setColor(surface_color)
                container.setBackground(panel_bg)
            except Exception:
                pass

            top_row = LinearLayout(ctx)
            top_row.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            top_row.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)

            hex_view = TextView(ctx)
            hex_view.setText("#{0:06X}".format(base_color & 0xFFFFFF))
            hex_view.setTextSize(18)
            hex_view.setTextColor(primary_text_color)
            hex_view.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            hex_view.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))
            hex_bg = GradientDrawable()
            hex_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(16)))
            hex_bg.setColor(input_bg_color)
            hex_view.setBackground(hex_bg)
            try:
                hex_view.setClickable(True)
            except Exception:
                pass
            lp_hex = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1.0)
            top_row.addView(hex_view, lp_hex)

            preview_wrap = FrameLayout(ctx)
            lp_preview = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(54), AndroidUtilities.dp(54))
            lp_preview.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(16)
            ring = View(ctx)
            ring_bg = GradientDrawable()
            ring_bg.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
            ring_bg.setColor(_ji(0x00000000))
            ring_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(3), secondary_ring_color)
            ring.setBackground(ring_bg)
            preview_wrap.addView(ring, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(54), AndroidUtilities.dp(54), Gravity.CENTER))
            preview = View(ctx)
            preview_bg = GradientDrawable()
            preview_bg.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
            preview_bg.setColor(_ji(base_color))
            preview.setBackground(preview_bg)
            preview_wrap.addView(preview, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(42), AndroidUtilities.dp(42), Gravity.CENTER))
            top_row.addView(preview_wrap, lp_preview)

            plus_view = TextView(ctx)
            plus_view.setText("+")
            plus_view.setTextSize(34)
            plus_view.setTextColor(primary_text_color)
            plus_view.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
            lp_plus = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(42), AndroidUtilities.dp(42))
            lp_plus.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(14)
            if allow_secondary:
                top_row.addView(plus_view, lp_plus)

            container.addView(top_row, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            slider_host = FrameLayout(ctx)
            lp_host = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, AndroidUtilities.dp(58))
            lp_host.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(18)

            gradient_bar = View(ctx)
            grad = GradientDrawable(GradientDrawable.Orientation.LEFT_RIGHT, jarray(jint)([-65536, -256, -16711936, -16711681, -16776961, -65281, -65536]))
            grad.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(12)))
            gradient_bar.setBackground(grad)
            slider_host.addView(gradient_bar, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(FrameLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, AndroidUtilities.dp(26), Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL))

            knob_wrap = FrameLayout(ctx)
            knob_ring = View(ctx)
            knob_ring_bg = GradientDrawable()
            knob_ring_bg.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
            knob_ring_bg.setColor(_ji(0x00000000))
            knob_ring_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(3), _ji(0xFFFFFFFF))
            knob_ring.setBackground(knob_ring_bg)
            knob_wrap.addView(knob_ring, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(34), AndroidUtilities.dp(34), Gravity.CENTER))
            knob_fill = View(ctx)
            knob_fill_bg = GradientDrawable()
            knob_fill_bg.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
            knob_fill_bg.setColor(_ji(base_color))
            knob_fill.setBackground(knob_fill_bg)
            knob_wrap.addView(knob_fill, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(26), AndroidUtilities.dp(26), Gravity.CENTER))
            slider_host.addView(knob_wrap, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(34), AndroidUtilities.dp(34), Gravity.TOP | Gravity.LEFT))
            second_slider_host = None
            second_knob_wrap = None
            second_preview_bg = None
            second_knob_fill_bg = None
            second_hex = None
            second_wrap = None

            def _apply_hue(progress):
                try:
                    hue = max(0, min(360, int(progress)))
                    rr, gg, bb = colorsys.hsv_to_rgb((float(hue) % 360.0) / 360.0, 1.0, 1.0)
                    color_value = (0xFF << 24) | (int(rr * 255) << 16) | (int(gg * 255) << 8) | int(bb * 255)
                    state["color"] = int(color_value) & 0xFFFFFFFF
                    state["hue"] = hue
                    preview_bg.setColor(_ji(state["color"]))
                    knob_fill_bg.setColor(_ji(state["color"]))
                    hex_view.setText("#{0:06X}".format(state["color"] & 0xFFFFFF))
                except Exception:
                    pass

            def _apply_hue2(progress):
                try:
                    if second_preview_bg is None or second_knob_fill_bg is None or second_hex is None:
                        return
                    hue = max(0, min(360, int(progress)))
                    rr, gg, bb = colorsys.hsv_to_rgb((float(hue) % 360.0) / 360.0, 1.0, 1.0)
                    color_value = (0xFF << 24) | (int(rr * 255) << 16) | (int(gg * 255) << 8) | int(bb * 255)
                    state["color2"] = int(color_value) & 0xFFFFFFFF
                    state["hue2"] = hue
                    second_preview_bg.setColor(_ji(state["color2"]))
                    second_knob_fill_bg.setColor(_ji(state["color2"]))
                    second_hex.setText("#{0:06X}".format(state["color2"] & 0xFFFFFF))
                except Exception:
                    pass

            def _position_knob():
                try:
                    width = int(slider_host.getWidth() or 0)
                    if width <= 0:
                        return
                    bar_left = AndroidUtilities.dp(2)
                    bar_right = width - AndroidUtilities.dp(2) - AndroidUtilities.dp(34)
                    travel = max(1, bar_right - bar_left)
                    ratio = float(state["hue"]) / 360.0
                    x = int(bar_left + (travel * ratio))
                    y = int((AndroidUtilities.dp(58) - AndroidUtilities.dp(34)) / 2)
                    lp_knob = knob_wrap.getLayoutParams()
                    if lp_knob is None:
                        lp_knob = FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(34), AndroidUtilities.dp(34), Gravity.TOP | Gravity.LEFT)
                    lp_knob.leftMargin = x
                    lp_knob.topMargin = y
                    knob_wrap.setLayoutParams(lp_knob)
                except Exception:
                    pass

            def _position_second_knob():
                try:
                    if second_slider_host is None or second_knob_wrap is None:
                        return
                    width = int(second_slider_host.getWidth() or 0)
                    if width <= 0:
                        return
                    bar_left = AndroidUtilities.dp(2)
                    bar_right = width - AndroidUtilities.dp(2) - AndroidUtilities.dp(34)
                    travel = max(1, bar_right - bar_left)
                    ratio = float(state["hue2"]) / 360.0
                    x = int(bar_left + (travel * ratio))
                    y = int((AndroidUtilities.dp(58) - AndroidUtilities.dp(34)) / 2)
                    lp_knob = second_knob_wrap.getLayoutParams()
                    if lp_knob is None:
                        lp_knob = FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(34), AndroidUtilities.dp(34), Gravity.TOP | Gravity.LEFT)
                    lp_knob.leftMargin = x
                    lp_knob.topMargin = y
                    second_knob_wrap.setLayoutParams(lp_knob)
                except Exception:
                    pass

            def _update_from_touch(event):
                try:
                    width = int(slider_host.getWidth() or 0)
                    if width <= 0:
                        return
                    bar_left = AndroidUtilities.dp(2)
                    bar_right = width - AndroidUtilities.dp(2) - AndroidUtilities.dp(34)
                    travel = max(1, bar_right - bar_left)
                    raw_x = float(event.getX()) - AndroidUtilities.dp(17)
                    x = max(float(bar_left), min(float(bar_right), raw_x))
                    ratio = (x - float(bar_left)) / float(travel)
                    _apply_hue(int(round(ratio * 360.0)))
                    _position_knob()
                except Exception:
                    pass

            def _update_from_touch2(event):
                try:
                    if second_slider_host is None:
                        return
                    width = int(second_slider_host.getWidth() or 0)
                    if width <= 0:
                        return
                    bar_left = AndroidUtilities.dp(2)
                    bar_right = width - AndroidUtilities.dp(2) - AndroidUtilities.dp(34)
                    travel = max(1, bar_right - bar_left)
                    raw_x = float(event.getX()) - AndroidUtilities.dp(17)
                    x = max(float(bar_left), min(float(bar_right), raw_x))
                    ratio = (x - float(bar_left)) / float(travel)
                    _apply_hue2(int(round(ratio * 360.0)))
                    _position_second_knob()
                except Exception:
                    pass

            class _HueTouch(dynamic_proxy(touch_cls)):
                def onTouch(self_obj, _v, event):
                    try:
                        action = int(event.getActionMasked())
                        if action == MotionEvent.ACTION_DOWN:
                            slider_host.getParent().requestDisallowInterceptTouchEvent(True)
                            _update_from_touch(event)
                            return True
                        if action == MotionEvent.ACTION_MOVE:
                            _update_from_touch(event)
                            return True
                        if action in (MotionEvent.ACTION_UP, MotionEvent.ACTION_CANCEL):
                            _update_from_touch(event)
                            try:
                                slider_host.getParent().requestDisallowInterceptTouchEvent(False)
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            return True
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    return False

            class _HueTouch2(dynamic_proxy(touch_cls)):
                def onTouch(self_obj, _v, event):
                    try:
                        if second_slider_host is None:
                            return False
                        action = int(event.getActionMasked())
                        if action == MotionEvent.ACTION_DOWN:
                            second_slider_host.getParent().requestDisallowInterceptTouchEvent(True)
                            _update_from_touch2(event)
                            return True
                        if action == MotionEvent.ACTION_MOVE:
                            _update_from_touch2(event)
                            return True
                        if action in (MotionEvent.ACTION_UP, MotionEvent.ACTION_CANCEL):
                            _update_from_touch2(event)
                            try:
                                second_slider_host.getParent().requestDisallowInterceptTouchEvent(False)
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            return True
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    return False

            slider_host.setOnTouchListener(_HueTouch())
            try:
                slider_host.post(_position_knob)
            except Exception:
                pass
            container.addView(slider_host, lp_host)

            second_wrap = LinearLayout(ctx)
            second_wrap.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            lp_second_wrap = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_second_wrap.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(12)

            second_top = LinearLayout(ctx)
            second_top.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            second_top.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)

            second_hex = TextView(ctx)
            second_hex.setText("#{0:06X}".format((state["color2"] if state["color2"] else 0xFFFFFFFF) & 0xFFFFFF))
            second_hex.setTextSize(18)
            second_hex.setTextColor(primary_text_color)
            second_hex.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            second_hex.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))
            second_hex_bg = GradientDrawable()
            second_hex_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(16)))
            second_hex_bg.setColor(input_bg_color)
            second_hex.setBackground(second_hex_bg)
            try:
                second_hex.setClickable(True)
            except Exception:
                pass
            second_top.addView(second_hex, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1.0))

            second_preview_wrap = FrameLayout(ctx)
            lp_second_preview = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(54), AndroidUtilities.dp(54))
            lp_second_preview.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(16)
            second_ring = View(ctx)
            second_ring_bg = GradientDrawable()
            second_ring_bg.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
            second_ring_bg.setColor(_ji(0x00000000))
            second_ring_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(3), secondary_ring_color)
            second_ring.setBackground(second_ring_bg)
            second_preview_wrap.addView(second_ring, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(54), AndroidUtilities.dp(54), Gravity.CENTER))
            second_preview = View(ctx)
            second_preview_bg = GradientDrawable()
            second_preview_bg.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
            second_preview_bg.setColor(_ji(state["color2"] if state["color2"] else 0xFFFFFFFF))
            second_preview.setBackground(second_preview_bg)
            second_preview_wrap.addView(second_preview, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(42), AndroidUtilities.dp(42), Gravity.CENTER))
            second_top.addView(second_preview_wrap, lp_second_preview)
            second_wrap.addView(second_top, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            second_slider_host = FrameLayout(ctx)
            lp_second_host = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, AndroidUtilities.dp(58))
            lp_second_host.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(12)
            second_gradient_bar = View(ctx)
            second_grad = GradientDrawable(GradientDrawable.Orientation.LEFT_RIGHT, jarray(jint)([-65536, -256, -16711936, -16711681, -16776961, -65281, -65536]))
            second_grad.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(12)))
            second_gradient_bar.setBackground(second_grad)
            second_slider_host.addView(second_gradient_bar, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(FrameLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, AndroidUtilities.dp(26), Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL))

            second_knob_wrap = FrameLayout(ctx)
            second_knob_ring = View(ctx)
            second_knob_ring_bg = GradientDrawable()
            second_knob_ring_bg.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
            second_knob_ring_bg.setColor(_ji(0x00000000))
            second_knob_ring_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(3), _ji(0xFFFFFFFF))
            second_knob_ring.setBackground(second_knob_ring_bg)
            second_knob_wrap.addView(second_knob_ring, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(34), AndroidUtilities.dp(34), Gravity.CENTER))
            second_knob_fill = View(ctx)
            second_knob_fill_bg = GradientDrawable()
            second_knob_fill_bg.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
            second_knob_fill_bg.setColor(_ji(state["color2"] if state["color2"] else 0xFFFFFFFF))
            second_knob_fill.setBackground(second_knob_fill_bg)
            second_knob_wrap.addView(second_knob_fill, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(26), AndroidUtilities.dp(26), Gravity.CENTER))
            second_slider_host.addView(second_knob_wrap, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(34), AndroidUtilities.dp(34), Gravity.TOP | Gravity.LEFT))
            second_wrap.addView(second_slider_host, lp_second_host)
            if allow_secondary:
                container.addView(second_wrap, lp_second_wrap)
                second_slider_host.setOnTouchListener(_HueTouch2())
                try:
                    second_slider_host.post(_position_second_knob)
                except Exception:
                    pass

            def _save(b, _w):
                try:
                    b.dismiss()
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    callback(int(state["color"]), int(state["color2"]) if state.get("second") else None)
                except Exception:
                    pass

            def _toggle_second():
                try:
                    enabled = not bool(state.get("second"))
                    state["second"] = enabled
                    plus_view.setText("-" if enabled else "+")
                    second_wrap.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if enabled else View.GONE)
                    if enabled and not int(state.get("color2") or 0):
                        state["color2"] = 0xFFFFFFFF
                        state["hue2"] = 0
                        second_preview_bg.setColor(_ji(0xFFFFFFFF))
                        second_knob_fill_bg.setColor(_ji(0xFFFFFFFF))
                        second_hex.setText("#FFFFFF")
                    try:
                        second_slider_host.post(_position_second_knob)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                except Exception:
                    pass

            if allow_secondary:
                plus_view.setOnClickListener(OnClickListener(lambda _v=None: _toggle_second()))
                second_wrap.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if state.get("second") else View.GONE)
                plus_view.setText("-" if state.get("second") else "+")

            def _show_hex_input(target_key):
                try:
                    ib = AlertDialogBuilder(ctx)
                    ib.set_title(self._tr("dialog_select_color"))
                    try:
                        hex_is_dark = bool(Theme.isCurrentThemeDark())
                    except Exception:
                        hex_is_dark = True
                    field_bg_color = _ji(0xFF243141 if hex_is_dark else 0xFFF4F7FB)
                    field_fill_color = _ji(0xFF1E2A39 if hex_is_dark else 0xFFFFFFFF)
                    field_text_color = _ji(0xFFFFFFFF if hex_is_dark else 0xFF111827)
                    field_hint_color = _ji(0xFF94A3B8 if hex_is_dark else 0xFF64748B)
                    field_stroke_color = _ji(0xFF334155 if hex_is_dark else 0xFFD7E0EA)
                    host = LinearLayout(ctx)
                    host.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
                    try:
                        host_bg = GradientDrawable()
                        host_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
                        host_bg.setColor(field_bg_color)
                        host.setBackground(host_bg)
                        host.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(4))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    et = EditText(ctx)
                    et.setSingleLine(True)
                    try:
                        et.setTextSize(20)
                        et.setTextColor(field_text_color)
                        et.setHintTextColor(field_hint_color)
                        et.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
                        et.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(14))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        et_bg = GradientDrawable()
                        et_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(16)))
                        et_bg.setColor(field_fill_color)
                        et_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), field_stroke_color)
                        et.setBackground(et_bg)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    et.setText("#{0:06X}".format((state["color"] if target_key == 1 else (state["color2"] if state["color2"] else 0xFFFFFFFF)) & 0xFFFFFF))
                    try:
                        et.setHint("#RRGGBB")
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        et.setSelection(len(str(et.getText() or "")))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        lp_et = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
                        lp_et.bottomMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(6)
                        host.addView(et, lp_et)
                        ib.set_view(host)
                    except Exception:
                        ib.set_view(et)
                    def _save_hex(d, _w):
                        try:
                            raw = str(et.getText() or "").strip().replace("#", "")
                            if len(raw) == 6:
                                color_value = (0xFF << 24) | int(raw, 16)
                                if target_key == 1:
                                    state["color"] = int(color_value) & 0xFFFFFFFF
                                    rr, gg, bb = ((color_value >> 16) & 0xFF) / 255.0, ((color_value >> 8) & 0xFF) / 255.0, (color_value & 0xFF) / 255.0
                                    hh, _ss, _vv = colorsys.rgb_to_hsv(rr, gg, bb)
                                    state["hue"] = max(0, min(360, int(round(hh * 360.0))))
                                    preview_bg.setColor(_ji(state["color"]))
                                    knob_fill_bg.setColor(_ji(state["color"]))
                                    hex_view.setText("#{0:06X}".format(state["color"] & 0xFFFFFF))
                                    _position_knob()
                                else:
                                    state["color2"] = int(color_value) & 0xFFFFFFFF
                                    rr, gg, bb = ((color_value >> 16) & 0xFF) / 255.0, ((color_value >> 8) & 0xFF) / 255.0, (color_value & 0xFF) / 255.0
                                    hh, _ss, _vv = colorsys.rgb_to_hsv(rr, gg, bb)
                                    state["hue2"] = max(0, min(360, int(round(hh * 360.0))))
                                    second_preview_bg.setColor(_ji(state["color2"]))
                                    second_knob_fill_bg.setColor(_ji(state["color2"]))
                                    second_hex.setText("#{0:06X}".format(state["color2"] & 0xFFFFFF))
                                    _position_second_knob()
                            d.dismiss()
                        except Exception:
                            try:
                                d.dismiss()
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                    ib.set_positive_button("OK", _save_hex)
                    ib.set_negative_button(self._tr("dialog_close"), lambda d, _w: d.dismiss() if d else None)
                    try:
                        dlg = ib.show()
                        try:
                            btn_pos = dlg.getButton(-1)
                            if btn_pos is not None:
                                btn_pos.setTextColor(action_text_color)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        try:
                            btn_neg = dlg.getButton(-2)
                            if btn_neg is not None:
                                btn_neg.setTextColor(action_text_color)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                    except Exception:
                        ib.show()
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"hex color input fail: {e}")

            hex_view.setOnClickListener(OnClickListener(lambda _v=None: _show_hex_input(1)))
            if allow_secondary:
                second_hex.setOnClickListener(OnClickListener(lambda _v=None: _show_hex_input(2)))

            builder = AlertDialogBuilder(ctx)
            builder.set_title(self._tr("dialog_select_color"))
            builder.set_view(container)
            builder.set_positive_button("OK", _save)
            builder.set_negative_button(self._tr("dialog_close"), lambda b, _w: b.dismiss() if b else None)
            try:
                dlg = builder.show()
                try:
                    btn_pos = dlg.getButton(-1)
                    if btn_pos is not None:
                        btn_pos.setTextColor(action_text_color)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    btn_neg = dlg.getButton(-2)
                    if btn_neg is not None:
                        btn_neg.setTextColor(action_text_color)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            except Exception:
                builder.show()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"advanced color picker fail: {e}")

    def _open_color_picker(self, ctx, title_text, setting_key):
        try:
            if ctx is None:
                return
            try:
                is_dark = bool(Theme.isCurrentThemeDark())
            except Exception:
                is_dark = True
            sheet_bg_color = _ji(0xFF243141 if is_dark else 0xFFF4F7FB)
            ring_border_color = _ji(0x221E293B if is_dark else 0xFFCBD5E1)
            current = 0xFF38A8FF
            try:
                current = int(self.get_setting(str(setting_key), current) or current)
            except Exception:
                pass

            def _apply_color(color_value):
                try:
                    self.set_setting(str(setting_key), int(color_value))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    self._sync_floating_button(self._chat_fragment_ref)
                except Exception:
                    pass

            b = AlertDialogBuilder(ctx)
            b.set_title(str(title_text or "Color"))

            container = LinearLayout(ctx)
            container.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            container.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(14))
            try:
                sheet_bg = GradientDrawable()
                sheet_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
                sheet_bg.setColor(sheet_bg_color)
                container.setBackground(sheet_bg)
            except Exception:
                pass

            row = LinearLayout(ctx)
            row.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            row.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)

            quick_colors = [
                0xFFFFFFFF,
                0xFF22C55E,
                0xFFF59E0B,
                0xFFEF4444,
                0xFF111111,
            ]
            try:
                row.setClipChildren(False)
                row.setClipToPadding(False)
                container.setClipChildren(False)
                container.setClipToPadding(False)
            except Exception:
                pass

            for c in quick_colors:
                wrapper = FrameLayout(ctx)
                try:
                    wrapper.setClipChildren(False)
                    wrapper.setClipToPadding(False)
                except Exception:
                    pass

                ring = View(ctx)
                ring_bg = GradientDrawable()
                ring_bg.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
                ring_bg.setColor(_ji(0x00000000))
                ring_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(2), _ji(c if (int(current) & 0xFFFFFFFF) == (int(c) & 0xFFFFFFFF) else 0x00000000))
                ring.setBackground(ring_bg)
                wrapper.addView(ring, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(40), AndroidUtilities.dp(40), Gravity.CENTER))

                circle = View(ctx)
                circle_bg = GradientDrawable()
                circle_bg.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
                circle_bg.setColor(_ji(c))
                try:
                    circle_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), _ji(0x22000000 if c != 0xFFFFFFFF else 0x33000000))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                circle.setBackground(circle_bg)
                wrapper.addView(circle, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(34), AndroidUtilities.dp(34), Gravity.CENTER))

                class _QuickClick(dynamic_proxy(find_class("android.view.View$OnClickListener"))):
                    def __init__(self_obj, selected_color):
                        super().__init__()
                        self_obj.selected_color = selected_color
                    def onClick(self_obj, _v):
                        try:
                            _apply_color(int(self_obj.selected_color))
                            if str(setting_key) == "tlite_floating_color":
                                try:
                                    self.set_setting("tlite_floating_color2", 0)
                                except Exception:
                                    pass
                            dialog.dismiss()
                        except Exception:
                            pass

                wrapper.setOnClickListener(_QuickClick(c))
                lp = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(50), AndroidUtilities.dp(50))
                lp.setMargins(AndroidUtilities.dp(2), AndroidUtilities.dp(2), AndroidUtilities.dp(2), AndroidUtilities.dp(2))
                row.addView(wrapper, lp)

            palette_wrap = FrameLayout(ctx)
            palette_ring = View(ctx)
            palette_ring_bg = GradientDrawable()
            palette_ring_bg.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
            palette_ring_bg.setColor(_ji(0x00000000))
            palette_ring_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(2), ring_border_color)
            palette_ring.setBackground(palette_ring_bg)
            palette_wrap.addView(palette_ring, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(42), AndroidUtilities.dp(42), Gravity.CENTER))

            palette_fill = GradientDrawable()
            palette_fill.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
            try:
                palette_fill.setColors(jarray(jint)([-3805, -9923, -9714825, -11692316, -4613121]))
            except Exception:
                palette_fill.setColor(_ji(0xFF64748B))
            palette_fill.setGradientType(GradientDrawable.SWEEP_GRADIENT)
            palette_fill.setOrientation(GradientDrawable.Orientation.LEFT_RIGHT)

            palette_inner = FrameLayout(ctx)
            palette_inner.setBackground(palette_fill)
            palette_wrap.addView(palette_inner, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(34), AndroidUtilities.dp(34), Gravity.CENTER))

            palette_icon = ImageView(ctx)
            try:
