                rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("msg_palette", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                if rid:
                    palette_icon.setImageResource(rid)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                palette_icon.setColorFilter(_ji(0xFFFFFFFF))
            except Exception:
                pass
            palette_wrap.addView(palette_icon, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(16), Gravity.CENTER))

            class _PaletteClick(dynamic_proxy(find_class("android.view.View$OnClickListener"))):
                def onClick(self_obj, _v):
                    try:
                        dialog.dismiss()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    if str(setting_key) == "tlite_floating_color":
                        current2 = 0
                        try:
                            current2 = int(self.get_setting("tlite_floating_color2", 0) or 0)
                        except Exception:
                            current2 = 0
                        def _apply_gradient(primary, secondary=None):
                            try:
                                self.set_setting("tlite_floating_color", int(primary))
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            try:
                                self.set_setting("tlite_floating_color2", int(secondary or 0))
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            try:
                                self._sync_floating_button(self._chat_fragment_ref)
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                        self._open_advanced_color_picker(ctx, current, _apply_gradient, allow_secondary=True, initial_secondary=current2)
                    else:
                        self._open_advanced_color_picker(ctx, current, _apply_color, allow_secondary=False, initial_secondary=0)

            palette_wrap.setOnClickListener(_PaletteClick())
            lp_palette = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(46), AndroidUtilities.dp(46))
            lp_palette.setMargins(AndroidUtilities.dp(3), 0, AndroidUtilities.dp(3), 0)
            row.addView(palette_wrap, lp_palette)

            container.addView(row, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            b.set_view(container)
            dialog = b.set_negative_button(self._tr("dialog_close"), lambda d, _w: d.dismiss() if d else None).show()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"color picker fail: {e}")

    def _open_floating_color_picker(self, ctx):
        current2 = 0
        try:
            current2 = int(self.get_setting("tlite_floating_color2", 0) or 0)
        except Exception:
            current2 = 0
        self._open_color_picker(ctx, "Floating BG", "tlite_floating_color")

    def _open_floating_icon_color_picker(self, ctx):
        self._open_color_picker(ctx, "Floating icon", "tlite_floating_icon_color")

    def _floating_compose_button_enabled(self):
        try:
            return bool(self.get_setting("tlite_floating_compose_button", False))
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _floating_alpha_options(self):
        return [
            self._tr("settings_floating_alpha_default"),
            "50%",
            "70%",
            "90%",
        ]

    def _floating_alpha_index(self):
        try:
            idx = int(self.get_setting("tlite_floating_alpha", 0) or 0)
            if 0 <= idx <= 3:
                return idx
        except Exception:
            pass
        return 0

    def _floating_alpha_value(self):
        return [1.0, 0.5, 0.7, 0.9][self._floating_alpha_index()]

    def _floating_base_color(self):
        try:
            return int(self.get_setting("tlite_floating_color", 0xFF38A8FF))
        except Exception:
            return 0xFF38A8FF

    def _floating_icon_base_color(self):
        try:
            return int(self.get_setting("tlite_floating_icon_color", 0xFFFFFFFF))
        except Exception:
            return 0xFFFFFFFF

    def _floating_second_bg_color(self):
        try:
            return int(self.get_setting("tlite_floating_color2", 0) or 0)
        except Exception:
            return 0

    def _signed_color(self, color_value):
        try:
            c = int(color_value) & 0xFFFFFFFF
            return c - 0x100000000 if c >= 0x80000000 else c
        except Exception:
            return int(color_value or 0)

    def _mix_color(self, color_a, color_b, amount):
        try:
            a = max(0.0, min(1.0, float(amount)))
            ca = int(color_a) & 0xFFFFFFFF
            cb = int(color_b) & 0xFFFFFFFF
            aa, ar, ag, ab = (ca >> 24) & 0xFF, (ca >> 16) & 0xFF, (ca >> 8) & 0xFF, ca & 0xFF
            ba, br, bg, bb = (cb >> 24) & 0xFF, (cb >> 16) & 0xFF, (cb >> 8) & 0xFF, cb & 0xFF
            na = int(aa + (ba - aa) * a) & 0xFF
            nr = int(ar + (br - ar) * a) & 0xFF
            ng = int(ag + (bg - ag) * a) & 0xFF
            nb = int(ab + (bb - ab) * a) & 0xFF
            return _ji((na << 24) | (nr << 16) | (ng << 8) | nb)
        except Exception:
            return _ji(color_a)

    def _with_alpha(self, color_value, alpha_factor):
        try:
            c = int(color_value) & 0xFFFFFFFF
            alpha = max(0, min(255, int(((c >> 24) & 0xFF) * float(alpha_factor))))
            return _ji((alpha << 24) | (c & 0x00FFFFFF))
        except Exception:
            return _ji(color_value)

    def _floating_bg_color(self):
        return self._mix_color(self._floating_base_color(), 0xFF000000, 0.28)

    def _floating_keyboard_height(self):
        try:
            root = getattr(self, "_floating_root", None)
            if root is None:
                return 0
            host = root.getParent()
            if host is None:
                return 0
            Rect = find_class("android.graphics.Rect")
            if Rect is None:
                return 0
            rect = Rect()
            host.getWindowVisibleDisplayFrame(rect)
            host_loc = [0, 0]
            try:
                host.getLocationOnScreen(host_loc)
            except Exception:
                host_loc = [0, 0]
            host_h = int(host.getHeight() or 0)
            host_top = int(host_loc[1] or 0)
            host_bottom = host_top + host_h
            visible_bottom = min(int(rect.bottom or 0), host_bottom)
            visible_height = max(0, visible_bottom - host_top)
            if host_h <= 0 or visible_height <= 0:
                return 0
            overlap = max(0, host_h - visible_height)
            return overlap if overlap > AndroidUtilities.dp(90) else 0
        except Exception:
            return 0

    def _position_floating_button(self):
        try:
            root = getattr(self, "_floating_root", None)
            if root is None or root.getParent() is None:
                return
            lp = root.getLayoutParams()
            host = root.getParent()
            if lp is None or host is None:
                return
            saved_top = int(self.get_setting("tlite_floating_tm", AndroidUtilities.dp(180)) or AndroidUtilities.dp(180))
            saved_right = int(self.get_setting("tlite_floating_rm", AndroidUtilities.dp(18)) or AndroidUtilities.dp(18))
            root_h = int(root.getHeight() or AndroidUtilities.dp(90))
            host_h = int(host.getHeight() or 0)
            kb = int(self._floating_keyboard_height() or 0)
            top = int(saved_top)
            if host_h > 0 and kb > 0:
                max_top = max(AndroidUtilities.dp(72), host_h - kb - root_h - AndroidUtilities.dp(12))
                top = min(top, max_top)
            changed = False
            if int(getattr(lp, "topMargin", 0) or 0) != top:
                lp.topMargin = top
                changed = True
            if int(getattr(lp, "rightMargin", 0) or 0) != saved_right:
                lp.rightMargin = saved_right
                changed = True
            if changed:
                root.setLayoutParams(lp)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"position floating fail: {e}")

    def _start_floating_position_tracker(self):
        try:
            th_existing = getattr(self, "_floating_pos_thread", None)
            evt_existing = getattr(self, "_floating_pos_stop", None)
            try:
                if th_existing is not None and bool(th_existing.is_alive()) and evt_existing is not None and not bool(evt_existing.is_set()):
                    return
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._stop_floating_position_tracker()
            stop_evt = threading.Event()
            self._floating_pos_stop = stop_evt
            plugin = self

            def _worker():
                while not stop_evt.is_set():
                    try:
                        run_on_ui_thread(plugin._position_floating_button)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    stop_evt.wait(0.65)

            th = threading.Thread(target=_worker, daemon=True)
            self._floating_pos_thread = th
            th.start()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"start floating tracker fail: {e}")

    def _stop_floating_position_tracker(self):
        try:
            evt = getattr(self, "_floating_pos_stop", None)
            if evt is not None:
                evt.set()
        except Exception:
            pass
        self._floating_pos_stop = None
        self._floating_pos_thread = None

    def _native_summary_min_chars(self):
        return 140

    def _extract_message_text_for_avatar_action(self, msg_obj):
        try:
            if msg_obj is None:
                return ""
            
            # 1. Tenta capturar a legenda (caption) primeiro, pois é o texto digitado pelo usuário em mídias
            text = None
            try:
                # O MessageObject costuma ter a legenda processada
                text = getattr(msg_obj, "caption", None)
                if not text:
                    # Se não estiver no MessageObject, busca no messageOwner nativo
                    mo = getattr(msg_obj, "messageOwner", None)
                    if mo is not None:
                        text = getattr(mo, "caption", None)
                        if not text:
                            # Algumas versões do Telegram usam o campo message para legendas de mídias
                            text = getattr(mo, "message", None)
            except Exception:
                pass

            # 2. Se não encontrou legenda, tenta o texto principal (Mensagem de texto comum)
            if not text:
                text = getattr(msg_obj, "messageText", None)

            final_text = str(text or "").strip()
            
            # 3. Filtro de mídias sem conteúdo real (evita mostrar "GIF", "Sticker", etc.)
            try:
                # Verifica se é uma mídia conhecida
                is_media = False
                if msg_obj.isSticker() or msg_obj.isGif() or msg_obj.isRoundVideo() or msg_obj.isVoice() or msg_obj.isPhoto() or msg_obj.isVideo():
                    is_media = True
                
                # Se for mídia e o texto for apenas o nome do tipo (case insensitive), limpamos
                if is_media:
                    u_text = final_text.upper()
                    if u_text in ["GIF", "STICKER", "PHOTO", "VIDEO", "VOICE MESSAGE", "ROUND VIDEO", "DOCUMENT"]:
                        return ""
            except Exception:
                pass
                
            return final_text
        except Exception:
            return ""

    def _get_non_text_message_type(self, msg_obj):
        try:
            if msg_obj is None:
                return None
            
            # Se a mensagem tem texto (ou legenda), não bloqueamos
            if self._avatar_action_text_strict(msg_obj):
                return None

            # Mapeamento para as chaves do dicionário
            m_key = None
            if msg_obj.isSticker() or msg_obj.isAnimatedSticker() or msg_obj.isAnyKindOfSticker():
                m_key = "media_type_sticker"
            elif msg_obj.isPhoto():
                m_key = "media_type_photo"
            elif msg_obj.isVideo():
                m_key = "media_type_video"
            elif msg_obj.isGif():
                m_key = "media_type_gif"
            elif msg_obj.isRoundVideo():
                m_key = "media_type_round"
            elif msg_obj.isVoice():
                m_key = "media_type_voice"
            elif msg_obj.isMusic():
                m_key = "media_type_audio"
            elif msg_obj.isLocation() or msg_obj.isLiveLocation():
                m_key = "media_type_location"
            elif msg_obj.isGame():
                m_key = "media_type_game"
            elif msg_obj.isDice() or msg_obj.isAnimatedEmoji():
                m_key = "media_type_emoji"
            elif msg_obj.isInvoice():
                m_key = "media_type_invoice"
            elif self._avatar_document_kind(msg_obj) == "plugin":
                m_key = "media_type_plugin"
            elif self._avatar_document_kind(msg_obj) == "document":
                m_key = "media_type_generic"
            else:
                m_key = "media_type_generic"
            
            # Retorna a tradução do termo original usando o dicionário
            return self._tr(m_key)
        except Exception:
            return None

    def _avatar_action_text_strict(self, msg_obj):
        try:
            if msg_obj is None:
                return ""
            text = self._extract_message_text_for_avatar_action(msg_obj)
            text = str(text or "").strip()
            if not text:
                return ""
            upper = text.upper()
            if upper in ["GIF", "STICKER", "PHOTO", "VIDEO", "VOICE MESSAGE", "ROUND VIDEO", "DOCUMENT", "FILE", "AUDIO"]:
                return ""
            if re.fullmatch(r"[\w\-. ]+\.(plugin|zip|rar|7z|apk|mp3|m4a|ogg|pdf|txt|json|py)", text, flags=re.IGNORECASE):
                return ""
            return text
        except Exception:
            return ""

    def _avatar_document_kind(self, msg_obj):
        try:
            mo = getattr(msg_obj, "messageOwner", None)
            media = getattr(mo, "media", None) if mo is not None else None
            document = getattr(media, "document", None) if media is not None else None
            attrs = getattr(document, "attributes", None) if document is not None else None
            if attrs is not None:
                try:
                    total = int(attrs.size())
                except Exception:
                    total = 0
                for idx in range(total):
                    try:
                        attr = attrs.get(idx)
                    except Exception:
                        attr = None
                    if attr is None:
                        continue
                    try:
                        file_name = str(getattr(attr, "file_name", "") or "").strip()
                    except Exception:
                        file_name = ""
                    if file_name.lower().endswith(".plugin"):
                        return "plugin"
                    if file_name:
                        return "document"
            return ""
        except Exception:
            return ""

    def _can_native_summarize_message(self, msg_obj):
        try:
            text = self._avatar_action_text_strict(msg_obj)
            if not text:
                return False
            words = re.findall(r"[^\W\d_]+", text, flags=re.UNICODE)
            return bool(len(text) >= self._native_summary_min_chars() and len(words) >= 8)
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _summary_compare_tokens(self, text):
        try:
            return re.findall(r"[^\W\d_]+", str(text or "").lower(), flags=re.UNICODE)
        except Exception:
            return []

    def _strip_summary_links(self, text):
        try:
            out = str(text or "").strip()
            if not out:
                return out
            out = re.sub(r"(?im)^[ \t]*(https?://\S+|www\.\S+|t\.me/\S+)[ \t]*$", "", out)
            out = re.sub(r"(?i)\b(?:https?://|www\.)\S+\b", "", out)
            out = re.sub(r"(?i)\bt\.me/\S+\b", "", out)
            out = re.sub(r"\n{3,}", "\n\n", out)
            out = re.sub(r"[ \t]{2,}", " ", out)
            out = re.sub(r"[ \t]+\n", "\n", out).strip()
            return out
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "").strip()

    def _summary_similarity_ratio(self, a_text, b_text):
        try:
            a_tokens = self._summary_compare_tokens(a_text)
            b_tokens = self._summary_compare_tokens(b_text)
            if not a_tokens or not b_tokens:
                return 0.0
            a_set = set(a_tokens)
            b_set = set(b_tokens)
            inter = len(a_set & b_set)
            union = len(a_set | b_set)
            if union <= 0:
                return 0.0
            return float(inter) / float(union)
        except Exception:
            return 0.0

    def _looks_weak_native_summary(self, source_text, summary_text):
        try:
            src = str(source_text or "").strip()
            out = str(summary_text or "").strip()
            if not src or not out:
                return True
            src_len = len(src)
            out_len = len(out)
            if out_len < 28:
                return True
            ratio = float(out_len) / float(max(1, src_len))
            similarity = self._summary_similarity_ratio(src, out)
            src_words = len(self._summary_compare_tokens(src))
            out_words = len(self._summary_compare_tokens(out))
            if out_words >= src_words:
                return True
            if ratio > 0.88:
                return True
            if similarity > 0.92:
                return True
            if src_len >= 260 and ratio > 0.72:
                return True
            return False
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _build_local_summary_text(self, source_text):
        try:
            text = str(source_text or "").strip()
            if not text:
                return ""
            def _pick_key_clause(sentence):
                sent = str(sentence or "").strip()
                if not sent:
                    return ""
                quoted = re.findall(r"[\"“”'`«](.*?)[\"“”'`»]", sent)
                if quoted:
                    lead = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", sent.split(quoted[0])[0]).strip(" ,;:-")
                    tail = quoted[0].strip()
                    if lead:
                        return f"{lead}: \"{tail}\""
                    return f"\"{tail}\""
                clauses = [c.strip() for c in re.split(r"\s*[,;]\s*", sent) if str(c or "").strip()]
                if len(clauses) <= 1:
                    return sent
                lowered = sent.lower()
                for marker in ("error", "erro", "ошиб", "message", "сообщ", "token", "code", "client id", "secret", "spotify", "спотиф"):
                    for clause in clauses:
                        if marker in clause.lower():
                            return clause
                if "?" in sent:
                    return clauses[0]
                return clauses[-1]

            paragraphs = [p.strip() for p in re.split(r"\n{2,}", text) if str(p or "").strip()]
            if not paragraphs:
                paragraphs = [text]
            picked = []
            for para in paragraphs:
                sentences = [s.strip() for s in re.split(r"(?<=[\.\!\?\u2026])\s+", para) if str(s or "").strip()]
                if not sentences:
                    continue
                if len(sentences) == 1:
                    picked.append(_pick_key_clause(sentences[0]))
                    continue
                picked.append(_pick_key_clause(sentences[0]))
                if len(sentences) >= 3:
                    picked.append(_pick_key_clause(sentences[-1]))
                elif len(sentences) == 2:
                    picked.append(_pick_key_clause(sentences[-1]))
            if not picked:
                picked = [text]
            compact = " ".join(picked).strip()
            compact = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", compact).strip()
            if len(text) <= 260 and len(compact) > 160:
                short_sentences = [s.strip() for s in re.split(r"(?<=[\.\!\?\u2026])\s+", compact) if str(s or "").strip()]
                if short_sentences:
                    compact = short_sentences[0]
                    if len(short_sentences) > 1 and len(compact) < 110:
                        compact = f"{compact} {short_sentences[1]}".strip()
            if len(compact) > 420:
                compact = compact[:417].rstrip(" ,;:-") + "..."
            return compact
        except Exception:
            return str(source_text or "").strip()

    def _get_avatar_summary_result(self, msg_obj, to_lang=None):
        try:
            source_text = self._avatar_action_text_strict(msg_obj)
            native_summary = None
            if self._can_native_summarize_message(msg_obj):
                native_summary = self._request_native_summary_message(msg_obj, to_lang)
            if native_summary and not self._looks_weak_native_summary(source_text, native_summary):
                self._dlog("avatar summary accepted native result")
                return str(native_summary or "").strip()
            self._dlog("avatar summary fallback engaged")
            fallback = self._build_local_summary_text(source_text)
            if not fallback:
                return str(native_summary or "").strip() or None
            target_lang = str(to_lang or "").strip()
            owner = getattr(msg_obj, "messageOwner", None)
            source_lang = str(getattr(owner, "originalLanguage", "") or "").strip().lower()
            if target_lang and target_lang.lower() not in ("und", source_lang):
                translated = self._translate_text_native(fallback, target_lang)
                if translated:
                    return str(translated or "").strip()
            return fallback
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"avatar summary result fail: {e}")
            return None

    def _request_native_summary_message(self, msg_obj, to_lang=None):
        try:
            if msg_obj is None:
                return None
            TLRPC = find_class("org.telegram.tgnet.TLRPC")
            ConnectionsManager = find_class("org.telegram.tgnet.ConnectionsManager")
            RequestDelegate = find_class("org.telegram.tgnet.RequestDelegate")
            if TLRPC is None or ConnectionsManager is None or RequestDelegate is None:
                self._dlog("native summary unavailable classes")
                return None
            req = TLRPC.TL_messages_summarizeText()
            did = int(msg_obj.getDialogId() or 0)
            msg_id = int(msg_obj.getId() or 0)
            if not did or not msg_id:
                return None
            req.peer = MessagesController.getInstance(int(UserConfig.selectedAccount)).getInputPeer(did)
            req.id = int(msg_id)
            lang = str(to_lang or "").strip()
            if lang:
                try:
                    req.flags |= 1
                except Exception:
                    pass
                req.to_lang = lang

            state = {"out": None, "err": None}
            done = threading.Event()

            class _ReqDelegate(dynamic_proxy(RequestDelegate)):
                def run(self_obj, response, error):
                    try:
                        if error is not None:
                            state["err"] = str(getattr(error, "text", "") or "summary_error")
                            return
                        if response is None:
                            state["err"] = "summary_null_response"
                            return
                        text = str(getattr(response, "text", "") or "").strip()
                        if text:
                            state["out"] = text
                        else:
                            state["err"] = "summary_empty_text"
                    except Exception as _e:
                        state["err"] = str(_e)
                    finally:
                        done.set()

            ConnectionsManager.getInstance(int(UserConfig.selectedAccount)).sendRequest(req, _ReqDelegate())
            if not done.wait(14):
                self._dlog("native summary timeout")
                return None
            if not state["out"]:
                err = str(state.get("err", "") or "summary_error")
                if err == "summary_empty_text":
                    self._dlog("native summary returned empty text; fallback may be required for this message/account")
                else:
                    self._dlog(f"native summary fail: {err}")
                return None
            self._dlog(f"native summary ok len_out={len(state['out'])}")
            return str(state["out"] or "").strip() or None
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"native summary error: {e}")
            return None

    def _show_avatar_native_result_sheet(self, fragment, title_text, subtitle_text, result_text, current_lang_code=None, on_pick_language=None):
        try:
            if fragment is None:
                return False
            activity = None
            try:
                activity = fragment.getParentActivity()
            except Exception:
                activity = None
            if activity is None:
                return False
            ctx = activity
            is_dark = bool(Theme.isCurrentThemeDark())
            bg_color = _ji(0xFF1F2937) if is_dark else _ji(0xFFF7F8FC)
            card_color = _ji(0xFF233041) if is_dark else _ji(0xFFFFFFFF)
            primary_text = _ji(0xFFFFFFFF) if is_dark else _ji(0xFF1F2937)
            secondary_text = _ji(0xFF9CA3AF) if is_dark else _ji(0xFF64748B)
            stroke = _ji(0x22FFFFFF) if is_dark else _ji(0x160F172A)
            accent = _ji(0xFF3B82F6)
            accent_text = _ji(0xFFFFFFFF)

            sheet = BottomSheet(ctx, False)
            outer = LinearLayout(ctx)
            outer.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            outer_bg = GradientDrawable()
            outer_bg.setColor(bg_color)
            outer_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(28)))
            outer.setBackground(outer_bg)
            outer.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18))

            title = TextView(ctx)
            title.setText(str(title_text or "Translatica"))
            title.setTextColor(primary_text)
            title.setTextSize(1, 19)
            try:
                title.setTypeface(title.getTypeface(), 1)
            except Exception:
                pass
            title.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL)
            outer.addView(title, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            subtitle = TextView(ctx)
            subtitle.setText(str(subtitle_text or ""))
            subtitle.setTextColor(secondary_text)
            subtitle.setTextSize(1, 13)
            subtitle.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL)
            subtitle.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(4), 0, 0)
            outer.addView(subtitle, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            card = LinearLayout(ctx)
            card.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            card_bg = GradientDrawable()
            card_bg.setColor(card_color)
            card_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(22)))
            try:
                card_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), stroke)
            except Exception:
                pass
            card.setBackground(card_bg)
            card.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(16))
            lp_card = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_card.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(16)
            outer.addView(card, lp_card)

            body = TextView(ctx)
            body.setText(str(result_text or ""))
            body.setTextColor(primary_text)
            body.setTextSize(1, 17)
            card.addView(body, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            actions = LinearLayout(ctx)
            actions.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            actions.setGravity(Gravity.END | Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            lp_actions = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_actions.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(16)
            outer.addView(actions, lp_actions)

            if current_lang_code and callable(on_pick_language):
                lang_btn = TextView(ctx)
                lang_btn.setText(str(self._lang_label_from_code(current_lang_code) or "").strip())
                lang_btn.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
                lang_btn.setTextSize(1, 15)
                lang_btn.setTextColor(accent)
                lang_bg = GradientDrawable()
                try:
                    lang_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(16)))
                    lang_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), stroke)
                    lang_bg.setColor(_ji(0x00000000))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                lang_btn.setBackground(lang_bg)
                try:
                    lang_btn.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))
                except Exception:
                    pass

                class _PickLang(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                    def onClick(self_obj, v):
                        try:
                            builder = AlertDialogBuilder(ctx)
                            builder.set_title(self._tr("settings_target_lang"))
                            root_lang = LinearLayout(ctx)
                            root_lang.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
                            try:
                                root_lang.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            current_code = str(current_lang_code or "en")
                            def _make_pick_listener(picked_code):
                                picked_code = str(picked_code or "en")
                                class _Pick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                                    def onClick(self_pick, _v):
                                        try:
                                            dlg.dismiss()
                                        except Exception:
                                            pass
                                        try:
                                            sheet.dismiss()
                                        except Exception:
                                            pass
                                        try:
                                            on_pick_language(picked_code)
                                        except Exception as inner_e:
                                            self._dlog(f"summary lang pick fail: {inner_e}")
                                return _Pick()
                            for i, label in enumerate(LANG_LABELS):
                                code = str(LANG_CODES[i])
                                row = TextView(ctx)
                                row.setText(f"{label}{'' if code != current_code else ' [x]'}")
                                try:
                                    row.setTextSize(16)
                                    row.setTextColor(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteBlackText))
                                    row.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))
                                except Exception:
                                    pass
                                row.setOnClickListener(_make_pick_listener(code))
                                root_lang.addView(row, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
                            builder.set_view(root_lang)
                            dlg = builder.create()
                            dlg.show()
                        except Exception as inner_e:
                            self._dlog(f"open summary lang dialog fail: {inner_e}")

                lang_btn.setOnClickListener(_PickLang())
                lp_lang = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
                lp_lang.rightMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
                actions.addView(lang_btn, lp_lang)

            copy_btn = TextView(ctx)
            copy_btn.setText(self._tr("live_preview_copy"))
            copy_btn.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
            copy_btn.setTextSize(1, 15)
            copy_btn.setTextColor(accent_text)
            copy_bg = GradientDrawable()
            copy_bg.setColor(accent)
            copy_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
            copy_btn.setBackground(copy_bg)
            copy_btn.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))

            class _Copy(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        self._copy_text_to_clipboard(result_text)
                        BulletinHelper.show_success(self._tr("live_preview_copied"))
                    except Exception:
                        pass

            copy_btn.setOnClickListener(_Copy())
            actions.addView(copy_btn, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            sheet.setCustomView(outer)
            sheet.show()
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"avatar native result sheet fail: {e}")
            return False

    def _show_native_message_action(self, fragment, msg_obj, do_summary=False):
        try:
            if fragment is None or msg_obj is None:
                return False
            ctx = None
            try:
                ctx = fragment.getParentActivity()
            except Exception:
                ctx = None
            if ctx is None:
                return False
            text = self._avatar_action_text_strict(msg_obj)
            if not text:
                return False
            mo = getattr(msg_obj, "messageOwner", None)
            from_lang = str(getattr(mo, "originalLanguage", "") or "und")
            to_lang = str(self._avatar_summary_lang_code() or "en")
            BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("avatar_ai_loading_summary") if bool(do_summary) else self._tr("avatar_ai_loading_translate"))
            def _worker():
                try:
                    if do_summary:
                        result = self._get_avatar_summary_result(msg_obj, to_lang)
                        title = self._tr("avatar_ai_native_summary_title")
                        subtitle = self._lang_label_from_code(to_lang)
                    else:
                        result = self._translate_text_native(text, to_lang, wait_sec=18)
                        title = "Translatica"
                        subtitle = self._tr("live_preview_pair").format(
                            self._lang_label_from_code(from_lang if from_lang and from_lang != "und" else self._global_target_lang()),
                            self._lang_label_from_code(to_lang),
                        )
                    def _finish():
                        if result:
                            try:
                                self._usage_stats_record("summary" if bool(do_summary) else "avatar", to_lang, msg_obj.getDialogId())
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            self._show_avatar_native_result_sheet(fragment, title, subtitle, result)
                        else:
                            BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty"))
                    run_on_ui_thread(_finish)
                except Exception as inner_e:
                    def _fail():
                        BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty"))
                        self._dlog(f"avatar native worker fail: {inner_e}")
                    run_on_ui_thread(_fail)
            try:
                from client_utils import run_on_queue
                run_on_queue(_worker)
            except Exception:
                threading.Thread(target=_worker, daemon=True).start()

            self._dlog(f"avatar native action queued | summary={bool(do_summary)}")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"avatar native action fail: {e}")
            return False

    def _show_avatar_ai_choice_sheet(self, fragment, msg_obj):
        try:
            if fragment is None or msg_obj is None:
                return False
            ctx = None
            try:
                ctx = fragment.getParentActivity()
            except Exception:
                ctx = None
            if ctx is None:
                return False
            is_dark = bool(Theme.isCurrentThemeDark())
            primary_text = _ji(0xFFFFFFFF) if is_dark else _ji(0xFF1F2937)
            secondary_text = _ji(0xFF9CA3AF) if is_dark else _ji(0xFF64748B)
            stroke = _ji(0x22FFFFFF) if is_dark else _ji(0x160F172A)
            accent = _ji(0xFF3B82F6)
            favorite_active = _ji(0xFFFACC15)
            favorite_idle = _ji(0xFF94A3B8 if is_dark else 0xFF64748B)
            sender_id = self._favorite_sender_id_from_message(msg_obj)
            sender_user = self._sender_user_from_message(msg_obj)
            is_favorite = bool(sender_id and sender_id in self._favorite_sender_ids)

            sheet = BottomSheet(ctx, False)
            root = LinearLayout(ctx)
            root.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            try:
                root.setBackgroundColor(0x00000000)
            except Exception:
                pass
            root.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18))

            title = TextView(ctx)
            title.setText(self._tr("avatar_ai_action_title"))
            title.setTextColor(primary_text)
            title.setTextSize(1, 19)
            try:
                title.setTypeface(title.getTypeface(), 1)
            except Exception:
                pass
            title.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL)
            root.addView(title, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            subtitle = TextView(ctx)
            subtitle.setText(self._tr("avatar_ai_action_desc"))
            subtitle.setTextColor(secondary_text)
            subtitle.setTextSize(1, 13)
            subtitle.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL)
            subtitle.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(5), 0, 0)
            root.addView(subtitle, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            body = LinearLayout(ctx)
            body.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            body.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            lp_body = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_body.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(16)
            root.addView(body, lp_body)

            def _build_action(text_value, icon_name, click_fn):
                card = LinearLayout(ctx)
                card.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
                card.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
                card.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(14))
                bg = GradientDrawable()
                bg.setColor(_ji(0x00000000))
                bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
                try:
                    bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), stroke)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                card.setBackground(bg)
                icon = ImageView(ctx)
                try:
                    rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier(str(icon_name or "msg_log"), "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                    if rid:
                        icon.setImageResource(rid)
                        icon.setColorFilter(accent)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                card.addView(icon, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(22), AndroidUtilities.dp(22)))
                label = TextView(ctx)
                label.setText(str(text_value or ""))
                label.setTextColor(primary_text)
                label.setTextSize(1, 15)
                try:
                    label.setTypeface(label.getTypeface(), 1)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                lp_label = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
                lp_label.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(12)
                card.addView(label, lp_label)

                class _Click(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                    def onClick(self_obj, v):
                        try:
                            sheet.dismiss()
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        click_fn()

                card.setOnClickListener(_Click())
                return card

            row_holder = LinearLayout(ctx)
            row_holder.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            body.addView(row_holder, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1.0))

            translate_card = _build_action(self._tr("settings_ai_avatar_action_translate"), "msg_translate", lambda: self._show_native_message_action(fragment, msg_obj, do_summary=False))
            row_holder.addView(translate_card, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            def _open_summary():
                self._show_native_message_action(fragment, msg_obj, do_summary=True)

            summary_card = _build_action(self._tr("ai_sheet_summary"), "menu_quote_specific", _open_summary)
            lp_summary = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_summary.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
            row_holder.addView(summary_card, lp_summary)

            avatar_size = AndroidUtilities.dp(108)
            profile_wrap = FrameLayout(ctx)
            lp_profile = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(avatar_size, avatar_size)
            lp_profile.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(14)
            body.addView(profile_wrap, lp_profile)

            avatar_bg = GradientDrawable()
            avatar_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(20)))
            avatar_bg.setColor(_ji(0x00000000))
            try:
                avatar_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), stroke)
            except Exception:
                pass

            avatar_view = BackupImageView(ctx)
            try:
                avatar_view.setRoundRadius(AndroidUtilities.dp(20))
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                avatar_view.setBackground(avatar_bg)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                avatar_view.setScaleType(ImageView.ScaleType.CENTER_CROP)
            except Exception:
                pass
            if sender_user is not None:
                try:
                    avatar_view.setForUserOrChat(sender_user, AvatarDrawable(sender_user))
                except Exception:
                    try:
                        avatar_view.setImageDrawable(AvatarDrawable(sender_user))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
            else:
                try:
                    avatar_view.setImageDrawable(self._make_avatar_fallback_drawable())
                except Exception:
                    pass
            profile_wrap.addView(avatar_view, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(avatar_size, avatar_size, Gravity.CENTER))

            favorite_badge = FrameLayout(ctx)
            fav_bg = GradientDrawable()
            fav_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(12)))
            fav_bg.setColor(_ji(0xCC0F172A if is_dark else 0xE5FFFFFF))
            try:
                fav_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), stroke)
            except Exception:
                pass
            favorite_badge.setBackground(fav_bg)
            fav_icon = ImageView(ctx)
            try:
                fav_rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("msg_fave", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                if not fav_rid:
                    fav_rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("msg_pin_solar", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                if fav_rid:
                    fav_icon.setImageResource(fav_rid)
                    fav_icon.setColorFilter(favorite_active if is_favorite else favorite_idle)
            except Exception:
                pass
            favorite_badge.addView(fav_icon, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), Gravity.CENTER))
            lp_badge = FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(28), AndroidUtilities.dp(28), Gravity.TOP | Gravity.RIGHT)
            lp_badge.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(6)
            lp_badge.rightMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(6)
            profile_wrap.addView(favorite_badge, lp_badge)

            if sender_user is not None:
                class _AvatarClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                    def onClick(self_obj, v):
                        try:
                            sheet.dismiss()
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        try:
                            self._open_user_profile(fragment, int(getattr(sender_user, "id", 0) or 0))
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                avatar_view.setOnClickListener(_AvatarClick())
                profile_wrap.setOnClickListener(_AvatarClick())

            sheet.setCustomView(root)
            sheet.show()
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"avatar choice sheet fail: {e}")
            return False

    def _handle_avatar_long_action(self, fragment, cell):
        try:
            if cell is None:
                return False
            try:
                from client_utils import get_last_fragment
                fragment = get_last_fragment() or self._chat_fragment_ref or fragment
            except Exception:
                fragment = self._chat_fragment_ref or fragment
            if fragment is None:
                self._native_log("avatar hold skipped: no fragment")
                return False
            msg_obj = None
            try:
                msg_obj = cell.getMessageObject()
            except Exception:
                msg_obj = None
            if msg_obj is None:
                self._native_log("avatar hold skipped: no message object")
                return False
            
            # Identifica se é uma mídia que não pode ser traduzida/resumida
            if self._avatar_document_kind(msg_obj) == "plugin" and not self._avatar_action_text_strict(msg_obj):
                try:
                    BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("avatar_ai_media_block_plugin"))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                return True
            media_desc = self._get_non_text_message_type(msg_obj)
            if media_desc:
                try:
                    # Bulletin amigável usando as chaves do dicionário
                    msg = self._tr("avatar_ai_media_block").format(media_desc)
                    BulletinHelper.show_info(msg)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                return True # Retorna True para indicar que o evento foi consumido

            text = self._avatar_action_text_strict(msg_obj)
            if not text:
                self._native_log("avatar hold skipped: empty text")
                return False
            mode = str(self._avatar_ai_action_mode() or "both").strip().lower()
            self._native_log("avatar hold triggered | mode={0} len={1}".format(mode, len(text)))
            if mode == "summary":
                return bool(self._show_native_message_action(fragment, msg_obj, do_summary=True))
            if mode == "translate":
                return bool(self._show_native_message_action(fragment, msg_obj, do_summary=False))
            return bool(self._show_avatar_ai_choice_sheet(fragment, msg_obj))
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"handle avatar long action fail: {e}")
            return False

    def _live_preview_options(self):
        return ["2", "3", "4", "5", "7", "10"]

    def _live_preview_enabled(self):
        try:
            return bool(self.get_setting("tlite_live_preview_enabled", False))
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _live_preview_delay_index(self):
        opts = self._live_preview_options()
        try:
            raw = self.get_setting("tlite_live_preview_delay", 1)
            if isinstance(raw, str):
                raw_str = str(raw or "").strip()
                if raw_str in opts:
                    return opts.index(raw_str)
                raw = int(raw_str or 1)
            else:
                raw = int(raw or 1)
        except Exception:
            raw = 1
        return raw if 0 <= raw < len(opts) else 1

    def _set_live_preview_delay(self, value):
        try:
            opts = self._live_preview_options()
            picked = None
            raw = value
            try:
                self._dlog(f"live preview selector raw value={raw}")
            except Exception:
                pass
            if isinstance(raw, str):
                raw_str = str(raw or "").strip()
                if raw_str in opts:
                    picked = raw_str
                else:
                    try:
                        idx = int(raw_str)
                        if 0 <= idx < len(opts):
                            picked = opts[idx]
                    except Exception:
                        picked = None
            else:
                try:
                    idx = int(raw)
                    if 0 <= idx < len(opts):
                        picked = opts[idx]
                except Exception:
                    picked = None
            if not picked:
                picked = opts[1]
            self.set_setting("tlite_live_preview_delay", str(picked))
            self._dlog(f"live preview selector saved={picked}")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"set live preview delay fail: {e}")

    def _live_preview_delay_value(self):
        try:
            raw = self.get_setting("tlite_live_preview_delay", self._live_preview_options()[0])
            if isinstance(raw, str):
                raw_str = str(raw or "").strip()
                if raw_str in self._live_preview_options():
                    item = raw_str
                else:
                    item = str(self._live_preview_options()[self._live_preview_delay_index()] or "2")
            else:
                item = str(self._live_preview_options()[self._live_preview_delay_index()] or "2")
        except Exception:
            item = "2"
        return max(2, int(item))

    def _guess_source_lang_code(self, text):
        try:
            value = str(text or "").strip()
            if not value:
                return ""
            if re.search(r"[\u0600-\u06FF]", value):
                return "ar"
            if re.search(r"[\u0590-\u05FF]", value):
                return "he"
            if re.search(r"[\u3040-\u30FF]", value):
                return "ja"
            if re.search(r"[\uAC00-\uD7AF]", value):
                return "ko"
            if re.search(r"[\u4E00-\u9FFF]", value):
                return "zh-CN"
            if re.search(r"[\u0370-\u03FF]", value):
                return "el"
            if re.search(r"[\u0900-\u097F]", value):
                return "hi"
            if re.search(r"[\u0400-\u04FF]", value):
                return "ru"
            low = value.lower()
            if re.search(r"\b(vamos|isso|porque|voce|você|nao|não|com|para|estou|gente|hoje)\b", low):
                return "pt"
            if re.search(r"\b(the|and|this|that|hello|please|because|with|today)\b", low):
                return "en"
            if re.search(r"\b(que|hola|gracias|porque|estoy|para|hoy)\b", low):
                return "es"
            if re.search(r"\b(und|danke|bitte|heute|weil|hallo|ich)\b", low):
                return "de"
            if re.search(r"\b(bonjour|merci|avec|pourquoi|aujourd'hui|je)\b", low):
                return "fr"
            if re.search(r"\b(ciao|grazie|oggi|perche|perché|con|sono)\b", low):
                return "it"
            return ""
        except Exception:
            return ""

    def _live_preview_source_label(self, text):
        try:
            code = str(self._guess_source_lang_code(text) or "").strip()
            if code:
                return self._lang_label_from_code(code)
        except Exception:
            pass
        return ""

    def _extract_dialog_id(self, params=None, fragment=None):
        try:
            if fragment is None:
                try:
                    from client_utils import get_last_fragment
                    fragment = get_last_fragment()
                except Exception:
                    fragment = None
            if fragment is not None and hasattr(fragment, "getDialogId"):
                try:
                    return int(fragment.getDialogId() or 0)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            if params is not None:
                for key in ("dialog_id", "dialogId", "peer", "peer_id"):
                    try:
                        v = getattr(params, key, None)
                        if v is not None:
                            iv = int(v)
                            if iv != 0:
                                return iv
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                try:
                    if isinstance(params, dict):
                        for key in ("dialog_id", "dialogId", "peer", "peer_id"):
                            v = params.get(key)
                            if v is not None:
                                iv = int(v)
                                if iv != 0:
                                    return iv
                except Exception:
                    pass
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            if int(getattr(self, "_chat_dialog_id_ref", 0) or 0) != 0:
                return int(self._chat_dialog_id_ref)
        except Exception:
            pass
        return 0

    def _chat_can_use_floating(self, fragment):
        try:
            if fragment is None:
                self._dlog("floating check: fragment missing")
                return False
            dialog_id = 0
            try:
                dialog_id = int(self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=fragment) or 0)
            except Exception:
                dialog_id = 0
            frag_cls = ""
            try:
                frag_cls = str(fragment.getClass().getSimpleName() or "")
            except Exception:
                try:
                    frag_cls = str(fragment.__class__.__name__ or "")
                except Exception:
                    frag_cls = ""
            current_chat = None
            try:
                if hasattr(fragment, "getCurrentChat"):
                    current_chat = fragment.getCurrentChat()
            except Exception:
                current_chat = None
            enter_view = None
            try:
                enter_view = self._get_enter_view(fragment)
            except Exception:
                enter_view = None
            fragment_view = None
            try:
                fragment_view = fragment.getFragmentView() if hasattr(fragment, "getFragmentView") else None
            except Exception:
                fragment_view = None
            ChatObject = None
            if current_chat is not None:
                try:
                    ChatObject = find_class("org.telegram.messenger.ChatObject")
                except Exception:
                    ChatObject = None
            if current_chat is not None and ChatObject is not None:
                try:
                    if bool(ChatObject.isChannel(current_chat)) and not bool(getattr(current_chat, "megagroup", False)):
                        allowed = bool(ChatObject.canPost(current_chat))
                        self._dlog(f"floating check channel canPost={allowed} dialog_id={dialog_id} frag={frag_cls}")
                        return allowed
                except Exception:
                    pass
            try:
                if hasattr(fragment, "canSendMessage"):
                    can_send = bool(fragment.canSendMessage())
                    if can_send:
                        self._dlog(f"floating check ok: canSendMessage dialog_id={dialog_id} frag={frag_cls}")
                        return bool(dialog_id != 0)
                    if enter_view is not None and fragment_view is not None and bool(dialog_id != 0):
                        self._dlog(f"floating check ok: enter+fragmentView fallback dialog_id={dialog_id} frag={frag_cls}")
                        return True
                    self._dlog(f"floating check denied: canSendMessage false dialog_id={dialog_id} frag={frag_cls} enter={enter_view is not None} view={fragment_view is not None}")
                    return False
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                if enter_view is not None and bool(dialog_id != 0):
                    self._dlog(f"floating check ok: enterView dialog_id={dialog_id} frag={frag_cls}")
                    return True
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                if fragment_view is not None and enter_view is not None and bool(dialog_id != 0):
                    self._dlog(f"floating check ok: fragmentView+enterView dialog_id={dialog_id} frag={frag_cls}")
                    return True
            except Exception:
                pass
            if current_chat is None:
                self._dlog(f"floating check final: no current chat dialog_id={dialog_id} enter={enter_view is not None} frag={frag_cls}")
                return bool(dialog_id != 0 and enter_view is not None)
            if ChatObject is None:
                self._dlog(f"floating check final: ChatObject missing dialog_id={dialog_id} enter={enter_view is not None} frag={frag_cls}")
                return bool(dialog_id != 0 and enter_view is not None)
            try:
                if bool(ChatObject.canSendMessages(current_chat)):
                    self._dlog(f"floating check ok: ChatObject.canSendMessages dialog_id={dialog_id} frag={frag_cls}")
                    return True
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                if bool(ChatObject.canWriteToChat(current_chat)):
                    self._dlog(f"floating check ok: ChatObject.canWriteToChat dialog_id={dialog_id} frag={frag_cls}")
                    return True
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._dlog(f"floating check denied: no send permission dialog_id={dialog_id} frag={frag_cls}")
            return False
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _schedule_floating_sync(self, fragment, delay_sec=0.1):
        try:
            nonce = int(getattr(self, "_floating_sync_nonce", 0) or 0) + 1
            self._floating_sync_nonce = nonce
            def _fire():
                try:
                    if int(getattr(self, "_floating_sync_nonce", 0) or 0) != nonce:
                        return
                    run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self._sync_floating_button(fragment))
                except Exception:
                    pass
            try:
                threading.Timer(float(delay_sec), _fire).start()
            except Exception:
                run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self._sync_floating_button(fragment))
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"schedule floating sync fail: {e}")

    def _chat_prefs(self):
        try:
            raw = self.get_setting("tlite_chat_prefs", {}) or {}
            if isinstance(raw, dict):
                return raw
        except Exception:
            pass
        return {}

    def _save_chat_prefs(self, prefs):
        try:
            self.set_setting("tlite_chat_prefs", prefs if isinstance(prefs, dict) else {})
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _chat_config(self, dialog_id):
        prefs = self._chat_prefs()
        key = str(int(dialog_id or 0))
        cfg = prefs.get(key) or {}
        if not isinstance(cfg, dict):
            cfg = {}
        enabled = bool(cfg.get("enabled", False))
        lang = str(cfg.get("lang", self._global_target_lang()) or self._global_target_lang())
        if lang not in LANG_CODES:
            lang = self._global_target_lang()
        return {"enabled": enabled, "lang": lang}

    def _set_chat_config(self, dialog_id, enabled=None, lang=None):
        try:
            did = int(dialog_id or 0)
            if did == 0:
                return
            prefs = self._chat_prefs()
            key = str(did)
            cfg = prefs.get(key) or {}
            if not isinstance(cfg, dict):
                cfg = {}
            if enabled is not None:
                cfg["enabled"] = bool(enabled)
            if lang is not None and str(lang or "") in LANG_CODES:
                cfg["lang"] = str(lang)
            cfg.pop("card", None)
            prefs[key] = cfg
            self._save_chat_prefs(prefs)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"set chat config fail: {e}")

    def _refresh_chat_action_buttons(self):
        try:
            self._refresh_apple_button()
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            self._refresh_floating_button()
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _schedule_compose_ui_refresh(self, fragment, delay_sec=0.09):
        try:
            if not (self._assist_fab_enabled() or self._assist_native_button_enabled()):
                return
            frag = fragment or self._chat_fragment_ref
            if frag is None:
                return
            nonce = int(getattr(self, "_compose_ui_refresh_nonce", 0) or 0) + 1
            self._compose_ui_refresh_nonce = nonce
            def _fire():
                try:
                    if int(getattr(self, "_compose_ui_refresh_nonce", 0) or 0) != nonce:
                        return
                    run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self._refresh_assist_button(frag))
                except Exception:
                    pass
            try:
                threading.Timer(float(delay_sec), _fire).start()
            except Exception:
                run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self._refresh_assist_button(frag))
        except Exception:
            try:
                run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self._refresh_assist_button(fragment))
            except Exception:
                pass

    def _refresh_floating_button(self):
        try:
            root = self._floating_root
            main = self._floating_main_btn
            lang_btn = self._floating_lang_btn
            if root is None or self._chat_fragment_ref is None or main is None:
                return
            did = self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=self._chat_fragment_ref)
            cfg = self._chat_config(did)
            active = bool(cfg.get("enabled", True))
            base = int(self._floating_base_color()) & 0xFFFFFFFF
            base2 = int(self._floating_second_bg_color()) & 0xFFFFFFFF
            icon_base = int(self._floating_icon_base_color()) & 0xFFFFFFFF
            alpha_factor = float(self._floating_alpha_value())
            accent = _ji(base)
            icon_accent = _ji(icon_base)
            idle = self._mix_color(base, 0xFF0F172A, 0.55)
            idle2 = self._mix_color(base2, 0xFF0F172A, 0.55) if base2 else 0
            main_bg = self._with_alpha(accent if active else idle, alpha_factor)
            lang_bg = self._with_alpha(self._mix_color(base, 0xFF111827, 0.42), alpha_factor)
            try:
                sig = (
                    int(did),
                    bool(active),
                    int(base),
                    int(base2),
                    int(icon_base),
                    round(float(alpha_factor), 3),
                    int(self._floating_keyboard_height() or 0),
                )
            except Exception:
                sig = None
            try:
                if sig is not None and sig == getattr(self, "_floating_visual_sig", None):
                    self._position_floating_button()
                    return
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                bg_main = main.getBackground()
                if isinstance(bg_main, GradientDrawable):
                    if base2:
                        c1 = self._signed_color((base if active else idle) & 0xFFFFFFFF)
                        c2 = self._signed_color((base2 if active else idle2) & 0xFFFFFFFF)
                        bg_main.setOrientation(GradientDrawable.Orientation.TL_BR)
                        bg_main.setColors(jarray(jint)([c1, c2]))
                        bg_main.setAlpha(max(0, min(255, int(255 * alpha_factor))))
                    else:
                        bg_main.setColor(main_bg)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                bg_lang = lang_btn.getBackground() if lang_btn is not None else None
                if isinstance(bg_lang, GradientDrawable):
                    bg_lang.setColor(lang_bg)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                if self._floating_main_icon is not None:
                    main_icon_color = self._with_alpha(icon_accent if active else self._mix_color(icon_base, 0xFF94A3B8, 0.35), alpha_factor)
                    self._floating_main_icon.setColorFilter(main_icon_color)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                if self._floating_lang_icon is not None:
                    self._floating_lang_icon.setColorFilter(self._with_alpha(icon_accent, alpha_factor))
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                root.setAlpha(alpha_factor)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                self._floating_visual_sig = sig
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._position_floating_button()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"refresh floating button fail: {e}")

    def _attach_floating_drag_listener(self, handle_view):
        try:
            touch_cls = find_class("android.view.View$OnTouchListener")
            MotionEvent = jclass("android.view.MotionEvent")
            if touch_cls is None or MotionEvent is None or handle_view is None:
                return
            plugin = self

            class _Drag(dynamic_proxy(touch_cls)):
                def onTouch(self_obj, _v, event):
                    try:
                        root = plugin._floating_root
                        if root is None:
                            return False
                        lp = root.getLayoutParams()
                        par = root.getParent()
                        if lp is None or par is None:
                            return False
                        action = int(event.getActionMasked())
                        dw = int(par.getWidth() or 0)
                        dh = int(par.getHeight() or 0)
                        if action == MotionEvent.ACTION_DOWN:
                            plugin._floating_drag_moved = False
                            plugin._floating_drag_sx = float(event.getRawX())
                            plugin._floating_drag_sy = float(event.getRawY())
                            plugin._floating_drag_rm0 = int(getattr(lp, "rightMargin", 0) or 0)
                            plugin._floating_drag_tm0 = int(getattr(lp, "topMargin", 0) or 0)
                            return True
                        if action == MotionEvent.ACTION_MOVE:
                            dx = float(event.getRawX()) - float(plugin._floating_drag_sx)
                            dy = float(event.getRawY()) - float(plugin._floating_drag_sy)
                            if abs(dx) > 6 or abs(dy) > 6:
                                plugin._floating_drag_moved = True
                            w = int(root.getWidth() or AndroidUtilities.dp(48))
                            h = int(root.getHeight() or AndroidUtilities.dp(88))
                            lp.rightMargin = max(0, min(int(plugin._floating_drag_rm0 - dx), max(0, dw - w)))
                            lp.topMargin = max(0, min(int(plugin._floating_drag_tm0 + dy), max(0, dh - h)))
                            root.setLayoutParams(lp)
                            return True
                        if action in (MotionEvent.ACTION_UP, MotionEvent.ACTION_CANCEL):
                            if plugin._floating_drag_moved:
                                plugin.set_setting("tlite_floating_rm", int(getattr(lp, "rightMargin", 0) or 0))
                                plugin.set_setting("tlite_floating_tm", int(getattr(lp, "topMargin", 0) or 0))
                                return True
                            try:
                                if action == MotionEvent.ACTION_UP and plugin._floating_main_btn is not None:
                                    plugin._floating_main_btn.performClick()
                                    return True
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    return False

            handle_view.setOnTouchListener(_Drag())
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"attach floating drag fail: {e}")

    def _attach_floating_button(self, fragment):
        try:
            try:
                if Looper.myLooper() != Looper.getMainLooper():
                    run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self._attach_floating_button(fragment))
                    return
            except Exception:
                pass
            if not self._floating_enabled() or not self._floating_visible():
                self._dlog("floating attach skipped: disabled or hidden")
                self._detach_floating_button()
                return
            host = self._get_overlay_host(fragment)
            if host is None:
                self._dlog("floating attach skipped: host missing")
                return
            try:
                self._dlog(f"floating attach host={host.__class__.__name__} frag={fragment.getClass().getSimpleName()} dialog_id={int(self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=fragment) or 0)}")
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                if hasattr(host, "setClipChildren"):
                    host.setClipChildren(False)
                if hasattr(host, "setClipToPadding"):
                    host.setClipToPadding(False)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                existing_root = getattr(self, "_floating_root", None)
                existing_parent = existing_root.getParent() if existing_root is not None else None
                if existing_root is not None and existing_parent is not None and existing_parent is not host:
                    try:
                        existing_parent.removeView(existing_root)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    self._floating_root = None
                    self._floating_main_btn = None
                    self._floating_lang_btn = None
                    self._floating_main_icon = None
                    self._floating_lang_icon = None
                    self._dlog("floating host changed -> reattach")
            except Exception:
                pass
            existing = None
            try:
                child_count = int(host.getChildCount() or 0)
            except Exception:
                child_count = 0
            for idx in range(child_count):
                try:
                    child = host.getChildAt(idx)
                    if str(getattr(child, "getTag", lambda: "")() or "") == "__tlite_floating_root__":
                        existing = child
                        break
                except Exception:
                    pass
            if existing is not None:
                self._dlog("floating attach reused existing root")
                self._floating_root = existing
                self._chat_fragment_ref = fragment
                try:
                    self._chat_dialog_id_ref = int(self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=fragment) or 0)
                except Exception:
                    self._chat_dialog_id_ref = 0
                try:
                    self._floating_main_btn = existing.getChildAt(0)
                    self._floating_lang_btn = existing.getChildAt(1) if existing.getChildCount() > 1 else None
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    self._floating_main_icon = self._floating_main_btn.getChildAt(0) if self._floating_main_btn is not None else None
                    self._floating_lang_icon = self._floating_lang_btn.getChildAt(0) if self._floating_lang_btn is not None else None
                except Exception:
                    pass
                self._refresh_floating_button()
                try:
                    if hasattr(host, "bringChildToFront"):
                        host.bringChildToFront(existing)
                    existing.bringToFront()
                    existing.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE)
                    existing.setAlpha(1.0)
                    self._position_floating_button()
                    host.requestLayout()
                    host.invalidate()
                except Exception:
                    pass
                self._start_floating_position_tracker()
                return
            ctx = host.getContext()
            root = LinearLayout(ctx)
            root.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            root.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_HORIZONTAL)
            try:
                root.setTag("__tlite_floating_root__")
            except Exception:
                pass
            main_btn = FrameLayout(ctx)
            main_bg = GradientDrawable()
            main_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(24)))
            main_bg.setColor(self._with_alpha(self._floating_bg_color(), self._floating_alpha_value()))
            main_btn.setBackground(main_bg)
            try:
                main_btn.setElevation(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(6)))
            except Exception:
                pass
            main_icon = self._build_apple_icon(ctx)
            main_btn.addView(main_icon, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(24), AndroidUtilities.dp(24), Gravity.CENTER))

            lang_btn = FrameLayout(ctx)
            lang_bg = GradientDrawable()
            lang_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(12)))
            lang_bg.setColor(self._with_alpha(self._mix_color(self._floating_base_color(), 0xFF111827, 0.42), self._floating_alpha_value()))
            lang_btn.setBackground(lang_bg)
            lang_icon = ImageView(ctx)
            try:
                rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("msg_language", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                if rid:
                    lang_icon.setImageResource(rid)
            except Exception:
                pass
            lang_btn.addView(lang_icon, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(16), Gravity.CENTER))

            class _MainClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, _v):
                    try:
                        did = self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=fragment)
                        cfg = self._chat_config(did)
                        new_state = not bool(cfg.get("enabled", True))
                        self._set_chat_config(did, enabled=new_state)
                        self._refresh_chat_action_buttons()
                        BulletinHelper.show_success(self._tr("bulletin_chat_enabled_saved") if new_state else self._tr("bulletin_chat_disabled_saved"))
                    except Exception as e:
                        self._dlog(f"floating click fail: {e}")

            class _LangClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, _v):
                    try:
                        self._show_language_dialog(fragment)
                    except Exception:
                        pass

            main_btn.setOnClickListener(_MainClick())
            class _MainLong(dynamic_proxy(View.OnLongClickListener)):
                def onLongClick(self_obj, _v):
                    try:
                        self._flash_assist_button_press(main_btn)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        self._open_plugin_settings()
                    except Exception as e:
                        self._dlog(f"floating long click fail: {e}")
                    return True
            main_btn.setOnLongClickListener(_MainLong())
            lang_btn.setOnClickListener(_LangClick())
            self._attach_floating_drag_listener(main_btn)

            root.addView(main_btn, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(48), AndroidUtilities.dp(48)))
            lp_lang = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(34), AndroidUtilities.dp(34))
            lp_lang.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(8)
            root.addView(lang_btn, lp_lang)
