            lp_root = FrameLayout.LayoutParams(FrameLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, FrameLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_root.gravity = Gravity.TOP | Gravity.RIGHT
            lp_root.topMargin = int(self.get_setting("tlite_floating_tm", AndroidUtilities.dp(180)) or AndroidUtilities.dp(180))
            lp_root.rightMargin = int(self.get_setting("tlite_floating_rm", AndroidUtilities.dp(18)) or AndroidUtilities.dp(18))
            host.addView(root, lp_root)
            self._floating_root = root
            self._floating_main_btn = main_btn
            self._floating_lang_btn = lang_btn
            self._floating_main_icon = main_icon
            self._floating_lang_icon = lang_icon
            self._refresh_floating_button()
            try:
                def _after_attach():
                    try:
                        if hasattr(host, "bringChildToFront"):
                            host.bringChildToFront(root)
                        root.bringToFront()
                        root.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE)
                        root.setAlpha(1.0)
                        self._position_floating_button()
                        host.requestLayout()
                        host.invalidate()
                        try:
                            self._dlog(f"floating attached metrics host={int(host.getWidth() or 0)}x{int(host.getHeight() or 0)} root={int(root.getWidth() or 0)}x{int(root.getHeight() or 0)}")
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                    except Exception as inner_e:
                        self._dlog(f"floating post-attach fail: {inner_e}")
                root.post(_after_attach)
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._start_floating_position_tracker()
            self._dlog("floating button attached")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"attach floating fail: {e}")

    def _detach_floating_button(self):
        try:
            self._stop_floating_position_tracker()
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            if self._floating_root is not None and self._floating_root.getParent() is not None:
                self._floating_root.getParent().removeView(self._floating_root)
        except Exception:
            pass
        self._floating_root = None
        self._floating_main_btn = None
        self._floating_lang_btn = None
        self._floating_main_icon = None
        self._floating_lang_icon = None

    def _sync_floating_button(self, fragment=None):
        try:
            try:
                if Looper.myLooper() != Looper.getMainLooper():
                    run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self._sync_floating_button(fragment))
                    return
            except Exception:
                pass
            frag = fragment or self._chat_fragment_ref
            if frag is not None:
                self._chat_fragment_ref = frag
            if not self._floating_enabled() or not self._floating_visible():
                self._dlog("floating sync -> detach: disabled or hidden")
                self._detach_floating_button()
                self._refresh_apple_button()
                return
            if frag is not None and not self._chat_can_use_floating(frag):
                self._dlog(f"floating sync -> detach: unsupported dialog_id={int(self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=frag) or 0)}")
                self._detach_floating_button()
                return
            try:
                root = getattr(self, "_floating_root", None)
                if root is not None and frag is not None:
                    parent = root.getParent()
                    current_host = self._get_overlay_host(frag)
                    if parent is not None and current_host is not None and parent is not current_host:
                        self._dlog("floating sync -> detach: host mismatch")
                        self._detach_floating_button()
            except Exception:
                pass
            if frag is not None:
                self._attach_floating_button(frag)
            self._refresh_chat_action_buttons()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"sync floating fail: {e}")

    def _build_apple_icon(self, ctx):
        icon = ImageView(ctx)
        loaded_custom = False
        try:
            if os.path.exists(CHAT_ICON_CACHE_FILE):
                bmp = BitmapFactory.decodeFile(CHAT_ICON_CACHE_FILE)
                if bmp:
                    icon.setImageBitmap(bmp)
                    loaded_custom = True
        except Exception:
            pass
        if not loaded_custom:
            try:
                from client_utils import run_on_queue
                def _dl():
                    try:
                        self._load_chat_icon_remote()
                        if os.path.exists(CHAT_ICON_CACHE_FILE):
                            bmp2 = BitmapFactory.decodeFile(CHAT_ICON_CACHE_FILE)
                            if bmp2:
                                def _apply():
                                    try:
                                        icon.setImageBitmap(bmp2)
                                        self._refresh_apple_button()
                                    except Exception:
                                        pass
                                run_on_ui_thread(_apply)
                    except Exception as e:
                        self._dlog(f"chat icon async load fail: {e}")
                run_on_queue(_dl)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("msg_translate", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                if rid:
                    icon.setImageResource(rid)
            except Exception:
                pass
        try:
            icon.setScaleType(ImageView.ScaleType.CENTER_INSIDE)
        except Exception:
            pass
        return icon

    def _apply_apple_icon_state(self, fragment, icon_view):
        try:
            did = self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=fragment)
            cfg = self._chat_config(did)
            if cfg["enabled"]:
                try:
                    color = int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_featuredStickers_addButton))
                except Exception:
                    color = 0xFF38A8FF
            else:
                try:
                    color = int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_chat_messagePanelIcons))
                except Exception:
                    color = 0xFF8A8A8A
            icon_view.setColorFilter(color)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _refresh_apple_button(self):
        try:
            if self._chat_apple_btn is None or self._chat_fragment_ref is None or self._chat_apple_icon is None:
                return
            if self._floating_enabled() and not self._floating_compose_button_enabled():
                try:
                    self._chat_apple_btn.setVisibility(View.GONE)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                return
            try:
                self._chat_apple_btn.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE)
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._apply_apple_icon_state(self._chat_fragment_ref, self._chat_apple_icon)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _schedule_apple_attach_retry(self, fragment, reason="retry"):
        try:
            if fragment is None:
                return
            key = str(id(fragment))
            if key in self._attach_retry_keys:
                return
            self._attach_retry_keys.add(key)
            from client_utils import run_on_queue
            def _worker():
                try:
                    for _ in range(5):
                        time.sleep(0.22)
                        done = {"ok": False}
                        def _try():
                            try:
                                self._attach_apple_button(fragment, from_retry=True)
                                done["ok"] = self._chat_apple_btn is not None
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                        run_on_ui_thread(_try)
                        if done["ok"]:
                            break
                finally:
                    try:
                        self._attach_retry_keys.discard(key)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
            run_on_queue(_worker)
            self._dlog(f"attach retry scheduled: {reason}")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"attach retry fail: {e}")

    def _schedule_apple_reorder(self, host, btn):
        try:
            if host is None or btn is None:
                return
            if not isinstance(host, LinearLayout):
                return
            def _once():
                try:
                    if btn.getParent() is not host:
                        return
                    self._reposition_apple_in_attach_layout(self._chat_fragment_ref, host, btn)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            run_on_ui_thread(_once)
            from client_utils import run_on_queue
            def _retry():
                for _ in range(4):
                    time.sleep(0.24)
                    run_on_ui_thread(_once)
            run_on_queue(_retry)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"apple reorder fail: {e}")

    def _reposition_apple_in_attach_layout(self, fragment, host, btn):
        try:
            if host is None or btn is None or not isinstance(host, LinearLayout):
                return
            enter_view = self._get_enter_view(fragment)
            attach_btn = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "attachButton") if enter_view is not None else None
            scheduled_btn = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "scheduledButton") if enter_view is not None else None
            notify_btn = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "notifyButton") if enter_view is not None else None
            bot_btn = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "botButton") if enter_view is not None else None
            lp = None
            try:
                lp = btn.getLayoutParams()
            except Exception:
                lp = None
            if lp is None or not isinstance(lp, LinearLayout.LayoutParams):
                lp = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(30), AndroidUtilities.dp(30))
            try:
                lp.width = AndroidUtilities.dp(30)
                lp.height = AndroidUtilities.dp(30)
                lp.gravity = Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL
                lp.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(4)
                lp.rightMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(4)
            except Exception:
                pass

            target_index = None
            try:
                if attach_btn is not None and attach_btn.getParent() is host:
                    target_index = int(host.indexOfChild(attach_btn))
            except Exception:
                target_index = None
            if target_index is None:
                last_native = -1
                for native in (bot_btn, notify_btn, scheduled_btn):
                    try:
                        if native is None or native.getParent() is not host:
                            continue
                        if int(native.getVisibility()) != int(View.VISIBLE):
                            continue
                        idx = int(host.indexOfChild(native))
                        if idx > last_native:
                            last_native = idx
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                target_index = max(0, last_native + 1)
            try:
                current_parent = btn.getParent()
                if current_parent is host:
                    current_index = int(host.indexOfChild(btn))
                    if current_index >= 0:
                        host.removeView(btn)
                        if current_index < target_index:
                            target_index -= 1
                elif current_parent is not None:
                    current_parent.removeView(btn)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                target_index = max(0, min(int(target_index), int(host.getChildCount())))
                host.addView(btn, target_index, lp)
            except Exception:
                try:
                    host.addView(btn, lp)
                except Exception:
                    host.addView(btn)
            try:
                btn.bringToFront()
            except Exception:
                pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"reposition apple fail: {e}")

    def _schedule_apple_stabilize(self, fragment):
        try:
            if fragment is None:
                return
            from client_utils import run_on_queue
            def _worker():
                for _ in range(5):
                    time.sleep(0.28)
                    run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self._attach_apple_button(fragment, from_retry=True))
            run_on_queue(_worker)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"apple stabilize fail: {e}")

    def _show_language_dialog(self, fragment=None, dialog_id=0):
        try:
            ctx = fragment.getParentActivity() if fragment and fragment.getParentActivity() else ApplicationLoader.applicationContext
            if not ctx:
                return
            try:
                self._dismiss_keyboard_focus(ctx)
            except Exception:
                pass
            did = int(dialog_id or 0)
            if did == 0:
                did = self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=fragment)
            if did == 0:
                return
            cfg = self._chat_config(did)
            current = str(cfg.get("lang", self._global_target_lang()))
            builder = AlertDialogBuilder(ctx)
            builder.set_title(self._tr("sheet_title_chat_language"))
            root = LinearLayout(ctx)
            root.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            try:
                root.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
            except Exception:
                pass

            for i, label in enumerate(LANG_LABELS):
                code = LANG_CODES[i]
                row = TextView(ctx)
                row.setText(f"{label}{'' if code != current else ' [x]'}")
                try:
                    row.setTextSize(16)
                    row.setTextColor(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteBlackText))
                    row.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))
                except Exception:
                    pass

                class _Click(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                    def __init__(self_obj, picked_code, picked_label):
                        super().__init__()
                        self_obj.picked_code = picked_code
                        self_obj.picked_label = picked_label
                    def onClick(self_obj, v):
                        try:
                            self._set_chat_config(did, lang=self_obj.picked_code)
                            self._refresh_apple_button()
                            try:
                                self._telemetry_queue_event("feature_use", feature=f"lang_select_{self_obj.picked_code}", count=1, force_flush=False)
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            BulletinHelper.show_success(
                                (self._tr("bulletin_chat_lang_saved")).replace("%s", self_obj.picked_label.split(" (")[0])
                            )
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        try:
                            if self._lang_dialog:
                                self._lang_dialog.dismiss()
                        except Exception:
                            pass

                row.setOnClickListener(_Click(code, label))
                root.addView(row)

            builder.set_view(root)
            builder.set_negative_button(self._tr("dialog_close"), lambda d, w: d.dismiss() if d else None)
            self._lang_dialog = builder.show()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"language dialog fail: {e}")

    def _on_target_lang_changed(self, index):
        try:
            idx = int(index or 0)
        except Exception:
            idx = 0
        if idx < 0 or idx >= len(LANG_CODES):
            idx = 0
        try:
            self.set_setting("tlite_target_lang", idx)
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            self._telemetry_queue_event("feature_use", feature=f"lang_select_{LANG_CODES[idx]}", count=1, force_flush=False)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _on_plugin_lang_selector_changed(self, index):
        try:
            idx = int(index or 0)
        except Exception:
            idx = 0
        if idx < 0 or idx >= len(PLUGIN_LANG_OPTIONS):
            idx = 0
        try:
            self.set_setting("tlite_plugin_lang", idx)
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            code = str(PLUGIN_LANG_OPTIONS[idx][1] or "system")
            self._telemetry_queue_event("feature_use", feature=f"ui_lang_{code}", count=1, force_flush=False)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _dismiss_keyboard_focus(self, ctx):
        try:
            if ctx is None:
                return
            try:
                focused = ctx.getCurrentFocus()
            except Exception:
                focused = None
            try:
                if focused is not None:
                    focused.clearFocus()
            except Exception:
                pass
            imm = None
            try:
                imm = ctx.getSystemService("input_method")
            except Exception:
                imm = None
            if imm is None:
                return
            token = None
            try:
                w = ctx.getWindow()
                dv = w.getDecorView() if w is not None else None
                token = dv.getWindowToken() if dv is not None else None
            except Exception:
                token = None
            if token is None:
                try:
                    focused = ctx.getCurrentFocus()
                    token = focused.getWindowToken() if focused is not None else None
                except Exception:
                    token = None
            if token is not None:
                try:
                    imm.hideSoftInputFromWindow(token, 0)
                except Exception:
                    pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"dismiss keyboard fail: {e}")

    def _attach_apple_button(self, fragment, from_retry=False):
        try:
            if not fragment:
                return
            enter_view = None
            try:
                enter_view = _get_private_field_silent(fragment, "chatActivityEnterView")
            except Exception:
                pass
            if enter_view is None:
                if not from_retry:
                    self._schedule_apple_attach_retry(fragment, "no_enter_view")
                return

            host = None
            try:
                host = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "attachLayout")
            except Exception:
                pass
            if host is None:
                try:
                    host = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "sendButtonContainer")
                except Exception:
                    pass
            if host is None:
                try:
                    host = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "textFieldContainer")
                except Exception:
                    pass
            if host is None:
                try:
                    host = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "messageEditTextContainer")
                except Exception:
                    pass
            if host is None:
                try:
                    for fname in ("attachLayout", "sendButtonContainer", "textFieldContainer", "messageEditTextContainer", "messageContainer", "topView", "parentView"):
                        try:
                            cand = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, fname)
                            if cand is not None and isinstance(cand, ViewGroup):
                                host = cand
                                break
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                except Exception:
                    pass
            if host is None:
                if not from_retry:
                    self._schedule_apple_attach_retry(fragment, "no_host")
                return
            if self._floating_enabled() and not self._floating_compose_button_enabled():
                self._detach_apple_button()
                self._chat_fragment_ref = fragment
                try:
                    self._chat_dialog_id_ref = int(self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=fragment) or 0)
                except Exception:
                    self._chat_dialog_id_ref = 0
                self._attach_compose_assist_button(fragment, host)
                return
            try:
                self._dlog(f"apple host={host.__class__.__name__} retry={from_retry}")
            except Exception:
                pass

            existing = None
            try:
                existing = host.findViewWithTag("__tlite_apple_btn__")
            except Exception:
                pass

            if existing is not None:
                self._chat_apple_btn = existing
                try:
                    self._chat_apple_icon = existing.getChildAt(0)
                except Exception:
                    self._chat_apple_icon = None
                self._chat_fragment_ref = fragment
                try:
                    self._chat_dialog_id_ref = int(self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=fragment) or 0)
                except Exception:
                    self._chat_dialog_id_ref = 0
                self._refresh_apple_button()
                self._attach_compose_assist_button(fragment, host)
                try:
                    self._reposition_apple_in_attach_layout(fragment, host, existing)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                return

            btn = FrameLayout(host.getContext())
            try:
                btn.setTag("__tlite_apple_btn__")
            except Exception:
                pass
            icon = self._build_apple_icon(host.getContext())
            try:
                btn.addView(icon, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(24), AndroidUtilities.dp(24), Gravity.CENTER))
            except Exception:
                btn.addView(icon)

            try:
                if isinstance(host, LinearLayout):
                    lp = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(30), AndroidUtilities.dp(30))
                    lp.gravity = Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL
                    lp.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(4)
                    lp.rightMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(4)
                    host.addView(btn, lp)
                else:
                    host.addView(btn)
            except Exception:
                host.addView(btn)

            class _Click(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        did = self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=fragment)
                        cfg = self._chat_config(did)
                        new_state = not bool(cfg["enabled"])
                        self._set_chat_config(did, enabled=new_state)
                        self._refresh_apple_button()
                        if new_state:
                            BulletinHelper.show_success(self._tr("bulletin_chat_enabled_saved"))
                        else:
                            BulletinHelper.show_success(self._tr("bulletin_chat_disabled_saved"))
                    except Exception as e:
                        self._dlog(f"apple click fail: {e}")

            class _Long(dynamic_proxy(View.OnLongClickListener)):
                def onLongClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        self._show_language_dialog(fragment)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    return True

            btn.setOnClickListener(_Click())
            btn.setOnLongClickListener(_Long())
            self._chat_apple_btn = btn
            self._chat_apple_icon = icon
            self._chat_fragment_ref = fragment
            try:
                self._chat_dialog_id_ref = int(self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=fragment) or 0)
            except Exception:
                self._chat_dialog_id_ref = 0
            self._refresh_apple_button()
            self._attach_compose_assist_button(fragment, host)
            try:
                self._reposition_apple_in_attach_layout(fragment, host, btn)
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._schedule_apple_reorder(host, btn)
            self._dlog("apple button attached")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"attach apple fail: {e}")

    def _detach_apple_button(self):
        try:
            if self._chat_apple_btn is not None and self._chat_apple_btn.getParent() is not None:
                self._chat_apple_btn.getParent().removeView(self._chat_apple_btn)
        except Exception:
            pass
        self._chat_apple_btn = None
        self._chat_apple_icon = None
        self._chat_fragment_ref = None
        self._chat_dialog_id_ref = 0

    def _detach_assist_button(self):
        try:
            self._stop_assist_position_tracker()
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            self._cancel_live_preview_timer()
            self._hide_live_preview_prompt()
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            if self._chat_assist_btn is not None and self._chat_assist_btn.getParent() is not None:
                self._chat_assist_btn.getParent().removeView(self._chat_assist_btn)
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            if self._chat_assist_fab is not None and self._chat_assist_fab.getParent() is not None:
                self._chat_assist_fab.getParent().removeView(self._chat_assist_fab)
        except Exception:
            pass
        self._chat_assist_btn = None
        self._chat_assist_icon = None
        self._chat_assist_fab = None
        self._chat_assist_fab_icon = None

    def _start_assist_position_tracker(self, fragment):
        try:
            try:
                th_existing = getattr(self, "_assist_pos_thread", None)
                evt_existing = getattr(self, "_assist_pos_stop", None)
                if th_existing is not None and bool(th_existing.is_alive()) and evt_existing is not None and not bool(evt_existing.is_set()):
                    return
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._stop_assist_position_tracker()
            stop_evt = threading.Event()
            self._assist_pos_stop = stop_evt

            def _worker():
                while not stop_evt.is_set():
                    try:
                        run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self._refresh_assist_button(fragment))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    stop_evt.wait(0.58)

            th = threading.Thread(target=_worker, daemon=True)
            self._assist_pos_thread = th
            th.start()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"start assist tracker fail: {e}")

    def _stop_assist_position_tracker(self):
        try:
            evt = getattr(self, "_assist_pos_stop", None)
            if evt is not None:
                evt.set()
        except Exception:
            pass
        self._assist_pos_stop = None
        self._assist_pos_thread = None

    def _count_compose_chars(self, text):
        try:
            return len(str(text or ""))
        except Exception:
            return 0

    def _should_show_assist_button(self, text):
        return False

    def _has_meaningful_word(self, text):
        try:
            t = str(text or "").strip()
            if not t:
                return False
            t = re.sub(r"(https?://\S+|www\.\S+)", " ", t, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
            return bool(re.search(r"[^\W\d_]+", t, flags=re.UNICODE))
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _assist_can_open_for_text(self, text):
        try:
            t = str(text or "").strip()
            if not t:
                return False
            if self._is_emoji_only(t):
                return False
            return self._has_meaningful_word(t)
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _assist_provider_options(self):
        return [
            "Custom",
            "Gemini",
            "OpenRouter",
            "Cerebras",
            "LLM7",
            "OnlySQ",
        ]

    def _assist_side_options(self):
        return [
            self._tr("settings_side_left"),
            self._tr("settings_side_right"),
        ]

    def _assist_entry_options(self):
        return [
            "Assist",
            self._tr("settings_ai_assist_entry_button"),
            self._tr("settings_ai_assist_entry_button_panel"),
            self._tr("settings_ai_assist_entry_both"),
        ]

    def _assist_entry_mode(self):
        try:
            raw = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_assist_entry_mode", "assist") or "assist").strip().lower()
            if raw in ("assist", "button", "button_panel", "both"):
                return raw
        except Exception:
            pass
        return "assist"

    def _assist_entry_index(self):
        raw = self._assist_entry_mode()
        if raw == "button":
            return 1
        if raw == "button_panel":
            return 2
        if raw == "both":
            return 3
        return 0

    def _assist_fab_enabled(self):
        return self._assist_entry_mode() in ("assist", "both")

    def _assist_native_button_enabled(self):
        return self._assist_entry_mode() in ("button", "button_panel", "both")

    def _assist_native_button_opens_panel(self):
        return self._assist_entry_mode() == "button_panel"

    def _on_assist_entry_mode_changed(self, idx):
        try:
            val = "assist"
            try:
                ival = int(idx)
            except Exception:
                ival = 0
            if ival == 1:
                val = "button"
            elif ival == 2:
                val = "button_panel"
            elif ival == 3:
                val = "both"
            self.set_setting("tlite_ai_assist_entry_mode", val)
            if not self._assist_native_button_enabled() and self._native_assist_cycle_mode() == "assist":
                self._set_native_assist_cycle_mode("audio")
            run_on_ui_thread(lambda: (self._refresh_assist_button(self._chat_fragment_ref), self._ensure_native_assist_cycle_ui(self._chat_fragment_ref), self._refresh_settings_screen()))
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"assist entry mode change fail: {e}")

    def _assist_side_index(self):
        try:
            raw = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_assist_side", "right") or "right").strip().lower()
            return 0 if raw == "left" else 1
        except Exception:
            return 1

    def _native_assist_cycle_mode(self):
        try:
            raw = str(self.get_setting("tlite_native_assist_cycle_mode", "audio") or "audio").strip().lower()
            if raw in ("audio", "video", "assist"):
                return raw
        except Exception:
            pass
        return "audio"

    def _set_native_assist_cycle_mode(self, value):
        try:
            mode = str(value or "audio").strip().lower()
            if mode not in ("audio", "video", "assist"):
                mode = "audio"
            self.set_setting("tlite_native_assist_cycle_mode", mode)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _native_assist_mode_selected(self):
        try:
            return bool(
                self._assist_native_button_enabled() and
                bool(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_assist_enabled", False)) and
                self._native_assist_cycle_mode() == "assist"
            )
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _native_assist_next_mode(self, current_mode):
        try:
            raw = str(current_mode or "audio").strip().lower()
            assist_enabled = bool(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_assist_enabled", False))
            if not self._assist_native_button_enabled() or not assist_enabled:
                return "video" if raw == "audio" else "audio"
            if raw == "audio":
                return "video"
            if raw == "video":
                return "assist"
            return "audio"
        except Exception:
            return "audio"

    def _set_native_record_mode(self, enter_view, is_video, animated=False):
        try:
            delegate = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "delegate")
        except Exception:
            delegate = None
        try:
            if delegate is not None and hasattr(delegate, "onSwitchRecordMode"):
                delegate.onSwitchRecordMode(bool(is_video))
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            methods = enter_view.getClass().getDeclaredMethods()
        except Exception:
            methods = []
        for method in methods:
            try:
                if str(method.getName() or "") != "setRecordVideoButtonVisible":
                    continue
                params = method.getParameterTypes()
                if params is None or len(params) != 2:
                    continue
                method.setAccessible(True)
                method.invoke(enter_view, bool(is_video), bool(animated))
                return True
            except Exception:
                pass
        try:
            method = enter_view.getClass().getMethod("setRecordVideoButtonVisible", jclass("java.lang.Boolean"), jclass("java.lang.Boolean"))
            method.invoke(enter_view, bool(is_video), bool(animated))
            return True
        except Exception:
            try:
                enter_view.setRecordVideoButtonVisible(bool(is_video), bool(animated))
                return True
            except Exception:
                return False

    def _ensure_native_assist_cycle_ui(self, fragment):
        try:
            if fragment is None:
                return
            enter_view = self._get_enter_view(fragment)
            if enter_view is None:
                return
            container = None
            try:
                container = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "audioVideoButtonContainer")
            except Exception:
                container = None
            if container is None:
                return
            frag_key = id(fragment)
            overlay = self._native_assist_overlay_views.get(frag_key)
            if overlay is None or overlay.getParent() is None:
                ctx = None
                try:
                    ctx = container.getContext()
                except Exception:
                    ctx = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext
                host = FrameLayout(ctx)
                try:
                    host.setClickable(False)
                    host.setFocusable(False)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                overlay = self._build_assist_icon(ctx)
                try:
                    overlay.setColorFilter(_ji(0xFFFFFFFF))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    overlay.setClickable(False)
                    overlay.setFocusable(False)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    icon_lp = FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(20), AndroidUtilities.dp(20), Gravity.CENTER)
                    host.addView(overlay, icon_lp)
                    try:
                        overlay.setTranslationX(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(3)))
                        overlay.setTranslationY(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(-1)))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    lp = FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(48), AndroidUtilities.dp(48), Gravity.CENTER)
                    container.addView(host, lp)
                    overlay = host
                except Exception:
                    try:
                        container.addView(host)
                        overlay = host
                    except Exception:
                        overlay = None
                if overlay is not None:
                    self._native_assist_overlay_views[frag_key] = overlay
            listener = self._native_assist_touch_listeners.get(frag_key)
            if listener is None:
                plugin = self
                class _NativeAssistTouch(dynamic_proxy(View.OnTouchListener)):
                    def __init__(self_inner):
                        super().__init__()
                        self_inner.down_ts = 0.0
                        self_inner.down_x = 0.0
                        self_inner.down_y = 0.0
                        self_inner.moved = False
                        self_inner.prev_mode = "audio"
                        self_inner.hold_timer = None
                        self_inner.hold_fired = False
                    def onTouch(self_inner, v, event):
                        compose_empty_assist = False
                        try:
                            current_text = str(plugin._get_compose_text(fragment) or "").strip()
                            compose_empty_assist = bool(plugin._native_assist_mode_selected() and not plugin._assist_can_open_for_text(current_text))
                        except Exception:
                            compose_empty_assist = False
                        try:
                            action = int(event.getAction())
                        except Exception:
                            action = -1
                        try:
                            if action == int(MotionEvent.ACTION_DOWN):
                                self_inner.down_ts = time.time()
                                self_inner.down_x = float(event.getX())
                                self_inner.down_y = float(event.getY())
                                self_inner.moved = False
                                self_inner.hold_fired = False
                                self_inner.prev_mode = plugin._native_assist_cycle_mode()
                                try:
                                    if self_inner.hold_timer is not None:
                                        self_inner.hold_timer.cancel()
                                except Exception:
                                    pass
                                self_inner.hold_timer = None
                                if compose_empty_assist:
                                    def _fire_hold():
                                        try:
                                            if self_inner.moved or self_inner.hold_fired:
                                                return
                                            self_inner.hold_fired = True
                                            run_on_ui_thread(plugin._open_plugin_settings)
                                        except Exception:
                                            pass
                                    try:
                                        self_inner.hold_timer = threading.Timer(0.32, _fire_hold)
                                        self_inner.hold_timer.daemon = True
                                        self_inner.hold_timer.start()
                                    except Exception:
                                        self_inner.hold_timer = None
                            elif action == int(MotionEvent.ACTION_MOVE):
                                dx = abs(float(event.getX()) - float(self_inner.down_x))
                                dy = abs(float(event.getY()) - float(self_inner.down_y))
                                if dx > float(AndroidUtilities.dp(8)) or dy > float(AndroidUtilities.dp(8)):
                                    self_inner.moved = True
                                    try:
                                        if self_inner.hold_timer is not None:
                                            self_inner.hold_timer.cancel()
                                    except Exception:
                                        pass
                                    self_inner.hold_timer = None
                            elif action == int(MotionEvent.ACTION_UP):
                                try:
                                    if self_inner.hold_timer is not None:
                                        self_inner.hold_timer.cancel()
                                except Exception:
                                    pass
                                self_inner.hold_timer = None
                                elapsed = float(time.time() - float(self_inner.down_ts or 0.0))
                                if not self_inner.moved and not self_inner.hold_fired:
                                    prev_mode = str(self_inner.prev_mode or "audio")
                                    if elapsed <= 0.22:
                                        try:
                                            threading.Timer(0.04, lambda: run_on_ui_thread(lambda: plugin._handle_native_assist_short_tap(fragment, prev_mode))).start()
                                        except Exception:
                                            run_on_ui_thread(lambda: plugin._handle_native_assist_short_tap(fragment, prev_mode))
                                        if compose_empty_assist:
                                            return True
                            elif action == int(MotionEvent.ACTION_CANCEL):
                                self_inner.moved = False
                                try:
                                    if self_inner.hold_timer is not None:
                                        self_inner.hold_timer.cancel()
                                except Exception:
                                    pass
                                self_inner.hold_timer = None
                        except Exception as e:
                            plugin._dlog(f"native assist touch fail: {e}")
                        return bool(compose_empty_assist)
                listener = _NativeAssistTouch()
                try:
                    container.setOnTouchListener(listener)
                    self._native_assist_touch_listeners[frag_key] = listener
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"native assist touch attach fail: {e}")
            self._sync_native_assist_cycle_visual(fragment)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"ensure native assist cycle ui fail: {e}")

    def _handle_native_assist_short_tap(self, fragment, previous_mode=None):
        try:
            prev_mode = str(previous_mode or self._native_assist_cycle_mode() or "audio").strip().lower()
            next_mode = self._native_assist_next_mode(prev_mode)
            self._set_native_assist_cycle_mode(next_mode)
            enter_view = self._get_enter_view(fragment)
            if enter_view is not None and next_mode == "assist":
                self._set_native_record_mode(enter_view, True, False)
            self._sync_native_assist_cycle_visual(fragment)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"handle native assist short tap fail: {e}")

    def _sync_native_assist_cycle_visual(self, fragment=None):
        try:
            if fragment is None:
                fragment = self._chat_fragment_ref
            if fragment is None:
                return
            enter_view = self._get_enter_view(fragment)
            if enter_view is None:
                return
            container = None
            native_icon = None
            try:
                container = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "audioVideoButtonContainer")
            except Exception:
                container = None
            try:
                native_icon = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "audioVideoSendButton")
            except Exception:
                native_icon = None
            if container is None:
                return
            overlay = self._native_assist_overlay_views.get(id(fragment))
            if overlay is None or overlay.getParent() is None:
                self._ensure_native_assist_cycle_ui(fragment)
                overlay = self._native_assist_overlay_views.get(id(fragment))
            overlay_icon = None
            try:
                if overlay is not None and hasattr(overlay, "getChildCount") and int(overlay.getChildCount() or 0) > 0:
                    overlay_icon = overlay.getChildAt(0)
            except Exception:
                overlay_icon = None
            compose_text = str(self._get_compose_text(fragment) or "").strip()
            show_assist_icon = bool(
                overlay is not None and
                self._native_assist_mode_selected() and
                not compose_text and
                int(container.getVisibility()) == int(View.VISIBLE)
            )
            if overlay is not None:
                try:
                    overlay.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if show_assist_icon else View.GONE)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                if show_assist_icon:
                    try:
                        overlay.bringToFront()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
            if overlay_icon is not None:
                try:
                    overlay_icon.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if show_assist_icon else View.GONE)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    overlay_icon.setAlpha(1.0 if show_assist_icon else 0.0)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    if show_assist_icon:
                        overlay_icon.bringToFront()
                except Exception:
                    pass
            if native_icon is not None:
                try:
                    native_icon.setAlpha(0.0 if show_assist_icon else 1.0)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    native_icon.setVisibility(View.INVISIBLE if show_assist_icon else View.VISIBLE)
                except Exception:
                    pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"sync native assist cycle visual fail: {e}")

    def _cleanup_native_assist_cycle_ui(self):
        try:
            for _, overlay in list(getattr(self, "_native_assist_overlay_views", {}).items()):
                try:
                    parent = overlay.getParent()
                except Exception:
                    parent = None
                try:
                    if parent is not None:
                        parent.removeView(overlay)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            self._native_assist_overlay_views = {}
            self._native_assist_touch_listeners = {}
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"cleanup native assist cycle ui fail: {e}")

    def _native_assist_apply_and_send(self, fragment, enter_view=None):
        try:
            if self._native_assist_send_running:
                return True
            if fragment is None:
                return False
            source_plain_text = str(self._get_compose_text(fragment) or "").strip()
            source_text = source_plain_text
            if not self._assist_can_open_for_text(source_plain_text):
                return False
            bulletins_enabled = bool(self._assist_send_bulletins_enabled())
            if not self._is_assist_ai_configured():
                if bulletins_enabled:
                    BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_missing_config"))
                return True
            dst = str(self._assist_target_lang(fragment) or "en")
            pinned_mode = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_pinned_mode", "") or "").strip().lower()
            self._native_assist_send_running = True
            try:
                if bulletins_enabled:
                    BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("ai_sheet_generating"))
            except Exception:
                pass

            def _worker():
                final_text = ""
                try:
                    translated = self._translate_text(source_text, dst)
                    translated = self._preserve_protected_names_in_output(source_text, translated)
                    translated = self._normalize_assist_output(translated, None)
                    corrected = self._request_ai_correction(source_text, translated, None, False, dst) or translated
                    corrected = self._preserve_protected_names_in_output(source_text, corrected)
                    if pinned_mode:
                        final_text = str(self._request_ai_mode(source_text, corrected, pinned_mode, False, dst) or corrected or "").strip()
                    else:
                        final_text = str(corrected or translated or "").strip()
                    final_text = self._normalize_assist_output(final_text, pinned_mode or None)
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"native assist worker fail: {e}")
                    final_text = ""

                def _apply():
                    try:
                        if not final_text:
                            if bulletins_enabled:
                                BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty"))
                            return
                        payload = self._prepare_assist_send_payload(final_text)
                        self._assist_pending_send = payload
                        sent = self._trigger_compose_send(fragment)
                        if sent:
                            if bulletins_enabled:
                                BulletinHelper.show_success(self._tr("ai_sheet_sent"))
                        else:
                            self._assist_pending_send = None
                            if bulletins_enabled:
                                BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_send_fail"))
                    finally:
                        self._native_assist_send_running = False

                run_on_ui_thread(_apply)

            try:
                from client_utils import run_on_queue
                run_on_queue(_worker)
            except Exception:
                threading.Thread(target=_worker, daemon=True).start()
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self._native_assist_send_running = False
            self._dlog(f"native assist apply and send fail: {e}")
            return False

    def _assist_send_bulletins_enabled(self):
        try:
            return bool(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_assist_send_bulletins", False))
        except Exception:
            return True

    def _assist_provider_idx(self):
        try:
            idx = int(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_provider", 0) or 0)
        except Exception:
            idx = 0
        try:
            if not bool(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_provider_reordered_v1", False)):
                legacy = idx
                if legacy == 0:
                    idx = 1
                elif legacy == 1:
                    idx = 2
                elif legacy == 2:
                    idx = 3
                elif legacy == 3:
                    idx = 4
                elif legacy == 4:
                    idx = 5
                elif legacy == 5:
                    idx = 6
                else:
                    idx = 0
                self.set_setting("tlite_ai_provider", int(idx))
                self.set_setting("tlite_ai_provider_reordered_v1", True)
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            if not bool(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_provider_removed_appleai_v1", False)):
                current = idx
                if current <= 1:
                    idx = 0
                elif current == 2:
                    idx = 1
                elif current == 3:
                    idx = 2
                elif current == 4:
                    idx = 3
                elif current == 5:
                    idx = 4
                elif current == 6:
                    idx = 5
                else:
                    idx = 0
                self.set_setting("tlite_ai_provider", int(idx))
                self.set_setting("tlite_ai_provider_removed_appleai_v1", True)
        except Exception:
            pass
        opts = self._assist_provider_options()
        if idx < 0 or idx >= len(opts):
            idx = 0
        return idx
