    def _assist_model_index(self, key, options):
        try:
            current = str(self.get_setting(key, options[0] if options else "") or "")
        except Exception:
            current = options[0] if options else ""
        try:
            return max(0, options.index(current))
        except Exception:
            return 0

    def _assist_native_available(self):
        try:
            TLRPC = find_class("org.telegram.tgnet.TLRPC")
            ConnectionsManager = find_class("org.telegram.tgnet.ConnectionsManager")
            RequestDelegate = find_class("org.telegram.tgnet.RequestDelegate")
            return bool(TLRPC is not None and ConnectionsManager is not None and RequestDelegate is not None)
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _assist_using_native_provider(self):
        try:
            cfg = self._resolve_assist_ai_config()
            return str(cfg.get("provider") or "") == "native"
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _resolve_assist_ai_config(self):
        try:
            prov_idx = self._assist_provider_idx()
            if prov_idx == 0:
                return {
                    "provider": "custom",
                    "base": str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_custom_url", "") or "").strip().rstrip("/"),
                    "model": str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_custom_model", "") or "").strip(),
                    "api_key": str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_custom_key", "") or "").strip(),
                    "prompt_capable": True,
                    "api_key_optional": False,
                }
            if prov_idx == 1:
                api_key = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_gemini_key", "") or "").strip()
                model = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_gemini_model", self._assist_gemini_models()[0]) or "").strip()
                return {
                    "provider": "gemini",
                    "base": "https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models",
                    "model": model,
                    "api_key": api_key,
                }
            if prov_idx == 2:
                api_key = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_openrouter_key", "") or "").strip()
                model = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_openrouter_model", self._assist_openrouter_models()[0]) or "").strip()
                return {
                    "provider": "openrouter",
                    "base": "https://openrouter.ai/api/v1",
                    "model": model,
                    "api_key": api_key,
                }
            if prov_idx == 3:
                api_key = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_cerebras_key", "") or "").strip()
                model = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_cerebras_model", self._assist_cerebras_models()[0]) or "").strip()
                return {
                    "provider": "cerebras",
                    "base": "https://api.cerebras.ai/v1",
                    "model": model,
                    "api_key": api_key,
                    "prompt_capable": True,
                    "api_key_optional": False,
                }
            if prov_idx == 4:
                api_key = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_llm7_key", "") or "").strip()
                model = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_llm7_model", self._assist_llm7_models()[0]) or "").strip()
                return {
                    "provider": "llm7",
                    "base": "https://api.llm7.io/v1",
                    "model": model,
                    "api_key": api_key,
                    "prompt_capable": True,
                    "api_key_optional": True,
                }
            if prov_idx == 5:
                api_key = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_onlysq_key", "") or "").strip()
                model = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_onlysq_model", self._assist_onlysq_models()[0]) or "").strip()
                return {
                    "provider": "onlysq",
                    "base": "https://api.onlysq.ru/ai/openai",
                    "model": model,
                    "api_key": api_key,
                    "prompt_capable": True,
                    "api_key_optional": False,
                }
            return {"provider": "custom", "base": "", "model": "", "api_key": ""}
        except Exception:
            return {"provider": "custom", "base": "", "model": "", "api_key": ""}

    def _is_assist_ai_configured(self):
        try:
            cfg = self._resolve_assist_ai_config()
            if str(cfg.get("provider") or "") == "native":
                return bool(self._assist_native_available())
            if not (str(cfg.get("base") or "").strip() and str(cfg.get("model") or "").strip()):
                return False
            if bool(cfg.get("api_key_optional")):
                return True
            return bool(str(cfg.get("api_key") or "").strip())
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _extract_protected_names(self, text):
        try:
            src = str(text or "")
            if not src:
                return []
            found = []
            seen = set()
            patterns = [
                r"@\w+",
                r"(?:^|[\s(\"\'])(([A-ZÀ-ÖØ-Þ][\wÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ'._-]{1,}))",
                r"(?:^|[\s(\"\'])(([A-Za-zÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ]+(?:[._][A-Za-zÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ]+)+))",
            ]
            for pat in patterns:
                for m in re.finditer(pat, src, flags=re.UNICODE):
                    token = ""
                    try:
                        token = str(m.group(1) if m.lastindex else m.group(0))
                    except Exception:
                        token = str(m.group(0))
                    token = token.strip().strip("()[]{}<>.,;:!?\"'")
                    if len(token) < 2:
                        continue
                    key = token.casefold()
                    if key in seen:
                        continue
                    seen.add(key)
                    found.append(token)
            return found[:12]
        except Exception:
            return []

    def _split_nonspace_tokens(self, text):
        try:
            return re.findall(r"\S+", str(text or ""), flags=re.UNICODE)
        except Exception:
            return []

    def _clean_outer_token(self, token):
        try:
            return str(token or "").strip().strip("()[]{}<>.,;:!?\"'“”‘’")
        except Exception:
            return str(token or "")

    def _is_protected_name_token(self, token):
        try:
            base = self._clean_outer_token(token)
            if not base or len(base) < 2:
                return False
            if re.match(r"^@\w+$", base, flags=re.UNICODE):
                return True
            if re.match(r"^[A-ZÀ-ÖØ-Þ][\wÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ'._-]+$", base, flags=re.UNICODE):
                return True
            if re.match(r"^[A-Za-zÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ]+(?:[._][A-Za-zÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ]+)+$", base, flags=re.UNICODE):
                return True
            return False
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _looks_like_common_sentence_word(self, token):
        try:
            base = self._clean_outer_token(token)
            if not base:
                return False
            common_words = {
                "vamos", "vamoss", "oi", "ola", "olá", "hello", "hi", "hey", "testar", "testen",
                "test", "please", "por", "favor", "bom", "boa", "boa", "good", "morning",
                "afternoon", "night", "sim", "não", "nao", "yes", "no", "ok", "okay", "então",
                "entao", "agora", "depois", "hoje", "amanhã", "amanha", "ontem", "quero",
                "preciso", "acho", "isso", "essa", "esse", "vou", "fazer", "usar", "teste"
            }
            return base.casefold() in common_words
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _protected_name_spans(self, text):
        try:
            tokens = self._split_nonspace_tokens(text)
            spans = []
            i = 0
            while i < len(tokens):
                if not self._is_protected_name_token(tokens[i]):
                    i += 1
                    continue
                start = i
                parts = [self._clean_outer_token(tokens[i])]
                i += 1
                while i < len(tokens) and self._is_protected_name_token(tokens[i]):
                    parts.append(self._clean_outer_token(tokens[i]))
                    i += 1
                phrase = " ".join([p for p in parts if p])
                if start == 0 and len(parts) == 1 and self._looks_like_common_sentence_word(phrase):
                    continue
                if phrase:
                    spans.append((start, len(parts), phrase))
            return spans
        except Exception:
            return []

    def _preserve_protected_names_in_output(self, original_text, output_text):
        try:
            out_tokens = self._split_nonspace_tokens(output_text)
            orig_tokens = self._split_nonspace_tokens(original_text)
            if not out_tokens or not orig_tokens:
                return str(output_text or "").strip()
            spans = self._protected_name_spans(original_text)
            if not spans:
                return str(output_text or "").strip()
            patched = list(out_tokens)
            offset = 0
            total_orig = max(1, len(orig_tokens))
            for start, span_len, phrase in spans:
                phrase_tokens = phrase.split()
                if not phrase_tokens:
                    continue
                if start <= 0:
                    out_start = 0
                elif (start + span_len) >= len(orig_tokens):
                    out_start = max(0, len(patched) - max(1, span_len))
                else:
                    out_start = int(round((float(start) / float(total_orig)) * max(1, len(patched))))
                    out_start = max(0, min(len(patched), out_start + offset))
                out_end = max(out_start, min(len(patched), out_start + max(1, span_len)))
                patched[out_start:out_end] = phrase_tokens
                offset += len(phrase_tokens) - max(1, out_end - out_start)
            return " ".join([str(x) for x in patched if str(x).strip()]).strip()
        except Exception:
            return str(output_text or "").strip()

    def _normalize_assist_output(self, text, selected_mode):
        try:
            out = str(text or "").strip()
            if not out:
                return out
            if str(selected_mode or "").strip().lower() != "custom":
                out = re.sub(r"\s*[—–]+\s*", ", ", out)
                out = re.sub(r"\s+-\s+", ", ", out)
                out = re.sub(r",\s*,+", ", ", out)
                out = re.sub(r"\s{2,}", " ", out).strip()
            return out
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "").strip()

    def _assist_has_telegram_formatting(self, text):
        try:
            t = str(text or "")
            if not t:
                return False
            patterns = [
                r"\*[^*\n]+\*",
                r"_[^_\n]+_",
                r"~[^~\n]+~",
                r"\|\|[^|\n]+\|\|",
                r"`[^`\n]+`",
                r"\[[^\]]+\]\([^)]+\)",
            ]
            return any(re.search(pat, t) for pat in patterns)
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _is_emoji_char(self, ch):
        try:
            if not ch:
                return False
            cp = ord(str(ch)[0])
            if cp in (0xFE0F, 0x200D):
                return True
            return (
                0x1F300 <= cp <= 0x1FAFF or
                0x2600 <= cp <= 0x27BF or
                0x2300 <= cp <= 0x23FF
            )
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _count_emojis(self, text):
        try:
            return sum(1 for ch in str(text or "") if self._is_emoji_char(ch))
        except Exception:
            return 0

    def _looks_like_over_aggressive_correction(self, original_text, corrected_text):
        try:
            src = str(original_text or "").strip()
            out = str(corrected_text or "").strip()
            if not src or not out:
                return True
            src_norm = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", src).strip().casefold()
            out_norm = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", out).strip().casefold()
            if src_norm == out_norm:
                return False
            if len(out_norm) < max(1, int(len(src_norm) * 0.82)):
                return True
            src_words = len(re.findall(r"\S+", src_norm))
            out_words = len(re.findall(r"\S+", out_norm))
            if out_words < max(1, int(src_words * 0.8)):
                return True
            return False
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _set_assist_result_text(self, view, value):
        try:
            text_value = str(value or "").strip()
            if not text_value:
                text_value = self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty")
            if self._count_emojis(text_value) > 0:
                try:
                    view.setText(text_value)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                return
            ssb = SpannableStringBuilder(text_value)
            start = None
            for idx, ch in enumerate(text_value):
                if self._is_emoji_char(ch):
                    if start is not None and idx > start:
                        ssb.setSpan(StyleSpan(Typeface.ITALIC), start, idx, Spanned.SPAN_EXCLUSIVE_EXCLUSIVE)
                        start = None
                else:
                    if start is None:
                        start = idx
            if start is not None and len(text_value) > start:
                ssb.setSpan(StyleSpan(Typeface.ITALIC), start, len(text_value), Spanned.SPAN_EXCLUSIVE_EXCLUSIVE)
            view.setText(ssb)
        except Exception:
            try:
                view.setText(str(value or ""))
            except Exception:
                pass

    def _assist_preview_limit(self):
        return 220

    def _assist_word_count(self, text):
        try:
            return len(re.findall(r"\S+", str(text or ""), flags=re.UNICODE))
        except Exception:
            return 0

    def _truncate_assist_preview(self, text):
        try:
            full = str(text or "").strip()
            limit = int(self._assist_preview_limit())
            if len(full) <= limit:
                return full, False
            cut = full[:limit]
            last_space = cut.rfind(" ")
            if last_space >= max(40, int(limit * 0.55)):
                cut = cut[:last_space]
            return (str(cut).rstrip(" ,;:") + "…").strip(), True
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "").strip(), False

    def _ensure_emojify_output(self, text, selected_mode=None):
        try:
            out = str(text or "").strip()
            return out
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "").strip()

    def _normalize_assist_output(self, text, selected_mode):
        try:
            out = str(text or "").strip()
            if not out:
                return out
            if str(selected_mode or "").strip().lower() != "custom":
                normalized_lines = []
                for line in re.split(r"(\n+)", out):
                    if not line:
                        continue
                    if "\n" in line:
                        normalized_lines.append(line)
                        continue
                    clean = str(line)
                    clean = re.sub(r"\s*[—–]+\s*", ", ", clean)
                    clean = re.sub(r"\s+-\s+", ", ", clean)
                    clean = re.sub(r",\s*,+", ", ", clean)
                    clean = re.sub(r"[ \t]{2,}", " ", clean).strip()
                    normalized_lines.append(clean)
                out = "".join(normalized_lines)
                out = re.sub(r"\n{3,}", "\n\n", out).strip()
            return out
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "").strip()

    def _is_assist_transient_text(self, text):
        try:
            value = str(text or "").strip()
            if not value:
                return True
            markers = {
                str(self._tr("ai_sheet_loading") or "").strip(),
                str(self._tr("ai_sheet_generating") or "").strip(),
                str(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty") or "").strip(),
            }
            return value in {m for m in markers if m}
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _should_show_expand_chip(self, text):
        try:
            full = str(text or "").strip()
            if not full or self._is_assist_transient_text(full):
                return False
            limit = int(self._assist_preview_limit())
            words = int(self._assist_word_count(full))
            if len(full) > limit:
                return True
            if "\n" in full and len(full) >= max(120, int(limit * 0.55)):
                return True
            if words >= 28:
                return True
            if len(full) <= limit:
                return False
            return True
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _truncate_assist_preview(self, text):
        try:
            full = str(text or "").strip()
            limit = int(self._assist_preview_limit())
            if len(full) <= limit or not self._should_show_expand_chip(full):
                return full, False
            cut = full[:limit]
            last_space = cut.rfind(" ")
            if last_space >= max(40, int(limit * 0.55)):
                cut = cut[:last_space]
            return (str(cut).rstrip(" ,;:") + "…").strip(), True
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "").strip(), False

    def _emojis_are_only_at_the_end(self, text):
        try:
            value = str(text or "")
            if self._count_emojis(value) <= 0:
                return False
            emoji_positions = [idx for idx, ch in enumerate(value) if self._is_emoji_char(ch)]
            if not emoji_positions:
                return False
            cutoff = int(len(value) * 0.72)
            if all(pos >= cutoff for pos in emoji_positions):
                return True
            tail = re.sub(r"[\s\.\,\!\?\;\:\)\]\}]+$", "", value)
            tail_match = re.search(r"([\U0001F300-\U0001FAFF\u2600-\u27BF\u2300-\u23FF\uFE0F\u200D\s]+)$", tail)
            return bool(tail_match and tail_match.start() >= int(len(value) * 0.68))
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _has_broken_emoji_glyphs(self, text):
        try:
            value = str(text or "")
            broken_tokens = ["ï¿½", "Ã¯Â¿Â½", "ï¿½ï¿½", "\ufffd"]
            return any(tok in value for tok in broken_tokens)
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _emojis_are_poorly_clustered(self, text):
        try:
            value = str(text or "")
            emoji_positions = [idx for idx, ch in enumerate(value) if self._is_emoji_char(ch)]
            if len(emoji_positions) <= 1:
                return False
            spread = max(emoji_positions) - min(emoji_positions)
            if spread <= 4:
                return True
            middle = value[min(emoji_positions):max(emoji_positions) + 1]
            non_emoji_core = "".join(ch for ch in middle if not self._is_emoji_char(ch)).strip()
            return len(non_emoji_core) <= 2
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _normalize_assist_output(self, text, selected_mode):
        try:
            out = str(text or "").strip()
            if not out:
                return out
            out = out.replace("\uFFFD", "")
            out = out.replace("ï¿½ï¿½", "")
            out = out.replace("…", "…")
            out = out.replace("…", "…")
            if str(selected_mode or "").strip().lower() != "custom":
                normalized_lines = []
                for line in re.split(r"(\n+)", out):
                    if not line:
                        continue
                    if "\n" in line:
                        normalized_lines.append(line)
                        continue
                    clean = str(line)
                    clean = clean.replace("—", ", ")
                    clean = clean.replace("–", ", ")
                    clean = clean.replace("―", ", ")
                    clean = re.sub(r"\s*[—–]+\s*", ", ", clean)
                    clean = re.sub(r"\s+-\s+", ", ", clean)
                    clean = re.sub(r",\s*,+", ", ", clean)
                    clean = re.sub(r"[ \t]{2,}", " ", clean).strip()
                    normalized_lines.append(clean)
                out = "".join(normalized_lines)
                out = re.sub(r"\n{3,}", "\n\n", out).strip()
            return out
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "").strip()

    def _truncate_assist_preview(self, text):
        try:
            full = str(text or "").strip()
            limit = int(self._assist_preview_limit())
            if len(full) <= limit or not self._should_show_expand_chip(full):
                return full, False
            cut = full[:limit]
            last_space = cut.rfind(" ")
            if last_space >= max(40, int(limit * 0.55)):
                cut = cut[:last_space]
            return (str(cut).rstrip(" ,;:") + "…").strip(), True
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "").strip(), False

    def _normalize_assist_output(self, text, selected_mode):
        try:
            out = str(text or "").strip()
            if not out:
                return out
            out = out.replace("\uFFFD", "")
            out = out.replace("�", "")
            out = out.replace("��", "")
            out = out.replace("ï¿½ï¿½", "")
            out = out.replace("…", "…")
            out = out.replace("…", "…")
            out = out.replace("…", "…")
            if str(selected_mode or "").strip().lower() != "custom":
                normalized_lines = []
                for line in re.split(r"(\n+)", out):
                    if not line:
                        continue
                    if "\n" in line:
                        normalized_lines.append(line)
                        continue
                    clean = str(line)
                    for bad_dash in ("—", "–", "―", "—", "–", "―"):
                        clean = clean.replace(bad_dash, ", ")
                    clean = re.sub(r"\s+-\s+", ", ", clean)
                    clean = re.sub(r",\s*,+", ", ", clean)
                    clean = re.sub(r"[ \t]{2,}", " ", clean).strip()
                    normalized_lines.append(clean)
                out = "".join(normalized_lines)
                out = re.sub(r"\n{3,}", "\n\n", out).strip()
            return out
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "").strip()

    def _truncate_assist_preview(self, text):
        try:
            full = str(text or "").strip()
            limit = int(self._assist_preview_limit())
            if len(full) <= limit or not self._should_show_expand_chip(full):
                return full, False
            cut = full[:limit]
            last_space = cut.rfind(" ")
            if last_space >= max(40, int(limit * 0.55)):
                cut = cut[:last_space]
            return (str(cut).rstrip(" ,;:") + "…").strip(), True
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "").strip(), False

    def _normalize_assist_output(self, text, selected_mode):
        try:
            out = str(text or "").strip()
            if not out:
                return out
            for bad in ("\uFFFD", "�", "��", "��"):
                out = out.replace(bad, "")
            for bad_ellipsis in ("…", "…", "…", "…"):
                out = out.replace(bad_ellipsis, "…")
            if str(selected_mode or "").strip().lower() != "custom":
                normalized_lines = []
                for line in re.split(r"(\n+)", out):
                    if not line:
                        continue
                    if "\n" in line:
                        normalized_lines.append(line)
                        continue
                    clean = str(line)
                    for bad_dash in ("—", "–", "―", "—", "–", "―", "—", "–", "―"):
                        clean = clean.replace(bad_dash, ", ")
                    clean = re.sub(r"\s+-\s+", ", ", clean)
                    clean = re.sub(r",\s*,+", ", ", clean)
                    clean = re.sub(r"[ \t]{2,}", " ", clean).strip()
                    normalized_lines.append(clean)
                out = "".join(normalized_lines)
                out = re.sub(r"\n{3,}", "\n\n", out).strip()
            return out
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "").strip()

    def _truncate_assist_preview(self, text):
        try:
            full = str(text or "").strip()
            limit = int(self._assist_preview_limit())
            if len(full) <= limit or not self._should_show_expand_chip(full):
                return full, False
            cut = full[:limit]
            last_space = cut.rfind(" ")
            if last_space >= max(40, int(limit * 0.55)):
                cut = cut[:last_space]
            return (str(cut).rstrip(" ,;:") + "…").strip(), True
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "").strip(), False

    def _looks_like_effective_summary(self, source_text, summary_text):
        try:
            src = str(source_text or "").strip()
            out = str(summary_text or "").strip()
            if not src or not out:
                return False
            src_norm = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", src).strip().casefold()
            out_norm = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", out).strip().casefold()
            if src_norm == out_norm:
                return False
            if len(out_norm) >= max(1, int(len(src_norm) * 0.94)):
                return False
            return True
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _fallback_summary_text(self, text):
        try:
            src = str(text or "").strip()
            if not src:
                return src
            sentences = re.split(r"(?<=[\.\!\?…])\s+", src)
            picked = []
            total = 0
            target = max(80, int(len(src) * 0.6))
            for sent in sentences:
                piece = str(sent or "").strip()
                if not piece:
                    continue
                picked.append(piece)
                total += len(piece) + 1
                if total >= target:
                    break
            out = " ".join(picked).strip()
            if not out:
                out = src
            if len(out) >= len(src):
                words = re.findall(r"\S+", src, flags=re.UNICODE)
                keep = max(8, int(len(words) * 0.65))
                out = " ".join(words[:keep]).strip()
                if keep < len(words):
                    out = out.rstrip(" ,;:") + "…"
            return out.strip()
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "").strip()

    def _native_local_mode_rewrite(self, text, mode_key=None):
        try:
            out = str(text or "").strip()
            mode = str(mode_key or "").strip().lower()
            if not out:
                return out
            def _capitalize_sentences(src):
                try:
                    parts = re.split(r"([.!?\u2026]+\s*)", str(src or "").strip(), flags=re.UNICODE)
                    built = []
                    for idx in range(0, len(parts), 2):
                        body = str(parts[idx] or "").strip()
                        tail = str(parts[idx + 1] or "") if idx + 1 < len(parts) else ""
                        if body:
                            body = body[:1].upper() + body[1:]
                        built.append((body + tail).strip())
                    return " ".join([x for x in built if str(x or "").strip()]).strip()
                except Exception:
                    return str(src or "").strip()
            def _replace_map(src, pairs):
                current = str(src or "")
                for old, new in pairs:
                    try:
                        current = re.sub(old, new, current, flags=re.IGNORECASE | re.UNICODE)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                return current
            out = re.sub(r"\s{2,}", " ", out).strip()
            if mode == "short":
                compact = self._fallback_summary_text(out)
                if compact:
                    out = compact
                words = re.findall(r"\S+", out, flags=re.UNICODE)
                if len(words) > 14:
                    out = " ".join(words[:14]).strip()
                out = re.sub(r"\b(please|por favor|пожалуйста)\b", "", out, flags=re.IGNORECASE | re.UNICODE)
                out = re.sub(r"\b(i think|acho que|мне кажется|maybe|talvez|возможно)\b", "", out, flags=re.IGNORECASE | re.UNICODE)
                out = re.sub(r"\s{2,}", " ", out).strip(" ,;:")
                if out and out[-1] not in ".!?\u2026":
                    out += "\u2026" if len(words) > 14 else "."
            elif mode == "clear":
                out = re.sub(r"\s*[,;:]\s*", ". ", out)
                out = re.sub(r"\.\s*\.", ". ", out)
                out = re.sub(r"\s{2,}", " ", out).strip()
                out = _capitalize_sentences(out)
            elif mode == "formal":
                out = _replace_map(out, [
                    (r"\b(can't)\b", "cannot"),
                    (r"\b(won't)\b", "will not"),
                    (r"\b(i'm)\b", "I am"),
                    (r"\b(it's)\b", "it is"),
                    (r"\b(don't)\b", "do not"),
                    (r"\b(vc)\b", "você"),
                    (r"\b(pra)\b", "para"),
                    (r"\b(ta|tá)\b", "está"),
                    (r"\b(tb|tbm)\b", "também"),
                    (r"\b(щас)\b", "сейчас"),
                    (r"\b(пж)\b", "пожалуйста"),
                ])
                out = re.sub(r"[!]{2,}", "!", out).strip()
                out = re.sub(r"\s*-\s*", " - ", out)
                out = _capitalize_sentences(out)
                if self._assist_word_count(out) < 9:
                    out = re.sub(r"^\s*(please note[:,]?\s*)?", "", out, flags=re.IGNORECASE | re.UNICODE)
                    out = "Please, " + out[:1].lower() + out[1:] if out else out
                if out and out[-1] not in ".!?…":
                    out += "."
            elif mode == "bruto":
                out = _replace_map(out, [
                    (r"\b(please|por favor|пожалуйста)\b", ""),
                    (r"\b(i think|acho que|мне кажется)\b", ""),
                    (r"\b(maybe|talvez|может быть)\b", ""),
                    (r"\b(just)\b", ""),
                    (r"\b(kind of|sort of)\b", ""),
                ])
                out = re.sub(r"\s{2,}", " ", out).strip()
                out = re.sub(r"[.]{2,}", ".", out)
                out = re.sub(r"\s*[,;:]\s*", ". ", out).strip()
                pieces = [p.strip() for p in re.split(r"(?<=[.!?\u2026])\s+", out, flags=re.UNICODE) if str(p or "").strip()]
                if len(pieces) > 1:
                    out = " ".join(pieces[:2]).strip()
                if len(out) > 180:
                    compact = self._fallback_summary_text(out)
                    if compact:
                        out = compact
                out = _capitalize_sentences(out)
                out = re.sub(r"[!]{2,}", "!", out).strip()
                if out.endswith("?"):
                    out = out[:-1].rstrip() + "."
            return self._normalize_assist_output(out, mode)
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "").strip()

    def _native_local_emojify(self, text, mode_key=None):
        try:
            out = str(text or "").strip()
            if not out:
                return out
            if self._count_emojis(out) > 0:
                return out
            low = out.casefold()
            picks = []
            if "?" in out:
                picks.append("🤔")
            if "!" in out:
                picks.append("✨")
            keyword_map = [
                (("thank", "thanks", "obrigad", "gracias", "спасибо"), "🙏"),
                (("love", "amor", "серд", "люб"), "❤️"),
                (("music", "song", "audio", "музык", "пес"), "🎵"),
                (("bug", "error", "issue", "problem", "ошиб", "проблем"), "🛠️"),
                (("idea", "tip", "hint", "совет", "иде"), "💡"),
            ]
            for words, emoji in keyword_map:
                if any(w in low for w in words):
                    picks.append(emoji)
            if not picks:
                picks.append({
                    "formal": "✨",
                    "short": "⚡",
                    "natural": "😊",
                    "clear": "💡",
                    "bruto": "🔥",
                }.get(str(mode_key or "").strip().lower(), "✨"))
            deduped = []
            seen = set()
            for emoji in picks:
                if emoji in seen:
                    continue
                seen.add(emoji)
                deduped.append(emoji)
            picks = deduped[:2]
            return f"{out} {' '.join(picks)}".strip() if picks else out
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "").strip()

    def _show_assist_expanded_sheet(self, fragment, full_text, target_lang):
        try:
            ctx = fragment.getParentActivity() if fragment and fragment.getParentActivity() else ApplicationLoader.applicationContext
            if ctx is None:
                return
            full_value = str(full_text or "").strip()
            meta_template = str(self._tr("ai_sheet_expanded_meta") or "{chars} chars | {words} words")
            try:
                meta_text = meta_template.format(chars=len(full_value), words=self._assist_word_count(full_value))
            except Exception:
                meta_text = f"{len(full_value)} | {self._assist_word_count(full_value)}"
            primary_text = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteBlackText))
            secondary_text = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteGrayText))
            bg_color = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_dialogBackground))
            card_color = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhite))
            stroke_color = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteGrayText3))
            sheet = BottomSheet(ctx, False)
            root = LinearLayout(ctx)
            root.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            root.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18))
            bg = GradientDrawable()
            bg.setColor(bg_color)
            bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(22)))
            root.setBackground(bg)
            title = TextView(ctx)
            title.setText(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation"))
            title.setTextColor(primary_text)
            title.setTextSize(1, 20)
            try:
                title.setTypeface(title.getTypeface(), 1)
            except Exception:
                pass
            title.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
            root.addView(title, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            meta = TextView(ctx)
            meta.setText(meta_text)
            meta.setTextColor(secondary_text)
            meta.setTextSize(1, 12)
            meta.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
            lp_meta = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_meta.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(6)
            root.addView(meta, lp_meta)
            card = LinearLayout(ctx)
            card.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            card.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(16))
            card_bg = GradientDrawable()
            card_bg.setColor(card_color)
            card_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
            try:
                card_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), stroke_color)
            except Exception:
                pass
            card.setBackground(card_bg)
            body = TextView(ctx)
            body.setText(full_value)
            body.setTextColor(primary_text)
            body.setTextSize(1, 16)
            body.setLineSpacing(0.0, 1.1)
            card.addView(body, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            lp_card = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_card.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(14)
            root.addView(card, lp_card)
            sheet.setCustomView(root)
            try:
                run_on_ui_thread(sheet.show)
            except Exception:
                sheet.show()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"show assist expanded fail: {e}")

    # Override the earlier lightweight heuristics with a stricter rule:
    # only preserve clear identifiers, @usernames and multi-word proper names.
    def _extract_protected_names(self, text):
        try:
            src = str(text or "")
            if not src:
                return []
            found = []
            seen = set()
            patterns = [
                r"@\w+",
                r"(?:^|[\s(\"\'])(([A-Za-zÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ]+(?:[._][A-Za-zÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ]+)+))",
                r"(?:^|[\s(\"\'])(([A-ZÀ-ÖØ-Þ][\wÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ'._-]{1,}\s+[A-ZÀ-ÖØ-Þ][\wÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ'._-]{1,}))",
            ]
            for pat in patterns:
                for m in re.finditer(pat, src, flags=re.UNICODE):
                    try:
                        token = str(m.group(1) if m.lastindex else m.group(0))
                    except Exception:
                        token = str(m.group(0))
                    token = self._clean_outer_token(token)
                    if len(token) < 2:
                        continue
                    key = token.casefold()
                    if key in seen:
                        continue
                    seen.add(key)
                    found.append(token)
            return found[:12]
        except Exception:
            return []

    def _is_protected_name_token(self, token):
        try:
            base = self._clean_outer_token(token)
            if not base or len(base) < 2:
                return False
            if re.match(r"^@\w+$", base, flags=re.UNICODE):
                return True
            if re.match(r"^[A-Za-zÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ]+(?:[._][A-Za-zÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ]+)+$", base, flags=re.UNICODE):
                return True
            if " " in base:
                return True
            return False
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _protected_name_spans(self, text):
        try:
            src = str(text or "")
            if not src:
                return []
            tokens = self._split_nonspace_tokens(src)
            spans = []
            i = 0
            while i < len(tokens):
                tok = self._clean_outer_token(tokens[i])
                if re.match(r"^@\w+$", tok, flags=re.UNICODE):
                    spans.append((i, 1, tok))
                    i += 1
                    continue
                if re.match(r"^[A-Za-zÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ]+(?:[._][A-Za-zÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ]+)+$", tok, flags=re.UNICODE):
                    spans.append((i, 1, tok))
                    i += 1
                    continue
                if re.match(r"^[A-ZÀ-ÖØ-Þ][\wÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ'._-]{1,}$", tok, flags=re.UNICODE):
                    if i + 1 < len(tokens):
                        nxt = self._clean_outer_token(tokens[i + 1])
                        if re.match(r"^[A-ZÀ-ÖØ-Þ][\wÀ-ÖØ-öø-ÿ'._-]{1,}$", nxt, flags=re.UNICODE):
                            spans.append((i, 2, f"{tok} {nxt}"))
                            i += 2
                            continue
                i += 1
            return spans
        except Exception:
            return []

    def _should_show_assist_fab(self, text):
        try:
            if not self._assist_fab_enabled():
                return False
            t = str(text or "").strip()
            if not t:
                return False
            return self._count_compose_chars(t) > 0
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _is_assist_allowed_for_chat(self, fragment=None):
        try:
            if not bool(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_assist_enabled", False)):
                return False
        except Exception:
            return False
        did = 0
        try:
            did = int(self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=fragment) or 0)
        except Exception:
            did = 0
        if did == 0:
            return True
        try:
            cfg = self._chat_config(did)
            return bool(cfg.get("enabled", True))
        except Exception:
            return True

    def _is_live_preview_allowed_for_chat(self, fragment=None):
        try:
            if not bool(self.get_setting("tlite_live_preview_enabled", False)):
                return False
        except Exception:
            return False
        did = 0
        try:
            did = int(self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=fragment) or 0)
        except Exception:
            did = 0
        if did == 0:
            return True
        try:
            cfg = self._chat_config(did)
            return bool(cfg.get("enabled", True))
        except Exception:
            return True

    def _get_enter_view(self, fragment=None):
        try:
            target = fragment if fragment is not None else self._chat_fragment_ref
            if target is None:
                return None
            return _get_private_field_silent(target, "chatActivityEnterView")
        except Exception:
            return None

    def _get_compose_text(self, fragment=None):
        try:
            enter_view = self._get_enter_view(fragment)
            if enter_view is None:
                return ""
            try:
                edit = enter_view.getEditField()
                if edit is not None:
                    return str(edit.getText() or "")
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                return str(enter_view.getFieldText() or "")
            except Exception:
                return ""
        except Exception:
            return ""

    def _get_compose_markdown(self, fragment=None):
        try:
            enter_view = self._get_enter_view(fragment)
            if enter_view is None:
                return ""
            edit = None
            try:
                edit = enter_view.getEditField()
            except Exception:
                edit = None
            if edit is None:
                return self._get_compose_text(fragment)
            editable = edit.getText()
            text = str(editable or "")
            if not text:
                return text
            if editable is None or not hasattr(editable, "getSpans"):
                return text
            try:
                obj_cls = JClass.forName("java.lang.Object")
                spans = list(editable.getSpans(0, len(text), obj_cls) or [])
            except Exception:
                spans = []
            if not spans:
                return text
            out = list(text)
            inserts = []
            for sp in spans:
                try:
                    start = int(editable.getSpanStart(sp))
                    end = int(editable.getSpanEnd(sp))
                    if start < 0 or end <= start or end > len(out):
                        continue
                    name = str(sp.getClass().getName() or "")
                    open_mark = close_mark = None
                    if "Bold" in name:
                        open_mark = close_mark = "*"
                    elif "Italic" in name:
                        open_mark = close_mark = "_"
                    elif "Underline" in name:
                        open_mark = close_mark = "__"
                    elif "Strike" in name or "Strikethrough" in name:
                        open_mark = close_mark = "~"
                    elif "Spoiler" in name:
                        open_mark = close_mark = "||"
                    elif "Code" in name or "Mono" in name or "TypefaceSpan" in name:
                        open_mark = close_mark = "`"
                    if open_mark:
                        inserts.append((end, close_mark))
                        inserts.append((start, open_mark))
                except Exception:
                    pass
            for pos, mark in sorted(inserts, key=lambda x: x[0], reverse=True):
                try:
                    out.insert(int(pos), str(mark))
                except Exception:
                    pass
            return "".join(out)
        except Exception:
            return self._get_compose_text(fragment)

    def _prepare_assist_send_payload(self, text):
        try:
            final_text = str(text or "").strip()
            if not final_text:
                return None
            parsed_text, parsed_entities = self._parse_markdown_to_entities(final_text)
            return {
                "text": str(parsed_text or final_text),
                "entities": list(parsed_entities or []),
            }
        except Exception:
            return {"text": str(text or "").strip(), "entities": []}

    def _quick_assist_send(self, fragment):
        try:
            if fragment is None:
                return False
            if not self._is_assist_ai_configured():
                BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_missing_config"))
                return False
            source_plain_text = str(self._get_compose_text(fragment) or "").strip()
            source_text = str(self._get_compose_markdown(fragment) or source_plain_text or "").strip()
            if not self._assist_can_open_for_text(source_plain_text):
                BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("ai_sheet_need_words"))
                return False
            dst = str(self._assist_target_lang(fragment) or "en")
            pinned_mode = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_pinned_mode", "") or "").strip().lower()
            translated = self._translate_text(source_text, dst)
            translated = self._preserve_protected_names_in_output(source_text, translated)
            translated = self._normalize_assist_output(translated, None)
            if not translated:
                BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty"))
                return False
            improved = self._request_ai_correction(
                source_text,
                translated,
                pinned_mode or None,
                False,
                dst,
            )
            final_text = str(improved or translated or "").strip()
            if not final_text:
                BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty"))
                return False
            source_code = self._guess_source_lang_code(source_plain_text)
            source_label = self._live_preview_source_label(source_plain_text)
            target_label = self._lang_label_from_code(dst)
            meta = self._tr("live_preview_pair").format(str(source_label or ""), str(target_label or dst or "").strip())
            self._show_live_preview_sheet(fragment, {
                "source": source_text,
                "source_plain": source_plain_text,
                "source_code": str(source_code or ""),
                "source_label": str(source_label or ""),
                "target_lang": str(dst or ""),
                "target_label": str(target_label or dst or ""),
                "translated": final_text,
                "meta": meta,
                "allow_send": False,
                "allow_copy": True,
            })
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"quick assist preview fail: {e}")
            return False

    def _flash_assist_button_press(self, button):
        try:
            if button is None:
                return
            def _press_on():
                try:
                    button.setPressed(True)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    button.setScaleX(0.93)
                    button.setScaleY(0.93)
                    button.setAlpha(0.82)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            def _press_off():
                try:
                    button.setPressed(False)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    button.setScaleX(1.0)
                    button.setScaleY(1.0)
                    button.setAlpha(1.0)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            run_on_ui_thread(_press_on)
            try:
                threading.Timer(0.18, lambda: run_on_ui_thread(_press_off)).start()
            except Exception:
                run_on_ui_thread(_press_off)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _set_compose_text(self, fragment, text):
        try:
            enter_view = self._get_enter_view(fragment)
            if enter_view is None:
                return False
            value = str(text or "")
            try:
                enter_view.setFieldText(value)
            except Exception:
                try:
                    enter_view.setFieldText(value, False)
                except Exception:
                    try:
                        edit = enter_view.getEditField()
                        if edit is not None:
                            edit.setText(value)
                    except Exception:
                        return False
            try:
                edit = enter_view.getEditField()
                if edit is not None:
                    edit.setSelection(edit.getText().length())
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                self._refresh_compose_after_programmatic_text(fragment)
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._refresh_assist_button(fragment)
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"set compose text fail: {e}")
            return False

    def _refresh_compose_after_programmatic_text(self, fragment):
        try:
            enter_view = self._get_enter_view(fragment)
            if enter_view is None:
                return

            def _refresh_once():
                try:
                    if hasattr(enter_view, "checkSendButton"):
                        enter_view.checkSendButton(True)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    if hasattr(enter_view, "updateFieldHint"):
                        enter_view.updateFieldHint(True)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    edit = enter_view.getEditField()
                except Exception:
                    edit = None
                try:
                    if edit is not None:
                        try:
                            edit.setSelection(edit.getText().length())
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        try:
                            edit.requestLayout()
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        try:
                            edit.invalidate()
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                    for fname in ("messageEditTextContainer", "textFieldContainer", "sendButtonContainer", "topView", "messageContainer"):
                        try:
                            view = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, fname)
                        except Exception:
                            view = None
                        if view is None:
                            continue
                        try:
                            view.requestLayout()
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        try:
                            view.invalidate()
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                    try:
                        enter_view.requestLayout()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        enter_view.invalidate()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        frag_view = fragment.getFragmentView() if fragment is not None else None
                    except Exception:
                        frag_view = None
                    if frag_view is not None:
                        try:
                            frag_view.requestLayout()
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        try:
                            frag_view.invalidate()
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                    try:
                        self._position_compose_assist_button(fragment)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"compose refresh pass fail: {e}")

            run_on_ui_thread(_refresh_once)
            try:
                threading.Timer(0.06, lambda: run_on_ui_thread(_refresh_once)).start()
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                threading.Timer(0.18, lambda: run_on_ui_thread(_refresh_once)).start()
            except Exception:
                pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"refresh compose after programmatic text fail: {e}")

    def _post_send_compose_cleanup(self, fragment, sent_text=None):
        try:
            def _cleanup_once():
                try:
                    frag = fragment
                    if frag is None:
                        try:
                            frag = get_last_fragment()
                        except Exception:
                            frag = getattr(self, "_chat_fragment_ref", None)
                    if frag is None:
                        return
                    try:
                        sent_value = str(sent_text or "")
                    except Exception:
                        sent_value = ""
                    try:
                        current_text = str(self._get_compose_text(frag) or "")
                    except Exception:
                        current_text = ""
                    if sent_value and current_text == sent_value:
                        try:
                            self._set_compose_text(frag, "")
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                    if not current_text.strip():
                        try:
                            enter_view = self._get_enter_view(frag)
                        except Exception:
                            enter_view = None
                        if enter_view is not None:
                            try:
                                if hasattr(enter_view, "hideTopView"):
                                    enter_view.hideTopView(True)
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            try:
                                if hasattr(enter_view, "setReplyingMessageObject"):
                                    enter_view.setReplyingMessageObject(None, None)
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                    self._refresh_compose_after_programmatic_text(frag)
                    try:
                        self._refresh_assist_button(frag)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        self._attach_assist_fab(frag)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        if hasattr(frag, "updateVisibleRows"):
                            frag.updateVisibleRows()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        if hasattr(frag, "scrollToLastMessage"):
                            frag.scrollToLastMessage(False, False)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        chat_list = _get_private_field_silent(frag, "chatListView")
                    except Exception:
                        chat_list = None
                    if chat_list is not None:
                        try:
                            chat_list.invalidate()
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                    try:
                        chat_adapter = _get_private_field_silent(frag, "chatAdapter")
                    except Exception:
                        chat_adapter = None
                    if chat_adapter is not None:
                        try:
                            if hasattr(chat_adapter, "notifyDataSetChanged"):
                                chat_adapter.notifyDataSetChanged(False)
                        except Exception:
                            try:
                                chat_adapter.notifyDataSetChanged()
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"post send cleanup pass fail: {e}")

            run_on_ui_thread(_cleanup_once)
            for delay in (0.05, 0.15, 0.35, 0.65):
                try:
                    threading.Timer(delay, lambda: run_on_ui_thread(_cleanup_once)).start()
                except Exception:
                    pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"post send compose cleanup fail: {e}")

    def _cancel_live_preview_timer(self):
        try:
            timer = getattr(self, "_live_preview_timer", None)
            if timer is not None and hasattr(timer, "cancel"):
                timer.cancel()
        except Exception:
            pass
        self._live_preview_timer = None

    def _hide_live_preview_prompt(self):
        try:
            prompt = getattr(self, "_live_preview_prompt", None)
            if prompt is not None and prompt.getParent() is not None:
                prompt.getParent().removeView(prompt)
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            host = self._get_overlay_host(self._chat_fragment_ref)
            if host is not None and hasattr(host, "findViewWithTag"):
                while True:
                    old = host.findViewWithTag("__tlite_live_preview_prompt__")
                    if old is None:
                        break
                    try:
                        if old.getParent() is not None:
                            old.getParent().removeView(old)
                    except Exception:
                        break
        except Exception:
            pass
        self._live_preview_prompt = None
        self._live_preview_data = None

    def _get_overlay_host(self, fragment):
        try:
            if fragment is None:
                return None
            try:
                frag_view = fragment.getFragmentView() if hasattr(fragment, "getFragmentView") else None
                if frag_view is not None:
                    return frag_view
            except Exception:
                pass
            activity = None
            try:
                activity = fragment.getParentActivity()
            except Exception:
                activity = None
            if activity is not None:
                try:
                    root = activity.findViewById(16908290)
                    if root is not None:
                        return root
                except Exception:
                    pass
            return None
        except Exception:
            return None

    def _position_live_preview_prompt(self, fragment):
        try:
            prompt = getattr(self, "_live_preview_prompt", None)
            if fragment is None or prompt is None:
                return
            enter_view = self._get_enter_view(fragment)
            if enter_view is None:
                return
            target = None
            send_host = None
            try:
                target = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "textFieldContainer")
            except Exception:
                target = None
            if target is None:
                try:
                    target = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "messageEditTextContainer")
                except Exception:
                    target = None
            try:
                send_host = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "sendButtonContainer")
            except Exception:
                send_host = None
            root_host = None
            try:
                root_host = prompt.getParent()
            except Exception:
                root_host = None
            if target is None or root_host is None:
                return
            loc_target = [0, 0]
            loc_root = [0, 0]
            try:
                target.getLocationOnScreen(loc_target)
                root_host.getLocationOnScreen(loc_root)
            except Exception:
                return
            prompt.measure(
                View.MeasureSpec.makeMeasureSpec(min(int(root_host.getWidth() or AndroidUtilities.displaySize.x) - AndroidUtilities.dp(52), AndroidUtilities.dp(332)), View.MeasureSpec.AT_MOST),
                View.MeasureSpec.makeMeasureSpec(0, View.MeasureSpec.UNSPECIFIED),
            )
            prompt_w = int(prompt.getMeasuredWidth() or AndroidUtilities.dp(250))
            prompt_h = int(prompt.getMeasuredHeight() or AndroidUtilities.dp(58))
            target_w = int(target.getWidth() or 0)
            target_left = int(loc_target[0]) - int(loc_root[0])
            x = target_left + max(0, int((target_w - prompt_w) / 2))
            y = (int(loc_target[1]) - int(loc_root[1])) - prompt_h - AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
            min_y = AndroidUtilities.dp(72)
            if y < min_y:
                y = min_y
            prompt.setX(float(max(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), x)))
            prompt.setY(float(max(0, y)))
            prompt.bringToFront()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"position live preview prompt fail: {e}")

    def _show_live_preview_sheet(self, fragment, data):
        try:
            if fragment is None or not isinstance(data, dict):
                return
            activity = None
            try:
                activity = fragment.getParentActivity()
            except Exception:
                activity = None
            if activity is None:
                return
            ctx = activity
            is_dark = bool(Theme.isCurrentThemeDark())
            bg_color = _ji(0xFF1F2937) if is_dark else _ji(0xFFF7F8FC)
            card_color = _ji(0xFF233041) if is_dark else _ji(0xFFFFFFFF)
            primary_text = _ji(0xFFFFFFFF) if is_dark else _ji(0xFF1F2937)
            secondary_text = _ji(0xFF9CA3AF) if is_dark else _ji(0xFF64748B)
            stroke = _ji(0x22FFFFFF) if is_dark else _ji(0x160F172A)
            accent_text = _ji(0xFFFFFFFF)
            allow_send = bool(data.get("allow_send", True))
            allow_copy = bool(data.get("allow_copy", False))

            sheet = BottomSheet(ctx, False)
            outer = LinearLayout(ctx)

            outer.addView(subtitle, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            lp_row.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(14)
            outer.addView(row, lp_row)
            row.setVisibility(View.GONE)

            target_chip = LinearLayout(ctx)
            target_chip.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            target_chip.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            target_chip.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(8))

            target_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(16)))

            try:

            except Exception:

            target_chip.setBackground(target_bg)
            target_icon = ImageView(ctx)
            try:
                rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("msg_log", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                if rid:
                    target_icon.setImageResource(rid)

            target_chip.addView(target_text, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            target_chip.setVisibility(View.GONE)

            card = LinearLayout(ctx)
            card.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            card.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(16))
            card_bg = GradientDrawable()
            card_bg.setColor(card_color)
            card_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(22)))
            try:

            outer.addView(action_row, lp_actions)

            if allow_copy:
                copy_btn = LinearLayout(ctx)
                copy_btn.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
                copy_btn.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
                copy_btn.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(12))
                copy_bg = GradientDrawable()

                copy_bg.setColor(card_color)
                try:
                    copy_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), stroke)
                except Exception:
                    pass

                copy_icon = ImageView(ctx)

                copy_text = TextView(ctx)
                copy_text.setText(self._tr("live_preview_copy"))
                copy_text.setTextColor(primary_text)

                    copy_text.setTypeface(copy_text.getTypeface(), 1)

                    pass
                copy_btn.addView(copy_text, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

                class _CopyClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                    def onClick(self_obj, v):
                        try:
                            final_text = str((data or {}).get("translated") or "")
                            if not final_text:
                                return
                            clipboard = ctx.getSystemService("clipboard")
                            if clipboard is not None:
                                clipboard.setPrimaryClip(ClipData.newPlainText("translatica_preview", final_text))
                                BulletinHelper.show_success(self._tr("live_preview_copied"))
                        except Exception as e:
                            self._dlog(f"live preview copy fail: {e}")

                copy_btn.setOnClickListener(_CopyClick())
                lp_copy = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1.0)
                action_row.addView(copy_btn, lp_copy)

            if allow_send:
                send_btn = TextView(ctx)
                send_btn.setText(self._tr("live_preview_apply_send"))
                send_btn.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
                send_btn.setTextSize(1, 16)
                send_btn.setTextColor(accent_text)
                send_bg = GradientDrawable()
                send_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(24)))
                send_bg.setColor(_ji(0xFF3B82F6))
                send_btn.setBackground(self._ripple_bg(send_bg, 0x45FFFFFF))
                send_btn.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(14))

                class _ApplySendClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                    def onClick(self_obj, v):
                        try:
                            final_text = str((data or {}).get("translated") or "").strip()
                            if not final_text:
                                return
                            payload = self._prepare_assist_send_payload(final_text)
                            self._preview_pending_send = payload
                            self._set_compose_text(fragment, str((payload or {}).get("text") or final_text))
                            self._hide_live_preview_prompt()
                            try:
                                sheet.dismiss()
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            sent = self._trigger_compose_send(fragment)
                            if sent:
                                BulletinHelper.show_success(self._tr("ai_sheet_sent"))
                            else:
                                self._preview_pending_send = None
                                BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("ai_sheet_send_fail"))
                        except Exception as e:
                            self._preview_pending_send = None
                            self._dlog(f"live preview send fail: {e}")

                send_btn.setOnClickListener(_ApplySendClick())
                lp_send = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT if not allow_copy else 0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1.0 if allow_copy else 0.0)
                if allow_copy:
                    lp_send.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(10)
                action_row.addView(send_btn, lp_send)
            sheet.setCustomView(outer)
            try:
                self._hide_live_preview_prompt()
            except Exception:
                pass
            sheet.show()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"show live preview sheet fail: {e}")

    def _show_live_preview_prompt(self, fragment, data):
        try:
            if fragment is None or not isinstance(data, dict):
                return
            host = self._get_overlay_host(fragment)
            if host is None:
                return
            self._hide_live_preview_prompt()
            ctx = host.getContext()
            is_dark = bool(Theme.isCurrentThemeDark())
            card_color = _ji(0xFF223041) if is_dark else _ji(0xFFFFFFFF)
            primary_text = _ji(0xFFFFFFFF) if is_dark else _ji(0xFF0F172A)
            secondary_text = _ji(0xFFCBD5E1) if is_dark else _ji(0xFF64748B)
            stroke = _ji(0x22FFFFFF) if is_dark else _ji(0x160F172A)

            wrap = LinearLayout(ctx)
            wrap.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            wrap.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            wrap.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(12))
            try:
                wrap.setMinimumWidth(AndroidUtilities.dp(280))
            except Exception:
                pass
            bg = GradientDrawable()
            bg.setColor(card_color)
            bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(22)))
            try:
                bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), stroke)
            except Exception:
                pass
            wrap.setBackground(self._ripple_bg(bg))
            try:
                wrap.setTag("__tlite_live_preview_prompt__")
            except Exception:
                pass

            texts = LinearLayout(ctx)
            texts.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            title = TextView(ctx)
            title.setText(self._tr("live_preview_ready"))
            title.setTextColor(primary_text)
            title.setTextSize(1, 14)
            try:
                title.setTypeface(title.getTypeface(), 1)
            except Exception:
                pass
            texts.addView(title, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            body = TextView(ctx)
            body.setText(self._tr("live_preview_ready_desc"))
            body.setTextColor(secondary_text)
            body.setTextSize(1, 12)
            body.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(2), 0, 0)
            texts.addView(body, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            wrap.addView(texts, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1.0))

            preview_btn = TextView(ctx)
            preview_btn.setText(self._tr("live_preview_open"))
            preview_btn.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
            preview_btn.setTextColor(_ji(0xFFFFFFFF))
            preview_btn.setTextSize(1, 13)
            try:
                preview_btn.setTypeface(preview_btn.getTypeface(), 1)
            except Exception:
                pass
            preview_bg = GradientDrawable()
            preview_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
            preview_bg.setColor(_ji(0xFF3B82F6))
            preview_btn.setBackground(self._ripple_bg(preview_bg, 0x45FFFFFF))
            preview_btn.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
            lp_preview_btn = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_preview_btn.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(14)
            wrap.addView(preview_btn, lp_preview_btn)

            class _PreviewClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    self._show_live_preview_sheet(fragment, data)

            class _PreviewDismiss(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    self._hide_live_preview_prompt()

            preview_btn.setOnClickListener(_PreviewClick())
            wrap.setOnClickListener(_PreviewDismiss())

            host.addView(wrap, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(FrameLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, FrameLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            self._live_preview_prompt = wrap
            self._live_preview_data = dict(data)
            self._position_live_preview_prompt(fragment)
            self._dlog("live preview prompt shown")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"show live preview prompt fail: {e}")

    def _animate_live_preview_to_compose(self, fragment, final_text):
        try:
            final_value = str(final_text or "")
            if fragment is None or not final_value:
                self._dlog("live preview auto apply skipped: empty final text or fragment")
                return False
            self._live_preview_animating = True
            total = len(final_value)
            step = max(1, int(total / 24))
            self._dlog(f"live preview auto apply start | len={total} step={step}")

            def _finish():
                try:
                    self._set_compose_text(fragment, final_value)
                    self._preview_pending_send = self._prepare_assist_send_payload(final_value)
                    self._dlog(f"live preview auto apply finish | len={len(final_value)}")
                finally:
                    self._live_preview_animating = False

            def _tick(index_value):
                if not self._live_preview_animating:
                    return
                try:
                    idx = int(index_value)
                except Exception:
                    idx = total
                if idx >= total:
                    run_on_ui_thread(_finish)
                    return
                run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self._set_compose_text(fragment, final_value[:idx]))
                try:
                    threading.Timer(0.018, lambda: _tick(idx + step)).start()
                except Exception:
                    run_on_ui_thread(_finish)

            _tick(step)
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self._live_preview_animating = False
            self._dlog(f"animate live preview fail: {e}")
            return False

    def _handle_live_preview_result(self, fragment, nonce, source_text, source_plain_text, translated_text, target_lang):
        try:
            if int(nonce) != int(getattr(self, "_live_preview_generation", 0) or 0):
                self._dlog(f"live preview result ignored | stale nonce={nonce} current={getattr(self, '_live_preview_generation', 0)}")
                return
            translated_value = str(translated_text or "").strip()
            if not translated_value:
                self._dlog("live preview result ignored | empty translation")
                return
            source_label = self._live_preview_source_label(source_plain_text)
            if not source_label:
                try:
                    fallback_code = str(self._guess_source_lang_code(source_plain_text) or self._guess_source_lang_code(source_text) or "").strip()
                    if fallback_code:
                        source_label = self._lang_label_from_code(fallback_code)
                        self._dlog(f"live preview source fallback | code={fallback_code} label={source_label}")
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"live preview source fallback fail: {e}")
            target_label = self._lang_label_from_code(target_lang)
            meta = self._tr("live_preview_pair").format(source_label, target_label)
            data = {
                "source": str(source_text or ""),
                "source_plain": str(source_plain_text or ""),
                "source_label": source_label,
                "target_lang": str(target_lang or ""),
                "target_label": target_label,
                "translated": translated_value,
                "meta": meta,
            }
            self._dlog(f"live preview result show-preview | target={target_lang} len={len(translated_value)}")
            self._show_live_preview_prompt(fragment, data)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"handle live preview result fail: {e}")

    def _schedule_live_preview(self, fragment):
        try:
            self._cancel_live_preview_timer()
            if fragment is None or not self._live_preview_enabled():
                return
            source_plain_text = str(self._get_compose_text(fragment) or "").strip()
            source_text = str(self._get_compose_markdown(fragment) or source_plain_text or "").strip()
            if not source_plain_text or not source_text:
                return
            if not bool(self.get_setting("tlite_enabled", True)):
                return
            if not self._is_live_preview_allowed_for_chat(fragment):
                return
            delay_seconds = int(self._live_preview_delay_value())
            self._live_preview_generation = int(getattr(self, "_live_preview_generation", 0) or 0) + 1
            nonce = int(self._live_preview_generation)
            self._dlog(f"live preview scheduled | mode=preview delay={delay_seconds}s nonce={nonce} len={len(source_plain_text)}")

            def _worker():
                try:
                    translated = self._translate_text(source_text, str(self._assist_target_lang(fragment) or "en"))
                    translated = str(translated or "").strip()
                except Exception:
                    translated = ""
                self._dlog(f"live preview translated | nonce={nonce} len={len(translated)}")
