                run_on_ui_thread(lambda: self._handle_live_preview_result(
                    fragment,
                    nonce,
                    source_text,
                    source_plain_text,
                    translated,
                    str(self._assist_target_lang(fragment) or "en"),
                ))

            self._live_preview_timer = threading.Timer(float(delay_seconds), _worker)
            self._live_preview_timer.daemon = True
            self._live_preview_timer.start()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"schedule live preview fail: {e}")

    def _handle_live_preview_text_changed(self, fragment):
        try:
            current_text = str(self._get_compose_text(fragment) or "")
            pending = getattr(self, "_preview_pending_send", None)
            if pending and str((pending or {}).get("text") or "") != str(current_text or ""):
                self._preview_pending_send = None
            if bool(getattr(self, "_live_preview_animating", False)):
                return
            self._cancel_live_preview_timer()
            self._hide_live_preview_prompt()
            if str(current_text or "").strip():
                self._schedule_live_preview(fragment)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"live preview text changed fail: {e}")

    def _trigger_compose_send(self, fragment):
        try:
            enter_view = self._get_enter_view(fragment)
            if enter_view is None:
                return False
            for fname in ("sendButton", "audioVideoSendButton", "doneButton", "sendButtonContainer"):
                try:
                    view = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, fname)
                    if view is not None and hasattr(view, "performClick"):
                        if bool(view.performClick()):
                            return True
                        try:
                            view.callOnClick()
                            return True
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                except Exception:
                    pass
            for mname in ("sendMessage", "processSendingText", "checkRoundVideo", "doneEditingMessage"):
                try:
                    meth = enter_view.getClass().getDeclaredMethod(mname)
                    meth.setAccessible(True)
                    meth.invoke(enter_view)
                    return True
                except Exception:
                    pass
            return False
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"trigger compose send fail: {e}")
            return False

    def _build_assist_icon(self, ctx):
        icon = ImageView(ctx)
        loaded_custom = False
        try:
            if os.path.exists(ASSIST_ICON_CACHE_FILE):
                bmp = BitmapFactory.decodeFile(ASSIST_ICON_CACHE_FILE)
                if bmp:
                    icon.setImageBitmap(bmp)
                    loaded_custom = True
        except Exception:
            loaded_custom = False
        try:
            if not loaded_custom:
                rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("ai_chat_solar", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                if rid:
                    icon.setImageResource(rid)
                else:
                    rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("ai_chat_remix", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                    if rid:
                        icon.setImageResource(rid)
                    else:
                        rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("msg_translate", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                        if rid:
                            icon.setImageResource(rid)
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            icon.setScaleType(ImageView.ScaleType.CENTER_INSIDE)
        except Exception:
            pass
        if not loaded_custom:
            try:
                icon.setPadding(0, 0, 0, AndroidUtilities.dp(1))
            except Exception:
                pass
        return icon

    def _style_assist_chip(self, view, force_circle=False):
        try:
            if force_circle:
                bg = GradientDrawable(
                    GradientDrawable.Orientation.TL_BR,
                    [_ji(0xFF6C5CE7), _ji(0xFF3B82F6), _ji(0xFF00CEC9)]
                )
            else:
                bg = GradientDrawable()
            if force_circle:
                bg.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
            else:
                bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(20)))
                try:
                    bg.setColor(int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_featuredStickers_addButton)))
                except Exception:
                    bg.setColor(_ji(0xFF2EA6FF))
            view.setBackground(bg)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def _ripple_bg(self, drawable, color=0x30FFFFFF):
        try:
            return RippleDrawable(ColorStateList.valueOf(_ji(color)), drawable, None)
        except Exception:
            return drawable

    def _refresh_assist_button(self, fragment=None):
        try:
            if fragment is None:
                fragment = self._chat_fragment_ref
            try:
                from client_utils import get_last_fragment
                current_fragment = get_last_fragment()
            except Exception:
                current_fragment = None
            if fragment is None or current_fragment is None or fragment != current_fragment:
                if self._chat_assist_btn is not None:
                    self._chat_assist_btn.setVisibility(View.GONE)
                if self._chat_assist_fab is not None:
                    self._chat_assist_fab.setVisibility(View.GONE)
                self._hide_live_preview_prompt()
                self._stop_assist_position_tracker()
                return
            btn = self._chat_assist_btn
            icon = self._chat_assist_icon
            source_text = self._get_compose_text(fragment)
            allowed = self._is_assist_allowed_for_chat(fragment)
            compose_visible = bool(allowed and self._should_show_assist_button(source_text))
            fab_visible = bool(allowed and self._should_show_assist_fab(source_text))
            assist_active = bool(allowed and self._assist_can_open_for_text(source_text))
            try:
                visual_sig = (
                    int(self._extract_dialog_id(fragment=fragment) or 0),
                    bool(compose_visible),
                    bool(fab_visible),
                    bool(assist_active),
                    str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_assist_side", "right") or "right").strip().lower(),
                )
            except Exception:
                visual_sig = None
            if btn is not None and icon is not None:
                try:
                    if visual_sig is None or visual_sig != getattr(self, "_assist_visual_sig", None):
                        btn.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if compose_visible else View.GONE)
                except Exception:
                    btn.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if compose_visible else View.GONE)
                try:
                    btn.setAlpha(1.0 if assist_active and compose_visible else (0.42 if compose_visible else 0.0))
                    btn.setEnabled(bool(assist_active and compose_visible))
                    btn.setClickable(bool(assist_active and compose_visible))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                if compose_visible:
                    self._position_compose_assist_button(fragment)
            fab = self._chat_assist_fab
            fab_icon = self._chat_assist_fab_icon
            if fab is not None and fab_icon is not None:
                try:
                    if visual_sig is None or visual_sig != getattr(self, "_assist_visual_sig", None):
                        fab.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if fab_visible else View.GONE)
                except Exception:
                    fab.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if fab_visible else View.GONE)
                try:
                    fab.setAlpha(1.0 if assist_active and fab_visible else (0.42 if fab_visible else 0.0))
                    fab.setEnabled(bool(assist_active and fab_visible))
                    fab.setClickable(bool(assist_active and fab_visible))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                if fab_visible:
                    self._position_assist_fab(fragment)
            try:
                if self._live_preview_prompt is not None:
                    self._position_live_preview_prompt(fragment)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                if bool(compose_visible or fab_visible or self._live_preview_prompt is not None):
                    self._start_assist_position_tracker(fragment)
                else:
                    self._stop_assist_position_tracker()
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                self._sync_native_assist_cycle_visual(fragment)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                self._assist_visual_sig = visual_sig
            except Exception:
                pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"refresh assist fail: {e}")

    def _position_compose_assist_button(self, fragment):
        try:
            if fragment is None or self._chat_assist_btn is None:
                return
            assist_side = "right"
            try:
                assist_side = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_assist_side", "right") or "right").strip().lower()
            except Exception:
                assist_side = "right"
            enter_view = self._get_enter_view(fragment)
            if enter_view is None:
                return
            target = None
            scheduled_btn = None
            notify_btn = None
            attach_btn = None
            try:
                target = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "textFieldContainer")
            except Exception:
                target = None
            try:
                scheduled_btn = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "scheduledButton")
            except Exception:
                scheduled_btn = None
            try:
                notify_btn = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "notifyButton")
            except Exception:
                notify_btn = None
            try:
                attach_btn = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "attachButton")
            except Exception:
                attach_btn = None
            root_host = None
            try:
                root_host = self._chat_assist_btn.getParent()
            except Exception:
                root_host = None
            if target is None or root_host is None:
                return
            loc_target = [0, 0]
            loc_root = [0, 0]
            try:
                target.getLocationOnScreen(loc_target)
                root_host.getLocationOnScreen(loc_root)
            except Exception:
                return
            try:
                target_w = int(target.getWidth() or 0)
                btn_w = int(self._chat_assist_btn.getWidth() or AndroidUtilities.dp(44))
            except Exception:
                target_w = 0
                btn_w = AndroidUtilities.dp(44)
            target_left = int(loc_target[0]) - int(loc_root[0])
            if assist_side == "left":
                x = target_left + AndroidUtilities.dp(14)
            else:
                x = target_left + target_w - btn_w - AndroidUtilities.dp(58)
                for extra_btn in (attach_btn, scheduled_btn, notify_btn):
                    try:
                        if extra_btn is None or int(extra_btn.getVisibility()) != int(View.VISIBLE):
                            continue
                        extra_loc = [0, 0]
                        extra_btn.getLocationOnScreen(extra_loc)
                        extra_left = int(extra_loc[0]) - int(loc_root[0])
                        x = min(int(x), extra_left - btn_w - AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
            y = (int(loc_target[1]) - int(loc_root[1])) + AndroidUtilities.dp(6)
            try:
                self._chat_assist_btn.setX(float(max(0, x)))
                self._chat_assist_btn.setY(float(y))
                self._chat_assist_btn.bringToFront()
            except Exception:
                pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"position compose assist fail: {e}")

    def _position_assist_fab(self, fragment):
        try:
            if fragment is None or self._chat_assist_fab is None:
                return
            assist_side = "right"
            try:
                assist_side = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_assist_side", "right") or "right").strip().lower()
            except Exception:
                assist_side = "right"
            enter_view = self._get_enter_view(fragment)
            if enter_view is None:
                return
            target = None
            send_host = None
            scheduled_btn = None
            notify_btn = None
            try:
                target = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "textFieldContainer")
            except Exception:
                target = None
            if target is None:
                try:
                    target = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "messageEditTextContainer")
                except Exception:
                    target = None
            try:
                send_host = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "sendButtonContainer")
            except Exception:
                send_host = None
            try:
                scheduled_btn = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "scheduledButton")
            except Exception:
                scheduled_btn = None
            try:
                notify_btn = _get_private_field_silent(enter_view, "notifyButton")
            except Exception:
                notify_btn = None
            root_host = None
            try:
                root_host = self._chat_assist_fab.getParent()
            except Exception:
                root_host = None
            if target is None or root_host is None:
                return
            loc_target = [0, 0]
            loc_root = [0, 0]
            try:
                target.getLocationOnScreen(loc_target)
                root_host.getLocationOnScreen(loc_root)
            except Exception:
                return
            try:
                target_w = int(target.getWidth() or 0)
                fab_w = int(self._chat_assist_fab.getWidth() or AndroidUtilities.dp(46))
                fab_h = int(self._chat_assist_fab.getHeight() or AndroidUtilities.dp(46))
            except Exception:
                target_w = 0
                fab_w = AndroidUtilities.dp(46)
                fab_h = AndroidUtilities.dp(46)
            target_left = int(loc_target[0]) - int(loc_root[0])
            if assist_side == "left":
                x = target_left + AndroidUtilities.dp(4)
            else:
                if send_host is not None:
                    send_loc = [0, 0]
                    try:
                        send_host.getLocationOnScreen(send_loc)
                        x = (int(send_loc[0]) - int(loc_root[0])) + int(send_host.getWidth() or 0) - fab_w - AndroidUtilities.dp(2)
                    except Exception:
                        x = target_left + target_w - fab_w - AndroidUtilities.dp(2)
                else:
                    x = target_left + target_w - fab_w - AndroidUtilities.dp(2)
                for extra_btn in (scheduled_btn, notify_btn):
                    try:
                        if extra_btn is None:
                            continue
                        visible = int(extra_btn.getVisibility()) == int(View.VISIBLE)
                        if not visible:
                            continue
                        extra_loc = [0, 0]
                        extra_btn.getLocationOnScreen(extra_loc)
                        extra_left = int(extra_loc[0]) - int(loc_root[0])
                        x = min(int(x), extra_left - fab_w - AndroidUtilities.dp(6))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
            y = (int(loc_target[1]) - int(loc_root[1])) - fab_h - AndroidUtilities.dp(8)
            min_y = AndroidUtilities.dp(72)
            if y < min_y:
                y = min_y
            try:
                self._chat_assist_fab.setX(float(max(0, x)))
                self._chat_assist_fab.setY(float(max(0, y)))
                self._chat_assist_fab.bringToFront()
            except Exception:
                pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"position assist fab fail: {e}")

    def _ensure_assist_watcher(self, fragment, enter_view):
        try:
            if fragment is None or enter_view is None:
                return
            edit = None
            try:
                edit = enter_view.getEditField()
            except Exception:
                edit = None
            if edit is None:
                return
            frag_key = id(fragment)
            if frag_key in self._compose_watchers:
                return

            class _ComposeWatcher(dynamic_proxy(TextWatcher)):
                def beforeTextChanged(self_watcher, s, start, count, after):
                    pass

                def onTextChanged(self_watcher, s, start, before, count):
                    pass

                def afterTextChanged(self_watcher, editable):
                    try:
                        self._schedule_compose_ui_refresh(fragment)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        if self._live_preview_enabled():
                            self._handle_live_preview_text_changed(fragment)
                    except Exception:
                        pass

            watcher = _ComposeWatcher()
            edit.addTextChangedListener(watcher)
            self._compose_watchers[frag_key] = watcher
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"ensure assist watcher fail: {e}")

    def _attach_compose_assist_button(self, fragment, host):
        try:
            if fragment is None:
                return
            enter_view = self._get_enter_view(fragment)
            if enter_view is None:
                return
            activity = None
            try:
                activity = fragment.getParentActivity()
            except Exception:
                activity = None
            overlay_host = None
            if activity is not None:
                try:
                    overlay_host = activity.findViewById(16908290)
                except Exception:
                    overlay_host = None
            if overlay_host is None:
                try:
                    overlay_host = fragment.getFragmentView()
                except Exception:
                    overlay_host = None
            if overlay_host is None:
                return
            existing = None
            try:
                existing = overlay_host.findViewWithTag("__tlite_assist_btn__")
            except Exception:
                pass
            if existing is not None:
                self._chat_assist_btn = existing
                try:
                    self._chat_assist_icon = existing.getChildAt(0)
                except Exception:
                    self._chat_assist_icon = None
                self._ensure_assist_watcher(fragment, enter_view)
                self._attach_assist_fab(fragment)
                self._refresh_assist_button(fragment)
                return

            btn = FrameLayout(overlay_host.getContext())
            try:
                btn.setTag("__tlite_assist_btn__")
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                btn.setClipChildren(False)
                btn.setClipToPadding(False)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                btn.setClickable(True)
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._style_assist_chip(btn, force_circle=True)
            icon = self._build_assist_icon(overlay_host.getContext())
            try:
                icon.setColorFilter(int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_featuredStickers_buttonText)))
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                btn.addView(icon, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(22), AndroidUtilities.dp(22), Gravity.CENTER))
            except Exception:
                btn.addView(icon)

            try:
                try:
                    overlay_host.setClipChildren(False)
                    overlay_host.setClipToPadding(False)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                lp = FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(44), AndroidUtilities.dp(44))
                lp.gravity = Gravity.TOP | Gravity.LEFT
                overlay_host.addView(btn, lp)
            except Exception:
                overlay_host.addView(btn)

            class _AssistClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        if not self._is_assist_ai_configured():
                            try:
                                BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_missing_config"))
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            return
                        if not self._assist_can_open_for_text(self._get_compose_text(fragment)):
                            try:
                                BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("ai_sheet_need_words"))
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            return
                        self._show_compose_assist_sheet(fragment)
                    except Exception as e:
                        self._dlog(f"assist click fail: {e}")

            btn.setOnClickListener(_AssistClick())
            self._chat_assist_btn = btn
            self._chat_assist_icon = icon
            self._ensure_assist_watcher(fragment, enter_view)
            self._attach_assist_fab(fragment)
            self._refresh_assist_button(fragment)
            self._position_compose_assist_button(fragment)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"attach assist fail: {e}")

    def _attach_assist_fab(self, fragment):
        try:
            if fragment is None:
                return
            activity = None
            try:
                activity = fragment.getParentActivity()
            except Exception:
                activity = None
            root_host = None
            if activity is not None:
                try:
                    root_host = activity.findViewById(16908290)
                except Exception:
                    root_host = None
            if root_host is None:
                try:
                    root_host = fragment.getFragmentView()
                except Exception:
                    root_host = None
            if root_host is None:
                try:
                    root_host = _get_private_field_silent(fragment, "fragmentView")
                except Exception:
                    root_host = None
            if root_host is None:
                return
            existing = None
            try:
                existing = root_host.findViewWithTag("__tlite_assist_fab__")
            except Exception:
                pass
            if existing is not None:
                self._chat_assist_fab = existing
                try:
                    self._chat_assist_fab_icon = existing.getChildAt(0)
                except Exception:
                    self._chat_assist_fab_icon = None
                self._refresh_assist_button(fragment)
                return

            if not isinstance(root_host, ViewGroup):
                return
            fab_ctx = activity if activity is not None else root_host.getContext()
            btn = FrameLayout(fab_ctx)
            try:
                btn.setTag("__tlite_assist_fab__")
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                btn.setClickable(True)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                btn.setFocusable(True)
            except Exception:
                pass
            self._style_assist_chip(btn, force_circle=True)

            icon = self._build_assist_icon(root_host.getContext())
            try:
                icon.setColorFilter(int(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_featuredStickers_buttonText)))
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                btn.addView(icon, FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(20), AndroidUtilities.dp(20), Gravity.CENTER))
            except Exception:
                btn.addView(icon)

            lp = FrameLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(46), AndroidUtilities.dp(46), Gravity.BOTTOM | Gravity.RIGHT)
            try:
                lp.setMargins(0, 0, AndroidUtilities.dp(16), AndroidUtilities.dp(96))
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                root_host.addView(btn, lp)
            except Exception:
                try:
                    root_host.addView(btn)
                except Exception:
                    return
            try:
                btn.bringToFront()
            except Exception:
                pass

            class _AssistFabClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        if not self._is_assist_ai_configured():
                            try:
                                BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_missing_config"))
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            return
                        if not self._assist_can_open_for_text(self._get_compose_text(fragment)):
                            try:
                                BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("ai_sheet_need_words"))
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            return
                        self._show_compose_assist_sheet(fragment)
                    except Exception as e:
                        self._dlog(f"assist fab click fail: {e}")

            btn.setOnClickListener(_AssistFabClick())
            class _AssistFabLong(dynamic_proxy(View.OnLongClickListener)):
                def onLongClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        self._flash_assist_button_press(btn)
                        self._open_plugin_settings()
                    except Exception as e:
                        self._dlog(f"assist fab long click fail: {e}")
                    return True
            btn.setOnLongClickListener(_AssistFabLong())
            self._chat_assist_fab = btn
            self._chat_assist_fab_icon = icon
            self._chat_fragment_ref = fragment
            self._refresh_assist_button(fragment)
            self._position_assist_fab(fragment)
            self._start_assist_position_tracker(fragment)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"attach assist fab fail: {e}")

    def _request_ai_correction(self, original_text, current_text, mode_key=None, emojify=False, target_code=None):
        try:
            return self._request_ai_rewrite(original_text, current_text, "correction", mode_key, emojify, target_code)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"ai correction fail: {e}")
            return None

    def _request_ai_mode(self, original_text, current_text, mode_key, emojify=False, target_code=None):
        try:
            return self._request_ai_rewrite(original_text, current_text, "mode", mode_key, emojify, target_code)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"ai mode fail: {e}")
            return None

    def _request_ai_summary(self, original_text, current_text, mode_key=None, emojify=False, target_code=None):
        try:
            return self._request_ai_rewrite(original_text, current_text, "summary", mode_key, emojify, target_code)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"ai summary fail: {e}")
            return None

    def _request_native_assist_rewrite(self, original_text, current_text, action_kind, mode_key, emojify=False, target_code=None):
        try:
            target_code = str(target_code or self._global_target_lang() or "en")
            original_text = str(original_text or "").strip()
            current_text = str(current_text or "").strip()
            if not original_text:
                return None

            translated = current_text if current_text and current_text != original_text else None
            if not translated:
                translated = self._translate_text_native(original_text, target_code)
            if not translated:
                self._dlog(f"ai native rewrite fail: native translation unavailable action={action_kind}")
                return None

            if str(action_kind) == "summary":
                base_summary = current_text if current_text and current_text != original_text else translated
                out = self._fallback_summary_text(base_summary)
            else:
                if str(action_kind) == "mode":
                    self._dlog(f"ai native mode fallback -> local rewrite mode={mode_key}")
                    out = self._native_local_mode_rewrite(translated, mode_key)
                else:
                    out = translated

            if bool(emojify):
                out = self._native_local_emojify(out, mode_key)

            out = self._preserve_protected_names_in_output(original_text, out)
            out = self._normalize_assist_output(out, mode_key)
            return out or None
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"ai native rewrite error: {e}")
            return None

    def _execute_ai_rewrite_request(self, base, model, api_key, system_prompt, user_prompt, selected_mode, current_text, action_kind):
        payload = {
            "model": model,
            "messages": [
                {"role": "system", "content": system_prompt},
                {"role": "user", "content": user_prompt},
            ],
            "temperature": 0.22 if selected_mode == "custom" else 0.35,
            "max_tokens": (
                max(120, min(700, int(len(str(current_text or "")) * 1.5)))
                if str(action_kind) == "summary"
                else max(256, min(1600, len(str(current_text or "")) * 3))
            ),
        }
        headers = {
            "Content-Type": "application/json",
            "Accept": "application/json",
            "User-Agent": "TranslaticaLite/1.0",
        }
        data = {}
        base_l = str(base or "").lower()
        if "generativelanguage.googleapis.com" in base_l and "/models" in base_l and ":generatecontent" not in base_l:
            gemini_url = f"{base}/{model}:generateContent"
            if api_key:
                gemini_url += f"?key={url_quote(api_key)}"
            gemini_payload = {
                "system_instruction": {
                    "parts": [{"text": str(system_prompt or "")}]
                },
                "contents": [
                    {
                        "parts": [{"text": str(user_prompt or "")}]
                    }
                ],
                "generationConfig": {
                    "temperature": 0.22 if selected_mode == "custom" else 0.35,
                    "maxOutputTokens": (
                        max(120, min(700, int(len(str(current_text or "")) * 1.5)))
                        if str(action_kind) == "summary"
                        else max(256, min(1600, len(str(current_text or "")) * 3))
                    ),
                },
            }
            raw = json.dumps(gemini_payload).encode("utf-8")
            req = Request(gemini_url, data=raw, headers=headers, method="POST")
            with urlopen(req, timeout=45) as resp:
                response_raw = resp.read().decode("utf-8", errors="replace")
            data = json.loads(response_raw or "{}")
            candidates = data.get("candidates") or []
            if not candidates:
                return None
            parts = (((candidates[0] or {}).get("content") or {}).get("parts") or [])
            content = []
            for item in parts:
                if isinstance(item, dict) and item.get("text"):
                    content.append(str(item.get("text")))
            return "\n".join(content).strip()
        if "generativelanguage.googleapis.com" in base_l and "/openai" in base_l and api_key and "?key=" not in base_l:
            url = f"{base}/chat/completions?key={url_quote(api_key)}"
        else:
            url = f"{base}/chat/completions"
            auth_key = str(api_key or "").strip()
            if "api.llm7.io" in base_l and not auth_key:
                auth_key = "unused"
            if auth_key:
                headers["Authorization"] = f"Bearer {auth_key}"
        raw = json.dumps(payload).encode("utf-8")
        req = Request(url, data=raw, headers=headers, method="POST")
        with urlopen(req, timeout=45) as resp:
            response_raw = resp.read().decode("utf-8", errors="replace")
        data = json.loads(response_raw or "{}")
        choices = data.get("choices") or []
        if not choices:
            return None
        msg = (choices[0] or {}).get("message") or {}
        content = msg.get("content")
        if isinstance(content, list):
            chunks = []
            for item in content:
                if isinstance(item, dict):
                    txt = item.get("text")
                    if txt:
                        chunks.append(str(txt))
            content = "\n".join(chunks)
        return str(content or "").strip()

    def _request_ai_rewrite(self, original_text, current_text, action_kind, mode_key, emojify=False, target_code=None):
        try:
            ai_cfg = self._resolve_assist_ai_config()
            if str(ai_cfg.get("provider") or "") == "native":
                return self._request_native_assist_rewrite(original_text, current_text, action_kind, mode_key, emojify, target_code)
            base = str(ai_cfg.get("base") or "").strip().rstrip("/")
            model = str(ai_cfg.get("model") or "").strip()
            api_key = str(ai_cfg.get("api_key") or "").strip()
            if not base or not model:
                return None
            current_text = self._preserve_protected_names_in_output(original_text, current_text)
            target_code = str(target_code or self._global_target_lang() or "en")
            target_name = target_code
            try:
                for label, code in LANG_OPTIONS:
                    if str(code) == target_code:
                        target_name = str(label)
                        break
            except Exception:
                pass
            protected_names = self._extract_protected_names(original_text)
            formatting_requested = bool(self._assist_has_telegram_formatting(original_text) or self._assist_has_telegram_formatting(current_text))
            formatting_block = ""
            if formatting_requested:
                formatting_block = (
                    "\n\nTelegram formatting rules:\n"
                    "Preserve Telegram markdown and inline formatting exactly when it exists. "
                    "Keep markers like *bold*, _italic_, ~strike~, ||spoiler||, `code` and markdown links intact. "
                    "Translate only the human-readable content inside the formatting, never remove or break the formatting syntax."
                )
            protected_block = ""
            if protected_names:
                protected_block = (
                    "\n\nProtected names and identifiers:\n- " +
                    "\n- ".join([str(x) for x in protected_names if str(x).strip()]) +
                    "\n\nThese items are locked. They must stay exactly as written above in the final text. "
                    "If the current translated text changed or transliterated them, restore the exact original spelling."
                )
            mode_directives = {
				"formal": "Rewrite it in a formal, polished and professional tone. Keep it elegant, natural and clear without changing the meaning.",
				"short": "Rewrite it to be shorter, cleaner and more direct. Keep the meaning intact and avoid sounding abrupt.",
				"natural": "Rewrite it to sound natural, human and smooth, like a native speaker wrote it. Keep it clear and true to the original meaning.",
				"clear": "Rewrite it to be clearer, better organized and easier to understand. Keep it natural and do not change the meaning.",
				"bruto": "Rewrite it in a blunt, raw and straightforward tone. Keep it direct, strong and concise without sounding robotic or unnatural.",
            }
            selected_mode = str(mode_key or "").strip().lower()
            if str(action_kind) == "summary":
                style_directive = ""
                if selected_mode == "custom":
                    style_directive = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_mode_custom_prompt", "") or "").strip()
                else:
                    style_directive = mode_directives.get(selected_mode, "").strip()
                emoji_directive = (
                    f"Keep a small, context-aware set of fitting emojis in {target_name}. Usually use 1 to 2 emojis for short text and 2 to 4 for medium or long text. "
                    "Distribute emojis naturally near the relevant words, clauses or sentences instead of stacking them only at the end. "
                    "Use only standard Unicode emojis, never replacement characters, broken symbols or placeholder glyphs. "
                    "The emojis must match the tone of the message. Do not use cheerful emojis for rough, blunt or negative text."
                    if bool(emojify)
                    else "Do not add decorative emojis while summarizing."
                )
                extra_style = f"\n\nActive style to preserve while summarizing:\n{style_directive}" if style_directive else ""
                system_prompt = (
                    "You summarize translated text. Keep the same target language already used in the current translation. "
                    "Preserve the meaning, proper names and identifying names exactly as written. "
                    "Write a real summary, not a light rewrite. "
                    "Make it clearly shorter than the current translated text whenever possible, while preserving the main context, intent, request and important facts. "
                    "Remove repetition, filler, side comments and secondary details first. "
                    "If the result is almost the same length as the current translated text, it is not a valid summary. "
                    "Keep the result coherent, natural and easy to read, like a native speaker wrote it. "
                    "Preserve paragraph breaks and line structure when they matter to the message. "
                    "Do not use stylistic hyphens or em dashes. "
                    "Do not explain anything. Return only the summarized text."
                )
                user_prompt = (
                    f"Target language: {target_name}\n\n"
                    f"Original text:\n{str(original_text or '').strip()}\n\n"
                    f"Current translated text:\n{str(current_text or '').strip()}\n\n"
                    "Summarize the current translated text while preserving the original meaning and names. "
                    "The result must be noticeably shorter than the current translated text, while keeping the important context. "
                    "Aim for roughly 35% to 70% of the current translated text length, depending on the content."
                    f" {emoji_directive}"
                    f"{formatting_block}"
                    f"{protected_block}"
                    f"{extra_style}"
                )
            elif str(action_kind) == "mode":
                if selected_mode == "custom":
                    directive = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_mode_custom_prompt", "") or "").strip()
                    if not directive:
                        directive = "Rewrite the translated text using the user's custom style request."
                else:
                    directive = mode_directives.get(selected_mode, mode_directives["natural"])
                    directive += " Avoid stylistic hyphens and em dashes. Prefer natural punctuation, native word order and idiomatic phrasing."
                if bool(emojify):
                    directive += (
                        f" You must include a small, context-aware set of fitting emojis in the rewritten text in {target_name}. "
                        "Usually use 1 to 2 emojis for short text and 2 to 4 for medium or long text. "
                        "Distribute emojis naturally near the related words, clauses or sentences instead of stacking them only at the end. "
                        "Use only standard Unicode emojis, never replacement characters, broken symbols or placeholder glyphs. "
                        "The emojis must match the tone of the message. Do not use cheerful emojis for rough, blunt or negative text."
                    )
                else:
                    directive += " Do not use decorative emojis. Remove unnecessary emojis if they appear."
                system_prompt = (
                    "You rewrite translated text. Keep the same target language already used in the current translation. "
                    "Respect the meaning of the original text. "
                    "Write like a native speaker of the target language. "
                    "Use punctuation, sentence rhythm, commas and word order that feel genuinely natural in that language, especially in casual messaging. "
                    "Do not sound translated, robotic, textbook-like or foreign. "
                    "Preserve paragraph breaks and line structure when they exist. "
                    "Never translate or replace proper names, usernames, nicknames, brands or other identifying names from the original text unless the user explicitly asked for that. "
                    "When such names exist, preserve them exactly as written in the original text. "
                    "Apply the requested style faithfully. "
                    "If a custom instruction is provided, treat it as the highest-priority style rule and follow it literally without replacing it with a safer default. "
                    "Do not explain anything. Return only the rewritten text."
                )
                user_prompt = (
                    f"Target language: {target_name}\n\n"
                    f"Original text:\n{str(original_text or '').strip()}\n\n"
                    f"Current translated text:\n{str(current_text or '').strip()}\n\n"
                    f"Requested style:\n{directive}\n\n"
                    "Preserve personal names and identifying names exactly as they appear in the original text."
                    f"{formatting_block}"
                    f"{protected_block}"
                )
            else:
                if selected_mode == "custom":
                    style_directive = str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_mode_custom_prompt", "") or "").strip()
                else:
                    style_directive = mode_directives.get(selected_mode, "").strip()
                emoji_directive = (
                    f"You must include a small, context-aware set of fitting emojis in the final text in {target_name}. "
                    "Usually use 1 to 2 emojis for short text and 2 to 4 for medium or long text. "
                    "Distribute emojis naturally through the message near the relevant words, clauses or sentences, not only at the end. "
                    "Use only standard Unicode emojis, never replacement characters, broken symbols or placeholder glyphs. "
                    "The emojis must match the tone of the message. Do not use cheerful emojis for rough, blunt or negative text."
                    if bool(emojify)
                    else "Do not use decorative emojis. Remove unnecessary emojis if they appear."
                )
                system_prompt = (
                    "You lightly correct translated text. Keep the same target language already used in the current translation. "
                    "If the current translated text is unchanged, still in the source language, or not properly translated yet, translate it correctly to the target language before correcting it. "
                    "Fix spelling, grammar, punctuation and awkward phrasing while staying faithful to the original meaning. "
                    "Do not summarize. Do not shorten the message. Do not rewrite the whole message in a different structure. "
                    "Keep the same sentence order, same amount of detail and nearly the same length whenever possible. "
                    "The final text should usually stay within about 90% to 115% of the current translated text length. "
                    "Write like a native speaker of the target language. "
                    "Make the sentence read naturally, with idiomatic wording and punctuation that fits the language, but only through minimal edits. "
                    "Preserve paragraph breaks and line structure when they exist. "
                    "Avoid inconsistent commas, awkward rhythm, strange emphasis and any tone that sounds robotic, foreign or machine-translated. "
                    "Never translate or replace proper names, usernames, nicknames, brands or other identifying names from the original text unless the user explicitly asked for that. "
                    "When such names exist, preserve them exactly as written in the original text. "
                    f"{'' if selected_mode == 'custom' else 'Never use stylistic hyphens or em dashes as separators. Prefer natural punctuation. '}"
                    f"{'If a custom instruction is active, follow it literally as the highest-priority style rule. ' if selected_mode == 'custom' else ''}"
                    "Do not explain anything. Return only the improved text."
                )
                extra_style = f"\n\nActive style to preserve:\n{style_directive}" if style_directive else ""
                user_prompt = (
                    f"Target language: {target_name}\n\n"
                    f"Original text:\n{str(original_text or '').strip()}\n\n"
                    f"Current translated text:\n{str(current_text or '').strip()}\n\n"
                    "If the current translated text is still identical to the original or still sounds like the source language, translate it correctly to the target language first. "
                    "Correct spelling, grammar, punctuation and unnatural phrasing without changing the meaning. "
                    "Keep the original structure and details. Do not summarize. Do not shorten. "
                    "Help the message sound like a native speaker wrote it, but only with small, necessary corrections. "
                    "Preserve personal names and identifying names exactly as they appear in the original text. "
                    f"{'' if selected_mode == 'custom' else 'Avoid stylistic hyphens and em dashes. '}"
                    f"{emoji_directive}"
                    f"{formatting_block}"
                    f"{protected_block}"
                    f"{extra_style}"
                )
            out = self._execute_ai_rewrite_request(
                base,
                model,
                api_key,
                system_prompt,
                user_prompt,
                selected_mode,
                current_text,
                action_kind,
            )
            if bool(emojify) and (
                self._count_emojis(out) <= 0
                or self._emojis_are_only_at_the_end(out)
                or self._emojis_are_poorly_clustered(out)
                or self._has_broken_emoji_glyphs(out)
            ):
                retry_system_prompt = str(system_prompt or "") + (
                    " This time emojis are mandatory. Return a context-aware version with multiple fitting emojis when the text is medium or long, or at least one fitting emoji when the text is short. "
                    "Place emojis inline near the relevant words or clauses. Do not place all emojis only at the end. "
                    "Do not place the emojis as one clustered block. Spread them across different relevant parts of the text when the content supports that. "
                    "Use only standard Unicode emojis, never replacement characters, broken symbols or placeholder glyphs. "
                    "Do not return a plain text answer without emojis."
                )
                retry_user_prompt = str(user_prompt or "") + (
                    "\n\nYour previous answer either did not include emojis, used broken glyphs, or placed them poorly. Rewrite it again with real Unicode emojis that match the tone and distribute them naturally through different relevant parts of the text."
                )
                retry_out = self._execute_ai_rewrite_request(
                    base,
                    model,
                    api_key,
                    retry_system_prompt,
                    retry_user_prompt,
                    selected_mode,
                    current_text,
                    action_kind,
                )
                if retry_out:
                    out = retry_out
            out = self._preserve_protected_names_in_output(original_text, out)
            out = self._normalize_assist_output(out, selected_mode)
            if bool(emojify):
                out = self._ensure_emojify_output(out, selected_mode)
            return out or None
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"ai rewrite fail: {e}")
            return None

    def _show_compose_assist_sheet(self, fragment):
        try:
            if fragment is None:
                try:
                    from client_utils import get_last_fragment
                    fragment = get_last_fragment() or self._chat_fragment_ref
                except Exception:
                    fragment = self._chat_fragment_ref
            source_plain_text = str(self._get_compose_text(fragment) or "").strip()
            source_text = str(self._get_compose_markdown(fragment) or source_plain_text or "").strip()
            if not self._is_assist_allowed_for_chat(fragment):
                return
            if not self._is_assist_ai_configured():
                BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_missing_config"))
                return
            if not self._assist_can_open_for_text(source_plain_text):
                BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("ai_sheet_need_words"))
                return
            ctx = None
            try:
                ctx = fragment.getParentActivity() if fragment is not None else None
            except Exception:
                ctx = None
            if ctx is None:
                ctx = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext
            if ctx is None:
                return
            try:
                if hasattr(ctx, "isFinishing") and bool(ctx.isFinishing()):
                    self._dlog("show assist sheet skipped: activity finishing")
                    return
                if hasattr(ctx, "isDestroyed") and bool(ctx.isDestroyed()):
                    self._dlog("show assist sheet skipped: activity destroyed")
                    return
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                wnd = ctx.getWindow() if hasattr(ctx, "getWindow") else None
                decor = wnd.getDecorView() if wnd is not None else None
                token = decor.getWindowToken() if decor is not None else None
                if token is None:
                    self._dlog("show assist sheet skipped: null window token")
                    return
            except Exception:
                pass

            sheet = BottomSheet(ctx, False)
            self._ai_sheet = sheet
            is_dark = bool(Theme.isCurrentThemeDark())
            bg_color = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_dialogBackground))
            card_color = _ji(0xFFF7F8FC) if not is_dark else _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhite))
            primary_text = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteBlackText))
            secondary_text = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteGrayText2))
            accent = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_featuredStickers_addButton))
            accent_text = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_featuredStickers_buttonText))
            chip_idle = _ji(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_actionBarDefaultSubmenuBackground)) if is_dark else _ji(0xFFEDEFF5)
            card_stroke_color = _ji(0x18000000) if is_dark else _ji(0x220F172A)
            toggle_stroke_color = _ji(0x24000000) if is_dark else _ji(0x281E293B)

            outer = LinearLayout(ctx)
            outer.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            try:
                outer.setBackgroundColor(bg_color)
            except Exception:
                pass

            scroll = ScrollView(ctx)
            try:
                scroll.setFillViewport(True)
            except Exception:
                pass
            content = LinearLayout(ctx)
            content.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            content.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18))
            scroll.addView(content, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            header = LinearLayout(ctx)
            header.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            header.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)

            title = TextView(ctx)
            title.setText("Assist")
            title.setTextColor(primary_text)
            title.setTextSize(1, 18)
            try:
                title.setTypeface(title.getTypeface(), 1)
            except Exception:
                pass
            header.addView(title, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1.0))

            close_btn = TextView(ctx)
            close_btn.setText("×")
            close_btn.setTextSize(1, 22)
            close_btn.setTextColor(primary_text)
            close_btn.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
            close_btn.setPadding(0, 0, 0, AndroidUtilities.dp(2))
            close_bg = GradientDrawable()
            close_bg.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
            close_bg.setColor(chip_idle)
            try:
                close_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), card_stroke_color)
            except Exception:
                pass
            close_btn.setBackground(self._ripple_bg(close_bg))
            settings_btn = ImageView(ctx)
            try:
                settings_rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("msg_settings", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                if settings_rid:
                    settings_btn.setImageResource(settings_rid)
                    settings_btn.setColorFilter(primary_text)
            except Exception:
                pass
            settings_bg = GradientDrawable()
            settings_bg.setShape(GradientDrawable.OVAL)
            settings_bg.setColor(chip_idle)
            try:
                settings_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), card_stroke_color)
            except Exception:
                pass
            settings_btn.setBackground(self._ripple_bg(settings_bg))
            settings_btn.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))
            class _SettingsClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        sheet.dismiss()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        self._open_plugin_settings()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
            settings_btn.setOnClickListener(_SettingsClick())
            lp_settings = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(38), AndroidUtilities.dp(38))
            lp_settings.rightMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(8)
            header.addView(settings_btn, lp_settings)
            class _CloseClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        sheet.dismiss()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
            close_btn.setOnClickListener(_CloseClick())
            lp_close = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(38), AndroidUtilities.dp(38))
            header.addView(close_btn, lp_close)
            content.addView(header, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            header_sub = TextView(ctx)
            header_sub.setText(self._tr("ai_sheet_subtitle"))
            header_sub.setTextColor(secondary_text)
            header_sub.setTextSize(1, 14)
            header_sub.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(4), 0, 0)
            content.addView(header_sub, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))

            toggle_card = LinearLayout(ctx)
            toggle_card.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            toggle_card.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            toggle_card.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))
            toggle_bg = GradientDrawable()
            toggle_bg.setColor(chip_idle)
            toggle_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
            try:
                toggle_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), toggle_stroke_color)
            except Exception:
                pass
            toggle_card.setBackground(toggle_bg)
            lp_toggle = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_toggle.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(14)
            content.addView(toggle_card, lp_toggle)
            assist_info_card = LinearLayout(ctx)
            assist_info_card.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            assist_info_card.setGravity(Gravity.TOP)
            assist_info_card.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14))
            assist_info_bg = GradientDrawable()
            assist_info_bg.setColor(card_color)
            assist_info_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
            try:
                assist_info_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), card_stroke_color)
            except Exception:
                pass
            assist_info_card.setBackground(assist_info_bg)
            assist_info_icon = ImageView(ctx)
            try:
                assist_info_rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("media_magic_cut", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                if assist_info_rid:
                    assist_info_icon.setImageResource(assist_info_rid)
                    assist_info_icon.setColorFilter(_ji(0xFF60A5FA))
            except Exception:
                pass
            lp_assist_info_icon = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18))
            lp_assist_info_icon.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(2)
            assist_info_card.addView(assist_info_icon, lp_assist_info_icon)
            assist_info_texts = LinearLayout(ctx)
            assist_info_texts.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
            assist_info_texts.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(12), 0, 0, 0)
            assist_info_title = TextView(ctx)
            assist_info_title.setText(self._tr("ai_sheet_assist_active_title"))
            assist_info_title.setText("Correção ativada")
            assist_info_title.setTextColor(primary_text)
            assist_info_title.setTextSize(1, 16)
            assist_info_title.setText(self._tr("ai_sheet_assist_active_title"))
            try:
                assist_info_title.setTypeface(assist_info_title.getTypeface(), 1)
            except Exception:
                pass
            assist_info_texts.addView(assist_info_title, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            assist_info_desc = TextView(ctx)
            assist_info_desc.setText(self._tr("ai_sheet_assist_active_desc"))
            assist_info_desc.setText("Abaixo, você confere a correção e melhoria de gramática e ortografia, mantendo seu estilo original.")
            assist_info_desc.setTextColor(secondary_text)
            assist_info_desc.setTextSize(1, 13)
            assist_info_desc.setText(self._tr("ai_sheet_assist_active_desc"))
            assist_info_desc.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(4), 0, 0)
            assist_info_texts.addView(assist_info_desc, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            assist_info_card.addView(assist_info_texts, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, 1.0))
            lp_assist_info = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_assist_info.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(12)
            content.addView(assist_info_card, lp_assist_info)
            assist_info_card.setVisibility(View.GONE)

            def _make_top_action(text_value, icon_name, weight=1.0, icon_only=False):
                wrap = LinearLayout(ctx)
                wrap.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
                wrap.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
                wrap.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))
                bg = GradientDrawable()
                bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(16)))
                bg.setColor(card_color)
                try:
                    bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), card_stroke_color)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                wrap.setBackground(self._ripple_bg(bg))
                icon_view = ImageView(ctx)
                try:
                    rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier(icon_name, "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                    if rid:
                        icon_view.setImageResource(rid)
                        icon_view.setColorFilter(primary_text)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                wrap.addView(icon_view, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(22), AndroidUtilities.dp(22)))
                label = None
                if not icon_only:
                    label = TextView(ctx)
                    label.setText(text_value)
                    label.setTextColor(primary_text)
                    label.setTextSize(1, 13)
                    try:
                        label.setTypeface(label.getTypeface(), 1)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    label.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(8), 0, 0, 0)
                    wrap.addView(label, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
                return wrap, bg, icon_view, label, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(0, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, weight)

            assist_tab_text = "Assist"
            correction_btn, correction_bg, correction_icon, correction_label, correction_lp = _make_top_action(
                assist_tab_text, "msg_translate"
            )
            modes_btn, modes_bg, modes_icon, modes_label, modes_lp = _make_top_action(
                self._tr("ai_sheet_modes"), "msg_channel_14_solar"
            )
            correction_lp.rightMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(8)
            modes_lp.leftMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(8)
            toggle_card.addView(correction_btn, correction_lp)
            toggle_card.addView(modes_btn, modes_lp)
            correction_selected_color = _ji(0xFFF59E0B)
            correction_idle_stroke = _ji(0x22F59E0B)
            modes_selected_color = _ji(0xFF3B82F6)
            modes_idle_stroke = _ji(0x223B82F6)

            def _make_section(label_text, body_text):
                holder = LinearLayout(ctx)
                holder.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
                holder.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14))
                bg = GradientDrawable()
                bg.setColor(card_color)
                bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
                try:
                    bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), card_stroke_color)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                holder.setBackground(bg)
                label = TextView(ctx)
                label.setText(label_text)
                label.setTextColor(primary_text)
                label.setTextSize(1, 15)
                try:
                    label.setTypeface(label.getTypeface(), 1)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                holder.addView(label)
                body = TextView(ctx)
                body.setText(body_text)
                body.setTextColor(primary_text)
                body.setTextSize(1, 16)
                body.setLineSpacing(0.0, 1.1)
                body.setPadding(0, AndroidUtilities.dp(10), 0, 0)
                holder.addView(body)
                return holder, body

            utility_row = LinearLayout(ctx)
            utility_row.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            utility_row.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER)
            lp_utility = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_utility.topMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(12)
            content.addView(utility_row, lp_utility)
            utility_row.setVisibility(View.GONE)

            original_chip_wrap = LinearLayout(ctx)
            original_chip_wrap.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            try:
                original_chip_wrap.setGravity(Gravity.LEFT | Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            except Exception:
                pass
            original_chip = LinearLayout(ctx)
            original_chip.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            original_chip.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            original_chip.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))
            original_chip_bg = GradientDrawable()
            original_chip_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(16)))
            original_chip_bg.setColor(card_color)
            try:
                original_chip_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), card_stroke_color)
            except Exception:
                pass
            original_chip.setBackground(self._ripple_bg(original_chip_bg))
            original_icon = ImageView(ctx)
            try:
                original_rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("msg_view_file", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                if original_rid:
                    original_icon.setImageResource(original_rid)
                    original_icon.setColorFilter(primary_text)
            except Exception:
                pass
            original_chip.addView(original_icon, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(AndroidUtilities.dp(18), AndroidUtilities.dp(18)))
            original_label = TextView(ctx)
            original_label.setText(self._tr("ai_sheet_original"))
            original_label.setTextColor(primary_text)
            original_label.setTextSize(1, 14)
            try:
                original_label.setTypeface(original_label.getTypeface(), 1)
            except Exception:
                pass
            original_label.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(8), 0, 0, 0)
            original_chip.addView(original_label, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            original_chip_wrap.addView(original_chip, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            lp_original_wrap = LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT)
            lp_original_wrap.rightMargin = AndroidUtilities.dp(8)
            utility_row.addView(original_chip_wrap, lp_original_wrap)

            correction_status_wrap = LinearLayout(ctx)
            correction_status_wrap.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            try:
                correction_status_wrap.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            except Exception:
                pass
            correction_status_chip = LinearLayout(ctx)
            correction_status_chip.setOrientation(LinearLayout.HORIZONTAL)
            correction_status_chip.setGravity(Gravity.CENTER_VERTICAL)
            correction_status_chip.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))
            correction_status_bg = GradientDrawable()
            correction_status_bg.setCornerRadius(float(AndroidUtilities.dp(16)))
            correction_status_bg.setColor(card_color)
            try:
