            outer.addView(scroll, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
            sheet.setCustomView(outer)

            state = {
                "source": source_text,
                "source_plain": source_plain_text,
                "translated": "",
                "current": "",
                "corrected_base": "",
                "modes_output": "",
                "loading": True,
                "correction_count": 0,
                "correction_running": False,
                "tab": "correction",
                "selected_mode": str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_pinned_mode", "") or "").strip().lower() or None,
                "pinned_mode": str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_pinned_mode", "") or "").strip().lower() or None,
                "emojify": False,
                "target_lang": str(self._assist_target_lang(fragment) or "en"),
                "assist_bootstrap_done": False,
                "assist_bootstrap_retry": False,
                "modes_nonce": 0,
            }
            if self._assist_using_native_provider() and str(state.get("selected_mode") or "").strip().lower() == "custom":
                state["selected_mode"] = None
            if self._assist_using_native_provider() and str(state.get("pinned_mode") or "").strip().lower() == "custom":
                state["pinned_mode"] = None

            def _open_temp_target_dialog():
                try:
                    builder = AlertDialogBuilder(ctx)
                    builder.set_title(self._tr("settings_target_lang"))
                    root_lang = LinearLayout(ctx)
                    root_lang.setOrientation(LinearLayout.VERTICAL)
                    try:
                        root_lang.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(12), AndroidUtilities.dp(8))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    current_code = str(state.get("target_lang") or self._assist_target_lang(fragment) or "en")
                    for i, label in enumerate(LANG_LABELS):
                        code = str(LANG_CODES[i])
                        row = TextView(ctx)
                        row.setText(f"{label}{'' if code != current_code else ' [x]'}")
                        try:
                            row.setTextSize(16)
                            row.setTextColor(Theme.getColor(Theme.key_windowBackgroundWhiteBlackText))
                            row.setPadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(10), AndroidUtilities.dp(8), AndroidUtilities.dp(10))
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        class _Pick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                            def __init__(self_obj, picked_code, picked_label):
                                super().__init__()
                                self_obj.picked_code = str(picked_code or "en")
                                self_obj.picked_label = str(picked_label or "")
                            def onClick(self_obj, v):
                                try:
                                    try:
                                        if hasattr(builder, "dismiss"):
                                            builder.dismiss()
                                    except Exception:
                                        pass
                                    state["target_lang"] = self_obj.picked_code
                                    try:
                                        target_lang_label.setText(self_obj.picked_label)
                                    except Exception:
                                        pass
                                    state["loading"] = True
                                    self._set_assist_result_text(translation_text_view, self._tr("ai_sheet_loading"))
                                    expand_chip.setVisibility(View.GONE)
                                    def _reload():
                                        try:
                                            translated = self._translate_text(state["source"], self_obj.picked_code)
                                            translated = self._preserve_protected_names_in_output(state["source"], translated)
                                            translated = self._normalize_assist_output(translated, None)
                                            translated = str(translated or "").strip() or self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty")
                                            def _apply():
                                                state["loading"] = False
                                                state["translated"] = translated
                                                state["corrected_base"] = translated
                                                state["modes_output"] = translated
                                                state["current"] = translated
                                                if state.get("tab") == "correction":
                                                    _run_correction()
                                                else:
                                                    if state.get("selected_mode"):
                                                        _run_mode(state.get("selected_mode"))
                                                    elif bool(state.get("emojify")):
                                                        _run_emojify_refresh()
                                                    else:
                                                        _update_translation_text(translated)
                                                        _apply_tab_styles()
                                            run_on_ui_thread(_apply)
                                        except Exception as inner_e:
                                            run_on_ui_thread(lambda: BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty")))
                                            self._dlog(f"assist temp target reload fail: {inner_e}")
                                    try:
                                        from client_utils import run_on_queue
                                        run_on_queue(_reload)
                                    except Exception:
                                        threading.Thread(target=_reload, daemon=True).start()
                                except Exception as inner_e:
                                    self._dlog(f"assist temp target pick fail: {inner_e}")
                        row.setOnClickListener(_Pick(code, label))
                        root_lang.addView(row, LinearLayout.LayoutParams(LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))
                    builder.set_view(root_lang)
                    builder.set_negative_button(self._tr("dialog_close"), lambda d, w: d.dismiss() if d else None)
                    builder.show()
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"assist temp target dialog fail: {e}")

            def _apply_tab_styles():
                active_bg = accent
                active_text = accent_text
                inactive_text = primary_text
                is_correction = state["tab"] == "correction"
                try:
                    correction_icon.setColorFilter(active_text if is_correction else inactive_text)
                    modes_icon.setColorFilter(active_text if not is_correction else inactive_text)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                if correction_label is not None:
                    correction_label.setTextColor(active_text if is_correction else inactive_text)
                if modes_label is not None:
                    modes_label.setTextColor(active_text if not is_correction else inactive_text)
                correction_bg.setColor(accent if is_correction else card_color)
                modes_bg.setColor(accent if not is_correction else card_color)
                show_modes = not is_correction
                utility_row.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if show_modes else View.GONE)
                modes_wrap.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if show_modes else View.GONE)
                modes_hint.setVisibility(View.GONE)
                target_lang_chip.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE)
                try:
                    header_sub.setText(self._tr("ai_sheet_modes_soon") if show_modes else self._tr("ai_sheet_subtitle"))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                original_chip_wrap.setVisibility(View.GONE)
                correction_status_wrap.setVisibility(View.GONE)
                assist_info_card.setVisibility(View.GONE)
                emojify_chip.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if show_modes else View.GONE)
                translation_card.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE)
                improve_btn.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if is_correction else View.GONE)
                try:
                    correction_bg.setColor(correction_selected_color if is_correction else card_color)
                    modes_bg.setColor(modes_selected_color if not is_correction else card_color)
                    correction_bg.setStroke(0, _ji(0x00000000))
                    modes_bg.setStroke(0, _ji(0x00000000))
                except Exception:
                    pass
                for mode_key, mode_pack in mode_chip_views.items():
                    chip_view, chip_bg = mode_pack
                    selected = bool((not is_correction) and str(state.get("selected_mode") or "") == str(mode_key))
                    pinned = bool(str(state.get("pinned_mode") or "") == str(mode_key))
                    chip_bg.setColor(mode_selected_colors.get(mode_key, accent) if selected else card_color)
                    chip_view.setTextColor(accent_text if selected else primary_text)
                    try:
                        chip_view.setCompoundDrawablePadding(AndroidUtilities.dp(5))
                        if pinned:
                            pin_rid = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getIdentifier("msg_pin_solar", "drawable", ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getPackageName())
                            pin_drawable = ApplicationLoader.applicationContext.getResources().getDrawable(pin_rid) if pin_rid else None
                            if pin_drawable is not None:
                                try:
                                    pin_drawable = pin_drawable.mutate()
                                except Exception:
                                    pass
                                pin_drawable.setColorFilter(mode_selected_colors.get(mode_key, _ji(0xFFF59E0B)))
                                pin_drawable.setBounds(0, 0, AndroidUtilities.dp(14), AndroidUtilities.dp(14))
                                try:
                                    chip_view.setCompoundDrawablesRelative(pin_drawable, None, None, None)
                                except Exception:
                                    chip_view.setCompoundDrawables(pin_drawable, None, None, None)
                            chip_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(2), mode_selected_colors.get(mode_key, _ji(0xFFF59E0B)))
                        else:
                            try:
                                chip_view.setCompoundDrawablesRelative(None, None, None, None)
                            except Exception:
                                chip_view.setCompoundDrawables(None, None, None, None)
                            chip_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), card_stroke_color)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                emojify_selected = bool((not is_correction) and state.get("emojify"))
                try:
                    emojify_bg.setColor(_ji(0xFFF97316) if emojify_selected else card_color)
                    emojify_bg.setStroke(AndroidUtilities.dp(1), _ji(0xFFF97316))
                    emojify_icon.setColorFilter(accent_text if emojify_selected else primary_text)
                    emojify_label.setTextColor(accent_text if emojify_selected else primary_text)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    apply_btn.setEnabled(True)
                    send_wrap.setEnabled(True)
                    apply_btn.setAlpha(1.0)
                    send_wrap.setAlpha(1.0)
                    apply_bg.setColor(_ji(0xFF3A86F6))
                    send_bg.setColor(_ji(0xFFEB3F44))
                except Exception:
                    pass

            def _update_translation_text(value):
                text_value = str(value or "").strip()
                if not text_value:
                    text_value = self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty")
                state["current"] = text_value
                preview_value, needs_expand = self._truncate_assist_preview(text_value)
                self._set_assist_result_text(translation_text_view, preview_value)
                force_expand = bool(preview_value != text_value) or bool(self._should_show_expand_chip(text_value))
                expand_visible = bool(needs_expand or force_expand)
                expand_chip.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if expand_visible else View.GONE)
                try:
                    expand_chip.setAlpha(1.0 if expand_visible else 0.0)
                    expand_chip.requestLayout()
                    expand_chip.invalidate()
                    translation_card.requestLayout()
                    translation_card.invalidate()
                    def _reaffirm_expand():
                        try:
                            reaffirm = bool((state.get("current") or "").strip() and (self._truncate_assist_preview(state.get("current") or "")[1] or self._should_show_expand_chip(state.get("current") or "")))
                            expand_chip.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE if reaffirm else View.GONE)
                            expand_chip.setAlpha(1.0 if reaffirm else 0.0)
                            expand_chip.requestLayout()
                            expand_chip.invalidate()
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                    threading.Timer(0.06, lambda: run_on_ui_thread(_reaffirm_expand)).start()
                except Exception:
                    pass
                if state["tab"] == "correction":
                    improve_btn.setVisibility(View.VISIBLE)

            def _load_preview():
                try:
                    dst = str(state.get("target_lang") or self._assist_target_lang(fragment) or "en")
                    translated = self._translate_text(source_text, dst)
                    translated = self._preserve_protected_names_in_output(source_text, translated)
                    translated = self._normalize_assist_output(translated, None)
                    if not translated:
                        translated = self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty")
                    def _apply_preview():
                        state["loading"] = False
                        state["translated"] = str(translated or "").strip()
                        state["corrected_base"] = str(state["translated"] or "").strip()
                        state["modes_output"] = str(state["translated"] or "").strip()
                        _update_translation_text(state["translated"])
                        if state.get("tab") == "correction" and not bool(state.get("assist_bootstrap_done")):
                            state["assist_bootstrap_done"] = True
                            _run_correction()
                    run_on_ui_thread(_apply_preview)
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"sheet preview fail: {e}")
                    def _apply_preview_fail():
                        state["loading"] = False
                        state["translated"] = self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty")
                        state["corrected_base"] = str(state["translated"] or "").strip()
                        state["modes_output"] = str(state["translated"] or "").strip()
                        _update_translation_text(state["translated"])
                    run_on_ui_thread(_apply_preview_fail)

            def _run_correction():
                if state["correction_running"]:
                    return
                if state["loading"]:
                    BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("ai_sheet_loading"))
                    return
                if not self._is_assist_ai_configured():
                    BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_missing_config"))
                    return
                state["correction_running"] = True
                if self._is_assist_transient_text(state.get("current")):
                    self._set_assist_result_text(translation_text_view, self._tr("ai_sheet_generating"))
                expand_chip.setVisibility(View.GONE)
                def _worker():
                    improved = self._request_ai_correction(
                        state["source"],
                        state["translated"],
                        None,
                        bool(state.get("emojify")),
                        state.get("target_lang"),
                    )
                    def _finish():
                        state["correction_running"] = False
                        if improved:
                            if self._looks_like_over_aggressive_correction(state["translated"], improved):
                                improved = state["translated"]
                            state["correction_count"] += 1
                            state["corrected_base"] = str(improved or "").strip()
                            if state.get("selected_mode"):
                                state["modes_output"] = str(state["corrected_base"] or "").strip()
                            if state.get("tab") == "correction":
                                _update_translation_text(state["corrected_base"])
                            if (
                                bool(state.get("assist_bootstrap_done"))
                                and not bool(state.get("assist_bootstrap_retry"))
                                and str(improved or "").strip().casefold() == str(state.get("source") or "").strip().casefold()
                            ):
                                state["assist_bootstrap_retry"] = True
                                try:
                                    threading.Timer(0.35, lambda: run_on_ui_thread(_run_correction)).start()
                                except Exception:
                                    pass
                        else:
                            if state.get("tab") == "correction":
                                _update_translation_text(state["corrected_base"] or state["translated"])
                            BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty"))
                        _apply_tab_styles()
                    run_on_ui_thread(_finish)
                try:
                    from client_utils import run_on_queue
                    run_on_queue(_worker)
                except Exception:
                    threading.Thread(target=_worker, daemon=True).start()

            def _run_emojify_refresh():
                if state["correction_running"]:
                    return
                if state["loading"]:
                    BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("ai_sheet_loading"))
                    return
                if not self._is_assist_ai_configured():
                    BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_missing_config"))
                    return
                if not bool(state.get("emojify")) and not state.get("selected_mode"):
                    state["modes_output"] = str(state["translated"] or "").strip()
                    if state.get("tab") == "modes":
                        _update_translation_text(state["modes_output"])
                    _apply_tab_styles()
                    return
                state["modes_nonce"] = int(state.get("modes_nonce") or 0) + 1
                request_nonce = int(state.get("modes_nonce") or 0)
                state["correction_running"] = True
                if self._is_assist_transient_text(state.get("current")):
                    self._set_assist_result_text(translation_text_view, self._tr("ai_sheet_generating"))
                expand_chip.setVisibility(View.GONE)
                _apply_tab_styles()
                def _worker():
                    if state.get("selected_mode"):
                        improved = self._request_ai_mode(
                            state["source"],
                            state["translated"],
                            state.get("selected_mode"),
                            bool(state.get("emojify")),
                            state.get("target_lang"),
                        )
                    else:
                        improved = self._request_ai_correction(
                            state["source"],
                            state["translated"],
                            None,
                            bool(state.get("emojify")),
                            state.get("target_lang"),
                        )
                    def _finish():
                        if int(state.get("modes_nonce") or 0) != request_nonce:
                            return
                        state["correction_running"] = False
                        if improved:
                            state["modes_output"] = str(improved or "").strip()
                            if state.get("tab") == "modes":
                                _update_translation_text(state["modes_output"])
                        else:
                            state["modes_output"] = str(state["translated"] or "").strip()
                            if state.get("tab") == "modes":
                                _update_translation_text(state["modes_output"])
                            BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty"))
                        _apply_tab_styles()
                    run_on_ui_thread(_finish)
                try:
                    from client_utils import run_on_queue
                    run_on_queue(_worker)
                except Exception:
                    threading.Thread(target=_worker, daemon=True).start()

            def _run_summary():
                if state["correction_running"]:
                    return
                if state["loading"]:
                    BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("ai_sheet_loading"))
                    return
                if not self._is_assist_ai_configured():
                    BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_missing_config"))
                    return
                state["correction_running"] = True
                if self._is_assist_transient_text(state.get("current")):
                    self._set_assist_result_text(translation_text_view, self._tr("ai_sheet_generating"))
                expand_chip.setVisibility(View.GONE)
                def _worker():
                    base_text = state["current"] or state["corrected_base"] or state["translated"]
                    improved = self._request_ai_summary(
                        state["source"],
                        base_text,
                        state.get("selected_mode"),
                        bool(state.get("emojify")),
                        state.get("target_lang"),
                    )
                    if not self._looks_like_effective_summary(base_text, improved):
                        improved = self._request_ai_summary(
                            state["source"],
                            base_text + "\n\nPlease make it significantly shorter while preserving the main context.",
                            state.get("selected_mode"),
                            bool(state.get("emojify")),
                            state.get("target_lang"),
                        )
                    if not self._looks_like_effective_summary(base_text, improved):
                        improved = self._fallback_summary_text(base_text)
                    def _finish():
                        state["correction_running"] = False
                        if improved:
                            _update_translation_text(improved)
                        else:
                            _update_translation_text(state["current"] or state["corrected_base"] or state["translated"])
                            BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty"))
                        _apply_tab_styles()
                    run_on_ui_thread(_finish)
                try:
                    from client_utils import run_on_queue
                    run_on_queue(_worker)
                except Exception:
                    threading.Thread(target=_worker, daemon=True).start()

            def _run_mode(mode_key):
                if state["correction_running"]:
                    return
                if state["loading"]:
                    BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("ai_sheet_loading"))
                    return
                normalized_mode = str(mode_key or "").strip()
                if normalized_mode and normalized_mode == str(state.get("selected_mode") or ""):
                    state["selected_mode"] = None
                    state["tab"] = "modes"
                    fallback_text = state["translated"]
                    if bool(state.get("emojify")):
                        _run_emojify_refresh()
                    else:
                        state["modes_output"] = str(fallback_text or "").strip()
                        _update_translation_text(fallback_text)
                        _apply_tab_styles()
                    return
                if not self._is_assist_ai_configured():
                    BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_missing_config"))
                    return
                if str(mode_key or "").strip().lower() == "custom":
                    if not str(self.get_setting("tlite_ai_mode_custom_prompt", "") or "").strip():
                        state["selected_mode"] = "custom"
                        state["tab"] = "modes"
                        self._set_assist_result_text(translation_text_view, self._tr("ai_mode_custom_missing_prompt"))
                        _apply_tab_styles()
                        return
                state["modes_nonce"] = int(state.get("modes_nonce") or 0) + 1
                request_nonce = int(state.get("modes_nonce") or 0)
                state["correction_running"] = True
                state["selected_mode"] = str(mode_key or "")
                if self._is_assist_transient_text(state.get("current")):
                    self._set_assist_result_text(translation_text_view, self._tr("ai_sheet_generating"))
                expand_chip.setVisibility(View.GONE)
                _apply_tab_styles()
                def _worker():
                    improved = self._request_ai_mode(
                        state["source"],
                        state["translated"],
                        mode_key,
                        bool(state.get("emojify")),
                        state.get("target_lang"),
                    )
                    def _finish():
                        if int(state.get("modes_nonce") or 0) != request_nonce:
                            return
                        state["correction_running"] = False
                        if improved:
                            state["modes_output"] = str(improved or "").strip()
                            if state.get("tab") == "modes":
                                _update_translation_text(state["modes_output"])
                        else:
                            state["modes_output"] = str(state["translated"] or "").strip()
                            if state.get("tab") == "modes":
                                _update_translation_text(state["modes_output"])
                            BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty"))
                        _apply_tab_styles()
                    run_on_ui_thread(_finish)
                try:
                    from client_utils import run_on_queue
                    run_on_queue(_worker)
                except Exception:
                    threading.Thread(target=_worker, daemon=True).start()

            class _CorrectionClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    state["tab"] = "correction"
                    _update_translation_text(state["corrected_base"] or state["translated"])
                    _apply_tab_styles()

            class _ModesClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    state["tab"] = "modes"
                    _update_translation_text(state["modes_output"] or state["corrected_base"] or state["translated"])
                    _apply_tab_styles()

            class _EmojifyClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    state["tab"] = "modes"
                    state["emojify"] = not bool(state.get("emojify"))
                    _apply_tab_styles()
                    _run_emojify_refresh()

            class _ImproveClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    _run_summary()

            class _ExpandClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    self._show_assist_expanded_sheet(fragment, state.get("current") or state.get("translated"), state.get("target_lang"))

            class _OriginalClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    try:
                        builder = AlertDialogBuilder(ctx)
                        builder.set_title(self._tr("ai_sheet_original"))
                        builder.set_message(str(state.get("source_plain") or state.get("source") or source_plain_text or ""))
                        builder.set_negative_button(self._tr("dialog_close"), lambda d, w: d.dismiss() if d else None)
                        builder.show()
                    except Exception as e:
                        self._dlog(f"original alert fail: {e}")

            class _TargetLangClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    _open_temp_target_dialog()

            class _ApplyClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    final_text = str(state["current"] or state["translated"] or "").strip()
                    if not final_text:
                        BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty"))
                        return
                    if self._set_compose_text(fragment, final_text):
                        BulletinHelper.show_success(self._tr("ai_sheet_applied"))
                        try:
                            sheet.dismiss()
                        except Exception:
                            pass

            class _SendClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                def onClick(self_obj, v):
                    final_text = str(state["current"] or state["translated"] or "").strip()
                    if not final_text:
                        BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("ai_sheet_translation_empty"))
                        return
                    payload = self._prepare_assist_send_payload(final_text)
                    self._assist_pending_send = payload
                    self._set_compose_text(fragment, str((payload or {}).get("text") or final_text))
                    sent = self._trigger_compose_send(fragment)
                    try:
                        sheet.dismiss()
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    if sent:
                        if self._assist_send_bulletins_enabled():
                            BulletinHelper.show_success(self._tr("ai_sheet_sent"))
                    else:
                        self._assist_pending_send = None
                        if self._assist_send_bulletins_enabled():
                            BulletinHelper.show_info(self._tr("ai_sheet_send_fail"))

            correction_btn.setOnClickListener(_CorrectionClick())
            modes_btn.setOnClickListener(_ModesClick())
            emojify_chip.setOnClickListener(_EmojifyClick())
            try:
                target_lang_chip.setOnClickListener(_TargetLangClick())
            except Exception:
                pass
            improve_btn.setOnClickListener(_ImproveClick())
            expand_chip.setOnClickListener(_ExpandClick())
            apply_btn.setOnClickListener(_ApplyClick())
            send_wrap.setOnClickListener(_SendClick())
            for mode_key, mode_pack in mode_chip_views.items():
                chip_view, _chip_bg = mode_pack
                class _ModeTouch(dynamic_proxy(View.OnTouchListener)):
                    def onTouch(self_inner, v, event):
                        try:
                            action = int(event.getAction())
                            parent = modes_wrap.getParent()
                            if parent is not None:
                                if action == 0:
                                    parent.requestDisallowInterceptTouchEvent(True)
                                elif action in (1, 3):
                                    parent.requestDisallowInterceptTouchEvent(False)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        return False
                class _ModeClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnClickListener)):
                    def __init__(self_inner, key_value):
                        super().__init__()
                        self_inner.key_value = key_value
                    def onClick(self_inner, v):
                        state["tab"] = "modes"
                        _run_mode(self_inner.key_value)
                class _ModeLongClick(dynamic_proxy(View.OnLongClickListener)):
                    def __init__(self_inner, key_value):
                        super().__init__()
                        self_inner.key_value = key_value
                    def onLongClick(self_inner, v):
                        try:
                            current_pinned = str(state.get("pinned_mode") or "")
                            next_pinned = "" if current_pinned == str(self_inner.key_value) else str(self_inner.key_value)
                            state["pinned_mode"] = next_pinned or None
                            self.set_setting("tlite_ai_pinned_mode", next_pinned)
                            if next_pinned:
                                state["selected_mode"] = next_pinned
                            elif current_pinned == str(state.get("selected_mode") or ""):
                                state["selected_mode"] = None
                            _apply_tab_styles()
                            if state.get("tab") == "correction":
                                _run_correction()
                            else:
                                if next_pinned:
                                    _run_mode(next_pinned)
                                elif bool(state.get("emojify")):
                                    _run_emojify_refresh()
                                else:
                                    state["modes_output"] = str(state["translated"] or "").strip()
                                    _update_translation_text(state["modes_output"])
                                    _apply_tab_styles()
                            try:
                                BulletinHelper.show_success(self._tr("ai_mode_pinned") if next_pinned else self._tr("ai_mode_unpinned"))
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                        except Exception as e:
                            self._dlog(f"mode pin fail: {e}")
                        return True
                chip_view.setOnTouchListener(_ModeTouch())
                chip_view.setOnClickListener(_ModeClick(mode_key))
                chip_view.setOnLongClickListener(_ModeLongClick(mode_key))
            _apply_tab_styles()

            try:
                from client_utils import run_on_queue
                run_on_queue(_load_preview)
            except Exception:
                threading.Thread(target=_load_preview, daemon=True).start()

            try:
                run_on_ui_thread(sheet.show)
            except Exception:
                sheet.show()
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"show assist sheet fail: {e}")

    def _has_entities(self, params):
        try:
            for key in ("entities", "messageEntities", "captionEntities"):
                ent = getattr(params, key, None)
                if ent is not None and len(ent) > 0:
                    return True
        except Exception:
            pass
        return False

    def _is_link_only(self, text):
        try:
            t = str(text or "").strip()
            if not t:
                return True
            no_urls = re.sub(r"(https?://\\S+|www\\.\\S+)", "", t, flags=re.IGNORECASE).strip()
            no_punct = re.sub(r"[\\s\\.,;:!?()\"'\\[\\]{}<>]+", "", no_urls)
            return no_punct == ""
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _is_emoji_only(self, text):
        try:
            t = str(text or "").strip()
            if not t:
                return True
            pat = re.compile(r"^[\\s\\U0001F300-\\U0001FAFF\\u2600-\\u27BF\\uFE0F\\u200D]+$")
            return bool(pat.match(t))
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _should_skip_text(self, text, params):
        t = str(text or "").strip()
        if not t:
            return True
        if t.startswith("/") or t.startswith("."):
            return True
        if self._is_link_only(t):
            self._dlog("skip: link-only")
            return True
        if self._is_emoji_only(t):
            self._dlog("skip: emoji-only")
            return True
        return False

    def _extract_entities_for_text(self, params, using_caption):
        keys = ("captionEntities", "entities", "messageEntities") if using_caption else ("entities", "messageEntities", "captionEntities")
        for k in keys:
            try:
                v = getattr(params, k, None)
                if v is not None and len(v) > 0:
                    return v
            except Exception:
                pass
        return None

    def _entities_to_markdown(self, text, entities):
        try:
            if not entities or not text:
                return text
            res = list(str(text))
            ents = list(entities)
            ents = sorted(ents, key=lambda e: int(getattr(e, "offset", 0)), reverse=True)
            for e in ents:
                try:
                    start = int(getattr(e, "offset", 0))
                    end = start + int(getattr(e, "length", 0))
                    if start < 0 or end < start or end > len(res):
                        continue
                    et = str(e.__class__.__name__)
                    if "Bold" in et:
                        res.insert(end, "*")
                        res.insert(start, "*")
                    elif "Italic" in et:
                        res.insert(end, "_")
                        res.insert(start, "_")
                    elif "Underline" in et:
                        res.insert(end, "__")
                        res.insert(start, "__")
                    elif "Strike" in et:
                        res.insert(end, "~")
                        res.insert(start, "~")
                    elif "Spoiler" in et:
                        res.insert(end, "||")
                        res.insert(start, "||")
                    elif "Code" in et and "Pre" not in et:
                        res.insert(end, "`")
                        res.insert(start, "`")
                    elif "Pre" in et:
                        lang = str(getattr(e, "language", "") or "")
                        res.insert(end, "```")
                        res.insert(start, f"```{lang}\n" if lang else "```")
                    elif "TextUrl" in et:
                        url = str(getattr(e, "url", "") or "")
                        res.insert(end, f"]({url})")
                        res.insert(start, "[")
                    elif "CustomEmoji" in et:
                        doc_id = str(getattr(e, "document_id", "") or "")
                        if doc_id:
                            res.insert(end, f"]({doc_id})")
                            res.insert(start, "[")
                except Exception:
                    pass
            return "".join(res)
        except Exception:
            return str(text or "")

    def _parse_markdown_to_entities(self, text):
        try:
            from markdown_utils import parse_markdown
            parsed = parse_markdown(str(text or ""))
            ents = []
            try:
                for raw in list(getattr(parsed, "entities", []) or []):
                    try:
                        ents.append(raw.to_tlrpc_object())
                    except Exception:
                        pass
            except Exception:
                pass
            return str(getattr(parsed, "text", "") or ""), ents
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"markdown parse unavailable/fail: {e}")
            return str(text or ""), []

    def _apply_outgoing_entities(self, params, using_caption, entities):
        try:
            j_ents = ArrayList()
            for ent in entities or []:
                try:
                    j_ents.add(ent)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            try:
                params.entities = j_ents
            except Exception:
                pass
            if using_caption:
                try:
                    params.captionEntities = j_ents
                except Exception:
                    pass
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"apply entities fail: {e}")

    def _mask_urls_for_translate(self, source_text):
        urls = []
        def _url_repl(match):
            idx = len(urls)
            urls.append(match.group(0))
            return f" __TL_URL_{idx}__ "
        masked = re.sub(r"(https?://\\S+|www\\.\\S+)", _url_repl, str(source_text or ""), flags=re.IGNORECASE)
        return masked, urls

    def _restore_masked_urls(self, translated_text, urls):
        out = str(translated_text or "")
        for i, u in enumerate(urls or []):
            out = out.replace(f"__TL_URL_{i}__", u)
        return out

    def _translate_text_google(self, text, dst):
        try:
            source_text = str(text or "")
            masked, urls = self._mask_urls_for_translate(source_text)
            url = (
                "https://translate.googleapis.com/translate_a/single"
                f"?client=gtx&sl=auto&tl={url_quote(dst)}"
                "&dt=t&ie=UTF-8&oe=UTF-8&otf=1&ssel=0&tsel=0&kc=7"
                "&dt=at&dt=bd&dt=ex&dt=ld&dt=md&dt=qca&dt=rw&dt=rm&dt=ss"
                f"&q={url_quote(masked)}"
            )
            req = Request(url, headers={"User-Agent": "TranslaticaLite/1.0"})
            with urlopen(req, timeout=15) as resp:
                raw = resp.read().decode("utf-8", errors="replace")
            data = json.loads(raw)
            blocks = data[0] if isinstance(data, list) and len(data) > 0 else []
            parts = []
            for b in blocks:
                try:
                    p = b[0]
                    if p is not None and str(p) != "null":
                        parts.append(str(p))
                except Exception:
                    pass
            out = "".join(parts).strip()
            out = self._restore_masked_urls(out, urls)
            self._dlog(f"translate google ok dst={dst} len_out={len(out)}")
            return out if out else None
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"translate google fail: {e}")
            return None

    def _translate_text_native(self, text, dst, wait_sec=None):
        try:
            source_text = str(text or "")
            if not source_text:
                return None
            masked, urls = self._mask_urls_for_translate(source_text)

            TLRPC = find_class("org.telegram.tgnet.TLRPC")
            ConnectionsManager = find_class("org.telegram.tgnet.ConnectionsManager")
            RequestDelegate = find_class("org.telegram.tgnet.RequestDelegate")
            if TLRPC is None or ConnectionsManager is None or RequestDelegate is None:
                self._dlog("translate native unavailable classes")
                return None

            req = TLRPC.TL_messages_translateText()
            req.flags |= 2
            req.to_lang = str(dst or "en")

            te = TLRPC.TL_textWithEntities()
            te.text = masked
            te.entities = ArrayList()
            req.text.add(te)

            state = {"out": None, "err": None}
            done = threading.Event()

            class _ReqDelegate(dynamic_proxy(RequestDelegate)):
                def run(self_obj, response, error):
                    try:
                        if error is not None:
                            state["err"] = str(getattr(error, "text", "") or "native_error")
                            return
                        if response is None:
                            state["err"] = "native_null_response"
                            return
                        result = getattr(response, "result", None)
                        if result is None or result.size() <= 0:
                            state["err"] = "native_empty_result"
                            return
                        first = result.get(0)
                        translated = str(getattr(first, "text", "") or "").strip()
                        if translated:
                            state["out"] = translated
                        else:
                            state["err"] = "native_empty_text"
                    except Exception as _e:
                        state["err"] = str(_e)
                    finally:
                        done.set()

            account = int(UserConfig.selectedAccount)
            ConnectionsManager.getInstance(account).sendRequest(req, _ReqDelegate())
            timeout_sec = float(wait_sec or 12)
            if timeout_sec < 4:
                timeout_sec = 4
            if not done.wait(timeout_sec):
                self._dlog("translate native timeout")
                return None
            if not state["out"]:
                self._dlog(f"translate native fail: {state['err']}")
                return None

            out = self._restore_masked_urls(state["out"], urls)
            self._dlog(f"translate native ok dst={dst} len_out={len(out)}")
            return out if out else None
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"translate native error: {e}")
            return None

    def _translate_text(self, text, dst):
        mode = str(self._translate_service_mode() or "appleai").strip().lower()

        if mode == "translatica":
            return self._translate_text_google(text, dst)

        if mode == "alternative":
            return self._translate_text_google(text, dst)

        if mode == "appleai":
            native_res = self._translate_text_native(text, dst)
            if native_res:
                return native_res
            self._dlog(f"translate {mode} fallback -> google")
            return self._translate_text_google(text, dst)

        txt = str(text or "")
        if len(txt) <= 220:
            native_res = self._translate_text_native(txt, dst)
            if native_res:
                return native_res
            self._dlog("translate dynamic fallback native -> google")
            return self._translate_text_google(txt, dst)

        google_res = self._translate_text_google(txt, dst)
        if google_res:
            return google_res
        self._dlog("translate dynamic fallback google -> native")
        return self._translate_text_native(txt, dst)

    def create_settings(self):
        try:
            run_on_ui_thread(self._maybe_show_first_install_welcome)
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            self._migrate_target_lang_index_order()
        except Exception:
            pass
        idx = 0
        pidx = 0
        try:
            idx = int(self.get_setting("tlite_target_lang", 0) or 0)
        except Exception:
            idx = 0
        if idx < 0 or idx >= len(LANG_LABELS):
            idx = 0
        try:
            pidx = int(self.get_setting("tlite_plugin_lang", 0) or 0)
        except Exception:
            pidx = 0
        if pidx < 0 or pidx >= len(PLUGIN_LANG_OPTIONS):
            pidx = 0
        sidx = self._translate_service_index()
        items = [
            Divider(),
            Selector(
                key="tlite_target_lang",
                text=self._tr("settings_target_lang"),
                items=LANG_LABELS,
                default=idx,
                icon="msg_language",
                on_change=lambda i: self._on_target_lang_changed(i),
            ),
            Selector(
                key="tlite_service",
                text=self._tr("settings_translate_service"),
                items=self._translate_service_option_labels(),
                default=sidx,
                icon="msg_arrow_avatar",
                on_change=lambda i: self.set_setting("tlite_service", str(SERVICE_OPTIONS[int(i)][0])),
            ),
            Selector(
                key="tlite_channel_summary_provider",
                text=self._tr("ai_sheet_summary"),
                items=self._channel_summary_provider_options(),
                default=self._channel_summary_provider_index(),
                icon="premium_ai_editor",
                on_change=lambda i: self.set_setting("tlite_channel_summary_provider", int(i)),
            ),
            Divider(text=self._tr("settings_channel_summary_intro")),
            Text(
                text="Assist",
                subtext=self._tr("settings_ai_custom_open_desc"),
                icon="ai_chat_remix",
                create_sub_fragment=self._create_ai_correction_subfragment,
                link_alias="tlite_ai_correction_subfragment",
            ),
            Text(
                text=self._tr("settings_ai_avatar_tools"),
                subtext=self._tr("settings_ai_avatar_tools_desc"),
                icon="tabs_chats_solar",
                create_sub_fragment=self._create_avatar_ai_tools_subfragment,
                link_alias="tlite_ai_avatar_tools_subfragment",
            ),
            Text(
                text="Core",
                subtext=self._tr("settings_performance_open_desc"),
                icon="boosts",
                create_sub_fragment=self._create_performance_subfragment,
                link_alias="tlite_performance_subfragment",
            ),
            Text(
                text="Insights",
                subtext=self._tr("settings_usage_stats_open_desc"),
                icon="msg_stats_solar",
                create_sub_fragment=self._create_usage_stats_subfragment,
                link_alias="tlite_usage_stats_subfragment",
            ),
            Divider(),
            Selector(
                key="tlite_plugin_lang",
                text=self._tr("settings_plugin_lang"),
                items=[x[0] for x in PLUGIN_LANG_OPTIONS],
                default=pidx,
                icon="msg_plugins_solar",
                on_change=lambda i: self._on_plugin_lang_selector_changed(i),
            ),
        ]
        items.append(
            Text(
                text=self._tr("settings_about"),
                icon="msg2_reactions2",
                on_click=self._on_about_click,
            )
        )
        return items

    def _create_performance_subfragment(self, parent_view=None):
        items = [Divider(text=self._tr("settings_performance_intro"))]
        for item_key, text_key, desc_key, flag, icon_name in self._performance_toggle_defs():
            current_enabled = bool(self._lite_mode_optimization_enabled(flag))
            items.append(
                Switch(
                    key=item_key,
                    text=self._tr(text_key),
                    subtext=self._tr(desc_key),
                    default=current_enabled,
                    icon=icon_name,
                    on_change=lambda value, lite_flag=flag: self._set_lite_mode_optimization(lite_flag, bool(value)),
                )
            )
        return items

    def _create_usage_stats_subfragment(self, parent_view=None):
        items = [Divider(text=self._tr("settings_usage_stats_intro"))]
        if not self._usage_stats_enabled():
            items.append(Divider(text=self._tr("settings_usage_stats_empty")))
            return items
        lang_rows = self._usage_stats_language_rows(5)
        chat_rows = self._usage_stats_chat_rows(5)
        items.append(Divider(text=self._tr("settings_usage_stats_languages")))
        if lang_rows:
            for row in lang_rows:
                items.append(
                    Text(
                        text=str(row.get("label", "")).strip(),
                        subtext=f"{int(row.get('percent', 0) or 0)}% • {int(row.get('count', 0) or 0)}",
                        icon="msg_language",
                    )
                )
        else:
            items.append(
                Text(
                    text=self._tr("settings_usage_stats_languages"),
                    subtext=self._tr("settings_usage_stats_empty"),
                    icon="msg_language",
                )
            )
        items.append(Divider(text=self._tr("settings_usage_stats_chats")))
        if chat_rows:
            for row in chat_rows:
                items.append(
                    Text(
                        text=str(row.get("title", "")).strip(),
                        subtext=f"{int(row.get('percent', 0) or 0)}% • {int(row.get('count', 0) or 0)}",
                        icon="msg_groups_new2",
                    )
                )
        else:
            items.append(
                Text(
                    text=self._tr("settings_usage_stats_chats"),
                    subtext=self._tr("settings_usage_stats_empty"),
                    icon="msg_groups_new2",
                )
            )
        return items

    def _setup_dialogs_push_hooks(self):
        try:
            cls = JClass.forName("org.telegram.ui.DialogsActivity")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"DialogsActivity resolve fail: {e}")
            return
        try:
            ctx_cls = find_class("android.content.Context")
            m = cls.getDeclaredMethod("createView", ctx_cls)
            m.setAccessible(True)
            self._hooks.append(self.hook_method(m, TLLiteDialogsCreateHook(self)))
            self._dlog("hook dialogs createView ok")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"hook dialogs createView fail: {e}")
        try:
            m = cls.getDeclaredMethod("onResume")
            m.setAccessible(True)
            self._hooks.append(self.hook_method(m, TLLiteDialogsResumeHook(self)))
            self._dlog("hook dialogs onResume ok")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"hook dialogs onResume fail: {e}")
        try:
            m = cls.getDeclaredMethod("onPause")
            m.setAccessible(True)
            self._hooks.append(self.hook_method(m, TLLiteDialogsPauseHook(self)))
            self._dlog("hook dialogs onPause ok")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"hook dialogs onPause fail: {e}")

    def _setup_chat_hooks(self):
        try:

        except Exception as e:

        try:

            self._dlog(f"hook chat createView fail: {e}")
        try:
            m = cls.getDeclaredMethod("onResume")
            m.setAccessible(True)
            self._hooks.append(self.hook_method(m, TLLiteChatResumeHook(self)))
            self._dlog("hook chat onResume ok")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"hook chat onResume fail: {e}")
        try:
            m = cls.getDeclaredMethod("onPause")
            m.setAccessible(True)
            self._hooks.append(self.hook_method(m, TLLiteChatPauseHook(self)))
            self._dlog("hook chat onPause ok")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"hook chat onPause fail: {e}")

    def _setup_avatar_action_hooks(self):
        try:
            dcls = find_class("org.telegram.ui.ChatActivity$ChatMessageCellDelegate")
            if dcls is None:
                self._dlog("avatar action hooks skipped: no ChatMessageCellDelegate")
                return
            methods = []
            try:
                methods = dcls.getDeclaredMethods()
            except Exception:
                try:
                    methods = dcls.getClass().getDeclaredMethods()
                except Exception:
                    methods = []
            user_long = None
            channel_long = None
            for m in methods:
                try:
                    n = str(m.getName() or "")
                    if n == "didLongPressUserAvatar" and user_long is None:
                        user_long = m
                    elif n == "didLongPressChannelAvatar" and channel_long is None:
                        channel_long = m
                except Exception:
                    pass
            if user_long is not None:
                try:
                    user_long.setAccessible(True)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                ref = self.hook_method(user_long, TLLiteAvatarLongUserHook(self), priority=2147483647)
                if ref is not None:
                    self._hooks.append(ref)
                    self._dlog("hook avatar user long ok")
            if channel_long is not None:
                try:
                    channel_long.setAccessible(True)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                ref = self.hook_method(channel_long, TLLiteAvatarLongChannelHook(self), priority=2147483647)
                if ref is not None:
                    self._hooks.append(ref)
                    self._dlog("hook avatar channel long ok")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"setup avatar action hooks fail: {e}")

    def _setup_message_context_hooks(self):
        try:
            cls = JClass.forName("org.telegram.ui.ChatActivity")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"message context ChatActivity resolve fail: {e}")
            return
        try:
            methods = cls.getDeclaredMethods()
        except Exception:
            methods = []
        for m in methods:
            try:
                if str(m.getName() or "") != "createMenu":
                    continue
                params = m.getParameterTypes()
                if params is None or len(params) < 6:
                    continue
                m.setAccessible(True)
                ref = self.hook_method(m, TLLiteMessageContextMenuHook(self))
                if ref is not None:
                    self._hooks.append(ref)
                    self._dlog("hook message context createMenu ok")
                    return
            except Exception:
                pass
        self._dlog("hook message context createMenu skipped")

    def _setup_favorite_incoming_hooks(self):
        try:
            cell_cls = find_class("org.telegram.ui.Cells.ChatMessageCell")
            if cell_cls is not None:
                refs = self.hook_all_methods(cell_cls, "setMessageObject", TLLiteFavoriteIncomingCellHook(self))
                if refs:
                    self._hooks.append(refs)
                    self._dlog("hook favorite incoming cell ok")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"hook favorite incoming cell fail: {e}")
        try:
            mo_cls = find_class("org.telegram.messenger.MessageObject")
            if mo_cls is not None:
                refs = self.hook_all_methods(mo_cls, "updateTranslation", TLLiteFavoriteTranslationGuardHook(self))
                if refs:
                    self._hooks.append(refs)
                    self._dlog("hook favorite translation guard ok")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"hook favorite translation guard fail: {e}")

    def _setup_native_assist_hooks(self):
        try:
            cls = JClass.forName("org.telegram.ui.Components.ChatActivityEnterView")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"native assist hooks resolve fail: {e}")
            return
        try:
            methods = cls.getDeclaredMethods()
        except Exception:
            methods = []
        for method in methods:
            try:
                if str(method.getName() or "") != "onSendLongClick":
                    continue
                params = method.getParameterTypes()
                if params is None or len(params) != 1:
                    continue
                method.setAccessible(True)
                ref = self.hook_method(method, TLLiteSendLongClickHook(self), priority=2147483647)
                if ref is not None:
                    self._hooks.append(ref)
                    self._dlog("hook native assist send long ok")
                    return
            except Exception:
                pass
        self._dlog("hook native assist send long skipped")

    def on_plugin_load(self):
        self._dlog("plugin load")
        self._load_telemetry_queue()
        self._load_usage_stats()
        try:
            self.add_on_send_message_hook()
            self._dlog("send hook registered")
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"failed to register send hook: {e}")
        self._load_favorite_sender_ids()
        self._load_favorite_incoming_cache()
        self._setup_dialogs_push_hooks()
        self._setup_chat_hooks()
        self._setup_avatar_action_hooks()
        self._setup_message_context_hooks()
        self._setup_favorite_incoming_hooks()
        self._setup_native_assist_hooks()
        self._setup_settings_header_hook()
        self._add_menu_items()
        self._load_translations_from_plugin_file()
        self._load_translations_local()
        try:
            def _boot_sync():
                try:
                    self._sync_translations()
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    self._sync_assets()
                except Exception:
                    pass
            threading.Timer(0.9, lambda: threading.Thread(target=_boot_sync, daemon=True).start()).start()
        except Exception:
            try:
                threading.Thread(target=lambda: (self._sync_translations(), self._sync_assets()), daemon=True).start()
            except Exception:
                pass
        try:
            run_on_ui_thread(self._maybe_show_first_install_welcome)
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            self._telemetry_queue_event("session_start", feature="", count=1, force_flush=True)
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            if not bool(self.get_setting("tlite_stats_install_event_sent_v1", False)):
                self._telemetry_queue_event("install", feature="", count=1, force_flush=True)
                self.set_setting("tlite_stats_install_event_sent_v1", True)
        except Exception:
            pass

    def on_plugin_unload(self):
        self._dlog("plugin unload")
        try:
            self._push_on_dialogs_hidden()
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            for h in list(self._hooks):
                try:
                    self.unhook_method(h)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            self._hooks = []
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            if self._settings_header_hook:
                self.unhook_method(self._settings_header_hook)
                self._settings_header_hook = None
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            if self._chat_menu_item:
                self.remove_menu_item(self._chat_menu_item)
                self._chat_menu_item = None
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            if self._chat_floating_menu_item:
                self.remove_menu_item(self._chat_floating_menu_item)
                self._chat_floating_menu_item = None
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            if self._chat_logs_menu_item:
                self.remove_menu_item(self._chat_logs_menu_item)
                self._chat_logs_menu_item = None
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            if self._favorite_incoming_dirty:
                self._save_favorite_incoming_cache_now()
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            if self._usage_stats_dirty:
                self._save_usage_stats_now()
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            run_on_ui_thread(self._detach_apple_button)
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            run_on_ui_thread(self._detach_floating_button)
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            run_on_ui_thread(self._detach_assist_button)
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            self._remove_live_log()
        except Exception:
            pass
        try:
            self._telemetry_flush_async()
        except Exception:
            pass

    def on_send_message_hook(self, account, params):
        try:
            if self._suppress_next_hook:
                self._suppress_next_hook = False
                return HookResult(strategy=HookStrategy.DEFAULT)
            if self._preview_pending_send:
                try:
                    pending = self._preview_pending_send or {}
                    self._preview_pending_send = None
                    using_caption = bool(str(getattr(params, "caption", "") or "").strip())
                    final_text = str(pending.get("text") or "")
                    final_entities = list(pending.get("entities") or [])
                    if using_caption:
                        params.caption = final_text
                    else:
                        params.message = final_text
                    if final_entities:
                        self._apply_outgoing_entities(params, using_caption, final_entities)
                    try:
                        frag = get_last_fragment()
                    except Exception:
                        frag = getattr(self, "_chat_fragment_ref", None)
                    try:
                        self._refresh_compose_after_programmatic_text(frag)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        self._post_send_compose_cleanup(frag, final_text)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    return HookResult(strategy=HookStrategy.MODIFY, params=params)
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"live preview pending send fail: {e}")
            if self._assist_pending_send:
                try:
                    pending = self._assist_pending_send or {}
                    self._assist_pending_send = None
                    using_caption = bool(str(getattr(params, "caption", "") or "").strip())
                    final_text = str(pending.get("text") or "")
                    final_entities = list(pending.get("entities") or [])
                    if using_caption:
                        params.caption = final_text
                    else:
                        params.message = final_text
                    if final_entities:
                        self._apply_outgoing_entities(params, using_caption, final_entities)
                    try:
                        frag = get_last_fragment()
                    except Exception:
                        frag = getattr(self, "_chat_fragment_ref", None)
                    try:
                        self._refresh_compose_after_programmatic_text(frag)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        self._post_send_compose_cleanup(frag, final_text)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    return HookResult(strategy=HookStrategy.MODIFY, params=params)
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"assist pending send fail: {e}")
            if self._skip_next_translation_send:
                self._skip_next_translation_send = False
                return HookResult(strategy=HookStrategy.DEFAULT)

            try:
                raw_msg = None
                if hasattr(params, "message") and isinstance(params.message, str):
                    raw_msg = params.message
                elif isinstance(params, dict):
                    mv = params.get("message", None)
                    if isinstance(mv, str):
                        raw_msg = mv
                if isinstance(raw_msg, str):
                    cmd = raw_msg.strip().lower()
                    first_token = (cmd.split(" ", 1)[0] if cmd else "")
                    if (
                        first_token == "!lite"
                        or first_token.startswith("!lite@")
                        or first_token == ".lite"
                        or first_token.startswith(".lite@")
                    ):
                        try:
                            params.message = ""
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        try:
                            params["message"] = ""
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        try:
                            run_on_ui_thread(self._open_plugin_settings)
                        except Exception:
                            self._open_plugin_settings()
                        return HookResult(strategy=HookStrategy.CANCEL)
            except Exception as e:
                self._dlog(f"command parse fail: {e}")

            if not bool(self.get_setting("tlite_enabled", True)):
                return HookResult()

            text = str(getattr(params, "caption", "") or "").strip()
            using_caption = bool(text)
            if not text:
                text = str(getattr(params, "message", "") or "")

            if self._should_skip_text(text, params):
                return HookResult()

            did = self._extract_dialog_id(params=params, fragment=self._chat_fragment_ref)
            if not did:
                try:
                    did = int(getattr(self, "_chat_dialog_id_ref", 0) or 0)
                except Exception:
                    did = 0
            if not did:
                self._dlog("send hook skipped: unresolved dialog id")
                return HookResult()
            cfg = self._chat_config(did)
            if not bool(cfg.get("enabled", True)):
                return HookResult()
            dst = str(cfg.get("lang") or self._global_target_lang())
            self._dlog(f"resolved target={dst} did={did}")
            entities_orig = self._extract_entities_for_text(params, using_caption)

            try:
                from client_utils import run_on_queue, get_send_messages_helper
            except Exception as e:
                self._dlog(f"queue api unavailable, fallback sync: {e}")
                source_for_translate = self._entities_to_markdown(text, entities_orig) if entities_orig else text
                translated = self._translate_text(source_for_translate, dst)
                if not translated:
                    BulletinHelper.show_error(self._tr("bulletin_failed"))
                    return HookResult()
                try:
                    self._usage_stats_record("send", dst, did)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    self._telemetry_queue_event("feature_use", feature="translate_send", count=1, force_flush=False)
                except Exception:
                    pass
                parsed_text, parsed_entities = self._parse_markdown_to_entities(translated) if entities_orig else (translated, [])
                if using_caption:
                    params.caption = parsed_text
                else:
                    params.message = parsed_text
                if entities_orig and parsed_entities:
                    self._apply_outgoing_entities(params, using_caption, parsed_entities)
                return HookResult(strategy=HookStrategy.MODIFY, params=params)

            def _translate_and_send():
                source_for_translate = self._entities_to_markdown(text, entities_orig) if entities_orig else text
                translated = self._translate_text(source_for_translate, dst)
                if translated:
                    try:
                        self._usage_stats_record("send", dst, did)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        self._telemetry_queue_event("feature_use", feature="translate_send", count=1, force_flush=False)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    try:
                        parsed_text, parsed_entities = self._parse_markdown_to_entities(translated) if entities_orig else (translated, [])
                        if using_caption:
                            params.caption = parsed_text
                        else:
                            params.message = parsed_text
                        if entities_orig and parsed_entities:
                            self._apply_outgoing_entities(params, using_caption, parsed_entities)
                    except Exception as e:
                        self._dlog(f"apply translated text fail: {e}")
                else:
                    self._dlog("translation returned empty, sending original")
                try:
                    self._suppress_next_hook = True
                except Exception:
                    pass
                try:
                    run_on_ui_thread(lambda: get_send_messages_helper().sendMessage(params))
                except Exception as e:
                    self._dlog(f"sendMessage error: {e}")

            run_on_queue(_translate_and_send)
            return HookResult(strategy=HookStrategy.CANCEL)
        except Exception as e:
            self._dlog(f"hook error: {e}")
            return HookResult()
